"书名白猿（约翰·高尔斯华绥《现代喜剧》三部曲之一）短简介迈克尔和弗勒，一个是贵族子弟，一个是名门望族的大小姐，他们的婚姻表面上令人称羡，实际却是暗潮汹涌。小说中的那幅中国名画《白猿》恰好是外表光鲜、内在腐朽的上层社会的写照——他们目光贪婪、恐惧，不顾一切地想把一切都攥在手中。长简介约翰·高尔斯华绥的长篇小说《白猿》是《现代喜剧》三部曲的第一部。小说通过对比两对身处不同的社会阶层的夫妻，揭示了在特定社会背景下，上流社会的腐朽虚荣和贫民阶级的痛苦和无奈。迈克尔和弗勒，贵族子弟和名门望族的联姻，表面上丰衣足食、令人称羡，实际却是貌合神离、同床异梦；托尼和维多琳一贫如洗、相濡以沫，却只能牺牲自己换取两人安稳度日的梦想，而那梦想也像蓝色蝴蝶，可望而不可即……小说中的那幅画《白猿》恰好是外表光鲜、内在腐朽的上层社会的写照——他们目光贪婪、恐惧，不顾一切地想把一切都攥在手中。关键字白猿；约翰·高尔斯华绥；外研社编译组；长篇；讽刺；小说；资产阶级作者（英）约翰·高尔斯华绥作者简介约翰·高尔斯华绥（1867-1933），英国小说家、剧作家，生于伦敦，曾在牛津大学读法律，后放弃律师工作从事文学创作。1906年出版长篇小说《有产业的人》，获得广泛好评，他也因此而被公认为英国第一流作家。高尔斯华绥最为人称道的是他的三个三部曲：《福尔赛世家》、《现代喜剧》和《尾声》，其中以《福尔赛世家》最为知名，他也凭此于1932年获得诺贝尔文学奖。书评他的作品语言简练、形象生动、讽刺辛辣。    在一个渐渐走向腐朽的社会，人人都贪婪、虚荣，不顾一切地想把一切都攥在手中。"
"The White Monkey","白猿"
"by John Galsworthy","作者：约翰·高尔斯华绥"

"Part I","第一卷"
"“No retreat, no retreat.They must conquer or die Who have no retreat!”","“没有退路，没有退路。没有退路的人必须获胜，否则就是死路一条！”"
"Mr. Gay.","盖伊先生"
"Chapter I","第一章"
"Promenade","散步"
"Coming down the steps of ‘Snooks’ Club, so nicknamed by George Forsyte in the late eighties, on that momentous mid-October afternoon of 1922, Sir Lawrence Mont, ninth baronet, set his fine nose towards the east wind, and moved his thin legs with speed.","1922年10月中旬的那个重要的下午，第九代准男爵劳伦斯·蒙特爵士迎着东风翘着俊美的鼻子，迈着两条细腿疾步走下“轻蔑”俱乐部的台阶——俱乐部这一绰号出自上世纪80年代末乔治·福赛特之口。"
"Political by birth rather than by nature, he reviewed the revolution which had restored his Party to power with a detachment not devoid of humour.","他虽出生于政治世家，却对政治不感兴趣，提起他所在的政党重夺政权的那次革命，他只是轻描淡写。"
"Passing the Remove Club, he thought: ‘Some sweating into shoes, there!","路过利姆夫俱乐部时，他想：“这次麻烦啦！"
"No more confectioned dishes.","再也没有甜点可吃啦。"
"A woodcock—without trimmings, for a change!’","山鹬没有了配料，得变口味喽！”"
"The captains and the kings had departed from ‘Snooks’ before he entered it, for he was not of ‘that catch-penny crew, now paid off, no sir; fellows who turned their tails on the land the moment the war was over. Pah!’","在他进入“轻蔑”俱乐部之前，那些大老板和王公贵族们早已离开，因为他并不属于“想方设法捞钱，而且已经捞个够本的那帮家伙，他绝不是那种人——那帮家伙在战争刚刚结束时就丢弃家园逃之夭夭了。呸！”"
"But for an hour he had listened to echoes, and his lively twisting mind, embedded in deposits of the past, sceptical of the present and of all political protestations and pronouncements, had recorded with amusement the confusion of patriotism and personalities left behind by the fateful gathering.","可是对过去忘事的回忆，他足足听了一个小时。他的大脑活跃地转动着，牢记往事，怀疑当下，也怀疑一切政治主张和声明。他饶有兴致地记录了这次意义重大的集会上所留下的爱国主义和个体攻击的混乱。"
"Like most landowners, he distrusted doctrine.","和大部分地主一样，他不相信教条。"
"If he had a political belief, it was a tax on wheat; and so far as he could see, he was now alone in it—but then he was not seeking election; in other words, his principle was not in danger of extinction from the votes of those who had to pay for bread.","如果非要说他有政治信仰的话，那就是征收小麦税了，并且就他所知，他势单力薄——但是，对他来说，选票不重要；换句话说，平民百姓的选票威胁不到他笃信的原则。"
"Principles—he mused—au fond were pocket; and he wished the deuce people wouldn’t pretend they weren’t!","原则——他沉思着——就是钱罢了。他真希望人们不要再装作不承认这一点了！"
"Pocket, in the deep sense of that word, of course, self-interest as member of a definite community.","当然，从深层含义来讲，钱无非就是特定社会群体成员的个人利益。"
"And how the devil was this definite community, the English nation, to exist, when all its land was going out of cultivation, and all its ships and docks in danger of destruction by aeroplanes?","而当它所有的土地都荒芜，所有的船只和港口都面临被飞机炸毁的危险时，这个特定社会群体——英国民族，倒是有什么办法生存下去啊？"
"He had listened that hour past for a single mention of the land.","在一个小时的倾听中，他希望听到有人谈及土地。"
"Not one!","竟无一人谈及！"
"It was not practical politics!","这根本不是实用政治！"
"Confound the fellows!","这帮该死的家伙！"
"They had to wear their breeches out—keeping seats or getting them.","他们不惜磨破了裤子——就为了保住席位或获得席位。"
"No connection between posteriors and posterity!","丝毫没考虑过子孙后代！"
"No, by George!","的确没有！"
"Thus reminded of posterity, it occurred to him rather suddenly that his son’s wife showed no signs as yet.","说起后代，他突然想起自己的儿媳至今还没有一点点的喜照。"
"Two years!","两年了！"
"Time they were thinking about children.","该是要孩子的时候了。"
"It was dangerous to get into the habit of not having them, when a title and estate depended.","不要孩子如果成为一种习惯，对于那些有爵位或是需要产业继承人的家庭来说是相当可怕的。"
"A smile twisted his lips and eyebrows which resembled spinneys of dark pothooks.","一丝微笑牵动了他的双唇和眉毛，那两道弯眉异常浓密。"
"A pretty young creature, most taking; and knew it, too!","一个漂亮的小孩，非常可爱，而且她也深知这一点啊！"
"Whom was she not getting to know?","有谁她不想去认识呢？"
"Lions and tigers, monkeys and cats—her house was becoming quite a menagerie of more or less celebrities.","狮子、老虎、猴子和猫——她的家成了这些大小名人的动物园了。"
"There was a certain unreality about that sort of thing!","这种事情总是有种不真实的感觉！"
"And opposite a British lion in Trafalgar Square Sir Lawrence thought: ‘She’ll be getting these to her house next!","劳伦斯爵士站在特拉法尔加广场上的一只不列颠之狮的对面，心里想：“下次她会把这些都弄到家里去！"
"She’s got the collecting habit.","她染上收藏的嗜好了。"
"Michael must look out—in a collector’s house there’s always a lumber room for old junk, and husbands are liable to get into it.","迈克尔必须小心了——收藏家的家里肯定有一间专门放置破旧货的储藏室，而丈夫是很容易被关进去的。"
"That reminds me: I promised her a Chinese Minister.","这倒提醒了我：我曾答应给她介绍一位中国公使。"
"Well, she must wait now till after the General Election.’","好吧，如今她得等到大选过后了。”"
"Down Whitehall, under the grey easterly sky, the towers of Westminster came for a second into view.","沿着白厅大街往南走，在东方灰色的天空下，威斯敏斯特教堂的塔楼瞬间映入眼帘。"
"‘A certain unreality in that, too,’ he thought.","“那里面似乎也有种不真实的东西，”他想，"
"‘Michael and his fads!","“迈克尔和他的狂热爱好！"
"Well, it’s the fashion—Socialistic principles and a rich wife.","哦，这的确是一种时尚——社会主义的原则和一个富有的妻子。"
"Sacrifice with safety!","有所牺牲但又很安全！"
"Peace with plenty!","和平且富足！"
"Nostrums—ten a penny!’","万能灵药——一便士十粒！"
"Passing the newspaper hubbub of Charing Cross, frenzied by the political crisis, he turned up to the left towards Danby and Winter, publishers, where his son was junior partner.","查林十字广场上买卖报纸的喧哗由于这次政治危机变得更加嘈杂。他穿过广场向左拐，朝丹比&温特出版社走去，他的儿子是那里的第二合伙人。"
"A new theme for a book had just begun to bend a mind which had already produced a ‘Life of Montrose,’ ‘Far Cathay,’ that work of Eastern travel, and a fanciful conversation between the shades of Gladstone and Disraeli—entitled ‘A Duet.’","他已经出版了《蒙特罗斯传》一书、一部东方游记《遥远的契丹》以及《二重唱》。《二重唱》是描述格莱斯顿和迪斯雷利两个幽灵之间的幻想谈话。如今他又开始专心筹备新书了。"
"With every step taken, from ‘Snooks’ eastward, his erect thin figure in Astrakhan-collared coat, his thin grey-moustached face, and tortoise-shell rimmed monocle under the lively dark eyebrow, had seemed more rare.","他身材挺拔细长，身着阿斯特拉罕皮领外衣，瘦削的脸上留着灰白胡子，生动的浓眉下架着玳瑁边的单片眼镜。他从“轻蔑”俱乐部出来往东走，每走一步，都显得更加与众不同。"
"It became almost a phenomenon in this dingy back street, where carts stuck like winter flies, and persons went by with books under their arms, as if educated.","在这条肮脏的后街上，车辆犹如冬天里的苍蝇一般紧挨着，人们夹着书本穿梭其中，看上去似乎很有学问。在这里，像他这样的人物极为引人注目。","像他这样的人物极为引人注目 翻译不准确"
"He had nearly reached the door of Danby’s when he encountered two young men.","快到丹比出版社时，他遇到了两位年轻人。"
"One of them was clearly his son, better dressed since his marriage, and smoking a cigar—thank goodness—instead of those eternal cigarettes; the other—ah! yes—Michael’s sucking poet and best man, head in air, rather a sleek head under a velour hat!","其中一位很明显是他的儿子。自从结婚后，他儿子的打扮比以前讲究一些了，这会儿正吸着一支雪茄——谢天谢地——吸的不是那种没完没了的烟卷；另一位——啊，没错——是迈克尔不成气候的诗人朋友和结婚时的男傧相，他头昂得高高的，活像个油头滑脑的家伙！"
"He said:","他说道："
"“Ha, Michael!”","“嗨，迈克尔！”"
"“HALLO, Bart!","“你好，准爵爷！"
"You know my governor, Wilfrid?","威尔弗里德，你认识我爸爸吧？"
"Wilfrid Desert.","这是威尔弗里德·德赛特。"
"‘Copper Coin’—some poet, Bart, I tell you.","准爵爷，我告诉您，他是位伟大的诗人，也是《铜币》的作者。"
"You must read him.","您一定要读读他的作品。"
"We’re going home.","我们准备回家了。"
"Come along!”","一起走吧！”"
"Sir Lawrence went along.","劳伦斯爵士与他们同行。"
"“What happened at ‘Snooks’?”","“‘轻蔑’俱乐部情况如何？”"
"“Le roi est mort.","“国王去世。"
"Labour can start lying, Michael—election next month.”","工党可以开始编谎话了，迈克尔——下个月要进行大选了。”"
"“Bart was brought up, Wilfrid, in days that knew not Demos.”","“威尔弗里德，准爵爷是在不了解民众的时代长大的。”"
"“Well, Mr. Desert, do you find reality in politics now?”","“哦，德赛特先生，您觉得如今的政治现实可行吗？”"
"“Do you find reality in anything, sir?”","“先生，您在哪些方面发现它现实可行呢？”"
"“In income tax, perhaps.”","“或许是在所得税方面。”"
"Michael grinned.","迈克尔咧嘴笑了。"
"“Above knighthood,” he said, “there’s no such thing as simple faith.”","“地位在爵士以上的人，”他说道，“单纯的信仰对他们而言根本不存在。”"
"“Suppose your friends came into power, Michael—in some ways not a bad thing, help ‘em to grow up—what could they do, eh?","“假设你的朋友掌权，迈克尔——在某些方面，这其实并不是一件坏事，帮助他们发展起来——他们又能干些什么呢？"
"Could they raise national taste?","他们能提高国民的品位吗？"
"Abolish the cinema?","能取缔电影吗？"
"Teach English people to cook?","能教会英国人厨艺吗？"
"Prevent other countries from threatening war?","能阻止其他国家发动战争吗？"
"Make us grow our own food?","能帮我们种出我们自己吃的粮食吗？"
"Stop the increase of town life?","能控制城市人口增长吗？"
"Would they hang dabblers in poison gas?","他们会用毒气杀死那些滥竽充数的人吗？"
"Could they prevent flying in war-time?","他们能在战时把飞机打下来吗？"
"Could they weaken the possessive instinct—anywhere?","无论在何处，他们能削弱人们占有欲强的本性吗？"
"Or do anything, in fact, but alter the incidence of possession a little?","或者，除了稍微改变一点儿占有欲的问题，还能做点儿其他的什么吗？"
"All party politics are top dressing.","一切党派政治都善于浮华的装饰。"
"We’re ruled by the inventors, and human nature; and we live in Queer Street, Mr. Desert.”","我们受到制定规则的人和人性的支配，并且我们经济上陷入了困境，德赛特先生。”"
"“Much my sentiments, sir.”","“我也深有同感，先生。”"
"Michael flourished his cigar.","迈克尔晃了晃他手中的雪茄。"
"“Bad old men, you two!”","“难缠的人啊，你们二位呀！”"
"And removing their hats, they passed the Cenotaph.","经过纪念碑时，他们都脱下帽子。"
"“Curiously symptomatic—that thing,” said Sir Lawrence; “monument to the dread of swank—most characteristic.","“非常有代表性——那个东西，”劳伦斯爵士说，“害怕出风头的纪念碑——这说法真准确。"
"And the dread of swank—”","说到害怕出风头——”"
"“Go on, Bart,” said Michael.","“准爵爷，说下去。”迈克尔说道。"
"“The fine, the large, the florid—all off!","“一切优雅、博大、华丽的事物——全都消失了！"
"No far-sighted views, no big schemes, no great principles, no great religion, or great art—aestheticism in cliques and backwaters, small men in small hats.”","没有远见的卓识，没有宏伟的规划，没有高尚的原则，没有崇高的信仰，没有伟大的艺术——只有沉湎于小派系和穷乡僻壤里的唯美主义，和一些鼠目寸光的小人物而已。”"
"“As panteth the heart after Byron, Wilberforce, and the Nelson Monument.","“所以人心切慕拜伦、威尔伯福斯以及纳尔逊纪念碑。"
"My poor old Bart!","我可怜的准爵爷！"
"What about it, Wilfrid?”","威尔弗里德，你的看法呢？”"
"“Yes, Mr. Desert—what about it?”","“是啊，德赛特先生，你是怎么看的呢？”"
"Desert’s dark face contracted.","德赛特皱了皱阴沉的脸。"
"“It’s an age of paradox,” he said.","“这是个自相矛盾的时代。”他说，"
"“We all kick up for freedom, and the only institutions gaining strength are Socialism and the Roman Catholic Church.","“我们都高喊着要自由，但只有社会主义和罗马天主教会真正受益。"
"We’re frightfully self-conscious about art—and the only art development is the cinema.","我们非常清楚艺术的重要性——而唯一有所发展的艺术却是电影。"
"We’re nuts on peace—and all we’re doing about it is to perfect poison gas.”","我们热爱和平——但我们实际为和平所做的却是造出了毒气。”"
"Sir Lawrence glanced sideways at a young man so bitter.","劳伦斯爵士挖苦地朝那个年轻人斜睨了一眼。"
"“And how’s publishing, Michael?”","“迈克尔，出版社情况如何？”"
"“Well, ‘Copper Coin’ is selling like hot cakes; and there’s quite a movement in ‘A Duet.’","“嗯，《铜币》正在热销，《二重唱》销量也很可观。"
"What about this for a new ad.: ‘A Duet, by Sir Lawrence Mont, Bart.","像这样做个新广告如何：‘《二重唱》——作者：劳伦斯·蒙特爵士，准爵爷。"
"The most distinguished Conversation ever held between the Dead.’","两位逝者之间有史以来最杰出的对话。’"
"That ought to get the psychic.","这样肯定能够吸引通灵人士的注意。"
"Wilfrid suggested ‘G.O.M. and Dizzy—broadcasted from Hell.’","威尔弗里德建议使用‘老夫子和迪齐——来自地狱的广播’。"
"Which do you like best?”","您更喜欢哪一个呢？”"
"They had come, however, to a policeman holding up his hand against the nose of a van horse, so that everything marked time.","然而此时，他们走到了一位警察身边，警察正举手拦住一辆运货马车，因此所有车辆和行人都停止不前了。"
"The engines of the cars whirred idly, their drivers’ faces set towards the space withheld from them; a girl on a bicycle looked vacantly about her, grasping the back of the van, where a youth sat sideways with his legs stretched out towards her.","汽车的发动机轰轰作响，司机们面目呆滞，凝视着前方被封住的路；一个骑自行车的女孩茫然环顾四周，一手抓住那辆货车的尾部，一个青年侧坐在车上，两条腿直伸着对着她。"
"Sir Lawrence glanced again at young Desert.","劳伦斯爵士又朝年轻的德赛特瞥了一眼。"
"A thin, pale-dark face, good-looking, but a hitch in it, as if not properly timed; nothing outre in dress or manner, and yet socially at large; less vivacious than that lively rascal, his own son, but as anchorless, and more sceptical—might feel things pretty deeply, though!","一张消瘦、浅黑色的脸庞，外貌英俊，但似乎缺少点儿什么，显得有些美中不足；穿戴和举止还算得体，肯定在社交上游刃有余；不如他那个活泼的儿子那么有生气，但一样不安定，而且更多疑——不过他对事物的看法倒是相当深刻！"
"The policeman lowered his arm.","警察放下了手臂。"
"“You were in the war, Mr. Desert?”","“你参过战吧，德赛特先生？”"
"“Oh, yes.”","“是的。”"
"“Air service?”","“空军？”"
"“And line.","“也在陆军干过。"
"Bit of both.”","两个都干过。”"
"“Hard on a poet.”","“成为诗人很困难。”"
"“Not at all.","“一点儿也不。"
"Poetry’s only possible when you may be blown up at any moment, or when you live in Putney.”","你只有在随时有可能被炸死时，或者是住在帕特尼时，才写得出来诗。”"
"Sir Lawrence’s eyebrow rose.","劳伦斯爵士的眉毛扬了扬。"
"“Yes?”","“您请讲？”"
"“Tennyson, Browning, Wordsworth, Swinburne—they could turn it out; ils vivaient, mais si peu.”","“丁尼生、勃朗宁、华兹华斯、斯温伯恩——他们都能创造出诗歌，但他们却很少经历过你说的那两种生活。”"
"“Is there not a third condition favourable?”","“不是有第三种有利条件吗？”"
"“And that, sir?”","“是什么呢，先生？”"
"“How shall I express it—a certain cerebral agitation in connection with women?”","“怎么说呢——和女人息息相关的大脑的兴奋吧？”"
"Desert’s face twitched, and seemed to darken.","德赛特的脸抽动了一下，似乎变得阴郁起来。"
"Michael put his latchkey into the lock of his front door.","迈克尔把钥匙插进他家前门的锁孔里。"

"Chapter II","第二章"
"Home","家"
"The house in South Square, Westminster, to which the young Monts had come after their Spanish honeymoon two years before, might have been called ‘emancipated.’","坐落在威斯敏斯特南广场的这幢房子是“解放式”的。两年前，年轻的蒙特夫妇在西班牙度完蜜月，回到了这里。"
"It was the work of an architect whose dream was a new house perfectly old, and an old house perfectly new.","设计它的那位建筑师梦想建造一幢完全古式的新房子和一幢全然一新的老房子。"
"It followed, therefore, no recognised style or tradition, and was devoid of structural prejudice; but it soaked up the smuts of the metropolis with such special rapidity that its stone already respectably resembled that of Wren.","因此，这幢房子并不循规蹈矩，也不墨守结构上的陈规，但它却以惊人的速度收集了这个大都市的煤尘，连砖块也已经快赶上雷恩设计的典雅的建筑物砖块了。"
"Its windows and doors had gently rounded tops.","房子的门窗都有圆润的穹顶。"
"The high-sloping roof, of a fine sooty pink, was almost Danish, and two ‘ducky little windows’ looked out of it, giving an impression that very tall servants lived up there.","高斜的屋顶刷着雅致的暗红色，很有丹麦的风格，上面的两扇“玲珑小窗”从屋顶往外探，让人以为上面住着一些魁梧的仆人。"
"There were rooms on each side of the front door, which was wide and set off by bay trees in black and gold bindings.","前门处很宽敞，装饰着金色和黑色的月桂树，门两侧各有几间房间。"
"The house was thick through, and the staircase, of a broad chastity, began at the far end of a hall which had room for quite a number of hats and coats and cards.","房子很深，宽大、典雅的楼梯从门厅尽头开始延伸，门厅很宽敞，足可以放下很多的帽子、大衣和卡片。"
"There were four bathrooms; and not even a cellar underneath.","房子里有四间盥洗室，却没有一间地下室。"
"The Forsyte instinct for a house had co-operated in its acquisition.","福赛特家族善于甄别房屋的天赋帮助他们买下了这座房子。"
"Soames had picked it up for his daughter, undecorated, at that psychological moment when the bubble of inflation was pricked, and the air escaping from the balloon of the world’s trade.","索姆斯是在极为恰当的时候为女儿挑选了这幢还未装修的房子，当时通货膨胀的气泡刚被戳破，世界贸易的大气球正在漏气。"
"Fleur, however, had established immediate contact with the architect—an element which Soames himself had never quite got over—and decided not to have more than three styles in her house: Chinese, Spanish, and her own.","可是，弗勒早已直接跟建筑师联系了——这恰是索姆斯自己不太具备的能力——并且决定在装修她的房子时仅限于三种风格：中国式、西班牙式以及自己独特的风格。"
"The room to the left of the front door, running the breadth of the house, was Chinese, with ivory panels, a copper floor, central heating, and cut glass lustres.","前门左侧的房间和房子的跨度一样宽，是中国式的，镶嵌着象牙色的护墙板，铺着红棕色地板，装有中央暖气，还有雕花玻璃吊灯。"
"It contained four pictures—all Chinese—the only school in which her father had not yet dabbled.","屋内挂着四幅画——都是中国国画——这是她父亲至今唯一没有尝试的画派。"
"The fireplace, wide and open, had Chinese dogs with Chinese tiles for them to stand on.","壁炉宽大开阔，底部镶有中国瓷砖，瓷砖上镶着中国狗的图案。"
"The silk was chiefly of jade green.","丝绸以翠绿色的居多。"
"There were two wonderful old black tea-chests, picked up with Soames’ money at Jobson’s—not a bargain.","屋内有两个古色古香的黑色茶柜，它们是索姆斯从乔布森拍卖行花钱买来的——绝不是廉价品。"
"There was no piano, partly because pianos were too uncompromisingly occidental, and partly because it would have taken up much room.","屋内没有钢琴，其一是因为钢琴带有西洋韵味，风格很不协调，其二是由于它占的空间太大。"
"Fleur aimed at space-collecting people rather than furniture or bibelots.","弗勒希望有空间来招待宾客，而不是收纳家具或者装饰品。"
"The light, admitted by windows at both ends, was unfortunately not Chinese.","可惜的是，从屋内两端窗户透进的光线不是中国的。"
"She would stand sometimes in the centre of this room, thinking—how to ‘bunch’ her guests, how to make her room more Chinese without making it uncomfortable; how to seem to know all about literature and politics; how to accept everything her father gave her, without making him aware that his taste had no sense of the future; how to keep hold of Sibley Swan, the new literary star, and to get hold of Gurdon Minho, the old; of how Wilfrid Desert was getting too fond of her; of what was really her style in dress; of why Michael had such funny ears; and sometimes she stood not thinking at all—just aching a little.","有时她会站在房子中间，思量着——该如何“汇拢”她的那些客人呢；该如何使她的房间更显中国化而又不失舒适呢；该如何显得自己精通文学和政治呢；该如何接纳父亲给予自己的一切，同时还让父亲察觉不到他的兴趣已跟不上潮流呢；该如何同时抓住文坛新秀西布莉·斯旺和文学泰斗格登·明霍呢；威尔弗里德·德赛特是如何越来越迷恋她呢；她的衣着究竟应该是什么风格呢，还有迈克尔为何长着一副如此滑稽的耳朵呢。但有时她站在那里，什么也不想——只是有一点点心痛。"
"When those three came in she was sitting before a red lacquer tea-table, finishing a very good tea.","当那三人走进来时，弗勒正坐在一张红漆茶桌前，刚刚吃完精致的茶点。"
"She always had tea brought in rather early, so that she could have a good quiet preliminary ‘tuck-in’ all by herself, because she was not quite twenty-one, and this was her hour for remembering her youth.","她总是吩咐仆人把茶点早一些送过来，这样一来，她便可以独自一人悠然自得地享受“一顿美餐”，因为她还未满21岁，而这正是她记住青春岁月的大好时候。"
"By her side Ting-a-ling was standing on his hind feet, his tawny forepaws on a Chinese footstool, his snubbed black and tawny muzzle turned up towards the fruits of his philosophy.","小叮铃正踮着后脚站在她身旁，它那黄褐色的前爪搁在一把中国式的脚凳上，那扁平的黑褐色口鼻朝上仰着，望着他眼中的“果子”。"
"“That’ll do, Ting.","“好了，叮铃。"
"No more, ducky!","没了，宝贝！"
"NO MORE!”","一点儿也没有了！”"
"The expression of Ting-a-ling answered:","小叮铃的表情仿佛回答道："
"‘Well, then, stop, too!","“哦，那你也别吃了！"
"Don’t subject me to torture!’","别再折磨我了！”"
"A year and three months old, he had been bought by Michael out of a Bond Street shop window on Fleur’s twentieth birthday, eleven months ago.","它一岁零三个月，是11个月前，迈克尔在弗勒20岁生日那天，从邦德大街的一家商店橱窗里买来的。"
"Two years of married life had not lengthened her short dark chestnut hair; had added a little more decision to her quick lips, a little more allurement to her white-lidded, dark-lashed hazel eyes, a little more poise and swing to her carriage, a little more chest and hip measurement; had taken a little from waist and calf measurement, a little colour from cheeks a little less round, and a little sweetness from a voice a little more caressing.","两年的婚姻生活，没有使她深栗色的短发变长，却让她那灵巧的嘴唇多了一份坚决神情，让那双白眼皮、黑睫毛、淡褐色的眼睛更加妩媚，给她的仪态平添了几分端庄和婀娜。她的胸围和臀部愈加丰满，腰身和小腿愈加纤细；她的面庞愈加清瘦，少了几分血色；她嗓音没有以前甜美了，却多了一丝柔情。"
"She stood up behind the tray, holding out her white round arm without a word.","她从茶盘后面站起来，一语不发地伸出她那白皙而丰润的手臂。"
"She avoided unnecessary greetings or farewells.","她回避了那些不必要的问候和道别。"
"She would have had to say them so often, and their purpose was better served by look, pressure, and slight inclination of head to one side.","她本该经常说这些话的，但使个眼色、握一下手、微微点头，似乎更能达到目的。"
"With circular movement of her squeezed hand, she said:","她用那只刚被紧握过的手划了个圆圈，说道："
"“Draw up.","“坐下来吧。"
"Cream, sir?","先生，要奶油吗？"
"Sugar, Wilfrid?","威尔弗里德，要糖吗？"
"Ting has had too much—don’t feed him!","叮铃吃的够多的了——别再喂它了！"
"Hand things, Michael.","迈克尔，递一下。"
"I’ve heard all about the meeting at ‘Snooks.’","‘轻蔑’俱乐部开会的情况我已经全听说了。"
"You’re not going to canvass for Labour, Michael—canvassing’s so silly.","迈克尔，你不要再去为工党拉选票了——那太愚蠢了。"
"If any one canvassed me, I should vote the other way at once.”","如果有人来找我拉票，我会毫不犹豫地给另一方投票。”"
"“Yes, darling; but you’re not the average elector.”","“是呀，亲爱的。不过你可不是普通的选民啊。”"
"Fleur looked at him.","弗勒看看他。"
"Very sweetly put!","话里有话！"
"Conscious of Wilfrid biting his lips, of Sir Lawrence taking that in, of the amount of silk leg she was showing, of her black and cream teacups, she adjusted these matters.","弗勒留意到威尔弗里德咬着双唇，而劳伦斯爵士也注意到了威尔弗里德的举动。她知道她露出了一截穿着丝袜的腿，还有她桌上奶油色和黑色相间的茶杯。她对这一切都心中有数。"
"A flutter of her white lids—Desert ceased to bite his lips; a movement of her silk legs—Sir Lawrence ceased to look at him.","她那白眼皮一翻，德赛特立刻不咬嘴唇了；她那穿丝袜的腿一动，劳伦斯爵士立刻不再看威尔弗里德了。"
"Holding out her cups, she said:","她伸手放下茶杯，说道："
"“I suppose I’m not modern enough?”","“我想我还不够时髦吧？”"
"Desert, moving a bright little spoon round in his magpie cup, said without looking up:","德赛特用一把光亮的小勺在他那只绘着喜鹊的茶杯里搅动着，头也不抬地说："
"“As much more modern than the moderns, as you are more ancient.”","“你比现代人更时髦，比时髦的人更复古。”"
"“‘Ware poetry!” said Michael.","“注意诗律！”迈克尔说。"
"But when he had taken his father to see the new cartoons by Aubrey Greene, she said:","待迈克尔带他父亲去参观奥布里·格林新创作的漫画时，她说："
"“Kindly tell me what you meant, Wilfrid.”","“威尔弗里德，你说这话是什么意思。”"
"Desert’s voice seemed to leap from restraint.","德赛特的声音似乎是强挤出来的。"
"“What does it matter?","“这话怎么了？"
"I don’t want to waste time with that.”","我不想为此耽误时间。”"
"“But I want to know.","“可是我想知道。"
"It sounded like a sneer.”","这话听上去像是在讽刺。”"
"“A sneer?","“讽刺？"
"From me?","我说的？"
"Fleur!”","弗勒！”"
"“Then tell me.”","“那告诉我到底是什么意思。”"
"“I meant that you have all their restlessness and practical get-thereness; but you have what they haven’t, Fleur—power to turn one’s head.","“我的意思是，你具有了他们那种不安分以及务实的定要成功的精神，但弗勒，你还具有他们所没有的东西——使人迷糊的能力。"
"And mine is turned.","我就是被你弄迷糊的。"
"You know it.”","这点你心里明白。”"
"“How would Michael like that—from YOU, his best man?”","“要是迈克尔听见这话该有何感想——出自你，他的男傧相之口？”"
"Desert moved quickly to the windows.","德赛特快速走到窗边。"
"Fleur took Ting-a-ling on her lap.","弗勒把小叮铃抱到腿上。"
"Such things had been said to her before; but from Wilfrid it was serious.","类似的话以前也有人对她说过，但出自威尔弗里德之口，事情就变得严重了。"
"Nice to think she had his heart, of course!","但想到她已经占有了他的心，自然值得高兴！"
"Only, where on earth could she put it, where it wouldn’t be seen except by her?","只是，她究竟要把这颗心放在哪里呢，一个除她之外别人都不知道的地方？"
"He was incalculable—did strange things!","他可是个让人猜不透的人——干些令人费解的古怪事。"
"She was a little afraid—not of him, but of that quality in him.","她有些害怕——不是怕他，而是害怕他那怪脾气。"
"He came back to the hearth, and said:","他走回到壁炉前，说："
"“Ugly, isn’t it?","“很丑恶，是不是？"
"Put that dam’ dog down, Fleur; I can’t see your face.","弗勒，把那只该死的狗放下去。我看不见你的脸了。"
"If you were really fond of Michael—I swear I wouldn’t; but you’re not, you know.”","你要是真心喜欢迈克尔的话——我发誓我不会这样做。但你并不喜欢他，你心里明白。”"
"Fleur said coldly:","弗勒冷冷地说："
"“You know very little; I AM fond of Michael.”","“你知道得太少了。我是喜欢迈克尔的。”"
"Desert gave his little jerky laugh.","德赛特急促地笑笑。"
"“Oh yes; not the sort that counts.”","“不错，但算不上爱。”"
"Fleur looked up.","弗勒抬起头来。"
"“It counts quite enough to make one safe.”","“能给人安全感，就算得上了。”"
"“A flower that I can’t pick.”","“这是一朵我采不到的花。”"
"Fleur nodded.","弗勒点点头。"
"“Quite sure, Fleur?","“弗勒，你肯定吗？"
"Quite, quite sure?”","非常、非常肯定吗？”"
"Fleur stared; her eyes softened a little, her eyelids, so excessively white, drooped over them; she nodded.","弗勒凝视着他。她的眼神变得柔和了一些，她闭上那白得过分的眼皮，点了点头。"
"Desert said slowly:","德赛特慢吞吞地说："
"“The moment I believe that, I shall go East.”","“一旦我相信你说的话，我就去东方。”"
"“East?”","“东方？”"
"“Not so stale as going West, but much the same—you don’t come back.”","“不像上西天那样乏味，但结果是一样的——一去就再也不回来了。”"
"Fleur thought: ‘The East?","弗勒心想：“东方？"
"I should love to know the East!","我倒很想去东方看看！"
"Pity one can’t manage that, too.","遗憾的是，这无法办到。"
"Pity!’","遗憾啊！”"
"“You won’t keep me in your Zoo, my dear.","“亲爱的，你不可能把我关在你的动物园里。"
"I shan’t hang around and feed on crumbs.","我也不会在此逗留，并以残羹冷炙为生。"
"You know what I feel—it means a smash of some sort.”","你知道我是什么感觉吗——那就意味着决裂。”"
"“It hasn’t been my fault, has it?”","“这不是我的过错，是吧？”"
"“Yes; you’ve collected me, as you collect everybody that comes near you.”","“是你的错，是你把我招揽来的，就像你招揽着每个来到你身边的人一样。”"
"“I don’t know what you mean.”","“我不明白你的意思。”"
"Desert bent down, and dragged her hand to his lips.","德赛特弯腰，把她的手慢慢拉近自己的唇边。"
"“Don’t be riled with me; I’m too unhappy.”","“别生我的气，我非常难过。”"

"“Sorry, Wilfrid.”","“对不起，威尔弗里德。”"
"“All right, dear.","“好吧，亲爱的。"
"I’ll go.”","我走了。”"
"“But you’re coming to dinner tomorrow?”","“那你明天来吃饭吗？”"
"Desert said violently:","德赛特激动地说："
"“TO-MORROW?","“明天？"
"Good God—no!","上帝啊——绝不来！"
"What d’you think I’m made of?”","在你眼里我算什么？”"
"He flung her hand away.","他甩开她的手。"
"“I don’t like violence, Wilfrid.”","“我不喜欢见你如此粗暴，威尔弗里德。”"
"“Well, good-bye; I’d better go.”","“好吧，再见。我还是走吧。”"
"The words “And you’d better not come again” trembled up to her lips, but were not spoken.","“你最好再也别来了”这句话已到嘴边，但她还是没说出口。"
"Part from Wilfrid—life would lose a little warmth!","如果和威尔弗里德分手——那么她的生活将失去一丝温暖。"
"She waved her hand.","她挥挥手。"
"He was gone.","他走了。"
"She heard the door closing.","她听到大门关上的声音。"
"Poor Wilfrid!—nice to think of a flame at which to warm her hands!","可怜的威尔弗里德！——一想到有一团可以暖手的火焰就令人兴奋！"
"Nice but rather dreadful!","兴奋，却更令人胆战心惊！"
"And suddenly, dropping Ting-a-ling, she got up and began to walk about the room.","突然，她放下小叮铃，站起来，在房间里踱起步来。"
"To-morrow!","明天！"
"Second anniversary of her wedding-day!","她结婚两周年纪念日！"
"Still an ache when she thought of what it had not been.","一想到还未实现的事，她心中不免难过。"
"But there was little time to think—and she made less.","可是没什么时间再去想了——况且她也不愿意再去想了。"
"What good in thinking?","想了又有什么好处呢？"
"Only one life, full of people, of things to do and have, of things wanted—a life only void of—one thing, and that—well, if people had it, they never had it long!","唯一的一种生活，充斥着人、要做的和拥有的事、想要得到的东西——这种生活唯一缺少的——一件东西，而且——对，人们即使得到它，也不会永远拥有它！"
"On her lids two tears, which had gathered, dried without falling.","两滴泪珠凝聚在她的眼睑上，干了，没有掉下来。"
"Sentimentalism!","多愁善感！"
"No!","不！"
"The last thing in the world—the unforgivable offence!","这是世界上最不应该有的东西——是不可饶恕的罪过！"
"Whom should she put next whom tomorrow?","明天她该把谁安排坐在谁的身旁呢？"
"And whom should she get in place of Wilfrid, if Wilfrid wouldn’t come—silly boy!","最重要的是，她到底找谁来填补威尔弗里德的位置呢？要是他不来的话——这个傻瓜！"
"One day—one night—what difference?","白天——晚上——有什么区别呢？"
"Who should sit on her right, and who on her left?","谁坐在她的右边，谁又该坐在她的左边呢？"
"Was Aubrey Greene more distinguished, or Sibley Swan?","奥布里·格林和西布莉·斯旺，谁更有名一些呢？"
"Were they either as distinguished as Walter Nazing or Charles Upshire?","他们两个人都像沃尔特·内津一样出名，还是都像查尔斯·厄普夏一样有名呢？"
"Dinner of twelve, exclusively literary and artistic, except for Michael and Alison Charwell.","晚宴的12人中，除了迈克尔和艾莉森·查韦尔之外，其他都是文学界和艺术界的。"
"Ah!","啊！"
"Could Alison get her Gurdon Minho—just one writer of the old school, one glass of old wine to mellow effervescence?","艾莉森能帮她请到格登·明霍吗？——一位老派作家，一杯令人兴奋的陈年佳酿。"
"He didn’t publish with Danby and Winter; but he fed out of Alison’s hand.","他没有在丹比&温特出版社出过书，但还是很给艾莉森面子的。"
"She went quickly to one of the old tea chests, and opened it.","她迅速走到一个陈旧的茶柜旁，打开它。"
"Inside was a telephone.","里面是一部电话。"
"“Can I speak to Lady Alison—Mrs. Michael Mont... Yes... That you, Alison?...","“我能和艾莉森夫人通话吗——是迈克尔·蒙特夫人……对……是你吗，艾莉森？"
"Fleur speaking.","我是弗勒啊。"
"Wilfrid has fallen through tomorrow night... Is there any chance of your bringing Gurdon Minho?","威尔弗里德明晚不来了……你能邀请格登·明霍来吗？"
"I don’t know him, of course; but he might be interested.","我当然不认识他了，但他也许会感兴趣的。"
"You’ll try?...","那你试试？……"
"That’ll be ever so delightful.","那可真让人兴奋。"
"Isn’t the ‘Snooks’ Club meeting rather exciting?","‘轻蔑’俱乐部的会议是不是很热闹？"
"Bart says they’ll eat each other now they’ve split... About Mr. Minho.","准爵爷说他们现在已经分裂了，一定要拼个你死我活……说关于明霍先生的事吧。"
"Could you let me know to-night?","今晚你能给我确切消息吗？"
"Thanks—thanks awfully!...","谢谢——真是万分感激！……"
"Goodbye!”","再见！”"
"Failing Minho, whom?","假如明霍先生邀请不到，那么该请谁好呢？"
"Her mind hovered over the names in her address book.","她的脑子里反复思考着通讯录中的人名。"
"At so late a minute it must be some one who didn’t stand on ceremony; but except Alison, none of Michael’s relations would be safe from Sibley Swan or Nesta Gorse, and their subversive shafts; as to the Forsytes—out of the question; they had their own sub-acid humour (some of them), but they were not modern, not really modern.","剩下的时间不多了，必须找一个不拘礼节的人。除了艾莉森以外，迈克尔的亲戚中还没有一个人能应付西布莉·斯旺或内丝塔·戈斯，并应对他们那些刻薄话；至于福赛特家族——就更不必多说了，他们具有独特的晦涩的幽默（他们中的一些人），但他们绝不是真正时髦的人。"
"Besides, she saw as little of them as she could—they dated, belonged to the dramatic period, had no sense of life without beginning or end.","此外，她对他们很看不上眼——毕竟他们已经过时了，他们属于戏剧时代，根本不懂得没有开始或结局的人生。"
"No!","不！"
"If Gurdon Minho was a frost, it would have to be a musician, whose works were hieroglyphical with a dash of surgery; or, better, perhaps, a psycho-analyst.","如果格登·明霍不肯来，那就得邀请一位音乐家，而他们的作品都像外科手术一样晦涩难懂。或许还是邀请一位精神分析学家更好一些。"
"Her fingers turned the pages till she came to those two categories.","她用手指一页页翻着，直到那两栏，她停了下来。"
"Hugo Solstis?","雨果·苏斯迪斯？"
"A possibility; but suppose he wanted to play them something recent?","值得考虑，但是如果他要表演近期的作品，该怎么办？"
"There was only Michael’s upright Grand, and that would mean going to his study.","家里只有迈克尔的那架竖式大钢琴，这就意味着大家只能到他书房去了。"
"Better Gerald Hanks—he and Nesta Gorse would get off together on dreams; still, if they did, there would be no actual loss of life.","还是杰拉尔德·汉克斯更适合一些——他会和内丝塔·戈斯一起讨论梦，而且，他们就是那样做了，也没有什么大不了的。"
"Yes, failing Gurdon Minho, Gerald Hanks; he would be free—and put him between Alison and Nesta.","对，要是不能邀请格登·明霍，那就邀请杰拉尔德·汉克斯，他应该有空——把他的座位安排在艾莉森和内丝塔两人之间。"
"She closed the book, and, going back to her jade-green settee, sat gazing at Ting-a-ling.","她合上通讯录，走回到那把翠绿色的长靠椅旁边，坐在那里盯着小叮铃。"
"The little dog’s prominent round eyes gazed back; bright, black, very old.","小狗突出的圆眼睛也盯着她，眼睛明亮、乌黑，是她非常熟悉的眼神。"
"Fleur thought: ‘I DON’T want Wilfrid to drop off.’","弗勒心想：“我不愿意让威尔弗里德就这么离开了。”"
"Among all the crowd who came and went, here, there and everywhere, she cared for nobody.","在所有来来往往的人中，无论是在此处、他处，或是任何其他地方，她从来没有喜欢上一个人。"
"Keep up with them, keep up with everything, of course!","当然，应该与他们保持联系，与所有的事情保持联系！"
"It was all frightfully amusing, frightfully necessary!","这一切都非常有趣，非常有必要！"
"Only—only—what?","只是——只是——又怎么样呢？"
"Voices!","有说话声！"
"Michael and Bart coming back.","迈克尔和准爵爷回来了。"
"Bart had noticed Wilfrid.","准爵爷已经注意到威尔弗里德的神情了。"
"He WAS a noticing old Bart.","他可是一位洞悉一切的老准爵爷。"
"She was never very comfortable when he was about—lively and twisting, but with something settled and ancestral in him; a little like Ting-a-ling—something judgmatic, ever telling her that she was fluttering and new.","每当他在身旁，她就感到不大自在——他活泼但又很偏执，在他身上有某种很难改变的遗传的东西。他有点儿像小叮铃——善于识别人，还总是说她不仅情绪不稳定，还不谙世事。"
"He was anchored, could only move to the length of his old-fashioned cord, but he could drop on to things disconcertingly.","他的性格已经固定不变，只能在固有的习惯约束下行动，但是他会对事情刨根问底。"
"Still, he admired her, she felt—oh! yes.","但她仍感觉，他是很欣赏她的——对！欣赏。"
"Well!","哦！"
"What had he thought of the cartoons?","他对那些漫画有什么看法呢？"
"Ought Michael to publish them, and with letterpress or without?","迈克尔究竟应该不应该把它们出版呢，是否该配上文字呢？"
"Didn’t he think that the cubic called ‘Still Life’—of the Government, too frightfully funny—especially the ‘old bean’ representing the Prime?","对于这幅叫做“静物画”的立体漫画——它描绘的是政府，他是不是觉得滑稽好笑呢？——尤其是那位影射首相的“老兄”。"
"For answer she was conscious of a twisting, rapid noise; Sir Lawrence was telling her of his father’s collection of electioneering cartoons.","她得到的答案含糊其辞，劳伦斯爵士正在给她讲他父亲收集选举漫画的事情。"
"She did wish Bart would not tell her about his father; he had been so distinguished, and he must have been so dull, paying all his calls on horseback, with trousers strapped under his boots.","她从内心希望准爵爷不要向她诉说他父亲的往事；他曾经是那样高贵，但肯定也很无趣：骑马去会客，裤脚掖在靴筒里。"
"He and Lord Charles Cariboo and the Marquis of Forfar had been the last three ‘callers’ of that sort.","他、查尔斯·卡列布勋爵和福法侯爵可以算得上是这类“访客”中最后的三位了。"
"If only they hadn’t, they’d have been clean forgot.","假如他们没有这些特征，也许早已被人遗忘了。"
"She had that dress to try, and fourteen things to see to, and Hugo’s concert began at eight-fifteen!","她还要试穿一件衣服，此外还有14件事要处理，而雨果的音乐会在八点一刻就要开始了！"
"Why did people of the last generation always have so much time?","为什么上一代人总有那么多空闲时间呢？"
"And, suddenly, she looked down.","就在这时，她突然往下望了望。"
"Ting-a-ling was licking the copper floor.","小叮铃正在舔着红棕色的地板。"
"She took him up: “Not that, darling; nasty!”","她一把抱起它：“亲爱的，脏啊，别再舔了！”"
"Ah! the spell was broken!","啊！危急解除了！"
"Bart was going, reminiscent to the last.","准爵爷要走了，直到最后，他还在回首往事。"
"She waited at the foot of the stairs till Michael shut the door on him, then flew.","她在楼梯下面等着，直到迈克尔把他送出门，把门关上后，她才又飞奔回去。"
"Reaching her room, she turned on all the lights.","回到自己的屋里，她打开了所有的灯。"
"Here was her own style—a bed which did not look like one, and many mirrors.","这里是她独有的风格——有一张怎么看都不像床的床，还有很多面镜子。"
"The couch of Ting-a-ling occupied a corner, whence he could see himself in three.","小叮铃的睡椅占据房间一角，在那里它能看见镜子反映出的三个自己。"
"She put him down, and said: “Keep quiet, now!”","她把它放下来，说：“从现在开始，安静！”"
"His attitude to the other dogs in the room had long become indifferent; though of his own breed and precisely his colouring, they had no smell and no licking power in their tongues—nothing to be done with them, imitative creatures, incredibly unresponsive.","对于屋里的其他几条狗，它早已丧失兴趣了；这些狗虽然跟小叮铃是同种，皮毛也一样，但它们全然没有嗅觉，也不会用舌头舔东西——拿它们没辙，他们就会模仿，极其迟钝。"
"Stripping off her dress, Fleur held the new frock under her chin.","弗勒脱下身上的衣服，用下巴夹着那件新衣服。"
"“May I kiss you?” said a voice, and there was Michael’s image behind her own reflection in the glass.","“我可以吻你吗？”一个声音说道，镜中映出了她身后站着的迈克尔。"

"The vice of our lot is, they say it pretty well, but they’ve nothing to say.","我们这群人的缺点是说起话来冠冕堂皇，但却言之无物。"
"They won’t last.”","这样的人终究不会太长久。”"

"Wilfrid has emotions, hates, pities, wants; at least, sometimes; when he has, his stuff is jolly good.","威尔弗里德爱憎分明，有怜悯之心，也有欲望，至少他有时是这样的。当他拥有这些情感时，他的作品就会很精彩。"
"Otherwise, he just makes a song about nothing—like the rest.”","否则，就是无病呻吟，无关痛痒——像其他人一样。”"
"Fleur tucked in the top of her undergarment.","弗勒把她的内衣上端掖进去。"
"“But, Michael, if that’s so, we—I’ve got the wrong lot.”","“但是，迈克尔，如果是这样，我们——我是请错人了。”"
"Michael grinned.","迈克尔咧嘴笑笑。"
"“My dear child!","“亲爱的宝贝！"
"The lot of the hour is always right; only you’ve got to watch it, and change it quick enough.”","一时之选总是对的，但你要时刻关注，及时更新。”"
"“But d’you mean to say that Sibley isn’t going to live?”","“那你的意思是说西布莉不会持久存在？”"
"“Sib?","“茜布？"
"Lord, no!”","上帝，绝不会的！”"
"“But he’s so perfectly sure that almost everybody else is dead or dying.","“但他很自信，他相信除他以外所有人都已死去，或正在死去。"
"Surely he has critical genius!”","但他的确是批判的高手！”"
"“If I hadn’t more judgment than Sib, I’d go out of publishing tomorrow.”","“如果我的判断力不如茜布，那我明天就离开出版社。”"
"“You—more than Sibley Swan?”","“你——比西布莉·斯旺还精明？”"
"“Of course, I’ve more judgment than Sib.","“当然，我的判断力肯定比茜布强。"
"Why!","咳！"
"Sib’s judgment is just his opinion of Sib—common or garden impatience of any one else.","茜布的判断力只是他自己书里的见解——陈词滥调，对于别人的观点一向不耐烦。"
"He doesn’t even read them.","他甚至都不读别人的作品。"
"He’ll read one specimen of every author and say: ‘Oh! that fellow!","他只是大略读一下每位作家的作品节选，然后说：‘啊！那家伙！"
"He’s dull, or he’s moral, or he’s sentimental, or he dates, or he drivels’—I’ve heard him dozens of times.","他是愚笨的，或者是说教的、多愁善感的、过时的、胡说八道的’——我已经听他这样说过几十遍了。"
"That’s if they’re alive.","如果那些作家还在世，他就会这样说。"
"Of course, if they’re dead, it’s different.","当然，如果他们已经去世，情况就不同了。"
"He’s always digging up and canonising the dead; that’s how he’s got his name.","他总是高举和吹捧死者，他就是这样出的名。"
"There’s always a Sib in literature.","在文学界，总是有像茜布这样的人。"

"But as to lasting—of course he won’t; he’s never creative, even by mistake.”","但提到持久——他自然是不会的，他自始至终就没有创造才能，哪怕是歪打正着。”"
"Fleur had lost the thread.","弗勒已经糊涂了。"
"Yes!","是的！"

"The really big people don’t talk—and don’t bunch—they paddle their own canoes in what seem backwaters.","真正的大人物是不会滔滔不绝的——也不会拉帮结伙的——他们只是独自一人，逆水行舟。"
"But it’s the backwaters that make the main stream.","但那逆流恰好成为了主流。"

"“Michael, if you were me, would you tell Frederic Wilmer that he’ll be meeting Hubert Marsland at lunch next week?","“迈克尔，假如你是我，你会通知弗雷德里克·威尔默下周午餐时他会遇见休伯特·马斯兰德吗？"

"“Marsland’s rather an old duck, Wilmer’s rather an old goose—I don’t know.”","“马斯兰德是个老好人，威尔默是个十足的傻瓜——我也不清楚。”"
"“Oh! do be serious, Michael—you never give me any help in arranging—No!","“啊！严肃点儿，迈克尔——我准备请客的事情，你从来没帮过我——从来都没有！"

"He’s almost a Mathew Mans for keeping out of the swim.","他简直就和马修·马里斯一样不入流。"

"“I didn’t ask you if he’d like to meet Wilmer; I asked you if Wilmer would like to meet him.”","“我并不是问你他是否愿意遇见威尔默，我想问的是威尔默是否愿意遇见他。”"
"“Wilmer will just say: ‘I like little Mrs. Mont, she gives deuced good grub’—and so you do, ducky.","“威尔默只会说：‘我喜欢娇小的蒙特夫人，她给我们准备美食’——你的确如此，宝贝。"
