"“Michael, your chin is like a bootbrush.”","“迈克尔，你的下巴像一把靴刷子。”"
"“Sorry, old thing; your shoulders shouldn’t be so smooth.","“不好意思，亲爱的，你的肩膀不该这么光滑。"
"Bart gave Wilfrid a tip as we were coming along.”","在我们来时的路上，准爵爷给了威尔弗里德一些提示。”"
"Fleur stopped writing.","弗勒停下笔来。"
"“Oh!”","“哦！”"
"“Reminded him that the state of love was a good stunt for poets.”","“爵爷提示他，对于诗人来说，恋爱可是施展才华的绝好机会。”"
"“A propos of what?”","“都说了些什么呢？”"
"“Wilfrid was complaining that he couldn’t turn it out now.”","“威尔弗里德一直在抱怨现在他创作不出来作品。”"
"“Nonsense!","“胡说！"
"His last things are his best.”","他最新的作品正是他最好的作品。”"
"“Well, that’s what I think.","“嗯，我也有同感。"
"Perhaps he’s forestalled the tip.","也许他早就实践过那个提示了。"
"Has he, d’you know?”","他有没有实践过，你知道吗？”"
"Fleur turned her eyes towards the face behind her shoulder.","弗勒转过头，望着身后的那张脸。"
"No, it had its native look—frank, irresponsible, slightly faun-like, with its pointed ears, quick lips, and nostrils.","还是那张脸——坦率真诚、不负责任，有点儿像尊农牧神像，有着尖尖的耳朵、灵巧的嘴唇和鼻孔。"
"She said slowly:","她缓缓地说："
"“If YOU don’t know, nobody does.”","“如果连你都不知道，那更没有人知道了。”"
"A snuffle interrupted Michael’s answer.","一阵鼻息声打断了迈克尔的回答。"
"Ting-a-ling, long, low, slightly higher at both ends, was standing between them, with black muzzle upturned.","是小叮铃——它身子长、个头矮，头和尾巴稍微高一些——正站在他们两个人中间，黑乎乎的脸朝上仰着。"
"‘My pedigree is long,’ he seemed to say; ‘but my legs are short—what about it?’","它好像在说：“我可是纯种，就是腿短——这又有什么关系呢？”"

"Chapter III","第三章"
"Musical","音乐会"
"According to a great and guiding principle, Fleur and Michael Mont attended the Hugo Solstis concert, not because they anticipated pleasure, but because they knew Hugo.","依照一个伟大的并具有指导性的原则，弗勒和迈克尔·蒙特参加了雨果·苏斯迪斯的音乐会。出席这项活动不是为了娱乐，而是因为他们认识雨果。"
"They felt, besides, that Solstis, an Englishman of Russo-Dutch extraction, was one of those who were restoring English music, giving to it a wide and spacious freedom from melody and rhythm, while investing it with literary and mathematical charms.","而且，他们认为，苏斯迪斯——这个混有俄罗斯与荷兰血统的英国人——是复兴英国音乐的中坚力量之一。他使英国音乐在节奏和旋律上都获得了充分的自由，又赋予了它文学和数学的魅力。"
"And one never could go to a concert given by any of this school without using the word ‘interesting’ as one was coming away.","无论是谁参加这一流派中任何一位音乐家的音乐会，在他离开时，总要发出“有趣”的称赞。"
"To sleep to this restored English music, too, was impossible.","听这种复兴的英国音乐，也不可能打瞌睡。"
"Fleur, a sound sleeper, had never even tried.","虽说弗勒是个嗜睡的人，在这种场合却从未试着瞌睡过。"
"Michael had, and complained afterwards that it had been like a nap in Liege railway station.","迈克尔倒是打过一次瞌睡，事后却抱怨说，这就像在列日火车站打了个盹。"
"On this occasion they occupied those gangway seats in the front row of the dress circle of which Fleur had a sort of natural monopoly.","这次，他们坐在特等包厢前排靠近通道的位子，这个位子似乎就是弗勒的专座。"
"There Hugo and the rest could see her taking her place in the English restoration movement.","坐在那里，雨果和其他人都能看见她参加了这次英国复兴运动。"
"It was easy, too, to escape into the corridor and exchange the word ‘interesting’ with side-whiskered cognoscenti; or, slipping out a cigarette from the little gold case, wedding present of Cousin Imogen Cardigan, get a whiff or two’s repose.","而且，在那里也方便她溜到走廊里，和那些留着络腮胡的鉴赏家们互道一声“有趣”；或拿出表姐伊莫金·卡迪根送的结婚礼物——一个小金盒，抽出一支香烟，吸两口休息休息。"
"To speak quite honestly, Fleur had a natural sense of rhythm which caused her discomfort during those long and ‘interesting’ passages which evidenced, as it were, the composer’s rise and fall from his bed of thorns.","坦率地说，弗勒的节奏感与生俱来，当演奏到那些冗长而“有趣”的乐章时，她仿佛对作曲家所表现的如坐针毡、坐立不安的情形感同身受，这不免让她十分难受。"
"She secretly loved a tune, and the impossibility of ever confessing this without losing hold of Solstis, Baff, Birdigal, MacLewis, Clorane, and other English restoration composers, sometimes taxed to its limit a nature which had its Spartan side.","她默默喜欢一支曲调，为了不失去苏斯迪斯、巴夫、博迪格尔、麦克刘易斯、克罗雷和其他英国复兴派作曲家，她永远不会承认这一点。有时，这使她那具有自虐倾向的性格压抑到了极点。"
"Even to Michael she would not ‘confess’; and it was additionally trying when, with his native disrespect of persons, accentuated by life in the trenches and a publisher’s office, he would mutter: “Gad!Get on with it!” or: “Cripes!Ain’t he took bad!” especially as she knew that Michael was really putting up with it better than herself, having a more literary disposition, and a less dancing itch in his toes.","即使对迈克尔，她也不会承认。迈克尔生来不尊重别人，而战场上的生活和出版家的身份使他的这种态度更加严重，因此，每当他咕噜着：“上帝！快点儿过去吧！”或者“天啊！他这下可弄错了！”时，她就感到格外难受，尤其是她知道迈克尔实际比她更能忍耐，更有文学气质，而对舞蹈则没有她那么入迷。"
"The first movement of the new Solstis composition—‘Phantasmagoria Piemontesque’—to which they had especially come to listen, began with some drawn-out chords.","他们专程来听苏斯迪斯新乐曲的第一乐章——《皮埃蒙特斯克幻想曲》，该乐章以几个悠长的和弦开始。"
"“What oh!” said Michael’s voice in her ear: “Three pieces of furniture moved simultaneously on a parquet floor!”","她耳边传来迈克尔的声音：“哇哦，三件家具同时在一块镶木地板上移动！”"
"In Fleur’s involuntary smile was the whole secret of why her marriage had not been intolerable.","弗勒不禁笑了，她的婚姻并非无法忍受，她的笑容把这个秘密完全暴露了。"
"After all, Michael was a dear!","迈克尔毕竟很可爱！"
"Devotion and mercury—jesting and loyalty—combined, they piqued and touched even a heart given away before it was bestowed on him.","他既专一又活泼，既幽默又忠诚——这一切都触动甚至是感动了她，虽然在嫁给他之前她就心有所属了。"
"‘Touch’ without ‘pique’ would have bored; ‘pique’ without ‘touch’ would have irritated.","没有“触动”的“感动”惹人厌恶，而没有“感动”的“触动”又惹人恼怒。"
"At this moment he was at peculiar advantage!","此刻，他处于极其有利的地位！"
"Holding on to his knees, with his ears standing up, eyes glassy from loyalty to Hugo, and tongue in cheek, he was listening to that opening in a way which evoked Fleur’s admiration.","为了表示对雨果的尊重，他双手抓牢膝盖，双耳竖起，目光呆滞，装模作样地听着序曲。他做出的这副样子引起了弗勒的钦佩。"
"The piece would be ‘interesting’—she fell into the state of outer observation and inner calculation very usual with her nowadays.","这段乐曲会很“有趣”——她陷入了一种状态：外表看上去在观察，而内心却在无限遐想，最近她一直这样。"
"Over there was L.S.D., the greater dramatist; she didn’t know him—yet.","那边坐着L. S. D.，一位更加伟大的剧作家，她还不认识他。"
"He looked rather frightening, his hair stood up so straight.","他看上去相当可怕，头发竖得直直的。"
"And her eye began picturing him on her copper floor against a Chinese picture.","于是，她眼前浮现出一个画面：他正站在她家的红棕色地板上，身后是一幅中国画。"
"And there—yes!","啊，快看那边！"
"Gurdon Minho!","是格登·明霍！"
"Imagine HIS coming to anything so modern!","想不到他竟会到如此时髦的地方来！"
"His profile WAS rather Roman—of the Aurelian period!","他的侧面颇有点儿罗马味道——奥勒利安皇帝时期的味道。"
"Passing on from that antique, with the pleased thought that by this time tomorrow she might have collected it, she quartered the assembly face by face—she did not want to miss any one important.","她把目光从那个古董身上移开，想到明晚这个时候她准会收罗到这件东西了，心里颇为高兴，一一打量了剧场里的每一个人——她可不想遗漏任何一个重要人物。"
"“The furniture” had come to a sudden standstill.","“那件家具”突然停住了。"
"“Interesting!” said a voice over her shoulder.","“有趣！”声音从她背后传来。"
"Aubrey Greene!","是奥布里·格林！"
"Illusive, rather moonlit, with his silky fair hair brushed straight back, and his greenish eyes—his smile always made her feel that he was ‘getting’ at her.","好像幻影一般，颇有点儿月朦胧的感觉。他柔亮的金色头发笔直地向后梳着；他淡绿色的眼眸以及他的微笑，总让她有种被“挑逗”的感觉。"
"But, after all, he was a cartoonist!","不管怎么说，毕竟他也是个漫画家！"
"“Yes, isn’t it?”","“嗯，可不是吗？”"
"He curled away.","他转身走了。"
"He might have stayed a little longer—there wouldn’t be time for any one else before those songs of Birdigal’s!","他本可以多呆一会儿的。因为在博迪格尔的那几首曲子之前，其他人是不会有时间表演的！"
"Here came the singer Charles Powls!","现在歌唱家查尔斯·波尔斯出场了！"
"How stout and efficient he looked, dragging little Birdigal to the piano.","他把个子矮小的博迪格尔拖到钢琴那边，这让他看起来既壮实又能干。"
"Charming accompaniment—rippling, melodious!","迷人的伴奏——轻轻荡漾着，和谐悦耳！"
"The stout, efficient man began to sing.","这位既壮实又能干的人开始唱了。"
"How different from the accompaniment!","怎么与伴奏如此不一样呢！"
"The song hit every note just off the solar plexus.","这首歌的每个音调都没有打动她的交感神经。"
"It mathematically prevented her from feeling pleasure.","精确地讲，没有一个音调让她感到快乐。"
"Birdigal must have written it in horror of some one calling it ‘vocal.’","博迪格尔创作这首歌时，一定害怕有人将之称为“声乐作品”。"
"Vocal!","声乐作品！"
"Fleur knew how catching the word was; it would run like a measle round the ring, and Birdigal would be no more!","弗勒知道这个词极具传染性，它会像麻疹一样迅速传遍全场，这样一来，博迪格尔就完蛋了！"
"Poor Birdigal!","可怜的博迪格尔！"
"But this was ‘interesting.’","但是这一点很“有趣”。"
"Only, as Michael was saying: “O, my Gawd!”","这时，迈克尔也发出感叹：“上帝啊！”"
"Three songs!","三首歌！"
"Powls was wonderful—so loyal!","波尔斯真了不起啊——如此忠诚！"
"Never one note hit so that it rang out like music!","没有一个音符听起来像音乐！"
"Her mind fluttered off to Wilfrid.","她的思绪跑到威尔弗里德那里去了。"
"To him, of all the younger poets, people accorded the right to say something; it gave him such a position—made him seem to come out of life, instead of literature.","在所有的年轻诗人中，人们给了他话语权；这给他奠定了一种地位——似乎他来自于生活而非来自文学。"
"Besides, he had done things in the war, was a son of Lord Mullyon, would get the Mercer Prize probably, for ‘Copper Coin.’","此外，他参加过战争，是马利昂勋爵的儿子，有望凭《铜币》获得默瑟奖。"
"If Wilfrid abandoned her, a star would fall from the firmament above her copper floor.","如果威尔弗里德离她而去的话，那么一颗明星将会从她家的红棕色地板上空落下。"
"He had no right to leave her in the lurch.","他无权让她陷入困境。"
"He must learn not to be violent—not to think physically.","他必须要学会不粗鲁——不随心所欲。"
"No! she couldn’t let Wilfrid slip away; nor could she have any more sob-stuff in her life, searing passions, cul de sacs, aftermaths.","不！她决不能让威尔弗里德溜走，她也不允许自己的生活中再出现任何痛苦的事情、枯萎的感情、走不通的路以及不幸的结果。"
"She had tasted of that; a dulled ache still warned her.","她曾经尝过这种滋味，旧伤疤还在隐隐作痛，时刻提醒着她。"
"Birdigal was bowing, Michael saying: “Come out for a whiff!","博迪格尔鞠躬致谢，迈克尔说道：“出去吸口烟吧！"
"The next thing’s a dud!”","下一个节目没什么可看的！”"
"Oh! ah!","哦！啊！"
"Beethoven.","贝多芬。"
"Poor old Beethoven!","可怜的老贝！"
"So out of date—one did RATHER enjoy him!","早就过时了——人们从前确实很欣赏他！"
"The corridor, and refectory beyond, were swarming with the restoration movement.","走廊和那一边的休息室都挤满了参与复兴运动的人。"
"Young men and women with faces and heads of lively and distorted character, were exchanging the word ‘interesting.’","青年们看起来活泼而又偏执，他们彼此交流，互道“有趣”。"
"Men of more massive type, resembling sedentary matadors, blocked all circulation.","体态魁梧的男子们，像岿然不动的斗牛士，把过道都堵住了。"
"Fleur and Michael passed a little way along, stood against the wall, and lighted cigarettes.","弗勒和迈克尔向前走了几步就靠墙站住了，点燃了香烟。"
"Fleur smoked hers delicately—a very little one in a tiny amber holder.","弗勒的香烟包在琥珀烟嘴里，显得格外小巧玲珑，她优雅地吸着烟。"
"She had the air of admiring blue smoke rather than of making it; there were spheres to consider beyond this sort of crowd—one never knew who might be about!—the sphere, for instance, in which Alison Charwell moved, politico-literary, catholic in taste, but, as Michael always put it, “Convinced, like a sanitary system, that it’s the only sphere in the world; look at the way they all write books of reminiscence about each other!”","与其说她在吸烟，倒不如说她在欣赏吐出的缕缕青烟；除了这些听众外，她还要考虑其他社会领域的人——具体那个领域里会涉及什么样的人物谁也不清楚！比如，艾莉森·查韦尔的活动领域：层次广泛的政治文学。但是，正如迈克尔常说的：“类似于一种卫生制度，相信自己是世界上仅有的社会领域；可以看看他们在回忆录里是怎么写彼此的！”"
"They might, she always felt, disapprove of women smoking in public halls.","她始终感觉他们似乎不赞成妇女在公共场合吸烟。"
"Consorting delicately with iconoclasm, Fleur never forgot that her feet were in two worlds at least.","弗勒巧妙地同反对传统的人交往，从不忘记她至少同时属于两个世界。"
"Standing there, observant of all to left and right, she noted against the wall one whose face was screened by his programme.","站在那里，她观察着周围的一切，突然看到一个人靠墙站着，用节目单挡着脸。"
"‘Wilfrid,’ she thought, ‘and doesn’t mean to see me!’","她心想：“是威尔弗里德，他还故意装作没看见我！”"
"Mortified, as a child from whom a sixpence is filched, she said:","她像一个被偷走了六便士的小孩一样，感觉十分受辱。她说道："
"“There’s Wilfrid!","“那是威尔弗里德！"
"Fetch him, Michael!”","迈克尔，请他过来！”"
"Michael crossed, and touched his best man’s sleeve; Desert’s face emerged, frowning.","迈克尔走过去，碰碰他的男傧相的袖子。德赛特的脸露了出来，愁容满面。"
"She saw him shrug his shoulders, turn and walk into the throng.","她看见他耸耸肩膀，转身走入人群中去了。"
"Michael came back.","迈克尔回来了。"
"“Wilfrid’s got the hump to-night; says he’s not fit for human society—queer old son!”","“威尔弗里德今晚闷闷不乐，说自己不适合人类社会了，真是个古怪的家伙！”"
"How obtuse men were!","男人多迟钝啊！"
"Because Wilfrid was his pal, Michael did not see; and that was lucky!","因为威尔弗里德是迈克尔的朋友，迈克尔就看不出来，这倒也算幸运！"
"So Wilfrid really meant to avoid her!","这样看来，威尔弗里德真的打算避开她了！"
"Well, she would see!","好吧，她倒要瞧瞧！"
"And she said:","于是她说："
"“I’m tired, Michael; let’s go home.”","“迈克尔，我累了，咱们回家吧。”"
"His hand slid round her arm.","他轻轻挽住她的胳膊。"
"“Sorry, old thing; come along!”","“对不起，宝贝，走吧！”"
"They stood a moment in a neglected doorway, watching Woomans, the conductor, launched towards his orchestra.","他们在一个无人注意的门口站了一会儿，望着乐队指挥伍曼士朝他的管弦乐队走去。"
"“Look at him,” said Michael; “guy hung out of an Italian window, legs and arms all stuffed and flying!","“你看他，”迈克尔说，“多像挂在意式小窗上，腿和胳膊把衣服撑得满当当的，还在那儿手舞足蹈着！"
"And look at the Frapka and her piano—that’s a turbulent union!”","再看看这位弗莱帕凯和她弹的钢琴曲——真是一团糟！”"
"There was a strange sound.","突然传来一阵奇怪的声音。"
"“Melody, by George!” said Michael.","“天啊，这旋律真好听！”迈克尔说道。"
"An attendant muttered in their ears: “Now, sir, I’m going to shut the door.”","一位服务生在他们耳边低声说：“先生，我要关门了。”"
"Fleur had a fleeting view of L.S.D. sitting upright as his hair, with closed eyes.","弗勒快速瞥了一眼L. S. D.，他坐得和他头发一样笔直，闭着眼睛。"
"The door was shut—they were outside in the hall.","门关上了，他们站在了外面的大厅里。"
"“Wait here, darling; I’ll nick a rickshaw.”","“亲爱的，在这等会儿，我去叫辆人力车。”"
"Fleur huddled her chin in her fur.","弗勒将下巴缩进毛皮领子里。"
"It was easterly and cold.","天刮着东风，很冷。"
"A voice behind her said:","有个声音在她背后说道："
"“Well, Fleur, am I going East?”","“喂，弗勒，我该去东方吗？”"
"Wilfrid!","威尔弗里德！"
"His collar up to his ears, a cigarette between his lips, hands in pockets, eyes devouring.","他的衣领竖到耳根，嘴里还叼着烟，双手插兜，眼睛直勾勾地盯着她。"
"“You’re very silly, Wilfrid!”","“你真傻，威尔弗里德！”"
"“Anything you like; am I going East?”","“随你怎么想，我该去东方吗?”"
"“No; Sunday morning—eleven o’clock at the Tate.","“别去，星期天上午11点，泰特美术馆见。"
"We’ll talk it out.”","咱俩好好谈谈。”"
"“Convenu!”","“同意！”"
"And he was gone.","说完他就走了。"
"Alone suddenly, like that, Fleur felt the first shock of reality.","突然就这样孤独地一个人呆在那里，弗勒第一次被现实震撼了。"
"Was Wilfrid truly going to be unmanageable?","难道威尔弗里德真的要变得难以掌控了吗？"
"A taxicab ground up; Michael beckoned; Fleur stepped in.","一辆出租车停了下来，迈克尔招呼她，弗勒跨了进去。"
"Passing a passionately lighted oasis of young ladies displaying to the interested Londoner the acme of Parisian undress, she felt Michael incline towards her.","他们经过一片灯红酒绿之地，一群年轻女子正向饶有兴致的伦敦人展示巴黎裸体艺术的最高成就，这时，她感觉迈克尔正朝她凑过来。"
"If she were going to keep Wilfrid, she must be nice to Michael.","如果想留住威尔弗里德，她就必须对迈克尔亲热些。"
"Only:","她只说："
"“You needn’t kiss me in Piccadilly Circus, Michael!”","“迈克尔，你没必要在皮卡迪利广场吻我！”"
"“Sorry, duckie!","“对不起，宝贝！"
"It’s a little previous—I meant to get you opposite the Partheneum.”","我看时间还早，想带你到对面先贤祠去。”"
"Fleur remembered how he had slept on a Spanish sofa for the first fortnight of their honeymoon; how he always insisted that she must not spend anything on him, but must always let him give her what he liked, though she had three thousand a year and he twelve hundred; how jumpy he was when she had a cold—and how he always came home to tea.","弗勒回想起，在他们度蜜月的头两个星期里，他一直睡在西班牙式的沙发上；他一直坚持不让她给他花钱，却总是送她他想送给她的东西，尽管她一年收入3 000镑，而他只有1200镑；在她感冒时，他又是多么担心——而且他总是会回家喝下午茶。"
"Yes, he was a dear!","的确，他真的很可爱！"
"But would she break her heart if he went East or West tomorrow?","但是，如果明天他打算去东方或者西方的话，她也会伤心吗？"
"Snuggled against him, she was surprised at her own cynicism.","她依偎在他怀里，不禁为自己的玩世不恭而惊讶。"
"A telephone message written out, in the hall, ran: “Please tell Mrs. Mont I’ve got Mr. Gurding Minner.","门厅里有一条电话留言，写着：“请转告蒙特太太，我已邀请到格亭·明纳先生。"
"Lady Alisson.”","艾莉森夫人。”"
"It was restful.","这让人感觉踏实了。"
"A real antique!","一件真正的古董！"
"She turned on the lights in her room, and stood for a moment admiring it.","她打开房间里的灯，站了一会儿，欣赏着屋子。"
"Truly pretty!","真美啊！"
"A slight snuffle from the corner—Ting-a-ling, tan on a black cushion, lay like a Chinese lion in miniature; pure, remote, fresh from evening communion with the Square railings.","房间的角落里传来一阵轻微的鼻息声——是小叮铃，在黑色垫子上的棕褐色的小家伙，像只小巧的中国狮子躺在那里一样；它纯净、淡漠，刚和广场围栏夜会了一场。"
"“I see you,” said Fleur.","“我看到你了。”弗勒说。"
"Ting-a-ling did not stir; his round black eyes watched his mistress undress.","小叮铃一动不动，用浑圆的黑眼睛望着女主人脱衣服。"
"When she returned from the bathroom he was curled into a ball.","当她从浴室出来，它已蜷缩成一团。"
"Fleur thought: ‘Queer!","弗勒心想：“奇怪！"
"How does he know Michael won’t be coming?’","它怎么知道迈克尔不会来？”"
"And slipping into her well warmed bed, she too curled herself up and slept.","于是它钻进了弗勒那张舒适而温暖的床里，她也蜷起身子睡了。"
"But in the night, contrary to her custom, she awoke.","但是，到了深夜，她反常地醒了。"
"A cry—long, weird, trailing, from somewhere—the river—the slums at the back—rousing memory—poignant, aching—of her honeymoon—Granada, its roofs below, jet, ivory, gold; the watchman’s cry, the lines in Jon’s letter:","叫喊声——悠长、怪异、拖曳，不知来自何处——可能来自后面河对岸的贫民窟——唤起了她在格拉纳达度蜜月时伤心刺骨的记忆——格拉纳达的屋顶下，泛起黑玉色、象牙白和金黄色；更夫的叫喊声，让她想起了乔恩信中的那些诗句："
"“Voice in the night crying, down in the old sleeping Spanish City darkened under her white stars.","“深夜里回荡着哭泣声，从古老的沉睡的西班牙城市下传来，在她银白色的星空下黯淡。"
"What says the voice—its clear, lingering anguish?","这声音在诉说什么——是它切肤的挥之不去的痛苦吗？"
"Just the watchman, telling his dateless tale of safety?","还是巡夜人报着他那无休止的平安？"
"Just a road-man, flinging to the moon his song?","抑或是筑路人对着明月诉说自己的心声？"
"No!","不！"
"‘Tis one deprived, whose lover’s heart is weeping,","这是一位被剥夺权利的人，他恋人的心正在哭泣。"
"Just his cry: ‘How long?’”","他在叫喊：‘还要多久？’”"
"A cry, or had she dreamed it?","是有人在叫喊，还是她在做梦？"
"Jon, Wilfrid, Michael!","乔恩、威尔弗里德、迈克尔！"
"No use to have a heart!","她的心已疲惫不堪！"

"Chapter IV","第四章"
"Dining","晚宴"
"Lady Alison Charwell, born Heathfield, daughter of the first Earl of Campden, and wife to Lionel Charwell, K.C., Michael’s somewhat young uncle, was a delightful Englishwoman brought up in a set accepted as the soul of society.","艾莉森·查韦尔夫人出嫁前姓希思菲尔德，是第一代坎普登伯爵之女，是迈克尔的小叔叔、王室法律顾问莱昂内尔·查韦尔之妻。她是个讨人喜欢的英国女士，从小接受的是公认的社会主流思想教育。"
"Full of brains, energy, taste, money, and tinctured in its politico-legal ancestry by blue blood, this set was linked to, but apart from ‘Snooks’ and the duller haunts of birth and privilege.","有这样一群人，他们有智慧、有活力、有品位、有财富，出身贵族并且具有政治法律的家世背景，同“轻蔑”俱乐部有联系却又不是其中的成员，也不去特权阶级常去的沉闷场所。"
"It was gay, charming, free-and-easy, and, according to Michael, “Snobbish, old thing, aesthetically and intellectually, but they’ll never see it.","他们快乐、有趣、自由自在，但是据迈克尔所说：“亲爱的，他们在审美和智力上都是自命不凡的，他们自己却永远意识不到。"
"They think they’re the top notch—quick, healthy, up-to-date, well-bred, intelligent; they simply can’t imagine their equals.","他们自以为是上等人——机敏、健康、时尚、有教养、聪明，根本无法想象谁能比得上他们。"
"But you see their imagination is deficient.","可是，他们缺乏想象力。"
"Their really creative energy would go into a pint pot.","他们把真正的创造力用在钻牛角尖上。"
"Look at their books—they’re always ON something—philosophy, spiritualism, poetry, fishing, themselves; why, even their sonnets dry up before they’re twenty-five.","看看他们写的书——他们总在高谈阔论——哲学、唯心论、诗歌、垂钓以及他们自己，这就是为什么他们不到25岁就再也写不出什么了。"
"They know everything—except mankind outside their own set.","他们事事精通，就是不懂自己圈子之外的世界。"
"Oh! they work—they run the show—they have to; there’s no one else with their brains, and energy, and taste.","哦！他们工作——他们筹划演出——他们不得不这样做，因为没人会比他们更有头脑、精力和情趣了。"
"But they run it round and round in their own blooming circle.","于是，他们在自己盛大的圈子里没完没了地办演出。"
"It’s the world to them—and it might be worse.","对他们而言，这就是世界——而且这个世界以后也许会更不遂人意。"
"They’ve patented their own golden age; but it’s a trifle flyblown since the war.”","他们已经给他们专属的黄金时代申请了专利。不过，自从大战以来，这种专利已经名声败坏了。”"
"Alison Charwell—in and of this world, so spryly soulful, debonnaire, free, and cosy—lived within a stone’s throw of Fleur, in a house pleasant, architecturally, as any in London.","艾莉森·查韦尔就是这个圈子的一员，她活泼热情、爽朗大方、平易近人。她和弗勒住得很近，她家的建筑风格十分宜人，可以同伦敦任何住宅相媲美。"
"Forty years old, she had three children and considerable beauty, wearing a little fine from mental and bodily activity.","她今年40岁，生过三个孩子，风韵犹存，自内而外的充沛活力让她显得格外年轻。"
"Something of an enthusiast, she was fond of Michael, in spite of his strange criticisms, so that his matrimonial venture had piqued her from the start.","尽管迈克尔好作奇谈怪论，她却很欣赏和喜欢他，因此，从一开始，她就对他在婚姻上的冒险十分好奇。"
"Fleur was dainty, had quick natural intelligence—this new niece was worth cultivation.","弗勒天生丽质，又生性机敏，所以，她认为这个新侄媳妇值得栽培。"
"But, though adaptable and assimilative, Fleur had remained curiously unassimilated; she continued to whet the curiosity of Lady Alison, accustomed to the close borough of choice spirits, and finding a certain poignancy in contact with the New Age on Fleur’s copper floor.","可是，虽然弗勒是个“可塑之才”，却很奇怪地一直未被同化，这更加激发了艾莉森夫人的好奇心。夫人习惯了上等人的小圈子，在弗勒家的红棕色地板上，和“新时代”接触，她感觉很不舒服。"
"She met with an irreverence there, which, not taken too seriously, flipped her mind.","在那里，她被怠慢了，虽然她不太看重这些，但这却扰乱了她的思绪。"
"On that floor she almost felt a back number.","站在那块地板上，她几乎觉得自己很落伍。"
"It was stimulating.","这一切对她来说是一种刺激。"
"Receiving Fleur’s telephonic enquiry about Gurdon Minho, she had rung up the novelist.","那天，她一接完弗勒打听格登·明霍的电话，便立刻给这位小说家打电话。"
"She knew him, if not well.","她虽然认识他，却不太相熟。"
"Nobody seemed to know him well; amiable, polite, silent, rather dull and austere; but with a disconcerting smile, sometimes ironical, sometimes friendly.","似乎谁和他都不太熟，他和蔼可亲、彬彬有礼，却沉默寡言，颇有些沉闷和严肃；最令人不舒服的是他的笑容，有时讥笑嘲讽，有时却又和善亲切。"
"His books were now caustic, now sentimental.","他的作品时而尖酸刻薄，时而多愁善感。"
"On both counts it was rather the fashion to run him down, though he still seemed to exist.","就这两种风格，当时颇有一种把他批评得一文不值的趋势，然而他仍旧在文坛占有一席之地。"
"She rang him up.","她给他打电话。"
"Would he come to a dinner tomorrow at her young nephew, Michael Mont’s, and meet the younger generation?","她问他明天能否赏光到她年轻的侄子迈克尔·蒙特家吃饭，和年轻人交流一下。"
"His answer came, rather high-pitched:","他说当然可以，嗓门还挺高："
"“Rather!","“当然好啦！"
"Full fig, or dinner jacket?”","穿正式礼服，还是一般晚礼服？”"
"“How awfully nice of you! they’ll be ever so pleased.","“您真是太好了！知道您能出席晚宴，他们一定非常高兴。"
"Full fig, I believe.","我想，穿正式礼服吧。"
"It’s the second anniversary of their wedding.”","这也是他们结婚两周年纪念日。”"
"She hung up the receiver with the thought: ‘He must be writing a book about them!’","她挂上电话时还在想：“他一定会以他们为原型写本书的！”"
"Conscious of responsibility, she arrived early.","出于责任感，她很早就到了。"
"It was a grand night at her husband’s Inn, so that she brought nothing with her but the feeling of adventure, pleasant after a day spent in fluttering over the decision at ‘Snooks’.","今晚，她丈夫的法律协会有场大应酬，因此她只身前来参加弗勒的晚宴，只想着过来凑凑热闹。在为“轻蔑”的决议忙碌了一整天后，她此时感到轻松愉快。"
"She was received only by Ting-a-ling, who had his back to the fire, and took no notice beyond a stare.","只有小叮铃接待了她。它背对着壁炉，只朝她瞪了一眼，就没再理会她。"
"Sitting down on the jade green settee, she said:","她在那张翠绿色的长靠椅上坐下，说道："
"“Well, you funny little creature, don’t you know me after all this time?”","“喂，你这滑稽的小家伙，都这么久了，你还不认识我吗？”"
"Ting-a-ling’s black shiny gaze seemed saying: “You recur here, I know; most things recur.","小叮铃那双黑亮的眼睛似乎在说：“我知道你又来了，绝大多数事情都是这样循环往复的。"
"There is nothing new about the future.”","未来也没什么新鲜可言。”"
"Lady Alison fell into a train of thought: The new generation!","艾莉森夫人不禁陷入沉思：这就是新的一代啊！"
"Did she want her own girls to be of it!","她是否希望自己的女儿也属于这一代呢！"
"She would like to talk to Mr. Minho about that—they had had a very nice talk down at Beechgroves before the war.","她想同明霍先生谈谈这个话题——战前，在比奇格罗夫，他们有过一次畅谈。"
"Nine years ago—Sybil only six, Joan only four then!","那是九年前了——那时西比尔只有六岁，琼才四岁！"
"Time went, things changed!","光阴似箭，时过境迁！"
"A new generation!","新的一代！"
"And what was the difference?","他们到底有什么特别的呢？"
"“I think we had more tradition!” she said to herself softly.","“我想我们更传统些吧!”她轻声自语道。"
"A slight sound drew her eyes up from contemplation of her feet.","一阵轻微的声响让她移开了凝视着自己双脚的目光。"
"Ting-a-ling was moving his tail from side to side on the hearthrug, as if applauding.","小叮铃在炉前的地毯上来回摆弄尾巴，仿佛在表示欢迎。"
"Fleur’s voice, behind her, said:","这时，她身后传来了弗勒的声音："
"“Well, darling, I’m awfully late.","“亲爱的，我来得太迟了。"
"It WAS good of you to get me Mr. Minho.","你真是太好了，替我邀请到明霍先生。"
"I do hope they’ll all behave.","我希望他们都能遵守常规。"
"He’ll be between you and me, anyway; I’m sticking him at the top, and Michael at the bottom, between Pauline Upshire and Amabel Nazing.","不管怎样，他会坐在你和我中间，我把他安排在主座，迈克尔在末座，迈克尔两旁分别是保利娜·厄普夏和阿玛贝尔·内津。"
"You’ll have Sibley on your left, and I’ll have Aubrey on my right, then Nesta Gorse and Walter Nazing; opposite them Linda Frewe and Charles Upshire.","西布莉坐在你左边，奥布里坐在我右边，挨着他们的是内丝塔·戈斯和沃尔特·内津，他们对面是琳达·弗鲁和查尔斯·厄普夏。"
"Twelve.","一共12个人。"
"You know them all.","你全都认识。"
"Oh! and you mustn’t mind if the Nazings and Nesta smoke between the courses.","哦！如果内津夫妇和内丝塔在上菜的间歇吸烟，你可别见怪啊。"
"Amabel will do it.","阿玛贝尔可能也抽烟。"
"She comes from Virginia—it’s the reaction.","她来自弗吉尼亚——那里的人都好抽烟。"
"I do hope she’ll have some clothes on; Michael always says it’s a mistake when she has; but having Mr. Minoho makes one a little nervous.","我真希望她穿点儿衣服在身上，迈克尔老是说她穿上衣服是个错误；不过，明霍先生在场，气氛会有点儿紧张。"
"Did you see Nesta’s skit in ‘The Bouquet’?","你看过《恭维话》里内丝塔的那篇讽刺短文吗？"
"Oh, too frightfully amusing—clearly meant for L.S.D.!","啊，那真是太有趣了——明明指的就是L. S. D.啊！"
"Ting, my Ting, are you going to stay and see all these people?","叮铃，我的叮铃，你想留在这见见所有客人吗？"
"Well, then, get up here or you’ll be trodden on.","那么，爬上来吧，不然你会被踩到的。"
"Isn’t he Chinese?","看它是不是中国狗？"
"He does so round off the room.”","它的确使整个房间熠熠生辉。”"
"Ting-a-ling laid his nose on his paws, in the centre of a jade green cushion.","小叮铃把鼻子放在爪子上，趴在了翠绿色的靠垫中央。"
"“Mr. Gurding Minner!”","“格亭·明纳先生来了！”"
"The well-known novelist looked pale and composed.","这位著名小说家脸色苍白、神态自若。"
"Shaking the two extended hands, he gazed at Ting-a-ling, and said:","他与两个人握手，眼睛盯着小叮铃，说道："
"“How nice!","“多可爱!"
"How are YOU, my little man?”","你好吗，小家伙？”"
"Ting-a-ling did not stir.","小叮铃动也不动。"
"“You take me for a common English dog, sir!” his silence seemed to say.","它的沉默似乎在说：“你把我当成一只普通的英国狗了，先生！”"
"""Mr. and Mrs. Walter Nazon, Miss Lende Frow. ""","“沃尔特·内森夫妇到了，琳达·弗劳小姐到了。”"
"Amabel Nazing came first, clear alabaster from her fair hair down to the six inches of gleaming back above her waist-line, shrouded alabaster from four inches below the knee to the gleaming toes of her shoes; the eminent novelist mechanically ceased to commune with Ting-a-ling.","阿玛贝尔·内津先走了进来。从她美丽的头发到腰上六寸若隐若现的背部，宛如明净的雪花石膏；从膝盖以下四寸到鞋里微微露出的脚趾，则像是裹着一层布的雪花石膏。这位著名的小说家也不由得停止了与小叮铃的交流。"
"Walter Nazing, who followed a long way up above his wife, had a tiny line of collar emergent from swathes of black, and a face, cut a hundred years ago, that slightly resembled Shelley’s.","沃尔特·内津一路跟在妻子后面，他身材高大，从黑色的衣服里露出一小截衣领，他的脸像是从一百年前雕刻出来的，有点儿像雪莱。"
"His literary productions were sometimes felt to be like the poetry of that bard, and sometimes like the prose of Marcel Proust.","他文学作品的风格有时像雪莱，有时又像马塞尔·普鲁斯特。"
"“What oh!” as Michael said.","就像迈克尔所说：“这算什么呀！”"
"Linda Frewe, whom Fleur at once introduced to Gurdon Minho, was one about whose work no two people in her drawing-room ever agreed.","弗勒立刻把琳达·弗鲁介绍给格登·明霍认识。对于琳达的作品，在这个客厅的客人们中，从来没有得到过统一的见解。"
"Her works ‘Trifles’ and ‘The Furious Don’ had quite divided all opinion.","人们对她的两部作品《琐事》和《狂怒的西班牙绅士》，意见分歧都很大。"
"Genius according to some, drivel according to others, those books always roused an interesting debate whether a slight madness enhanced or diminished the value of art.","有些人认为是上乘之作，有些人认为是胡说八道，她的作品总是会引起一场有趣的辩论——小小的疯狂到底是会加强艺术的价值，还是会贬低艺术的价值？"
"She herself paid little attention to criticism—she produced.","她本人对此类评论并不介怀，她只管继续创作。"
"“THE Mr. Minho?","“您就是明霍先生？"
"How interesting!","多有趣啊!"
"I’ve never read anything of yours.”","我还没读过您的任何一部作品。”"
"Fleur gave a little gasp.","弗勒微微喘了口气。"
"“What—don’t you know Mr. Minho’s cats?","“什么——你不知道明霍先生写的猫吗？"
"But they’re wonderful.","写得好极了。"
"Mr. Minho, I do want Mrs. Walter Nazing to know you.","明霍先生，我再介绍你认识沃尔特·内津夫人。"
"Amabel—Mr. Gurdon Minho.”","这位是阿玛贝尔，这位是格登·明霍先生。”"
"“Oh!","“哦！"
"Mr. Minho—how perfectly lovely!","明霍先生，见到您真荣幸！"
"I’ve wanted to know you ever since my cradle.”","我老早就想认识您了。”"
"Fleur heard the novelist say quietly:","弗勒听到这位小说家平静地说："
"“I could wish it had been longer;” and passed on in doubt to greet Nesta Gorse and Sibley Swan, who came in, as if they lived together, quarrelling over L.S.D., Nesta upholding him because of his ‘panache’, Sibley maintaining that wit had died with the Restoration; this fellow was alive!","“我也希望更早些认识您。”然后疑惑地走过去和刚进来的内丝塔·戈斯和西布莉·斯旺打招呼。她们两人一同进来，好像住在一起似的，边走边争论着，争论的焦点好像是L. S. D.。内丝塔因为他的作品《羽饰》而拥护他，西布莉则认为，机智已经随着复兴运动而死亡，这个人却还活着！"
"Michael followed with the Upshires and Aubrey Greene, whom he had encountered in the hall.","迈克尔跟在厄普夏夫妇和奥布里·格林后面一起进来，他在门厅碰见了他们。"
"The party was complete.","宴会的客人到齐了。"
"Fleur loved perfection, and that evening was something of a nightmare.","弗勒追求事事完美，而那天晚上有点儿噩梦的感觉。"
"Was it a success?","这算成功吗？"
"Minho was so clearly the least brilliant person there; even Alison talked better.","宴会上，明霍显然是最没意思的人，连艾莉森的谈吐都比他强。"
"And yet he had such a fine skull.","不过，他却头脑精明。"
"She did hope he would not go away early.","她真希望他不会过早离开。"
"Some one would be almost sure to say ‘Dug up!’ or ‘Thick and bald!’ before the door closed behind him.","只要他起身离开，门还没关严，肯定就会有人说：“出土的古董！”或“又呆又秃！”。"
"He was pathetically agreeable, as if trying to be liked, or, at least, not despised too much.","他忍气吞声地附和别人，试图讨好大家，或者，至少不要太招人鄙视。"
"And there must, of course, be more in him than met the sense of hearing.","当然，他脑子里的东西肯定比他讲给大家听的要多。"
"After the crab souffle he did seem to be talking to Alison, and all about youth.","吃过蟹粉蛋奶酥后，他好像确实在和艾莉森聊天，内容全是关于年轻人的。"
"Fleur listened with one ear.","弗勒竖起耳朵听着。"
"“Youth feels... main stream of life... not giving it what it wants.","“青春年少时感觉到……生活的主流……没有得到它所向往的东西。"
"Past and future getting haloes... Quite!","过去和未来获得光荣……的确如此！"
"Contemporary life no earthly just now... No... Only comfort for us—we’ll be antiquated, some day, like Congreve, Sterne, Defoe... have our chance again... WHY?","在当代生活中，已经没有正义可言了……不……对我们只有安慰——总有一天我们都会过时，像康格里夫、斯特恩、笛福……我们还会有机会……为什么？"
"What IS driving them out of the main current?","是什么正在把他们赶出主流？"
"Oh!","哦！"
"Probably surfeit... newspapers... photographs.","可能是暴饮暴食……报纸……照片。"
"Don’t see life itself, only reports... reproductions of it; all seems shoddy, lurid, commercial... Youth says ‘Away with it, let’s have the past or the future!’”","不思考生活本身，只看报道……生活的复制品，一切都显得质量低劣、耸人听闻和商业化……年轻人常说：‘管它呢，让我们享受过去或未来！’”"
"He took some salted almonds, and Fleur saw his eyes stray to the upper part of Amabel Nazing.","他吃了几颗盐渍杏仁，弗勒发现他的眼神落到了阿玛贝尔·内津的上半身。"
"Down there the conversation was like Association football—no one kept the ball for more than one kick.","宴会进行到这里，谈话就像踢英式足球——没人留住球，每个人只是踢一脚出去。"
"It shot from head to head.","球在大家之间被踢来踢去。"
"And after every set of passes some one would reach out and take a cigarette, and blow a blue cloud across the unclothed refectory table.","而且每传过一圈之后，就有人伸手拿支烟，把一团青烟喷到那张未铺桌布的狭长的餐桌上。"
"Fleur enjoyed the glow of her Spanish room—its tiled floor, richly coloured fruits in porcelain, its tooled leather, copper articles, and Soames’ Goya above a Moorish divan.","弗勒对她这间西班牙式房间的富丽堂皇的装修风格十分欣赏——花砖地面上印着盛满各色水果的瓷器，还有精工细刻的皮革、铜制品以及挂在摩尔式长沙发上的那幅索米斯画的戈雅。"
"She headed the ball promptly when it came her way, but initiated nothing.","她只在球飞到她这里时，才立即用头顶过去，她并不发球。"
"Her gift was to be aware of everything at once.","她有眼观六路、耳听八方的本领。"
"“Mrs. Michael Mont presented” the brilliant irrelevancies of Linda Frewe, the pricks and stimulations of Nesta Gorse, the moonlit sliding innuendoes of Aubrey Greene, the upturning strokes of Sibley Swan, Amabel Nazing’s little cool American audacities, Charles Upshire’s curious bits of lore, Walter Nazing’s subversive contradictions, the critical intricacies of Pauline Upshire; Michael’s happy-go-lucky slings and arrows, even Alison’s knowledgeable quickness, and Gurdon Minho’s silences—she presented them all, showed them off, keeping her eyes and ears on the ball of talk lest it should touch earth and rest.","在“迈克尔·蒙特夫人呈现”中，她把大家的特点全都展示出来，呈现给大家——琳达·弗鲁的才华横溢与文不对题、内丝塔·戈斯的一针见血与激励刺激，奥布里·格林不动声色的含沙射影、西布莉·斯旺天翻地覆式的出击、阿玛贝尔·内津不顾一切的美国式鲁莽、查尔斯·厄普夏奇特的奇闻轶事、沃尔特·内津颠覆性的矛盾说辞、保利娜·厄普夏批判性的论点、迈克尔心不在焉的讽刺话，还有艾莉森的见识和机敏、格登·明霍的沉默——她时刻关注着那个谈话的“球”，唯恐它落在地上不动了。"
"Brilliant evening; but—a success?","美好的夜晚，可是——这算成功吗？"
"On the jade green settee, when the last of them had gone and Michael was seeing Alison home, she thought of Minho’s ‘Youth—not getting what it wants.’","等到最后一位客人离去，迈克尔也去送艾莉森回家了，她坐在翠绿长椅上，想起明霍刚才那句话：“青春年少时——没有得到向往的东西。”"
"No!","不！"
"Things didn’t fit.","事情不该如此。"
"“They don’t fit, do they, Ting!”","“现在事情不妥，是吗，叮铃？”"
"But Ting-a-ling was tired, only the tip of one ear quivered.","但是小叮铃已经累了，只是一只耳尖动了动。"
"Fleur leaned back and sighed.","弗勒靠在椅背上，叹了口气。"
"Ting-a-ling uncurled himself, and putting his forepaws on her thigh, looked up in her face.","小叮铃舒展开身体，前爪趴在她的大腿上，抬头望着她。"
"“Look at me,” he seemed to say, “I’m all right.","它似乎在说：“你看看我，我很好。"
"I get what I want, and I want what I get.","我得到了我所要的，我要我所得到的。"
"At present I want to go to bed.”","现在，我想去睡觉。”"
"“But I don’t,” said Fleur, without moving.","“但是我不想睡。”弗勒说，一动也不动。"
"“Just take me up!” said Ting-a-ling.","“那就抱我起来吧！”小叮铃说。"
"“Well,” said Fleur, “I suppose—It’s a nice person, but not the right person, Ting.”","弗勒说：“嗯，我想这个人不错，但不合适，叮铃。”"
"Ting-a-ling settled himself on her bare arms.","小叮铃在她的怀里安静下来。"
"“It’s all right,” he seemed to say.","“没关系的，”它好像在说，"
"“There’s a great deal too much sentiment and all that, out of China.","“除了在中国，此类多愁善感的感情事多的是。"
"Come on!”","振作起来吧!”"

"Chapter V","第五章"
"Eve","夏娃"
"The Honourable Wilfrid Desert’s rooms were opposite a picture gallery off Cork Street.","尊敬的威尔弗里德·德赛特先生的寓所位于科克大街一家画廊的对面。"
"The only male member of the aristocracy writing verse that any one would print, he had chosen them for seclusion rather than for comfort.","他出身贵族，是本家族中唯一一位男性诗人，而且很多人都肯为其出版。他选择住在这里，不是为了舒适，而是图其隐蔽。"
"His ‘junk,’ however, was not devoid of the taste and luxury which overflows from the greater houses of England.","然而，他的那些“破烂”摆设并不缺乏英国上流社会所富有的品位和奢华。"
"Furniture from the Hampshire seat of the Cornish nobleman, Lord Mullyon, had oozed into two vans, when Wilfrid settled in.","威尔弗里德搬进去的时候，曾从康沃尔贵族马利昂勋爵在汉普郡的宅邸悄悄运来了两大车的家具。"
"He was seldom to be found, however, in his nest, and was felt to be a rare bird, owing his rather unique position among the younger writers partly to his migratory reputation.","可是，人们很少能在他家里找到他。多半由于他飘忽不定的行踪，他在年轻一代作家中占据了相当独特的地位，人们都感觉他是稀有物种。"
"He himself hardly, perhaps, knew where he spent his time, or did his work, having a sort of mental claustrophobia, a dread of being hemmed in by people.","因其患有一种精神上的幽闭恐惧症，害怕人们的包围，也许就连他自己也不一定知道是在哪里消磨时间的，或是在什么地方工作的。"
"When the war broke out he had just left Eton; when the war was over he was twenty-three, as old a young man as ever turned a stave.","战争爆发的时候，他刚从伊顿公学毕业；战争结束时，23岁的他已经是一名舞文弄墨的青年诗人了。"
"His friendship with Michael, begun in hospital, had languished and renewed itself suddenly, when in 1920 Michael joined Danby and Winter, publishers, of Blake Street, Covent Garden.","他和迈克尔的友谊始于一家医院，两人的关系也曾一度转淡，但是在1920年又突然升温了。因为那时，迈克尔加入了位于科芬园布莱克街上的丹比&温特出版社。"
"The scattery enthusiasm of the sucking publisher had been roused by Wilfrid’s verse.","这位初出茅庐的出版商的沉睡的热情被威尔弗里德的诗句激发了出来。"
"Hob-nobbing lunches over the poems of one in need of literary anchorage, had been capped by the firm’s surrender to Michael’s insistence.","而这位诗人正需要找家出版社当靠山。经过多次共进午餐，两人密切地探讨了这些诗歌，最终在迈克尔的坚持下，出版社做出了让步。"
"The mutual intoxication of the first book Wilfrid had written and the first book Michael had sponsored was crowned at Michael’s wedding.","两个人都很兴奋：威尔弗里德写成了第一本书，这也是迈克尔资助出版的第一本书。两人的这份兴奋之情在迈克尔的婚礼上达到了顶峰。"
"Best man!","伴郎！"
"Since then, so far as Desert could be tied to anything, he had been tied to those two; nor, to do him justice, had he realised till a month ago that the attraction was not Michael, but Fleur.","从那时起，威尔弗里德那颗浪子的心便有了羁绊，他开始牵挂这对新人。说句公道话，直到一个月前，他才意识到吸引自己的并非迈克尔，而是弗勒。"
"Desert never spoke of the war, it was not possible to learn from his own mouth an effect which he might have summed up thus: “I lived so long with horror and death; I saw men so in the raw; I put hope of anything out of my mind so utterly, that I can never more have the faintest respect for theories, promises, conventions, moralities, and principles.","德赛特从不开口谈论战争，想从他的嘴里得出他对战争的印象是不可能的。这种印象他也许已经总结成这样：“我在恐怖和死亡中生活了那么久；我看到人们过着那种野蛮的、非人的生活；我对任何事都彻底绝望，对各种理论、诺言、协约、道德和原则不会再抱有一丝尊重。"
"I have hated too much the men who wallowed in them while I was wallowing in mud and blood.","当我在泥水和血水中打滚时，我恨透了那些沉湎于这些玩意的人。"
"Illusion is off.","幻想破灭了。"
"No religion and no philosophy will satisfy me—words, all words.","宗教和哲学都无法说服我——空话，全是空话。"
"I have still my senses—no thanks to them; am still capable—I find—of passion; can still grit my teeth and grin; have still some feeling of trench loyalty, but whether real or just a complex, I don’t yet know.","我仍有感觉——并不是由于上述这些玩意产生的感觉；我发现——我仍有热情，仍旧能够咬紧牙关咧着嘴笑，也还有一些战壕里的忠诚感，但这究竟是真实的反应还是某种情结，我就不得而知了。"
"I am dangerous, but not so dangerous as those who trade in words, principles, theories, and all manner of fanatical idiocy to be worked out in the blood and sweat of other men.","我是个危险人物，但同那些用别人的血汗来换取各种空话、原则、理论以及具有狂热愚蠢的行为的人相比，我远不及他们危险。"
"The war’s done one thing for me—converted life to comedy.","那场战争为我做了一件事——把人生变成了滑稽喜剧。"
"Laugh at it—there’s nothing else to do!”","对它笑吧——除此以外，别无他法！”"
"Leaving the concert hall on the Friday night, he had walked straight home to his rooms.","周五晚上离开音乐厅后，他径直走回自己的寓所。"
"And lying down full length on a monk’s seat of the fifteenth century, restored with down cushions and silk of the twentieth, he crossed his hands behind his head and delivered himself to these thoughts: ‘I am not going on like this.","他伸直了腿，躺在一张15世纪的僧侣坐榻上——这张坐榻是用20世纪的绒毛坐垫和丝绸修复而成的，双手交叉叠放在脑后，陷入了沉思：“我不能再这样下去了。"
"She has bewitched me.","我已经被她迷住了。"
"It doesn’t mean anything to her.","这对她来说算不上什么。"
"But it means hell to me.","但对我却意味着毁灭。"
"I’ll finish with it on Sunday—Persia’s a good place.","我会在周日解决这件事——波斯是个好地方。"
"Arabia’s a good place—plenty of blood and sand!","阿拉伯半岛是个好地方——鲜血和沙砾多的是！"
"She’s incapable of giving anything up.","她是不会放弃任何东西的。"
"How has she hooked herself into me!","她一直费尽心思地与我纠缠！"
"By trick of eyes, and hair, by her walk, by the sound of her voice—by trick of warmth, scent, colour.","她会用眼神、头发、走路的姿势、说话的声音，还有温情、气味、颜色等等小手段来吸引我。"
"Fling her cap over the windmill—not she!","可是，她会冒上身败名裂的危险吗？不，她不会。"
"What then?","那怎么办？"
"Am I to hang about her Chinese fireside and her little Chinese dog; and have this ache and this fever because I can’t be kissing her?","难道要我围着她的中式壁炉和中国小狗打转，还要忍受不能亲她的痛苦和狂热吗？"
"I’d rather be flying again in the middle of Boche whiz-bangs!","我宁愿再到德国人的枪林弹雨中去驰骋！"
"Sunday!","周日！"
"How women like to drag out agonies!","女人怎么都喜欢拖拖拉拉，让痛苦的时间更久啊！"
"It’ll be just this afternoon all over again.","到时候只会是今天下午的情形再次上演。"
"“How unkind of you to go, when your friendship is so precious to me!","‘你的友情对我而言非常珍贵，你怎么这么残忍地要走啊！"
"Stay, and be my tame cat, Wilfrid!”","留下来，做我听话的小猫吧，威尔弗里德！’"
"No, my dear, for once you’re up against it!","不，亲爱的，这一次你要有大麻烦了！"
"And—so am I, by the Lord!...’","同样——我也惹上麻烦了，上帝啊！……”"
"When in that gallery which extends asylum to British art, those two young people met so accidentally on Sunday morning in front of Eve smelling at the flowers of the Garden of Eden, there were present also six mechanics in various stages of decomposition, a custodian and a couple from the provinces, none of whom seemed capable of observing anything whatever.","周日上午，在那个成为英国艺术品收容所的美术馆里，这两个年轻人“很凑巧”地在一幅夏娃嗅着伊甸园花香的画前相遇了。当时附近还有六个不同年纪的工匠、一个看管员和一对外地来的夫妻，这些人看起来都不像会注意观察周围的事情。"
"And, indeed, that meeting was inexpressive.","而且那次会面是平静的。"
"Two young people, of the disillusioned class, exchanging condemnations of the past.","两个属于幻想破灭阶级的年轻人互相谴责对方此前的行为。"
"Desert with his off-hand speech, his smile, his well-tailored informality, suggested no aching heart.","德赛特以他那随意的谈吐、微笑和精心剪裁的休闲着装，让人觉得他并不心痛。"
"Of the two Fleur was the paler and more interesting.","相比之下，还是弗勒面色更苍白，也更引人关注。"
"Desert kept saying to himself: “No melodrama—that’s all it would be!”","德赛特不住地提醒自己：“不要煽情——只有这样才好！”"
"And Fleur was thinking: ‘If I can keep him ordinary like this, I shan’t lose him, because he’ll never go away without a proper outburst.’","而弗勒却在想：“要是我能让他保持这样平常的状态，我就不会失去他了。因为他不适当发泄一下是不会罢休的。”"
"It was not until they found themselves a second time before the Eve, that he said:","直到两个人再次在那幅夏娃的画前相遇，他才说："
"“I don’t know why you asked me to come, Fleur.","“我不明白你为什么要叫我来，弗勒。"
"It’s playing the goat for no earthly reason.","你这是在无理取闹。"
"I quite understand your feeling.","我很理解你的心情。"
"I’m a bit of ‘Ming’ that you don’t want to lose.","我只不过是你不愿失去的一件‘明朝’古玩。"
"But it’s not good enough, my dear; and that’s all about it.”","但是这件古玩又不够好，亲爱的。仅此而已。”"
"“How horrible of you, Wilfrid!”","“你太可怕了，威尔弗里德！”"
"“Well!","“好了！"
"Here we part!","就此分手吧！"
"Give us your flipper.”","伸出你的小手来。”"
"His eyes—rather beautiful—looked dark and tragic above the smile on his lips, and she said stammering:","他的眼睛——很美丽的眼睛——在他微笑的双唇上方显得深邃而悲哀。她结结巴巴地说："
"“Wilfrid—I—I don’t know.","“威尔弗里德——我——我不知道。"
"I want time.","我需要时间。"
"I can’t bear you to be unhappy.","我不希望你不快乐。"
"Don’t go away!","别离开我！"
"Perhaps I—I shall be unhappy, too; I—I don’t know.”","也许——我也会不快乐的。我——我不知道。”"
"Through Desert passed the bitter thought: ‘She CAN’T let go—she doesn’t know how.’","德赛特心头里掠过一丝苦涩：“她不会放手的——她不知道怎么放手。”"
"But he said quite softly: “Cheer up, my child; you’ll be over all that in a fortnight.","但是他的话却很温柔：“开心一点儿，我的宝贝。半个月之后你就会把这些都忘掉的。"
"I’ll send you something to make up.","我会送你点儿东西作为补偿的。"
"Why shouldn’t I make it China—one place is as good as another?","我为什么不到中国去呢——那里和其他地方有区别吗？"
"I’ll send you a bit of real ‘Ming,’ of a better period than this.”","我会送你一件真正的‘明朝’古玩，比我这件更古老。”"
"Fleur said passionately:","弗勒激动地说："
"“You’re insulting!","“你这是在侮辱人！"
"Don’t!”","不要这样！”"
"“I beg your pardon.","“对不起。"
"I don’t want to leave you angry.”","我不想让你生气。”"
"“What is it you want of me?”","“你想要我怎样？”"
"“Oh! no—come!","“哦！不——得了！"
"This is going over it twice.","这已经是第二遍了。"
"Besides, since Friday I’ve been thinking.","何况，我从周五开始就一直在思考。"
"I want nothing, Fleur, except a blessing and your hand.","我什么都不要，弗勒，我只想要你的祝福和握别。"
"Give it me!","把手递给我！"
"Come on!”","快点儿！”"
"Fleur put her hand behind her back.","弗勒把手放在自己身后。"
"It was too mortifying!","这太气人了！"
"He took her for a cold-blooded, collecting little cat—clutching and playing with mice that she didn’t want to eat!","他把她当作一只有收藏嗜好的冷血小猫——用爪子玩弄它不想吃的老鼠！"
"“You think I’m made of ice,” she said, and her teeth caught her upper lip: “Well, I’m not!”","“你以为我是冰做的吗，”她用牙咬着上唇说，“不，我不是！”"
"Desert looked at her; his eyes were very wretched.","德赛特看着她，眼神非常沮丧。"
"“I didn’t mean to play up your pride,” he said.","“我并不是有意嘲弄你的自尊心，”他说，"
"“Let’s drop it, Fleur.","“我们丢开自尊吧，弗勒。"
"It isn’t any good.”","它一点儿用处都没有。”"
"Fleur turned and fixed her eyes on the Eve—rumbustious-looking female, care-free, avid, taking her fill of flower perfume!","弗勒转过身去，凝视着那幅画中的夏娃——这个神情放荡的女人，她无所顾忌、贪婪，正满心享受着花香！"
"Why not be care-free, take anything that came along?","我为什么就不能像她这样无所顾忌、来者不拒呢？"
"Not so much love in the world that one could afford to pass, leaving it unsmelled, unplucked.","世上没有太多的爱情供人放弃，不闻不采。"
"Run away!","私奔吧！"
"Go to the East!","到东方去！"
"Of course, she couldn’t do anything extravagant like that!","当然，这些放肆的事情，她一件也不会做！"
"But, perhaps—What did it matter? one man or another, when neither did you really love!","但是，也许会——这有什么关系呢？这个男人或是那个男人，反正都不是你爱的那个人！"
"From under her drooped, white, dark-lashed eyelids she saw the expression on his face, and that he was standing stiller than the statues.","她白净的眼睑低垂着，透过浓密的睫毛，她看到了他脸上的表情以及那比雕像还要凝固的站姿。"
"And suddenly she said: “You will be a fool to go.","突然她说道：“你要是走了，你就是个傻瓜。"
"Wait!”","等着！”"
"And without another word or look, she walked away, leaving Desert breathless before the avid Eve.","然后，她没有再说一句话或是再看一眼他就走开了，撇下连气都透不过来的德赛特一个人站在那贪婪的夏娃面前。"

"Chapter VI","第六章"
"‘Old Forsyte’ and ‘Old Mont’","“老福赛特”和“老蒙特”"
"Moving away, in the confusion of her mood, Fleur almost trod on the toes of a too-familiar figure standing before an Alma Tadema with a sort of grey anxiety, as if lost in the mutability of market values.","弗勒心烦意乱地走着，险些踩到一个极熟悉的人的脚。这个人面色阴沉、神情焦急地站在一幅阿尔玛·塔德玛的作品前，仿佛迷失在那涨跌不定的市场价值里。"
"“Father!","“爸爸!"
"YOU up in town?","您到城里来了？"
"Come along to lunch, I have to get home quick.”","一起吃午饭吧，我得快点儿回家。”"
"Hooking his arm and keeping between him and Eve, she guided him away, thinking: ‘Did he see us?","她挽着父亲的手臂站在他和夏娃之间，一边引着他离开，一边想：“他看见我们了吗？"
"Could he have seen us?’","会不会已经看到了？”"
"“Have you got enough on?” muttered Soames.","“你穿得够多吗？”索姆斯低声埋怨着。"
"“Heaps!”","“多得很呢！”"
"“That’s what you women always say.","“你们女人总是这么说。"
"East wind, and your neck like that!","外面刮着东风，可你的脖子就那么露着！"
"Well, I don’t know.”","唉，我真弄不懂。”"
"“No, dear, but I do.”","“亲爱的爸爸，您不懂，但是我懂。”"
"The grey eyes appraised her from head to foot.","那双灰色的眼睛从头到脚地打量着她。"
"“What are you doing here?” he said.","“你在这儿做什么？”他问道。"
"And Flour thought: ‘Thank God he didn’t see.","弗勒心想：“感谢上帝，他没看见。"
"He’d never have asked if he had.’","要是看见了，他绝不会问的。”"
"And she answered:","于是她回答说："
"“I take an interest in art, darling, as well as you.”","“我对艺术感兴趣了，亲爱的，和您一样啊。”"
"“Well, I’m staying with your aunt in Green Street.","“嗯，我现在住在格林街你姑妈那里。"
"This east wind has touched my liver.","这阵东风让我的肝脏很不舒服。"
"How’s your—how’s Michael?”","你的——迈克尔最近怎么样？”"
"“Oh, he’s all right—a little cheap.","“哦，他还好，只是有点儿提不起精神。"
"We had a dinner last night.”","我们昨晚举办了一场宴会。”"
"Anniversary!","结婚纪念日！"
"The realism of a Forsyte stirred in him, and he looked under her eyes.","福赛特一家的现实主义精神涌上他的心头，于是他凝视着她的眼睛。"
"Thrusting his hand into his overcoat pocket, he said:","他把手插进外衣口袋里，说道："
"“I was bringing you this.”","“我带了这个来给你。”"
"Fleur saw a flat substance wrapped in pink tissue paper.","弗勒看到一个用粉红色的薄纸包裹着的扁平的东西。"
"“Darling, what is it?”","“亲爱的，这是什么？”"
"Soames put it back into his pocket.","索姆斯把东西放回自己的口袋。"
"“We’ll see later.","“我们待会儿再看。"
"Anybody to lunch?”","有人来吃午饭吗？”"
"“Only Bart.”","“就准爵爷一个人。”"
"“Old Mont!","“老蒙特！"
"Oh, Lord!”","哦，上帝！”"
"“Don’t you like Bart, dear?”","“您不喜欢准爵爷吗，亲爱的？”"
"“Like him?","“喜欢他？"
"He and I have nothing in common.”","我和他毫无共同语言。”"
"“I thought you fraternised rather over the state of things.”","“我还以为你们对事情的看法很一致呢。”"
"“He’s a reactionary,” said Soames.","“他是个反动分子。”索姆斯说道。"
"“And what are you, ducky?”","“那么您呢，亲爱的？”"
"“I?","“我？"
"What should I be?”","我该是什么样子的？”"
"With these words he affirmed that policy of non-commitment which, the older he grew, the more he perceived to be the only attitude for a sensible man.","他说着的这些话都遵从着“不承诺”的方针。他年纪越大，越觉得这一方针是明智者的唯一选择。"
"“How is Mother?”","“妈妈还好吗？”"
"“Looks well.","“看起来很好。"
"I see nothing of her—she’s got her own mother down—they go gadding about.”","我没看到她——她和她的母亲一起进城闲逛了。”"
"He never alluded to Madame Lamotte as Fleur’s grandmother—the less his daughter had to do with her French side, the better.","他从不提起弗勒的外祖母拉莫特夫人——自己的女儿越少和那些法国亲戚来往越好。"
"“Oh!” said Fleur.","“啊！”弗勒说道，"
"“There’s Ting and a cat!”","“是叮铃和一只猫！”"
"Ting-a-ling, out for a breath of air, and tethered by a lead in the hands of a maid, was snuffling horribly and trying to climb a railing whereon was perched a black cat, all hunch and eyes.","女仆正牵着小叮铃出来透风。此时它正呼哧呼哧地抽着鼻子，试图爬上栏杆。那上面有只黑猫，背部弓起、双目圆睁。"
"“Give him to me, Ellen.","“埃伦，把它交给我。"
"Come with Mother, darling!”","亲爱的，过来找妈妈！”"
"Ting-a-ling came, indeed, but only because he couldn’t go, bristling and snuffling and turning his head back.","小叮铃还真的来了，但这只是因为它走不了。它毛发竖立，抽搭着鼻子，头扭向后面。"
"“I like to see him natural,” said Fleur.","“我喜欢看它不做作的样子。”弗勒说。"
"“Waste of money, a dog like that,” Soames commented.","“浪费钱，养这么条狗，”索姆斯评论道，"
"“You should have had a bull-dog and let him sleep in the hall.","“你应该养只斗牛犬，让它睡在门厅里。"
"No end of burglaries.","夜盗多极了。"
"Your aunt had her knocker stolen.”","你姑妈让人把门环都偷走了。”"
"“I wouldn’t part with Ting for a hundred knockers.”","“就是被偷掉一百个门环，我也不会跟叮铃分离。”"
"“One of these days you’ll be having HIM stolen—fashionable breed.”","“总有一天会有人把它偷走的——这么个时髦的品种。”"
"Fleur opened her front door.","弗勒打开自家的前门。"
"“Oh!” she said, “Bart’s here, already!”","“啊！”她说，“准爵爷已经到了！”"
"A shiny hat was reposing on a marble coffer, present from Soames, intended to hold coats and discourage moth.","一顶锃亮的帽子挂在大理石镶板上，这块镶板是索姆斯送来的礼物，用来挂外套和防虫蛀。"
"Placing his hat alongside the other, Soames looked at them.","索姆斯把自己的帽子挂在那顶帽子旁边，然后望着它们。"
"They were too similar for words, tall, high, shiny, and with the same name inside.","这两顶帽子实在太像了，都是高高的、昂贵的、锃亮的，连里面的商标都是一样的。"
"He had resumed the ‘tall hat’ habit after the failure of the general and coal strikes in 1921, his instinct having told him that revolution would be at a discount for some considerable period.","自从1921年大罢工和煤矿罢工失败后，他又恢复了戴“高帽子”的习惯。他的直觉告诉他，在相当长的时间内，都不会有革命浪潮了。"
"“About this thing,” he said, taking out the pink parcel, “I don’t know what you’ll do with it, but here it is.”","“这件东西，”他一边说，一边掏出那个粉红色的包裹，“我不知道你会怎么处理它，不过你先拿着吧。”"
"It was a curiously carved and coloured bit of opal in a ring of tiny brilliants.","那是一颗彩色蛋白石，雕工奇特，上面镶了一圈细钻。"
"“Oh!”","“哦！”"
"Fleur cried: “What a delicious thing!”","弗勒叫道，“多美的东西啊！”"
"“Venus floating on the waves, or something,” murmured Soames.","“浮在水面上的维纳斯，或者诸如此类的名称，”索姆斯低声说道，"
"“Uncommon.","“此物非比寻常。"
"You want a strong light on it.”","你得在亮点儿的地方看它才行。”"
"“But it’s lovely.","“但是它好可爱。"
"I shall put it on at once.”","我现在就要戴上它。”"
"Venus!","维纳斯！"
"If Dad had known!","要是爸爸已经知道的话！"
"She put her arms round his neck to disguise her sense of a propos.","她伸开双臂搂着爸爸的脖子，以此来掩饰她对这件凑巧的事情的感想。"
"Soames received the rub of her cheek against his own well-shaved face with his usual stillness.","索姆斯任由女儿的脸颊在自己那刮得很干净的脸上蹭来蹭去，保持着一贯的镇静。"
"Why demonstrate when they were both aware that his affection was double hers?","既然父女俩都知道他对女儿的钟爱两倍于女儿对他的爱，又何必挑明了呢？"
"“Put it on then,” he said, “and let’s see.”","“那就戴上吧，”他说，“咱们一起看看。”"
"Fleur pinned it at her neck before an old lacquered mirror.","弗勒站在一面古老的亮漆镜子前，把这颗蛋白石别在自己的衣领上。"
"“It’s a jewel.","“这是件宝贝。"
"Thank you, darling!","谢谢亲爱的爸爸！"
"Yes, your tie is straight.","看，您的领带笔挺笔挺的。"
"I like that white piping.","我喜欢那上面白色的滚边。"
"You ought always to wear it with black.","您只能用黑色的衣服来配它。"
"Now, come along!”","现在，跟我来吧！”"
"And she drew him into her Chinese room.","说着就把他拉进她的中国式的房间里去了。"
"It was empty.","里面没有人。"
"“Bart must be up with Michael, talking about his new book.”","“准爵爷一定是和迈克尔在楼上，谈论他的新书。”"
"“Writing at his age?” said Soames.","“他那把年纪了，还写书？”索姆斯问。"
"“Well, ducky, he’s a year younger than you.”","“可是，亲爱的爸爸，他比您还小一岁呢。”"
"“I don’t write.","“我又不写书。"
"Not such a fool.","我才不像他那么傻呢。"
"Got any more newfangled friends?”","你有没有新交有趣的朋友呢？”"
"“Just one—Gurdon Minho, the novelist.”","“就一个——格登·明霍，是个小说家。”"
"“Another of the new school?”","“又是一个新派作家？”"
"“Oh, no, dear!","“哦，不是，亲爱的爸爸！"
"Surely you’ve heard of Gurdon Minho; he’s older than the hills.”","您一定听过格登·明霍的，他可是古董级别的。”"
"“They’re all alike to me,” muttered Soames.","“在我看来，他们都差不多。”索姆斯嘟哝着，"
"“Is he well thought of?”","“他的名气大吗？”"
"“I should think his income is larger than yours.","“我想他比您挣得多。"
"He’s almost a classic—only waiting to die.”","他基本上是经典了——只是等待死亡罢了。”"
"“I’ll get one of his books and read it.","“我会找本他的书看看的。"
"What name did you say?”","你说哪一本好呢？”"
"“Get ‘Big and Little Fishes,’ by Gurdon Minho.","“就格登·明霍的那本《大鱼和小鱼》吧。"
"You can remember that, can’t you?","您总能记住这个书名吧，是不是？"
"Oh! here they are!","哟，他们来了！"
"Michael, look at what Father’s given me.”","迈克尔，看看爸爸给了我什么啦。”"
"Taking his hand, she put it up to the opal at her neck.","她拉着迈克尔的手，放在那颗别在衣领上的蛋白石上。"
"‘Let them both see,’ she thought, ‘what good terms we’re on.’","“让他们都看看，”她心想，“我们的夫妻关系有多好。”"
"Though her father had not seen her with Wilfrid in the gallery, her conscience still said: “Strengthen your respectability, you don’t quite know how much support you’ll need for it in future.”","尽管她的父亲没有在美术馆看到她和威尔弗里德在一起，她潜意识仍在说：“增强你的声誉，将来为了这声誉，你还不知道你会需要多大的支持呢。”"
"And out of the corner of her eye she watched those two.","她用眼角的余光观察着那两位。"
"The meetings between ‘Old Mont’ and ‘Old Forsyte’—as she knew Bart called her father when speaking of him to Michael—always made her want to laugh, but she never quite knew why.","“老蒙特”和“老福赛特”——她知道准爵爷和迈克尔谈起她父亲时是这样称呼他的——他俩一见面，总是会让她忍俊不禁，可是她从不知道为什么要笑。"
"Bart knew everything, but his knowledge was beautifully bound, strictly edited by a mind tethered to the ‘eighteenth century.’","准爵爷什么都知道，但是他的知识就像一本精装的书，由那颗遗留在“18世纪”的头脑严格编辑过。"
"Her father only knew what was of advantage to him, but the knowledge was unbound, and subject to no editorship.","而她的父亲只知道那些有利于他的事情，他的知识是本没有装订的书，而且不受编辑的限制。"
"If he WAS late Victorian, he was not above profiting if necessary by even later periods.","如果父亲生在维多利亚晚期，甚至是在最后时期，那么只要有利可图，他都不会放弃谋利。"
"‘Old Mont’ had faith in tradition; ‘Old Forsyte’ none.","“老蒙特”相信传统；“老福赛特”什么都不信。"
"Fleur’s acuteness had long perceived a difference which favoured her father.","以弗勒的精明，早就觉察到两个老人家的不同，而且这种差异对她的父亲更有利。"
"Yet ‘Old Mont’s’ talk was so much more up-to-date, rapid, glancing, garrulous, redolent of precise information; and ‘Old Forsyte’s’ was constricted, matter-of-fact.","然而，“老蒙特”的谈吐却是如此时尚、迅速、随便、饶舌，让人联想到准确的报道；而“老福赛特”说起话来却是拘谨的、实事求是的。"
"Really impossible to tell which of the two was the better museum specimen; and both so well-preserved!","要分辨出两个人中哪一个会是较好博物馆的收藏品，确实是不可能。更何况，两个人都保养得那么好！"
"They did not precisely shake hands; but Soames mentioned the weather.","他们的确没有握手，但是索姆斯谈了天气。"
"And almost at once they all four sought that Sunday food which by a sustained effort of will Fleur had at last deprived of reference to the British character.","然后他们四个人几乎都想立刻开始周日的午餐。在弗勒坚持不懈的努力下，这些食物终于摆脱了英国风味。"
"They partook, in fact, of lobster cocktails, and a mere risotto of chickens’ livers, an omelette au rhum, and dessert trying to look as Spanish as it could.","实际上，他们吃的是龙虾冷盘、意式鸡肝煨饭、朗姆炒蛋，还有一份做得尽可能看起来像西班牙式的甜点。"
"“I’ve been in the Tate,” Fleur said; “I do think it’s touching.”","“我刚才去泰特美术馆了，”弗勒说，“我真的觉得那儿让人有所感触。”"
"“Touching?” queried Soames with a sniff.","“感触？”索姆斯嗤了一声表示质疑。"
"“Fleur means, sir, that to see so much old English art together is like looking at a baby show.”","“先生，弗勒的意思是，一下子看到那么多古老的英国艺术作品，就好像在看宝宝秀一样。”"
"“I don’t follow,” said Soames stiffly.","“我不同意，”索姆斯生硬地说，"
"“There’s some very good work there.”","“那里有一些非常好的作品呢。”"
"“But not grown-up, sir.”","“但还不够成熟，先生。”"
"“Ah!","“啊！"
"You young people mistake all this crazy cleverness for maturity.”","你们年轻人把那些疯狂的小聪明全当成是成熟了。”"
"“That’s not what Michael means, Father.","“迈克尔不是那个意思，爸爸。"
"It’s quite true that English painting has no wisdom teeth.","英国的绘画作品的确就像是牙还没长齐的小孩。"
"You can see the difference in a moment, between it and any Continental painting.”","你一眼就能看出英国绘画和欧洲绘画的差异。”"
"“And thank God for it!” broke in Sir Lawrence.","“这正是我们要感谢上帝的地方。”劳伦斯爵士插嘴说，"
"“The beauty of this country’s art is its innocence.","“这个国家的艺术之美在于它的纯朴天真。"
"We’re the oldest country in the world politically, and the youngest aesthetically.","从政治上来说，我们是世界上最古老的国家，而从艺术上来说，是最年轻的国家。"
"What do you say, Forsyte?”","福赛特，你觉得呢？”"
"“Turner is old and wise enough for me,” said Soames curtly.","“对我来说，特纳足够古老、足够智慧的了。”索姆斯简短地说，"
"“Are you coming to the P.P.R.S. Board on Tuesday?”","“周二你去参加天佑再保险公司的董事会吗？”"
"“Tuesday?","“周二吗？"
"We were going to shoot the spinneys, weren’t we, Michael?”","我们本打算去丛林打猎的，对吧，迈克尔？”"
"Soames grunted.","索姆斯哼了一声。"
"“I should let them wait,” he said.","“我要让他们等着，”他说，"
"“We settle the report.”","“我们要完成那个报告。”"
"It was through ‘Old Mont’s’ influence that he had received a seat on the Board of that flourishing concern, the Providential Premium Reassurance Society, and, truth to tell, he was not sitting very easily in it.","正是在“老蒙特”的关照下，他才获得了那个生意兴隆的公司——天佑再保险公司——董事会的一个席位。说实话，这个位子他坐得并不轻松。"
"Though the law of averages was, perhaps, the most reliable thing in the world, there were circumstances which had begun to cause him disquietude.","尽管平均定律也许是世界上最可靠的东西，但是已经有些情况引起他的不安了。"
"He looked round his nose.","他定睛看看身边这家伙。"
"Light weight, this narrow-headed, twisting-eyebrowed baronet of a chap—like his son before him!","准男爵身子薄、脑瓜尖，眉毛拧成了一团——和坐在他面前的儿子一个模样！"
"And he added suddenly: “I’m not easy.","然后他突然补充道：“我并不轻松。"
"If I’d realised how that chap Elderson ruled the roost, I doubt if I should have come on to that Board.”","要是我早知道埃尔德森那家伙大权独揽，我怀疑我还会不会进入董事会。”"
"One side of ‘Old Mont’s’ face seemed to try to leave the other.","“老蒙特”脸上顿时挂不住了。"
"“Elderson!” he said.","“埃尔德森！”他说，"
"“His grandfather was my grandfather’s parliamentary agent at the time of the Reform Bill; he put him through the most corrupt election ever fought—bought every vote—used to kiss all the farmer’s wives.","“改革法案时期，他的祖父是我祖父所在党的法律顾问，帮助我祖父在有史以来最腐败的选举中获胜——每一张选票都是买来的——常常讨好所有农民的妻子。"
"Great days, Forsyte, great days!”","伟大的时代，福赛特，伟大的时代！”"
"“And over,” said Soames.","“但已经过去了，”索姆斯说，"
"“I don’t believe in trusting a man’s judgment as far as we trust Elderson’s; I don’t like this foreign insurance.”","“我觉得我们不应该这么相信埃尔德森的判断力，我不喜欢这种国外保险。”"
"“My dear Forsyte—first-rate head, Elderson; I’ve known him all my life, we were at Winchester together.”","“亲爱的福赛特——埃尔德森的头脑是一流的，我从小就认识他，我们一起在温切斯特读过书。”"
"Soames uttered a deep sound.","索姆斯发出一声深沉的声音。"
"In that answer of ‘Old Mont’s’ lay much of the reason for his disquietude.","“老蒙特”的话里也有很多让他不安的理由。"
"On the Board they had all, as it were, been at Winchester together!","董事会的所有人，看起来都像在温切斯特一起读过书似的。"
"It was the very deuce!","真是见鬼了！"
"They were all so honourable that they dared not scrutinise each other, or even their own collective policy.","大家都这么体面，以至于不敢互相审查，也不敢审查大家共同的保险单。"
"Worse than their dread of mistake or fraud was their dread of seeming to distrust each other.","他们害怕表现出对彼此的不信任，甚于害怕错误或是欺诈。"
"And this was natural, for to distrust each other was an immediate evil.","这是很正常的，因为彼此不信任是一种直接的罪孽。"
"And, as Soames knew, immediate evils are those which one avoids.","而就索姆斯所知，直接的罪孽就是人们要回避的。"
"Indeed, only that tendency, inherited from his father, James, to lie awake between the hours of two and four, when the chrysalis of faint misgiving becomes so readily the butterfly of panic, had developed his uneasiness.","其实，单是从他父亲那里遗传来的秉性，已经让索姆斯的不安日益加深了。他会在夜里2点到4点间惊醒，然后他蠢蠢欲动的小担忧就会变成大恐慌，像蝴蝶一样破茧而出。"
"The P.P.R.S. was so imposing a concern, and he had been connected with it so short a time, that it seemed presumptuous to smell a rat; especially as he would have to leave the Board and the thousand a year he earned on it if he raised smell of rat without rat or reason.","天佑再保险公司是这么有影响力的一家大公司，而他加入公司的时间尚短，如果就此怀疑它有问题未免显得冒昧，尤其是如果他光说有问题却找不出问题或是理由的话，他就可能得离开董事会和那一千英镑的年薪。"
"But what if there were a rat?","但是要是真的有问题怎么办？"
"That was the trouble!","难就难在这里了！"
"And here sat ‘Old Mont’ talking of his spinneys and his grandfather.","而“老蒙特”却坐在这里谈着他的丛林打猎和他的祖父。"
"The fellow’s head was too small!","这家伙的脑瓜太小了！"
"And visited by the cheerless thought: ‘There’s nobody here, not even my own daughter, capable of taking a thing seriously,’ he kept silence.","然后他脑子里又涌现出一个让人压抑的念头：“在座的所有人，甚至包括我女儿在内，没有一个人会严肃对待事情。”他不吭声了。"
"A sound at his elbow roused him.","这时，肘边的声音惊动了他。"
"That marmoset of a dog, on a chair between him and his daughter, was sitting up!","他和他女儿之间的椅子上的那只像“狨”一样的小狗居然坐起来了！"
"Did it expect him to give it something?","这是盼着他能给点儿吃的吗？"
"Its eyes would drop out one of these days.","它那双眼珠早晚有一天会掉出来的。"
"And he said: “Well, what do YOU want?”","于是他问道：“喂，你想要什么？”"
"The way the little beast stared with those boot-buttons!","看看这小畜生的那副样子，瞪着它那对靴扣般大小的眼睛！"
"“Here,” he said, offering it a salted almond.","“来，”他一边说，一边拿了一颗盐渍杏仁给它，"
"“You don’t eat these.”","“你不吃这些东西的。”"
"Ting-a-ling did.","小叮铃吃了。"
"“He has a passion for them, Dad.","“爸爸，它挺爱吃那个的。"
"Haven’t you, darling?”","对不对啊，小宝贝？”"
"Ting-a-ling turned his eyes up at Soames, through whom a queer sensation passed.","小叮铃抬眼望着索姆斯，从那双眼睛里，索姆斯体会到一种怪异的感觉。"
"‘Believe the little brute likes me,’ he thought, ‘he’s always looking at me.’","“我认为这小畜生喜欢我，”他想，“它总是看着我。”"
"He touched the dog’s nose with the tip of his finger.","他用指尖碰了碰狗鼻子。"
"Ting-a-ling gave it a slight lick with his curly blackish tongue.","小叮铃用它那黑乎乎的卷舌头舔了他一下。"
"“Poor fellow!” muttered Soames involuntarily, and turned to ‘Old Mont.’","“可怜的小东西！”索姆斯不禁咕哝了一声，然后转向“老蒙特”。"
"“Don’t mention what I said.”","“别再提我刚才的话了。”"
"“My dear Forsyte, what was that?”","“刚才的什么话，亲爱的福赛特？”"
"Good Heavens!","天啊！"
"And he was on a Board with a man like this!","他居然和这样的人同在一个董事会里！"
"What had made him come on, when he didn’t want the money, or any more worries—goodness knew.","这人为何加入董事会——他又不在乎那点儿钱，也不想操那份心——天晓得。"
"As soon as he had become a director, Winifred and others of his family had begun to acquire shares to neutralise their income tax—seven per cent, preference—nine per cent, ordinary—instead of the steady five they ought to be content with.","自从他当上了董事，威妮弗雷德和家里的其他人就开始买股票来抵消他们的所得税——优先股百分之七，普通股百分之九——以此取代原先他们本该满足的稳定的百分之五。"
"There it was, he couldn’t move without people following him.","你看，他一动就会有人跟着动。"
"He had always been so safe, so perfect a guide in the money maze!","过去，在金钱的迷宫里，他一直是位非常稳妥和精确的向导！"
"To be worried at his time of life!","他都这把年纪了还在操心！"
"His eyes sought comfort from the opal at his daughter’s neck—pretty thing, pretty neck!","他的目光落在女儿衣领上的那颗蛋白石上，借此寻求安慰——漂亮的玩意！漂亮的脖子！"
"Well!","啊！"
"She seemed happy enough—had forgotten her infatuation of two years ago!","她显得很开心——已经忘记两年前的迷恋了！"
"That was something to be thankful for.","这是件令人欣慰的事情。"
"What she wanted now was a child to steady her in all this modern scrimmage of twopenny-ha’penny writers and painters and musicians.","她现在需要的是一个孩子，这样她就能在那些时尚的骚闹中安定下来，不再纠缠于那些微不足道的作家、画家和音乐家了。"
"A loose lot, but she had a good little head on her.","她虽然是一个放浪不羁的人，但是小脑瓜还是挺管用的。"
"If she had a child, he would put another twenty thousand into her settlement.","要是她有孩子了，他会在赠与她的财产上再加上两万英镑。"
"That was one thing about her mother—steady in money matters, good French method.","这是她母亲的一个优点——把钱管得很稳，优秀的法国方式。"
"And Fleur—so far as he knew—cut her coat according to her cloth.","至于弗勒——据他所知——是量入为出的。"
"What was that?","他们在说什么？"
"The word ‘Goya’ had caught his ear.","耳朵里钻进一个词——“戈雅”。"
"New life of him coming out?","他的新传记要出版了吗？"
"H’m!","哈！"
"That confirmed his slowly growing conviction that Goya had reached top point again.","那就更坚定了他那慢慢增强的信念——戈雅已经再次攀上顶峰。"
"“Think I shall part with that,” he said, pointing to the picture.","“我正想着把那东西卖掉，”他一边说，一边指着那幅画，"
"“There’s an Argentine over here.”","“来了个阿根廷人。”"
"“Sell your Goya, sir?”","“您要把您那幅戈雅卖掉吗，先生？”"
"It was Michael speaking.","迈克尔说道，"
"“Think of the envy with which you’re now regarded!”","“想想人们对您的尊敬和羡慕吧！”"
"“One can’t have everything,” said Soames.","“人总不能拥有一切吧。”索姆斯说。"
"“That reproduction we’ve got for ‘The New Life’ has turned out first-rate.","“我们给《新生活》做的那张复制品已经是一流的了。"
"‘Property of Soames Forsyte, Esquire.’","‘索姆斯·福赛特先生收藏’。"
"Let’s get the book out first, sir, anyway.”","先生，无论如何，等书出来再说吧。”"
"“Shadow or substance, eh, Forsyte?”","“虚名还是实名，嗯，福赛特？”"
"Narrow-headed baronet chap—was he mocking?","这头脑狭窄的准男爵，他是在嘲笑我吗？"
"“I’VE no family place,” he said.","“我可没有世袭的爵位。”他说。"
"“No, but we have, sir,” murmured Michael; “you could leave it to Fleur, you know.”","“可我们有啊，先生，”迈克尔小声嘀咕，“您可以把它留给弗勒，这您知道的。”"
"“Well,” said Soames, “we shall see if that’s worth while.”","“嗯，”索姆斯说，“我们还要看看这么做值不值。”"
"And he looked at his daughter.","他一边说着，一边看着他女儿。"
"Fleur seldom blushed, but she picked up Ting-a-ling and rose from the Spanish table.","弗勒难得地脸红了，抱起小叮铃，从那张西班牙式的餐桌旁站了起来。"
"Michael followed suit.","迈克尔也跟着站起来了。"
"“Coffee in the other room,” he said.","“咖啡在另一间屋里。”他说。"
"‘Old Forsyte’ and ‘Old Mont’ stood up, wiping their moustaches.","“老福赛特”和“老蒙特”站了起来，捋着他们的胡子。"

"Chapter VII","第七章"
"‘Old Mont’ and ‘Old Forsyte’","“老蒙特”和“老福赛特”"
"The offices of the P.P.R.S. were not far from the College of Arms.","天佑再保险公司的办事处离纹章院不远。","编者注：英国纹章院（College of Arms）于1484年建立。在12世纪就已有纹章官（Herald）的出现。开始时，纹章官类似依附于贵族之奴仆，地位相当于魔术师及吟游诗人。后来被当成比武会上的司仪，宣布比武项目及骑士名单。为识别骑士，必须对盾牌上之盾纹有所了解及认识，因而产生了纹章艺术的知识和技能。13世纪时，纹章官主要的工作是处理贵族事务。到了14世纪，纹章官之权力有所扩大。15世纪初，最高纹章官（Kings of Arms）已能授命给低级贵族颁赠封号。到了国王停止直接授与纹章时，此一权力便由纹章院代行。"


"Soames, who knew that ‘three dexter buckles on a sable ground gules’ and a ‘pheasant proper’ had been obtained there at some expense by his Uncle Swithin in the ‘sixties of the last century, had always pooh-poohed the building, until, about a year ago, he had been struck by the name Golding in a book which he had absently taken up at the Connoisseurs’ Club.","索姆斯记得在上世纪60年代，他的叔叔斯威森在那里花了一大笔钱淘到了一个“带有三个盾形右侧扣的黑底红色”纹章和一个“纯色雉鸡”纹章。因此，他总是对这幢建筑物不屑一顾。一直到大约一年前，在鉴赏家俱乐部里，他无意间从一本书里发现了戈尔丁的名字，不禁大吃一惊。"
"The affair purported to prove that William Shakespeare was really Edward de Vere, Earl of Oxford.","他找这本书意在证实威廉·莎士比亚的确就是爱德华·德·威尔，牛津伯爵。"
"The mother of the earl was a Golding—so was the mother of Soames!","伯爵的母亲来自戈尔丁家族——与索姆斯的母亲同宗！"
"The coincidence struck him; and he went on reading.","这个巧合引起了他的兴趣，他继续阅读下去。"
"The tome left him with judgment suspended over the main issue, but a distinct curiosity as to whether he was not of the same blood as Shakespeare.","尽管这本书使他对主要问题的判断仍然犹豫不定，但是却引发了他对自己是否和莎士比亚同属一个血统的明显好奇。"
"Even if the earl were not the bard, he felt that the connection could only be creditable, though, so far as he could make out, Oxford was a shady fellow.","即使此伯爵并非彼诗人，但他还是觉得这种联系令人信服，尽管据他现在的了解，牛津伯爵是一位疑点重重的人物。"
"Recently appointed on the Board of the P.P.R.S., so that he passed the college every other Tuesday, he had thought: ‘Shan’t go spending a lot of money on it, but might look in one day.’","最近，由于被任命为天佑再保险公司的董事，他隔周的星期二都要经过纹章院。他心想：“没必要在这方面花费太多，但哪天可以进去瞧瞧。”"
"Having looked in, it was astonishing how taken he had been by the whole thing.","可是当他进去之后，他对一切事物的迷恋程度令人震惊。"
"Tracing his mother had been quite like a criminal investigation, nearly as ramified and fully as expensive.","追溯他母亲的家世就像进行刑事侦查——错综复杂、全面彻底、耗资甚大。"
"Having begun, the tenacity of a Forsyte could hardly bear to leave him short of the mother of Shakespeare de Vere, even though she would be collateral; unfortunately, he could not get past a certain William Gouldyng, Ingerer—whatever that might be, and he was almost afraid to enquire—of the time of Oliver Cromwell.","从一开始，福赛特家族倔强的脾性就使他不能放弃调查莎士比亚·德·威尔的母亲，即便她也许是旁系血统；但不幸的是，他追查到奥利弗·克伦威尔时代的一个人，那人名叫威廉·古尔丁·英格勒——管他到底可能叫什么，他几乎不敢去追究他到底姓甚名谁——就再也进行不下去了。"
"There were still four generations to be unravelled, and he was losing money and the hope of getting anything for it.","仍有四代人需要调查清楚，但是他已经花费不少了，而且也不再奢望能够从中获得什么重要东西了。"
"This it was which caused him to gaze askance at the retired building while passing it on his way to the Board on the Tuesday after the lunch at Fleur’s.","周二在弗勒家吃过午饭后，他在去董事会的路上经过这幢僻静的建筑时，只是斜眼瞅了瞅，原因就在于此了。"
"Two more wakeful early mornings had screwed him to the pitch of bringing his doubts to a head and knowing where he stood in the matter of the P.P.R.S.; and this sudden reminder that he was spending money here, there and everywhere, when there was a possibility, however remote, of financial liability somewhere else, sharpened the edge of a nerve already stropped by misgivings.","连续两个无眠的清晨迫使他要尽早把这些谜团解开，同时也必须要搞清楚现在自己在天佑再保险公司所处的地位。他突然想到，自己四处花钱，有可能已经在某个地方背负债务了，尽管这个可能性微乎其微，但这种压力使他那本来因为担惊受怕而饱受折磨的神经变得更加脆弱敏感。"
"Neglecting the lift and walking slowly up the two flights of stairs, he ‘went over’ his fellow-directors for the fifteenth time.","他不坐电梯，慢慢爬了两层楼梯，此时在他脑海里已经对那些董事会的同事们做了第十五次分析。"
"Old Lord Fontenoy was there for his name, of course; seldom attended, and was what they called ‘a dud’—h’m!—nowadays; the chairman, Sir Luke Sharman, seemed always to be occupied in not being taken for a Jew.","当然，老勋爵福坦诺能进入董事会是因为他的名声，他难得出席会议，而且最近被称作“废物”。董事长卢克·沙曼爵士似乎整天都在想着不要被人误认为是犹太人。"
"His nose was straight, but his eyelids gave cause for doubt.","他的鼻梁直挺，可眼皮不免引人怀疑。"
"His surname was impeccable, but his Christian dubious; his voice was reassuringly roughened, but his clothes had a suspicious tendency towards gloss.","他的姓氏没有问题，但是他的教名却让人怀疑；他的嗓音粗糙，让人放心，但他的衣着却有可疑的虚饰倾向。"
"Altogether a man who, though shrewd, could not be trusted—Soames felt—to be giving his whole mind to other business.","整体来看，索姆斯认为这个人虽然精明，但绝不能指望他全心全意专注于其他事务。"
"As for ‘Old Mont’—what was the good of a ninth baronet on a Board?","至于“老蒙特”——董事会里安排一个第九代准男爵有什么好处呢？"
"Guy Meyricke, King’s Counsel, last of the three who had been ‘together,’ was a good man in court, no doubt, but with no time for business and no real sense of it!","英国王室法律顾问盖伊·迈里克，是曾经“一起读过书”的三人中的最后一名。毫无疑问，他在法庭上表现优秀，但对于做生意可以说是既没时间又没常识！"
"Remained that converted Quaker, old Cuthbert Mothergill—whose family name had been a by-word for successful integrity throughout the last century, so that people still put Mothergills on to boards almost mechanically—rather deaf, nice clean old chap, and quite bland, but nothing more.","剩下的是那个改变了信仰的教友派信徒，老卡思伯特·莫德吉尔——他家族的名字在上世纪一直是廉洁正直的代名词，所以如今人们依旧机械地把莫德吉尔家的人安排在董事会中——一个耳背、谨慎、干净的老人，为人温和，别无其他。"
"A perfectly honest lot, no doubt, but perfunctory.","毫无疑问，这群人为人诚实，但却敷衍了事。"
"None of them really giving their minds to the thing!","他们当中没有一个人真正把心思放在事业上！"
"In Elderson’s pocket, too, except perhaps Sharman, and he on the wobble.","这些人都在埃尔德森的控制下，或许沙曼除外，但是他也是摇摆不定。"
"And Elderson himself—clever chap, bit of an artist, perhaps; managing director from the start, with everything at his finger-tips!","埃尔德森本人——是个聪明的家伙，也许还有点儿艺术家的风度，从一开始就担任总经理，业务上样样精通！"
"Yes!","对！"
"That was the mischief!","事情坏就坏在这里！"
"Prestige of superior knowledge, and years of success—they all kowtowed to him, and no wonder!","渊博的知识和多年的成功，使他具有一定的威望——他们都对他唯命是从，这不足为奇！"
"Trouble with a man like that was that if he once admitted to having made a mistake he destroyed the legend of his infallibility.","但是像他那样的人有这么一种麻烦，一旦他承认自己犯过错误，那自然就毁掉了他一贯正确的传奇。"
"Soames had enough infallibility of his own to realise how powerful was its impetus towards admitting nothing.","索姆斯自己也算是个一贯正确的人，所以他深知这种不肯承认错误的抑制力是多么强大。"
"Ten months ago, when he had come on to the Board, everything had seemed in full sail; exchanges had reached bottom, so they all thought—the ‘reassurance of foreign contracts’ policy, which Elderson had initiated about a year before, had seemed, with rising exchanges, perhaps the brightest feather in the cap of possibility.","10个月前，他来参加董事会时，似乎一切都顺风顺水，汇率跌到了谷底，大家都认为——埃尔德森一年前倡导的“国外合同再保险”政策会随着汇率上涨而变成最值得炫耀的业绩。"
"And now, a twelvemonth later, Soames suspected darkly that they did not know where they were—and the general meeting only six weeks off!","而如今，12个月后，索姆斯暗暗怀疑他们是否清楚自己所背负的风险——而且距离召开股东大会只剩下六周的时间了！"
"Probably not even Elderson knew; or, if he did, he was keeping knowledge which ought to belong to the whole directorate severely to himself.","或许，就连埃尔德森本人都不了解事态；又或者，假如他了解，那么他就是把本应对全体董事会成员宣布的事封锁起来，让它成为秘密。"
"He entered the board room without a smile.","他面无表情地走进董事会。"
"All there—even Lord Fontenoy and ‘Old Mont’—given up his spinneys, had he!","所有的人都在——甚至福坦诺勋爵和“老蒙特”也在——“老蒙特”居然放弃了打猎！"
"Soames took his seat at the end on the fireside.","索姆斯走到火炉边的位子上坐下。"
"Staring at Elderson, he saw, with sudden clearness, the strength of the fellow’s position; and, with equal clearness, the weakness of the P.P.R.S. With this rising and falling currency, they could never know exactly their liability—they were just gambling.","他凝视着埃尔德森，忽然清楚地意识到这个人的地位是多么有利。同时，他也清楚地意识到了天佑再保险公司是多么不堪一击。货币忽涨忽跌，但他们从来没意识到他们肩负的债务——他们只是一味地投机。"
"Listening to the minutes and other routine business, with his chin clasped in his hand, he let his eyes move from face to face—old Mothergill, Elderson, Mont opposite; Sharman at the head; Fontenoy, Meyricke, back to himself—decisive board of the year.","他一手托着下巴，听着会议内容和其他例行汇报，眼睛扫视着在场的每个人——老莫德吉尔、埃尔德森、坐在对面的蒙特、坐在上座的沙曼、福坦诺、迈里克，最后回到自己——这可是今年的一次决定性会议。"
"He could not, must not, be placed in any dubious position!","他不能，也绝不可以置身于一个模棱两可的立场了！"
"At his first general meeting on this concern, he must not face the shareholders without knowing exactly where he stood.","他第一次参加这样的股东大会，绝不能在面对股东时没有自己鲜明的立场。"
"He looked again at Elderson—sweetish face, bald head rather like Julius Caesar’s, nothing to suggest irregularity or excessive optimism—in fact, somewhat resembling that of old Uncle Nicholas Forsyte, whose affairs had been such an example to the last generation but one.","他又看了埃尔德森一眼——和善的面庞，光秃的头倒是和尤利乌斯·恺撒有几分相像，表情正常，也没有过分乐观的迹象——实际上，他很像老尼古拉斯·福赛特叔叔，对于上上一代人来说，他的事迹是很好的榜样。"
"The managing director having completed his exposition, Soames directed his gaze at the pink face of dosey old Mothergill, and said:","总经理刚刚汇报完，索姆斯就将目光投在昏昏欲睡的老莫德吉尔那张红润的脸上，他说："
"“I’m not satisfied that these accounts disclose our true position.","“我认为这些账目没有如实反映我们的实际情况。"
"I want the Board adjourned to this day week, Mr. Chairman, and during the week I want every member of the Board furnished with exact details of the foreign contract commitments which do NOT mature during the present financial year.","董事长，我要求董事会休会至下周这个时间再继续召开。这一周内，我要求根据本财政年度还没到期的国外合同协议，做出正确详细的报告，并交给董事会的每一位成员。"
"I notice that those are lumped under a general estimate of liability.","我还留意到那些还没到期的钱款都已合并到负债总款之中了。"
"I am not satisfied with that.","我不赞同这样做。"
"They ought to be separately treated.”","应该把那些没到期的款项分出来。”"
"Shifting his gaze past Elderson to the face of ‘Old Mont,’ he went on: “Unless there’s a material change for the better on the Continent, which I don’t anticipate (quite the contrary), I fully expect those commitments will put us in Queer Street next year.”","他的目光掠过埃尔德森转到“老蒙特”的脸上。他继续说：“除非欧洲大陆情况确实好转，而我认为不会有好转（恰恰相反），我敢肯定，那些协议明年就会使我们陷入经济困境。”"
"The scraping of feet, shifting of legs, clearing of throats which accompany a slight sense of outrage greeted the words ‘Queer Street’; and a sort of satisfaction swelled in Soames; he had rattled their complacency, made them feel a touch of the misgiving from which he himself was suffering.","“陷入经济困境”的说法引发了大家轻微的怒火，席间传来了脚搓地声、翘着的两腿移动的声响，还有几声清喉声，这使得索姆斯心上涌起一种满足感。他扰乱了他们安于现状的打算，使他们也感受到一点点正在煎熬他的忧虑担心。"
"“We have always treated our commitments under one general estimate, Mr. Forsyte.”","“我们一向都把所有钱款归在一起计算的，福赛特先生。”"
"Plausible chap!","花言巧语的家伙！"
"“And to my mind wrongly.","“但我认为这是错误的。"
"This foreign contract business is a new policy.","这种国外合同业务是一种新兴业务。"
"For all I can tell, instead of paying a dividend, we ought to be setting this year’s profits against a certain loss next year.”","依我看，现在我们不应该发股息，反而要把今年的利润预备着抵偿明年的某笔亏损。”"
"Again that scrape and rustle.","又是一阵刚才那样的骚动声。"
"“My dear sir, absurd!”","“我亲爱的先生，这简直是荒谬！”"
"The bulldog in Soames snuffled.","索姆斯犹如斗牛犬的鼻子发出呼哧呼哧的声音。"
"“So you say!” he said.","“随你去说！”他说，"
"“Am I to have those details?”","“那我能看到那些详细账目吗？”"
"“The Board can have what details it likes, of course.","“当然了，董事会要看什么账目都可以。"
"But permit me to remark on the general question that it CAN only be a matter of estimate.","但允许我就基本问题说明一下，这只是一种估算。"
"A conservative basis has always been adopted.”","估算时，我们向来都是采取保守的态度。”"
"“That is a matter of opinion,” said Soames; “and in my view it should be the Board’s opinion after very careful discussion of the actual figures.”","“这是见仁见智的问题，”索姆斯说，“并且依我看，该用什么态度，这应该由董事会在认真讨论过实际数字后才决定吧。”"
"‘Old Mont’ was speaking.","“老蒙特”开口了。"
"“My dear Forsyte, to go into every contract would take us a week, and then get us no further; we can but average it out.”","“我亲爱的福赛特，如果我们仔细研究每一份合同，那就得花费一周的时间，也许还不会有任何结果，我们也只是大概计算一个均值。”"
"“What we have not got in these accounts,” said Soames, “is the relative proportion of foreign risk to home risk—in the present state of things a vital matter.”","“但在这些账目里，我没有看到，”索姆斯说，“国外投资风险对本国投资风险的相关比例——这在现阶段是一个尤为关键的问题。”"
"The Chairman spoke.","董事长说话了。"
"“There will be no difficulty about that, I imagine, Elderson!","“埃尔德森，我想应该不会有太大问题吧！"
"But in any case, Mr. Forsyte, we should hardly be justified in penalising the present year for the sake of eventualities which we hope will not arise.”","但不管怎样，福赛特先生，我们为了预防将来可能发生的不测——尽管我们希望不会发生这样的事——而取消今年股息的发放，恐怕这不合情理吧。"
"“I don’t know,” said Soames.","“我不知道，”索姆斯说，"
"“We are here to decide policy according to our common sense, and we must have the fullest opportunity of exercising it.","“在这里我们是根据常识来决定方针政策的，而且我们必须有运用常识的最充分的机会。"
"That is my point.","这就是我的观点。"
"We have not enough information.”","我们没有足够的信息。”"
"That ‘plausible chap’ was speaking again:","那个“花言巧语的家伙”又开口了："
"“Mr. Forsyte seems to be indicating a lack of confidence in the management.”","“福赛特先生似乎表现出对于管理层的不信任。”"
"Taking the bull by the horns—was he?","他是在铤而走险吗？"
"“Am I to have that information?”","“我究竟能否获得那些信息呢？”"
"The voice of old Mothergill rose cosy in the silence.","老莫德吉尔悦耳的声音划破了一片沉寂。"
"“The Board could be adjourned, perhaps, Mr. Chairman; I could come up myself at a pinch.","“董事长，或许董事会可以休会，如果必要的话，我还会出席的。"
"Possibly we could all attend.","我们也许都可以参加。"
"The times are very peculiar—we mustn’t take any unnecessary risks.","这次情况极为特殊——我们绝对不能冒任何不必要的风险。"
"The policy of foreign contracts is undoubtedly somewhat new to us.","对于我们来说，国外合同方针毫无疑问是新鲜事物。"
"We have no reason so far to complain of the results.","到目前为止，我们还没有理由对结果有所抱怨。"
"And I am sure we have the utmost confidence in the judgment of our managing director.","我可以肯定地说，我们对我们总经理的判断能力绝对有信心。"
"Still, as Mr. Forsyte has asked for this information, I think perhaps we ought to have it.","但是，既然福赛特先生已经提出要这样一份资料，那我想我们或许应该有这样一份材料。"
"What do you say, my lord?”","你说呢，勋爵？”"
"“I can’t come up next week.","“下周我来不了。"
"I agree with the chairman that on these accounts we couldn’t burke this year’s dividend.","我同意董事长的说法，按照现在的账目，我们不能克扣今年的股息。"
"No good getting the wind up before we must.","不到万不得已，没必要草木皆兵。"
"When do the accounts go out, Elderson?”","账目什么时候能有结果，埃尔德森？”"
"“Normally at the end of this week.”","“一切顺的话，本周末就有结果了。”"
"“These are not normal times,” said Soames.","“现在可不是一切顺利。”索姆斯说，"
"“To be quite plain, unless I have that information I must tender my resignation.”","“开诚布公地说，假如我拿不到这份材料，那我就只好提出辞职了。”"
"He saw very well what was passing in their minds.","他非常了解他们脑子里都想些什么。"
"A newcomer making himself a nuisance—they would take his resignation readily—only it would look awkward just before a general meeting unless they could announce “wife’s ill-health” or something satisfactory, which he would take very good care they didn’t.","新人总是很麻烦——他们会非常愿意接受他的辞呈的——只是在开股东大会之前出现这样的情况，不免有些尴尬，除非他们以“夫人身体欠佳”或类似令人心服口服的理由为借口，但是他会很小心避免他们利用这些借口的。"
"The chairman said coldly:","董事长冷冷地说："
"“Well, we will adjourn the Board to this day week; you will be able to get us those figures, Elderson?”","“那好吧，董事会休会，下周这个时间再召开；到时账目能有结果了吗，埃尔德森？”"
"“Certainly.”","“肯定能。”"
"Into Soames’ mind flashed the thought: ‘Ought to ask for an independent scrutiny.’","索姆斯脑海里闪过这样一个念头：“应该请求做一次独立审查。”"
"But he looked round.","但是他环顾四周。"
"Going too far—perhaps—if he intended to remain on the Board—and he had no wish to resign—after all, it was a big thing, and a thousand a year!","如果他打算继续留在这里的话，这样做确实有些过分了——何况他并不想辞职——毕竟，这是份好差事，一年1000英镑的收入啊！"
"No!","不！"
"Mustn’t overdo it!","千万不能做得太过分！"
"Walking away, he savoured his triumph doubtfully, by no means sure that he had done any good.","他一边走，一边略带怀疑地品味着自己的胜利，他根本就不能确定这样做是否能给他带来好处。"
"His attitude had only closed the ‘all together’ attitude round Elderson.","他这样做只是把他们和埃尔德森更加紧密地绑在了一起。"
"The weakness of his position was that he had nothing to go on, save an uneasiness, which when examined was found to be simply a feeling that he hadn’t enough control himself.","他所处境地的不利因素就在于，除了疑虑的感觉外，他缺乏切实有力的证据，而且仔细考虑一下，就不难看出这纯粹是他感情用事。"
"And yet, there couldn’t be two managers—you must trust your manager!","除此以外，一个公司总不可能有两个经理吧——你必须要相信你的经理！"
"A voice behind him tittupped: “Well, Forsyte, you gave us quite a shock with your alternative.","他背后响起了一个欢快的声音：“喂，福赛特，刚才你提到不查账就辞职时，我们真是吓了一大跳。"
"First time I remember anything of the sort on that Board.”","我记得在董事会还是第一次发生这样的事。”"
"“Sleepy hollow,” said Soames.","“这个地方让人打不起精神。”索姆斯说。"
"“Yes, I generally have a nap.","“是啊，我总是打瞌睡。"
"It gets very hot in there.","那里面太热了。"
"Wish I’d stuck to my spinneys.","要是能到丛林里就好了。"
"They come high, even as early as this.”","即使现在这么早的时候，丛林也已经长得很茂盛了。”"

"“By the way, Forsyte, I wanted to say: With all this modern birth control and the rest of it, one gets uneasy.","“顺便说一声，福赛特，我想说的是，面对这些现代的节制生育和其他与之相关的事情，确实使人不安啊。"
"We’re not the royal family; but don’t you feel with me it’s time there was a movement in heirs?”","我们不是皇室家族，但你是不是也认为该动员大家传宗接代了？”"
"Soames did, but he was not going to confess to anything so indelicate about his own daughter.","索姆斯有同感，但这事关他自己女儿的名声，所以他不想袒露心声。"
"“Plenty of time,” he muttered.","“时间还多着呢。”他嘀咕着。"
"“I don’t like that dog, Forsyte.”","“福赛特，我不喜欢那条狗。”"
"Soames stared.","索姆斯瞪起眼睛。"
"“Dog!” he said.","“狗！”他说，"
"“What’s that to do with it?”","“它跟这事有什么关系？”"
"“I like a baby to come before a dog.","“我希望先有孩子再养狗。"
"Dogs and poets distract young women.","狗和诗人一样，会使年轻的女人分心。"
"My grandmother had five babies before she was twenty-seven.","我的祖母在27岁前就已经有5个孩子了。"
"She was a Montjoy; wonderful breeders, you remember them—the seven Montjoy sisters—all pretty.","她是一位芒乔伊家的人，出色的芒乔伊家的后代，你记得她们吧——那七个芒乔伊姐妹——每一个都很漂亮。"
"Old Montjoy had forty-seven grandchildren.","老芒乔伊有47个孙儿。"

"“Ah! but they think us fogeys, you know.","“是啊！但你应该知道，他们肯定认为我们因循守旧。"

"But it’s difficult, Forsyte, it’s difficult.”","但这很难，福赛特，难啊。”"
"“They’ve got everything they want,” said Soames.","“他们已经要什么有什么了。”索姆斯说。"
"“Not enough, my dear Forsyte, not enough; the condition of the world is on the nerves of the young.","“这还不够，我亲爱的福赛特，这些还不够，当今世界的形势使这些年轻人感到局促不安。"
