"You can’t breed in the air; at least, I doubt it—the difficulties are considerable.”","你不能在忐忑中抚养后代吧，至少，我觉得不行——困难重重啊。”"
"Soames sniffed.","索姆斯哼了一声。"
"“If only the journalists would hold their confounded pens,” he said; for, more and more of late, with the decrescendo of scare in the daily Press, he was regaining the old sound Forsyte feeling of security.","“但愿新闻媒体业者能够控制那令人生厌的笔。”他说。因为最近一段时间，日报上的恐慌消息愈加减少，他也恢复了福赛特家的古老祥和的安全感。"
"“We’ve only to keep clear of Europe,” he added.","“我们只要不管欧洲的事情就好了。”他补充了一句。"
"“Keep clear and keep the ring!","“既不介入但又保持中立！"
"Forsyte, I believe you’ve hit it.","福赛特，你这话算是说着了。"
"Good friendly terms with Scandinavia, Holland, Spain, Italy, Turkey—all the outlying countries that we can get at by sea.","与斯堪的纳维亚、荷兰、西班牙、意大利、土耳其——所有那些我们能够通过航海到达的遥远国家保持友好关系。"
"And let the others dree their weirds.","让其他国家听天由命。"
"It’s an idea!”","这可是个好主意！”"
"How the chap rattled on!","这家伙怎么这么喋喋不休！"

"The new formula.","这是个新原则。"
"It’s what we’ve been coming to unconsciously!","这正是我们一直没有察觉而又一直在做的！"

"Thus charged with inspiration, Soames said hastily:","一条妙计涌上心头，索姆斯匆忙地说："

"I’m going to my son’s.","我要去儿子家。"
"Look at these poor devils!”","看看这些苦命的人！”"
"Down by the Embankment at Blackfriars a band of unemployed were trailing dismally with money-boxes.","一群失业的人手捧钱盒子，在泰晤士河堤旁的黑衣修士桥上慢慢地走着，神情忧郁。"
"“Revolution in the bud!","“革命正在萌芽！"
"There’s one thing that’s always forgotten, Forsyte, it’s a great pity.”","有件事总是被忘记，福赛特，这真令人太遗憾了。”"
"“What’s that?” said Soames, with gloom.","“什么事？”索姆斯阴郁地说。"
"The fellow would tittup all the way to Fleur’s!","这家伙看样子要一路喋喋不休到弗勒家！"
"“Wash the working-class, put them in clean, pleasant-coloured jeans, teach ‘em to speak like you and me, and there’d be an end of class feeling.","“给那些工人洗洗身，给他们穿上整洁、漂亮的工装裤，教他们像咱们这样与人交流，这样就没有等级感觉了。"
"It’s all a matter of the senses.","这完全是一个感觉问题。"
"Wouldn’t you rather share a bedroom with a clean, neat-clothed plumber’s assistant who spoke and smelled like you than with a profiteer who dropped his aitches and reeked of opoponax?","你是愿意跟一个穿着干净整齐，谈吐像你我这样的管道工助手同睡一间屋呢，还是喜欢跟一个言语粗俗，浑身散发恶臭的投机奸商同睡一起呢？"

"“Never tried,” said Soames, “so don’t know.”","“我从来没试过，”索姆斯说，“所以我不知道。”"
"“Pragmatist!","“实用主义者！"

"Did you ever catch an impecunious professor wishing he was the King?”","你遇到过幻想变成国王的穷教授吗？”"
"“No,” said Soames, opening his paper.","“从没有。”索姆斯一边说，一边翻开报纸。"

"Chapter VIII","第八章"
"Bicket","比克特"
"Beneath its veneer of cheerful irresponsibility, the character of Michael Mont had deepened during two years of anchorage and continuity.","成家立业的这两年，使迈克尔·蒙特表面上玩世不恭的性格变得多了几分稳重。"
"He had been obliged to think of others; and his time was occupied.","他不得不顾及到周围人的事情，而且他把时间安排得满满的。"
"Conscious, from the fall of the flag, that he was on sufferance with Fleur, admitting as whole the half-truth: ‘Il y a toujours un qui baise, et l’autre qui tend la joue,’ he had developed real powers of domestic consideration; and yet he did not seem to redress the balance in his public or publishing existence.","自从他向弗勒妥协的那天起，他就意识到要时时处处对弗勒忍让。他完全认同那句有一定道理的名言：“世界上既然存在亲吻别人的人，那就存在伸出面颊让别人吻的人。”他在家中事事体贴，关心家人，却似乎无法平衡他的公众角色和出版人角色。"
"He found the human side of his business too strong for the monetary.","他感觉自己在处理事情上过分注重人情关系，而不是金钱。"
"Danby and Winter, however, were bearing up against him, and showed, so far, no signs of the bankruptcy prophesied for them by Soames on being told of the principles which his son-inlaw intended to introduce.","然而，丹比&温特出版社还在靠他费力支撑着，而且就目前情况来看，没有丝毫破产的迹象——当初索姆斯在听了他自己女婿想要采取一些策略时，做出过这样的断言。"
"No more in publishing than in any other walk of life was Michael finding it possible to work too much on principle.","迈克尔发现，出版业与其他任何行业一样，不能太循规蹈矩了。"
"The field of action was so strewn with facts—human, vegetable and mineral.","在行动领域处处是客观事实——人、植物，还有矿物。"
"On this same Tuesday afternoon, having long tussled with the price of those vegetable facts, paper and linen, he was listening with his pointed ears to the plaint of a packer discovered with five copies of ‘Copper Coin’ in his overcoat pocket, and the too obvious intention of converting them to his own use.","就在这周二的下午，在他卖力地就蔬菜、纸张和布料的价格讨价还价过后，他竖起耳朵倾听着一个包装工人的哭诉，因为人们在他的外套口袋里发现了五本《铜币》，显然他要将它们占为己有。"
"Mr. Danby had ‘given him the sack’—he didn’t deny that he was going to sell them, but what would Mr. Mont have done?","丹比先生已经把他解雇了——这个工人也没有否认他要把这几本书卖掉，但如果事情放在蒙特先生身上的话，他又会怎样做呢？"
"He owed rent—and his wife wanted nourishing after pneumonia—wanted it bad.","他欠了房租——他的妻子在肺炎初痊后要及时补充营养——他很需要钱。"
"‘Dash it!’ thought Michael, ‘I’d snoop an edition to nourish Fleur after pneumonia!’","“见鬼！”迈克尔想，“假若弗勒肺炎后需要补充营养，我肯定会偷走整套书换钱给她买。”"
"“And I can’t live on my wages with prices what they are.","“如今物价这么高，光靠这点儿工资根本养活不了全家。"
"I can’t, Mr. Mont, so help me!”","蒙特先生，我真的活不下去了，快救救我吧！”"
"Michael swivelled.","迈克尔在转椅上转来转去。"
"“But look here, Bicket, if we let you snoop copies, all the packers will snoop copies; and if they do, where are Danby and Winter?","“可是你想想，比克特，假如我默许了你的偷书行为，那就意味着默许所有的包装工人偷书了，如果大家都这么做，那丹比&温特出版社会怎么样？"
"In the cart.","关门啦。"
"And, if they’re in the cart, where are all of you?","再说，出版社关门，大家去哪儿？"
"In the street.","上街流浪。"
"It’s better that one of you should be in the street than that all of you should, isn’t it?”","与其大家流落大街，不如你们中间的一个人去，难道不是吗？”"
"“Yes, sir, I quite see your point—it’s reason; but I can’t live on reason, the least thing knocks you out, when you’re on the bread line.","“是啊，先生，我明白您的话——很有道理，但道理不能当饭吃，肚子吃不饱的时候，人就容易干傻事。"
"Ask Mr. Danby to give me another chance.”","请您帮我求求丹比先生，让他再给我一次机会。”"
"“Mr. Danby always says that a packer’s work is particularly confidential, because it’s almost impossible to keep a check on it.”","“丹比先生总是说，包装工人的工作特别需要诚信，因为我们无法监督它。”"
"“Yes, sir, I should feel that in future; but with all this unemployment and no reference, I’ll never get another job.","“您说的对，先生，今后我一定记着您的话，但是看看如今普遍失业的现象，我又没有推荐信，我肯定是不可能再找到工作的。"
"What about my wife?”","那我的妻子怎么活啊？”"
"To Michael it was as if he had said “What about Fleur?”","迈克尔听到这句话，就如同自己在说：“弗勒怎么办？”"
"He began to pace the room; and the young man Bicket looked at him with large dolorous eyes.","他在屋里走来走去，年轻的比克特用忧伤的大眼睛注视着他。"
"Presently he came to a standstill, with his hands deep plunged into his pockets and his shoulders hunched.","过了一会儿，他停了下来，双手深深地插在口袋里，耸起肩膀。"
"“I’ll ask him,” he said; “but I don’t believe he will; he’ll say it isn’t fair on the others.","“我跟他求求情，”他说，“但我不保证他会同意，他也许会说这样做对别人不公平。"
"You had five copies; it’s pretty stiff, you know—means you’ve had ‘em before, doesn’t it?","你这次拿了五本书，情况不乐观，你清楚——这就意味着你以前干过，是不是？"
"What?”","嗯？”"
"“Well, Mr. Mont, anything that’ll give me a chance, I don’t mind confessin’.","“唉，蒙特先生，假如能再给我一次机会，我愿意坦白一切。"
"I have ‘ad a few previous, and it’s just about kept my wife alive.","我以前的确拿过几本，但那都是为了救我妻子的命。"
"You’ve no idea what that pneumonia’s like for poor people.”","您根本无法想象肺炎对于贫困人家意味着什么。”"
"Michael pushed his fingers through his hair.","迈克尔用手捋着头发。"
"“How old’s your wife?”","“你妻子多大了？”"
"“Only a girl—twenty.”","“很年轻——刚刚20岁。”"
"Twenty!","20岁！"
"Just Fleur’s age!","正好和弗勒同岁！"
"“I’ll tell you what I’ll do, Bicket; I’ll put it up to Mr. Desert; if he speaks for you, perhaps it may move Mr. Danby.”","“比克特，我告诉你我打算怎么做。我会把这件事告诉德赛特先生，要是他肯替你求情，也许丹比先生会同意。”"
"“Well, Mr. Mont, thank you—you’re a gentleman, we all sy that.”","“嗯，蒙特先生，非常感谢您——您是位好人，我们都这么说。”"
"“Oh! hang it!","“啊！该死！"
"But look here, Bicket, you were reckoning on those five copies.","比克特，你完全是靠这五本书接济。"
"Take this to make up, and get your wife what’s necessary.","把这个拿去贴补生活吧，给你妻子买些必需品。"
"Only for goodness’ sake don’t tell Mr. Danby.”","但你千万别告诉丹比先生。”"
"“Mr. Mont, I wouldn’t deceive you for the world—I won’t sy a word, sir.","“蒙特先生，我肯定不会欺骗您的——先生，我绝对不会透漏半个字的。"
"And my wife—well!”","至于我的妻子——咳！”"
"A sniff, a shuffle—Michael was alone, with his hands plunged deeper, his shoulders hunched higher.","一声鼻子吸溜声和一阵拖沓的脚步声过后，屋里只剩下迈克尔一人了。他双手往口袋里插得更深，肩膀耸得更高。"
"And suddenly he laughed.","突然，他笑了起来。"
"Pity!","怜悯！"
"Pity was pop!","怜悯是时髦！"
"It was all dam’ funny.","这一切真滑稽。"
"Here he was rewarding Bicket for snooping ‘Copper Coin!’","比克特偷了《铜币》，他反而奖赏了他！"
"A sudden longing possessed him to follow the little packer and see what he did with the two pounds—see whether ‘the pneumonia’ was real or a figment of the brain behind those dolorous eyes.","他忽然特别想尾随着这个小包装工，看看他究竟怎么花这两镑钱——看看那“肺炎”是真的呢，还是这个有着一双忧伤眼睛的人捏造出来的。"
"Impossible, though!","可是，这不可能！"
"Instead he must ring up Wilfrid and ask him to put in a word with old Danby.","他倒是必须得给威尔弗里德打电话，请他在老丹比那里美言几句。"
"His own word was no earthly.","他的话不管用了。"
"He had put it in too often!","他替人说情说得太多了！"
"Bicket!","比克特！"
"Little one knew of anybody, life was deep and dark, and upside down!","人们对旁人知之甚少，生活深奥费解，是非颠倒！"
"What was honesty?","诚实算什么？"
"Pressure of life versus power of resistance—the result of that fight, when the latter won, was honesty!","生活的压力与反抗的力量对抗——后者胜利了，那么这场战斗的结果才叫诚实！"
"But why resist?","但为什么反抗呢？"
"Love thy neighbour as thyself—but not more!","爱人如己——但适可而止！"
"And wasn’t it a darned sight harder for Bicket on two pounds a week to love him, than for him on twenty-four pounds a week to love Bicket?...","让一周赚两镑的比克特关爱他，比让一周赚二十四镑的他关爱比克特要难得多，不是吗？……"
"“Hallo!...","“喂！……"
"That you, Wilfrid?...","威尔弗里德，是你吗？……"
"Michael speaking....","我是迈克尔……"
"One of our packers has been sneaking copies of ‘Copper Coin.’","我们这有个包装工人偷了几本《铜币》。"
"He’s ‘got the sack’—poor devil!","他已经被解雇了——真可怜！"
"I wondered if you’d mind putting in a word for him—old Dan won’t listen to me... yes, got a wife—Fleur’s age; pneumonia, so he says.","我不知道你愿不愿意替他求求情——老丹比不听我的……是啊，他有一个妻子——跟弗勒同龄，他说她得了肺炎。"
"Won’t do it again with yours anyway, insurance by common gratitude—what!...","无论如何下次不会再偷书了，用我和他共同的感激之情作担保——什么！……"
"Thanks, old man, awfully good of you—will you bob in, then?","非常感谢，老朋友，你真是太善良了——你马上就到吗？"
"We can go round home together... Oh!","我们一起回家吧……啊！"
"Well!","好啊！"
"You’ll bob in anyway.","你无论如何一定要来。"
"Aurev!”","再见！”"
"Good chap, old Wilfrid!","威尔弗里德真够朋友！"
"Real good chap—underneath!","他是真正的好朋友——打心眼里说！"
"Underneath—what?","打心眼里说——是什么呢？"
"Replacing the receiver, Michael saw a sudden great cloud of sights and scents and sounds, so foreign to the principles of his firm that he was in the habit of rejecting instantaneously every manuscript which dealt with them.","放下电话，迈尔克忽然发现一大堆有关景象、气味和声音的稿件。这些稿件与他出版社的原则相悖，所以他习惯性地立即将它们退回。"
"The war might be ‘off ‘; but it was still ‘on’ within Wilfrid, and himself.","战争也许“结束”了，但在威尔弗里德的内心和他本人的战争继续着。"
"Taking up a tube, he spoke:","他拿起电话，说道："
"“Mr. Danby in his room?","“丹比先生在吗？"
"Right!","好的！"
"If he shows any signs of flitting, let me know at once.”...","如果他要出去，请立刻通知我。”……"
"Between Michael and his senior partner a gulf was fixed, not less deep than that between two epochs, though partially filled in by Winter’s middle-age and accommodating temperament.","迈克尔和那位年长的合伙人之间存在一定代沟，其深度不亚于两个时代的距离。不过温特先生人到中年，脾气温和，或多或少弥补了一些隔阂。"
"Michael had almost nothing against Mr. Danby except that he was always right—Philip Norman Danby, of Sky House, Campden Hill, a man of sixty and some family, with a tall forehead, a preponderance of body to leg, and an expression both steady and reflective.","除了认为他永远正确之外，迈克尔对丹比先生几乎没有什么异议——菲利普·诺曼·丹比住在坎普登山上的摩天大厦，年已六十，出身名门，有着高高的前额，身材魁梧，神情坚定而又善于深思。"
"His eyes were perhaps rather close together, and his nose rather thin, but he looked a handsome piece in his well-proportioned room.","或许他的眼睛长得有些太靠近了，鼻子又略微瘦削，但从他比例恰当的五官来看，他倒是位英俊的男子。"
"He glanced up from the formation of a correct judgment on a matter of advertisement when Wilfrid Desert came in.","他正在埋头斟酌批阅一项广告业务，威尔弗里德·德赛特走进来，他抬头看了他一眼。"
"“Well, Mr. Desert, what can I do for you?","“嗯，德赛特先生，有什么能为您效劳的？"
"Sit down!”","请坐！”"
"Desert did not sit down, but looked at the engravings, at his fingers, at Mr. Danby, and said:","德赛特没坐下，而是看看那几幅版画，看看自己的手指，又看看丹比先生，说道："
"“Fact is, I want you to let that packer chap off, Mr. Danby.”","“丹比先生，我来这儿的目的就是想让您对那个包装工人高抬贵手。”"

"Oh!","哦！"
"Ah!","啊！"
"Bicket.","比克特。"
"Mont told you, I suppose?”","我猜是蒙特告诉您的吧？”"
"“Yes; he’s got a young wife down with pneumonia.”","“是啊，他的妻子年纪轻轻，得了肺炎。”"
"“They all go to our friend Mont with some tale or other, Mr. Desert—he has a very soft heart.","“德赛特先生，他们编了好多故事去哄骗我们的朋友蒙特——他心肠太软了。"
"But I’m afraid I can’t keep this man.","但是恐怕我不能留下这个人。"
"It’s a most insidious thing.","这样做后患无穷。"
"We’ve been trying to trace a leak for some time.”","为了找出这个漏洞，我们已经花费很长时间了。”"
"Desert leaned against the mantelpiece and stared into the fire.","德赛特斜倚着壁炉架，眼睛盯着炉火。"
"“Well, Mr. Danby,” he said, “your generation may like the soft in literature, but you’re precious hard in life.","“嗯，丹比先生，”他说，“你们那一代人也许喜欢文学中所具有的宽厚仁爱，但在实际生活中你们却是如此冷酷无情。"
"Ours won’t look at softness in literature, but we’re a deuced sight less hard in life.”","而我们这一代人呢，虽然对文学中具有的宽厚仁爱不屑一顾，但在实际生活中却显得软弱无能。”"
"“I don’t think it’s hard,” said Mr. Danby, “only just.”","“我可不认为这是冷酷无情，”丹比先生说，“这仅代表公正。”"
"“Are you a judge of justice?”","“您是一位公正的法官吗？”"
"“I hope so.”","“我希望如此。”"
"“Try four years’ hell, and have another go.”","“您去体验一下四年的地狱生活，再回来试试。”"
"“I really don’t see the connection.","“我确实看不出这之间有什么联系。"
"The experience you’ve been through, Mr. Desert, was bound to be warping.”","德赛特先生，你所体验的生活肯定是不同寻常的。”"
"Wilfrid turned and stared at him.","威尔弗里德转身盯着他。"
"“Forgive my saying so, but sitting here and being just is much more warping.","“请原谅我这样说话，但是坐在这里自诩公正就更不正常了。"
"Life is pretty good purgatory, to all except about thirty percent. of grown-up people.”","对于成年人来说，除了他们中的30%，生活简直就是炼狱。”"
"Mr. Danby smiled.","丹比先生笑了笑。"
"“We simply couldn’t conduct our business, my dear young man, without scrupulous honesty in everybody.","“没有了最起码的诚实，亲爱的年轻人，我们这一行根本维持不下去。"
"To make no distinction between honesty and dishonesty would be quite unfair.","不区分诚实与否是很不公平的。"
"You know that perfectly well.”","这一点你应该很清楚。”"
"“I don’t know anything perfectly well, Mr. Danby; and I mistrust those who say they do.”","“丹比先生，我对任何事情都不甚了解，而且我也不信任那些标榜什么都清楚的人。”"
"“Well, let us put it that there are rules of the game which must be observed, if society is to function at all.”","“好吧，换句话说，社会要想运作，那么每个行业就一定会有必须遵守的规章原则。”"
"Desert smiled, too: “Oh! hang rules!","德赛特也笑了：“啊！该死的原则！"
"Do it as a favour to me.","就算帮我一次。"

"No trace of struggle showed in Mr. Danby’s face; but his deep-set, close-together eyes shone a little.","丹比先生的脸上仍然平静，不过他那双深陷的、聚拢的眼睛闪了闪。"
"“I should be only too glad, but it’s a matter—well, of conscience, if you like.","“能帮您的忙是我的荣幸，但这是一个——关乎良心的问题，可以这么说。"
"I’m not prosecuting the man.","我不想起诉那个人。"

"On the mat was Michael in two minds.","迈克尔站在脚垫上，进退为难。"
"“Well?”","“怎么样？”"
"“No go.","“没戏。"
"The old blighter’s too just.”","那个老家伙太公正了。”"
"Michael stivered his hair.","迈克尔挠了挠头发。"
"“Wait in my room five minutes while I let the poor beggar know, then I’ll come along.”","“在我屋里等五分钟，我去告诉那个可怜的家伙，然后咱俩一起走。”"
"“No,” said Desert, “I’m going the other way.”","“不，”德赛特说，“咱俩不顺道。”"
"Not the fact that Wilfrid was going the other way—he almost always was—but something in the tone of his voice and the look on his face obsessed Michael’s imagination while he went downstairs to seek Bicket.","迈克尔跑下楼找比克特的时候，心里起了猜疑，让他困惑的并不是威尔弗里德的不顺道——他几乎总是这样——而是他说话时的语气和表情。"
"Wilfrid was a rum chap—he went “dark” so suddenly!","威尔弗里德是个古怪的家伙——一下子变得“阴郁”了！"
"In the nether regions he asked:","到了地下车间，他问："

"“No, sir, there he is.”","“没有，先生，他还在那里。”"
"There he was, in his shabby overcoat, with his pale narrow face, and his disproportionately large eyes, and his sloping shoulders.","他站在那里，穿着一件破旧的大衣，苍白瘦长的脸上长着一双不成比例的大眼睛，肩膀耷拉着。"
"“Sorry, Bicket, Mr. Desert has been in, but it’s no go.”","“非常抱歉，比克特，德赛特先生去替你求情了，但是很遗憾行不通。”"
"“No, sir?”","“行不通吗，先生？”"
"“Keep your pecker up, you’ll get something.”","“振作起来，你会找到工作的。”"

"Well, I thank you very ‘eartily; and I thank Mr. Desert.","嗯，我从心里感谢您，也感谢德赛特先生。"
"Good-night, sir; and good-bye!”","晚安，先生，再见！”"
"Michael watched him down the corridor, saw him waver into the dusky street.","迈克尔看着他从走廊向外走去，看见他摇摇晃晃地走进一条阴暗的街道。"
"“Jolly!” he said, and laughed....","“妙极了！”他说着笑了起来……"
"The natural suspicions of Michael and his senior partner that a tale was being pitched were not in fact justified.","迈克尔和他那年长的合伙人对这个让人心生怜悯的故事产生的合理怀疑其实是有失公允的。"
"Neither the wife nor the pneumonia had been exaggerated; and wavering away in the direction of Blackfriars Bridge, Bicket thought not of his turpitude nor of how just Mr. Danby had been, but of what he should say to her.","无论是他的妻子，还是肺炎，都是确凿的事实。此时，比克特正摇晃着身子朝黑衣修士桥走去，他想的不是自己的堕落，也不是丹比先生在此事上坚决的态度，而是回到家里应该如何向妻子交代。"
"He should not, of course, tell her that he had been detected in stealing; he must say he had ‘got the sack for cheeking the foreman’; but what would she think of him for doing that, when everything as it were depended on his not cheeking the foreman?","当然，他是肯定不会告诉妻子自己因为偷窃被当场发现而被开除，他必须说是“因为顶撞领班而被解雇的”。但是如今他不应该去顶撞领班，而他又偏偏这么做了，妻子对他会有什么想法呢？"
"This was one of those melancholy cases of such affection that he had been coming to his work day after day feeling as if he had ‘left half his guts’ behind him in the room where she lay, and when at last the doctor said to him:","他对妻子的爱已经到了一种忧郁的状态，以至于他每天去上班的时候，感觉自己“半个灵魂”留在了妻子躺着的那间屋里。当医生最后跟他说："
"“She’ll get on now, but it’s left her very run down—you must feed her up,” his anxiety had hardened into a resolution to have no more.","“她会慢慢恢复好的，但这场疾病使她非常虚弱——你必须给她加强营养。”他的种种忧虑一下子变成了坚定的决心，不让自己再忧虑徘徊。"
"In the next three weeks he had ‘pinched’ eighteen ‘Copper Coins,’ including the five found in his overcoat.","在接下来的三周里，他一共“扔掉”18本《铜币》，包括在他大衣里发现的那5本。"
"He had only ‘pitched on’ Mr. Desert’s book because it was ‘easy sold,’ and he was sorry now that he hadn’t pitched on some one else’s.","他只“选中”德赛特的书，缘于这本书“容易卖”，他现在真后悔为什么当初没有选中其他作者的书。"
"Mr. Desert had been very decent.","德赛特先生非常慷慨。"
"He stopped at the corner of the Strand, and went over his money.","他在斯特兰德大街的拐角站住，数了数钱。"
"With the two pounds given him by Michael and his wages he had seventy-five shillings in the world, and going into the Stores he bought a meat jelly and a tin of Benger’s food that could be made with water.","加上迈克尔给的两镑钱和工资，他一共有75先令。他走进百货商店，买了一瓶肉冻和一罐加水即食的本杰牌食品。"
"With pockets bulging he took a ‘bus, which dropped him at the corner of his little street on the Surrey side.","他口袋鼓鼓的，坐上了公共汽车，在萨里区边上他住的那条街道的拐角处下车。"
"His wife and he occupied the two ground floor rooms, at eight shillings a week, and he owed for three weeks.","他和妻子住在底层两间屋里，一周租金八先令，而他已经欠了三周租金了。"
"‘Py that!’ he thought, ‘and have a roof until she’s well.’","“付了吧！”他想，“住到她痊愈了再说吧。”"
"It would help him over the news, too, to show her a receipt for the rent and some good food.","再说，他拿着结租金的收据和好吃的给妻子，也好帮助他说出那个消息。"
"How lucky they had been careful to have no baby!","他们一直没有生养小孩，真是万幸！"
"He sought the basement.","他来到地下室。"
"His landlady was doing the week’s washing.","房东太太正在洗一周堆积的衣服。"
"She paused, in sheer surprise at such full and voluntary payment, and inquired after his wife.","她怔了一下，对他一下子那么主动地付清租金大为惊讶，接着询问了他妻子的情况。"
"“Doing nicely, thank you.”","“谢谢您，情况还不错。”"
"“Well, I’m glad of that, it must be a relief to your mind.”","“哦，这真让人高兴，这下你可以宽宽心了。”"
"“It is,” said Bicket.","“是啊。”比克特说。"
"The landlady thought: ‘He’s a thread-paper—reminds me of a shrimp before you bile it, with those eyes.’","房东太太心想：“他太瘦了——那双眼睛让我一下想到了没有煮过的虾。”"
"“Here’s your receipt, and thank you.","“给你，这是收据，谢谢你。"
"Sorry to ‘ave seemed nervous about it, but times are ‘ard.”","请原谅我曾经多次催你交房租，但是日子确实难以维持啊。”"
"“They are,” said Bicket.","“的确啊，”比克特说，"
"“So long!”","“再见！”"
"With the receipt and the meat jelly in his left hand, he opened the door of his front room.","他左手拿着肉冻和收据，右手推开了房门。"
"His wife was sitting before a very little fire.","他妻子正坐在一小盆炉火的前面。"
"Her bobbed black hair, crinkly towards the ends, had grown during her illness; it shook when she turned her head and smiled.","她的黑色短发发梢卷曲，自生病以来已经长长了不少。当她回头冲比克特微笑时，她的头发也跟着晃动起来。"
"To Bicket—not for the first time—that smile seemed queer, ‘pathetic-like,’ mysterious—as if she saw things that one didn’t see oneself.","对于比克特来说——这已经不是第一次了——她的微笑有些奇怪，略带忧伤，让人猜不透——好像她看到了旁人无法看到的东西。"
"Her name was Victorine, and he said: “Well, Vic.?","她叫维多琳。他说：“好些吗，维？"
"This jelly’s a bit of all right, and I’ve pyde the rent.”","肉冻看起来不错，而且房租也结了。”"
"He sat on the arm of the chair and she put her hand on his knee—her thin arm emerging blue-white from the dark dressing-gown.","他坐在椅子的扶手上，维多琳把手放在他的膝盖上——苍白细长的胳膊从深色睡衣里伸出来。"
"“Well, Tony?”","“你怎么样，托尼？”"
"Her face—thin and pale with those large dark eyes and beautifully formed eyebrows—was one that “looked at you from somewhere; and when it looked at you—well! it got you right inside!”","她的脸——苍白消瘦，上面有一双黑色的大眼睛和两道漂亮的弯眉——是那种“从某个地方看着你，而且它看着你的时候——嗯！就看透你的心思！”"
"It got him now and he said: “How’ve you been breathin’?”","此时此刻她就看透了他的心思。他说：“你这会儿呼吸感觉如何？”"
"“All right—much better.","“不错——比之前好多了。"
"I’ll soon be out now.”","再过一阵就能出门了。”"
"Bicket twisted himself round and joined his lips to hers.","比克特扭过身子，亲吻着维多琳。"
"The kiss lasted some time, because all the feelings which he had not been able to express during the past three weeks to her or to anybody, got into it.","他们吻了许久，这一吻包含了以前三周他对妻子或旁人无法表示的感情。"
"He sat up again, “sort of exhausted,” staring at the fire, and said: “News isn’t bright—lost my job, Vic.”","他重新坐好，说：“有些累了，”他盯着炉火，“维，有个坏消息，我被解雇了。”"
"“Oh!","“啊！"
"Tony!","托尼！"
"Why?”","为什么啊？”"
"Bicket swallowed.","比克特咽了一下唾沫。"
"“Fact is, things are slack, and they’re reducin’.”","“因为生意惨淡，公司裁员。”"
"There had surged into his mind the certainty that sooner than tell her the truth he would put his head under the gas!","他心里有个坚定的信念，宁愿把头放在煤气炉里自杀，也绝不能对妻子说实情。"
"“Oh! dear!","“啊！亲爱的！"
"What shall we do, then?”","那我们可怎么办啊？”"
"Bicket’s voice hardened.","比克特语气坚定起来。"
"“Don’t you worry—I’ll get something”; and he whistled.","“别担心——我会找着工作的。”说着，他还吹起了口哨。"
"“But you liked that job.”","“但你很喜欢那份工作。”"
"“Did I?","“是吗？"
"I liked some o’ the fellers; but as for the job—why, what was it?","我喜欢那里的同事，但是至于工作嘛——嗨，那算得了什么？"
"Wrappin’ books up in a bysement all dy long.","天天就是在地下室包装书本。"
"Let’s have something to eat and get to bed early—I feel as if I could sleep for a week, now I’m shut of it.”","我们吃完饭就早点儿休息吧——我感觉现在没有工作的束缚，可以睡上一整周呢。”"
"Getting their supper ready with her help, he carefully did not look at her face for fear it might “get him agyne inside!”","她帮他做好了晚饭，他尽量避免看妻子的脸，担心那会更“让他心痛”！"
"They had only been married a year, having made acquaintance on a tram, and Bicket often wondered what had made her take to him, eight years her senior and C3 during the war!","他们是在电车上认识的，结婚刚刚一年。比克特常常感觉新奇，究竟自己身上具有什么魅力，会让妻子嫁给自己！他大她八岁，而且大战期间体检结果是丙下！"
"And yet she must be fond of him, or she’d never look at him as she did.","但她一定是爱他的，要不然绝不会这样望着他。"
"“Sit down and try this jelly.”","“坐下尝尝刚买的肉冻。”"
"He himself ate bread and margarine and drank cocoa, he seldom had any particular appetite.","他自己吃面包抹黄油，喝可可，他很少吃其他特别的东西。"
"“Shall I tell you what I’d like?” he said; “I’d like Central Austrylia.","“我告诉你我喜欢什么吧？”他说，“我喜欢澳大利亚中部。"
"We had a book in there about it; they sy there’s quite a movement.","我们那儿有一本描述那个地方的书，书上说有很多人移民到那儿了。"
"I’d like some sun.","我喜欢晒太阳。"
"I believe if we ‘ad sun we’d both be twice the size we are.","我相信，如果能多晒晒太阳，咱俩的身体肯定比现在更健康。"
"I’d like to see colour in your cheeks, Vic.”","维，我希望你脸上有点儿血色。”"
"“How much does it cost to get out there?”","“去那里要花多少钱呢？”"
"“A lot more than we can ly hands on, that’s the trouble.","“很多的钱，多得我们无法去，这是个难题。"
"But I’ve been thinkin’.","但我一直就想去那儿。"
"England’s about done.","英国快要衰败了。"
"There’s too many like me.”","像我这样的人数不胜数。”"
"“No,” said Victorine; “there aren’t enough.”","“不，”维多琳说，“像你的人可不多。”"
"Bicket looked at her face, then quickly at his plate.","比克特看看她，然后快速将目光移向盘子。"
"“What myde you take a fancy to me?”","“你怎么会喜欢我呢？”"
"“Because you don’t think first of yourself, that’s why.”","“因为你凡事总为别人着想，就是这个原因。”"
"“Used to before I knew you.","“在认识你之前，我是先考虑自己的。"
"But I’d do anything for you, Vic.”","但为了你，维，我愿意做任何事情。”"
"“Have some of this jelly, then, it’s awful good.”","“吃点儿肉冻吧，特别好吃。”"
"Bicket shook his head.","比克特摇摇头。"
"“If we could wyke up in Central Austrylia,” he said.","“假如一觉醒来，我们已经在澳大利亚中部了，那就好了。”他说，"
"“But there’s only one thing certain, we’ll wyke up in this blighted little room.","“但唯一有一件事我能肯定——我们一觉醒来肯定还会在这间破旧的小屋里。"
"Never mind, I’ll get a job and earn the money yet.”","没关系，我会找到工作的，挣够去那儿的钱的。”"
"“Could we win it on a race?”","“我们能不能赌马赚钱呢？”"
"“Well, I’ve only got forty-seven bob all told, and if we lose it, where’ll you be?","“哦，我现在一共就有47个先令，如果我们输了，你打算住哪儿？"
"You’ve got to feed up, you know.","你是知道的，你必须要多补充营养。"
"No, I must get a job.”","不行，我无论如何要找到一份工作。”"
"“They’ll give you a good recommend, won’t they?”","“他们会为你提供一份不错的介绍信吗？会不会呢？”"
"Bicket rose and stacked his plate and cup.","比克特站起来，把盘子和杯子摞起来。"
"“They would, but that job’s off—overstocked.”","“会的，但是那份工作不行了——干的人太多了。”"
"Tell her the truth?","告诉她实情吗？"
"Never!","绝不！"
"So help him!","上帝保佑！"
"In their bed, one of those just too wide for one and just not wide enough for two, he lay, with her hair almost in his mouth, thinking what to say to his Union, and how to go to work to get a job.","他躺在那张一人睡太宽、两人睡太窄的床上，她的头发几乎挨到他的嘴唇。他在心里盘算着该如何跟工会商讨，该怎样找份工作。"
"And in his thoughts as the hours drew on he burned his boats.","一个小时一个小时地过去了，他思来想去，决定要破釜沉舟。"
"To draw his unemployment money he would have to tell his Union what the trouble was.","想要失业救济金，就得跟工会说出困难所在。"
"Blow the Union!","该死的工会！"
"He wasn’t going to be accountable to them!","他不想去跟他们解释情况！"
"HE knew why he’d pinched the books; but it was nobody else’s business, nobody else could understand his feelings, watching her so breathless, pale and thin.","他自己非常清楚为什么会去偷书，但是这跟别人没关系。当他看着妻子呼吸困难、脸色苍白、身体消瘦，那种感觉没有人能够理解。"
"Strike out for himself!","只有依靠自己的拼搏！"
"And a million and a half out o’ work!","150万人都失业了！"
"Well, he had a fortnight’s keep, and something would turn up—and he might risk a bob or two and win some money, you never knew.","嗯，他们的生活还足以勉强维持两周，说不定会发生什么——他也许会拿一两个先令去冒冒险，说不定会赢钱，这谁都说不准。"
"She turned in her sleep.","她翻个身继续睡着。"
"‘Yes,’ he thought, ‘I’d do it agyne...’","“对，”他想，“我要再拼一下……”"
"Next day, after some hours on foot, he stood under the grey easterly sky in the grey street, before a plate-glass window protecting an assortment of fruits and sheaves of corn, lumps of metal, and brilliant blue butterflies, in the carefully golden light of advertised Australia.","隔天，走了几个小时后，在东方灰蒙蒙的天空下，他来到了灰色的街道。透过大玻璃橱窗，他看见各种各样的水果、一束束谷物、一块块的金属和色彩艳丽的蓝蝴蝶，这一切都映衬在金色的灯光下，原来这些精心布置都是为了宣传澳大利亚。"
"To Bicket, who had never been out of England, not often out of London, it was like standing outside Paradise.","比克特从来没有离开过英国半步，也很少离开伦敦，对他来说，这一切似乎意味着站在天堂之外。"
"The atmosphere within the office itself was not so golden, and the money required considerable; but it brought Paradise nearer to take away pamphlets which almost burned his hands, they were so warm.","办事处的气氛可不是那般宜人，咨询费很是昂贵。但当他拿走几乎烫手的那几本宣传册子时，似乎他离天堂又近了一步——那些宣传册子真是温暖人心。"
"Later, he and she, sitting in the one armchair—advantage of being thin—pored over these alchemised pages and inhaled their glamour.","过后，他和她挤坐在一张扶椅上——瘦人的优势——仔细端详着这些带着魔力的书，啧啧惊叹。"
"“D’you think it’s true, Tony?”","“你觉得这是真的吗，托尼？”"
"“If it’s thirty per cent. true it’s good enough for me.","“即便只有30%是真的，对我来说也够好的了。"
"We just must get there somehow.","我们必须想办法去那里。"
"Kiss me.”","亲一下。”"
"From around the corner in the main road the rumbling of the trams and carts, and the rattling of their window-pane in the draughty dry easterly wind increased their feeling of escape into a gas-lit Paradise.","从大街的拐角处传来了主路上电车和火车的隆隆声，屋里的窗户被强劲又干燥的东风吹得嘎吱作响。这周围的环境使他们愈发想要快些逃到那个点着煤气灯的天堂。"

"Chapter IX","第九章"
"Confusion","混乱"
"Two hours behind Bicket, Michael wavered towards home.","比克特离开两个小时以后，迈克尔摇摇摆摆地回家了。"
"Old Danby was right as usual—if you couldn’t trust your packers, you might shut up shop!","老丹比一如既往地正确——信不过自己店里的包装工，还是关店大吉吧！"
"Away from Bicket’s eyes, he doubted.","比克特走后，他心生疑虑了。"
"Perhaps the chap hadn’t a wife at all!","也许这家伙根本就没有妻子！"
"Then Wilfrid’s manner usurped the place of Bicket’s morals.","随后，比克特的道德问题让位给了威尔弗里德的怪异举止。"
"Old Wilfrid had been abrupt and queer the last three times of meeting.","最近三次会面，威尔弗里德老兄显得唐突而古怪。"
"Was he boiling-up for verse?","他是因为作诗而情绪不稳吗？"
"He found Ting-a-ling at the foot of the stairs in a conservative attitude.","他发现小叮铃在楼梯角那里一动不动，态度十分固执。"
"“I am not going up,” he seemed saying, “until some one carries me—at the same time it is later than usual!”","它似乎在说：“没人抱我，我就不上去，平时早就有人抱我上去了！”"
"“Where’s your mistress, you heraldic little beast?”","“女主人呢，你这个传令官小畜生？”"
"Ting-a-ling snuffled.","小叮铃抽了抽鼻子。"
"“I could put up with it,” he implied, “if YOU carried me—these stairs are laborious!”","它似乎在说：“如果抱我上去，我就不计较您这句话了。上楼梯太费劲了！”"
"Michael took him up.","迈克尔把它抱起来。"
"“Let’s go and find her.”","“咱们去找找她吧。”"
"Squeezed under an arm harder than his mistress’, Ting-a-ling stared as if with black-glass eyes; and the plume of his emergent tail quivered.","夹在比女主人更硬的手臂下，小叮铃瞪着它那黑玻璃球似的眼睛，尾巴翘起，上面的毛发微微颤动着。"
"In the bedroom Michael dropped him so absent-mindedly that he went to his corner plume pendent, and couched there in dudgeon.","到了卧室，迈克尔心不在焉地把它丢下，它便垂着尾巴走到自己的角落，愤愤地蹲在那里。"
"Nearly dinner time and Fleur not in!","快开饭了，弗勒还没回来！"
"Michael went over his sketchy recollection of her plans.","迈克尔把自己大概记得的她今天的日程安排回想了一遍。"
"To-day she had been having Hubert Marsland and that Vertiginist—what was his name?—to lunch.","今天，她约了休伯特·马斯兰德和那个旋转派画家——忘了他叫什么名字了——吃午饭。"
"There would have been fumes to clear off.","那里一定闹得乌烟瘴气，不可开交。"
"Vertiginists—like milk—made carbonic acid gas in the lungs!","旋转派画家，像牛奶一样，会在胃里制造碳酸气体！"
"Still!","还不回来！"
"Half-past seven!","都7点半了！"
"What was happening to-night?","难道今晚发生了什么事情？"
"Weren’t they going to that play of L.S.D.’s?","他们该不会去看L. S. D.写的那部戏了吧？"
"No—that was tomorrow!","不对呀，那是明天啊！"
"Was there conceivably nothing?","或许没什么事？"
"If so, of course she would shorten her unoccupied time as much as possible.","如果这样的话，她自然会尽量缩短非应酬的时间。"
"He made that reflection humbly.","他这么保守估计着。"
"Michael had no illusions, he knew himself to be commonplace, with only a certain redeeming liveliness, and, of course, his affection for her.","迈克尔没有任何奢望，他知道自己很普通，唯一可取之处就是活泼，当然，还有对她的爱。"
"He even recognised that his affection was a weakness, tempting him to fussy anxieties, which on principle he restrained.","他甚至认为对她的爱是自己的弱点，因为爱，他总是惶恐不安，原则却又极力克制这一点。"
"To enquire, for instance, of Coaker or Philps—their man and their maid—when she had gone out, would be thoroughly against that principle.","比如，他会向家里的仆人科克和菲尔普斯询问她何时出去的，这就完全违背了他的原则。"
"The condition of the world was such that Michael constantly wondered if his own affairs were worth paying attention to; but then the condition of the world was also such that sometimes one’s own affairs seemed all that were worth paying attention to.","世事就是如此，自己的事情是否值得关注，这常常让迈克尔困惑不已；可是，世事又是这样，有时，自己的事情才是唯一值得关心的。"
"And yet his affairs were, practically speaking, Fleur; and if he paid too much attention to them, he was afraid of annoying her.","可实际上，他的事只与弗勒有关，如果他抓得太紧，又怕惹恼了她。"
"He went into his dressing-room and undid his waistcoat.","他走进更衣室，脱下马甲。"
"‘But no!’ he thought; ‘if she finds me “dressed” already, it’ll put too much point on it.’","他心想：“不妥，如果她发现我‘穿戴整齐’，那未免做得太明显了。”"
"So he did up his waistcoat and went downstairs again.","所以，他又穿上马甲，又下楼去了。"
"Coaker was in the hall.","科克在门厅里。"
"“Mr. Forsyte and Sir Lawrence looked in about six, sir.","“先生，福赛特先生和劳伦斯爵士大约6点钟来过。"
"Mrs. Mont was out.","蒙特夫人已经出去了。"
"What time shall I serve dinner?”","您准备什么时候开饭？”"
"“Oh! about a quarter past eight.","“嗯，8点15分左右吧。"
"I don’t think we’re going out.”","我想我们不会出去了。”"
"He went into the drawing-room and passing down its Chinese emptiness, drew aside the curtain.","他走进客厅，在这间空荡荡的中国式房间里走着，拉开了窗帘。"
"The square looked cold and dark and draughty; and he thought: ‘Bicket—pneumonia—I hope she’s got her fur coat.’","外面起风了，广场显得又冷又黑，于是他想：“比克特——肺炎——希望她穿那件皮大衣了。”"
"He took out a cigarette and put it back.","他拿出一支烟，又放了回去。"
"If she saw him at the window she would think him fussy; and he went up again to see if she had put on her fur!","如果她发现我站在窗旁，她又会认为我大惊小怪了。于是他又上楼了，看看她穿没穿皮大衣！"
"Ting-a-ling, still couchant, greeted him plume dansetti arrested as at disappointment.","小叮铃仍旧蹲在那里，以为主人回来了，立刻摇尾表示欢迎，一看不对，又失望地停住了。"
"Michael opened a wardrobe.","迈克尔打开衣橱。"
"She had!","她穿了！"
"Good!","很好！"
"He was taking a sniff round, when Ting-a-ling passed him trottant, and her voice said: “Well, my darling!”","就在他打量衣橱时，小叮铃忽然从他身边走过，同时，响起了她的声音：“嗨，亲爱的！”"
"Wishing that he was, Michael emerged from behind the wardrobe door.","迈克尔希望这是在叫他，立刻从衣橱门后走出来。"
"Heaven!","天啊！"
"She looked pretty, coloured by the wind!","她太美了，被风吹红了面颊！"
"He stood rather wistfully silent.","他默然地站在那里，若有所思。"
"“Hallo, Michael!","“嗨，迈克尔！"
"I’m rather late.","我回来晚了。"
"Been to the Club and walked home.”","我去俱乐部了，走着回来的。”"
"Michael had a quite unaccountable feeling that there was suppression in that statement.","迈克尔有种说不出来的感觉，他认为弗勒对自己有所保留。"
"He also suppressed, and said: “I was just looking to see that you’d got your fur, it’s beastly cold.","他也有所保留，说道：“我刚才在那儿，是看你穿没穿大衣出去，天气挺冷的。"
"Your dad and Bart have been and went away fasting.”","你父亲和准爵爷来过，没吃饭就离开了。”"
"Fleur shed her coat and dropped into a chair.","弗勒脱下大衣，往椅子上一靠。"
"“I’m tired.","“我累了。"
"Your ears are sticking up so nicely to-night, Michael.”","迈克尔，今晚，你的耳朵竖得特别好看。”"
"Michael went on his knees and joined his hands behind her waist.","迈克尔跪了下去，双手搂着她的腰。"
"Her eyes had a strange look, a scrutiny which held him in suspense, a little startled.","她审视着他，眼神奇怪，让他感到不安，还有点儿摸不着头脑。"
"“If YOU got pneumonia,” he said, “I should go clean out of curl.”","“如果你染上肺炎，”他说，“那我就完了。”"
"“Why on earth should I?”","“为什么我偏要得这种病呢？”"
"“You don’t know the connection—never mind, it wouldn’t interest you.","“你不知道这其中的联系——没什么，你不会感兴趣的。"
"We’re not going out, are we?”","我们不出去了，是吗？”"
"“Of course we are.","“我们当然出去了。"
"It’s Alison’s monthly.”","今天是艾莉森的每月例会啊。”"
"“Oh!","“哦！"
"Lord!","哎呀！"
"If you’re tired we could cut that.”","如果你累了，我们可以不去。”"
"“My dear!","“亲爱的！"
"Impos.!","这可不行！"
"She’s got all sorts of people coming.”","她请了很多人来。”"
"Stifling a disparagement, he sighed out: “Right-o!","他忍下了一句轻蔑的话，叹了口气，说道：“那好吧！"
"War-paint?”","穿礼服吗？”"
"“Yes, white waistcoat.","“是的，还要穿白马甲。"
"I like you in white waistcoats.”","我喜欢看你穿白马甲。”"
"Cunning little wretch?","狡猾的小坏蛋！"
"He squeezed her waist and rose.","他紧紧抱了一下她的腰，然后站起身来。"
"Fleur laid a light stroke on his hand, and he went into his dressing-room comforted....","弗勒轻轻拍了一下他的手，他感到很满足，朝更衣室走去……"
"But Fleur sat still for at least five minutes—not precisely ‘a prey to conflicting emotions,’ but the victim of very considerable confusion.","可是，弗勒在那里静静地坐了至少五分钟——虽然不全是挣扎的情感所致，但却是目前极其混乱的局面造成的。"
"TWO men within the last hour had done this thing—knelt at her knees and joined their fingers behind her waist.","在刚才的一个小时里，两个男人在她面前做了同一件事情——跪在她膝前，搂住她的腰。"
"Undoubtedly she had been rash to go to Wilfrid’s rooms.","无疑，她去威尔弗里德家的举动过于鲁莽了。"
"The moment she got there she had perceived how entirely unprepared she really was to commit herself to what was physical.","她一到那里，就发现自己并非想要委身于肉欲。"
"True he had done no more than Michael.","他所做的也不过同迈克尔刚才一样。"
"But—Goodness!—she had seen the fire she was playing with, realised what torment he was in.","可是——天哪！——她发觉自己在玩火，也意识到了他的痛苦。"
"She had strictly forbidden him to say a word to Michael, but intuitively she knew that in his struggle between loyalties she could rely on nothing.","她告诫他，绝对不能对迈克尔透露一个字，但她的直觉告诉她，如果要他在情和义中间选一个，她毫无胜算。"
"Confused, startled, touched, she could not help a pleasant warmth in being so much loved by two men at once, nor an itch of curiosity about the upshot.","她感到混乱、惊恐、还有感动，想到同时被两个男人这样深爱着，一丝愉快的暖意不由得涌上心头。她对未来也充满好奇，渴望知道结局。"
"And she sighed.","她不禁叹了口气。"
"She had added to her collection of experiences—but how to add further without breaking up the collection, and even perhaps the collector, she could not see.","她增加了一份收藏经验——但是如何进一步增加，而不破坏整个收藏乃至收藏者，她却不知道。"
"After her words to Wilfrid before the Eve: “You will be a fool to go—wait!” she had known he would expect something before long.","自从上次在夏娃画像前，她对威尔弗里德说了“你要是走了，你就是个傻瓜。等着！”之后，她知道他会期待不久的将来发生什么事情。"
"Often he had asked her to come and pass judgment on his ‘junk.’","他经常请她帮忙鉴定他的“旧货”。"
"A month, even a week, ago she would have gone without thinking more than twice about it, and discussed his ‘junk’ with Michael afterwards!","要是在一个月前，哪怕是一周前，她会想也不想就去了，事后还会和迈克尔讨论这些“旧货”！"
"But now she thought it over many times, and but for the fumes of lunch, and the feeling, engendered by the society of the ‘Vertiginist,’ of Amabel Nazing, of Linda Frewe, that scruples of any kind were ‘stuffy,’ sensations of all sorts ‘the thing,’ she would probably still have been thinking it over now.","可是现在，她却反复考虑这件事了，一直到乌烟瘴气的午餐会上，“旋转派画家”、阿玛贝尔·内津和琳达·弗鲁的讨论提醒了她——任何性质的顾虑都是“乏味的”，各种各样的感觉才是“正事”——她可能到现在都想不明白呢。"
"When they departed, she had taken a deep breath and her telephone receiver from the Chinese tea chest.","大家走后，她才深吸了一口气，同时打开中国式茶柜，拿出电话听筒。"
"If Wilfrid were going to be in at half-past five, she would come and see his ‘junk.’","如果威尔弗里德五点半在家的话，她就去看他的“旧货”。"
"His answer: “My God!","他回答道：“上帝啊！"
"Will you?” almost gave her pause.","你会来吗？”这又让她踌躇了。"
"But dismissing hesitation with the thought: ‘I WILL be Parisian—Proust!’ she had started for her Club.","但是，她用“我一定要有普鲁斯特式的巴黎气派”排解了自己的踌躇，动身去了俱乐部。"
"Three-quarters of an hour, with no more stimulant than three cups of China tea, three back numbers of the ‘Glass of Fashion,’ three back views of country members ‘dead in chairs,’ had sent her forth a careful quarter of an hour behind her time.","俱乐部里没有更令她兴奋的事可做，只是在三刻钟的时间里喝了三杯茶，看了三本过期的《时装镜》，看了“三个呆坐在椅子上”的乡村会员的背影，然后特意比约定时间晚了一刻钟动身了。"
"On the top floor Wilfrid was standing in his open doorway, pale as a soul in purgatory.","他家的门敞开着，威尔弗里德站在楼顶，脸色苍白，就像饱受煎熬的幽灵。"
"He took her hand gently, and drew her in.","他轻轻地拉牵着她的手，引她进去。"
"Fleur thought with a little thrill: ‘Is this what it’s like?","弗勒有点儿激动，她想：“这事就像这样吗？"
"Du cote de chez Swann!’","在斯万家里！”"
"Freeing her hand, she began at once to flutter round the ‘junk,’ clinging to it piece by piece.","她松开手，即刻开始打量那些“旧货”，着迷地一件件看起来。"
"Old English ‘junk’ rather manorial, with here and there an eastern or First Empire bit, collected by some bygone Desert, nomadic, or attached to the French court.","这些古老的英国“旧货”颇有点儿庄园气息，其中还散落着几件东方或是第一帝国时期的物件，东西是某个德赛特先人的藏品，这位收藏者若不是一位流浪者，就是曾经出入法兰西宫廷的人。"
"She was afraid to sit down, for fear that he might begin to follow the authorities; nor did she want to resume the intense talk of the Tate Gallery.","弗勒不敢坐下，怕他会顺势对自己做出越矩的行为；她也不愿意继续他们在泰特美术馆的那场激烈的谈话。"
"‘Junk’ was safe, and she only looked at him in those brief intervals when he was not looking at her.","看“旧货”显得很安全，在他不看她的瞬间，她才瞟他一眼。"
"She knew she was not playing the game according to ‘La Garconne’ and Amabel Nazing; that, indeed, she was in danger of going away without having added to her sensations.","她知道自己没按照《独身女人》和阿玛贝尔·内津的方式耍手段；事实上，她明白这样离开，会一无所获。"
"And she couldn’t help being sorry for Wilfrid; his eyes yearned after her, his lips were bitter to look at.","她禁不住为威尔弗里德而忧伤；他的目光充满渴望，双唇饱含了苦涩。"
"When at last from sheer exhaustion of ‘junk’ she sat down, he had flung himself at her feet.","后来，她实在看累了，就坐了下来，这时，威尔弗里德扑到她的脚旁。"
"Half hypnotised, with her knees against his chest, as safe as she could hope for, she really felt the tragedy of it—his horror of himself, his passion for herself.","她陷入了半梦半醒的状态，用双膝顶着他的胸部，希望这种方式会尽可能安全些。她感觉到了事态的严重性——他如此不顾自己，如此迷恋她。"
"It was painful, deep; it did not fit in with what she had been led to expect; it was not in the period, and how—how was she to get away without more pain to him and to herself?","这是撕心裂肺的痛苦，这种做法不符合大家对她的期望，这种爱也不为这个时代所接受——要怎样脱身，才不会增加彼此的痛苦呢？"
"When she HAD got away, with one kiss received but not answered, she realised that she had passed through a quarter of an hour of real life, and was not at all sure that she liked it....","带着她无法回应的一吻离开后，她才意识到刚才那一刻钟才是真爱的生活，但对于自己是否喜欢这种生活，她还不确定……"
"But now, safe in her own room, undressing for Alison’s monthly, she felt curious as to what she would have been feeling if things had gone as far as was proper according to the authorities.","此刻，她终于安全地呆在自己的房间里，为参加艾莉森的每月例会更衣。她很好奇，如果事情真发展到书上所写的肉欲程度，她又会作何感想呢。"
"Surely she had not experienced one-tenth of the thoughts or sensations that would have been assigned to her in any advanced piece of literature!","诚然，她体会到的感受还不及任何优秀的文学作品里描绘的十分之一！"
"It had been disillusioning, or else she was deficient, and Fleur, could not bear to feel deficient.","这就是幻想破灭，要不然，就是她还不完美，可弗勒无法容忍自己有任何欠缺。"
"And, lightly powdering her shoulders, she bent her thoughts towards Alison’s monthly.","然后，她轻轻在肩膀扑了些粉，便把思想集中到艾莉森的每月例会上了。"
"Though Lady Alison enjoyed an occasional encounter with the younger generation, the Aubrey Greenes and Linda Frewes of this life were not conspicuous by their presence at her gatherings.","尽管艾莉森夫人偶尔也喜欢和年轻人见见面，可像奥布里·格林和琳达·弗鲁这类人，却很少出现在她的聚会上。"
"Nesta Gorse, indeed, had once attended, but one legal and two literary politicos who had been in contact with her, had complained of it afterwards.","内丝塔·戈斯确实参加过一次，但是一个法律政客和两个文学政客同她接触后，都表示不满。"
"She had, it seemed, rent little spiked holes in the garments of their self-esteem.","她似乎伤了他们的自尊心。"
"Sibley Swan would have been welcome, for his championship of the past, but he seemed, so far, to have turned up his nose and looked down it.","大家倒是十分欢迎昔日的文坛巨匠西布莉·斯旺出席例会，可是，斯旺对此类聚会不屑一顾，不愿现身。"
"So it was not the intelligentsia, but just intellectual society, which was gathered there when Fleur and Michael entered, and the conversation had all the sparkle and all the ‘savoir faire’ incidental to talk about art and letters by those who—as Michael put it—“fortunately had not to faire”","当迈克尔和弗勒进去时，他们发现那里并不是知识分子的聚会，而是有知识的社交人物的聚会。这些人偶尔谈及文艺，却也显出些机敏和才华，只是正如迈克尔所说，他们幸亏是些“不干事的人”。"
"“All the same, these are the guys,” he muttered in Fleur’s ear, “who make the names of artists and writers.","“这些人全是捧场的。”他在弗勒耳边轻声低语，“就是他们这些人把艺术家和作家给捧起来的。"
"What’s the stunt, to-night?”","今晚的特别节目是什么？”"
"It appeared to be the London debut of a lady who sang Balkan folk songs.","原来有一位初登伦敦社交界的女士来唱巴尔干民歌。"
"But in a refuge to the right were four tables set out for bridge.","但是，右边的角落里摆着四张桥牌桌。"
"They were already filled.","桌边坐满了人。"
"Among those who still stood listening, were, here and there, a Gurdon Minho, a society painter and his wife, a sculptor looking for a job.","还有些人分散站在各处，继续听歌。这其中包括格登·明霍、一位社交界的画家和他的妻子，还有一位正在找工作的雕刻家。"
"Fleur, wedged between Lady Feynte, the painter’s wife, and Gurdon Minho himself, began planning an evasion.","弗勒正挤在那位画家的妻子芬特夫人和格登·明霍之间，设法脱身。"
"There—yes, there was Mr. Chalfont!","查尔方特先生也来了——就是他没错！"
"At Lady Alison’s, Fleur, an excellent judge of ‘milieu’ never wasted her time on artists and writers—she could meet THEM anywhere.","在艾莉森夫人的每月例会上，弗勒对社交环境极具判断力，她从来不在那些艺术家和作家身上浪费时间，因为这些人在随便什么地方都能碰到。"
"Here she intuitively picked out the biggest ‘bug,’ politico-literary, and waited to pin him.","在这里，她凭借直觉挑选出最重要的政界和文学界的名流，然后伺机盯住他们。"
"Absorbed in the idea of pinning Mr. Chalfont, she overlooked a piece of drama passing without.","她一心想盯住查尔方特先生，却忽视了外面发生的一出闹剧。"
"Michael had clung to the top of the stairway, in no mood for talk and skirmish; and, leaning against the balustrade, wasp-thin in his long white waistcoat, with hands deep thrust into his trousers’ pockets, he watched the turns and twists of Fleur’s white neck, and listened to the Balkan songs, with a sort of blankness in his brain.","迈克尔一直站在上面的楼梯口处，没有什么心情和旁人交谈或者争论，只是靠着栏杆站着，那件白色长马甲让他看上去瘦骨嶙峋。他双手深深地插在裤兜里，望着弗勒那雪白的脖子扭来扭去，听着巴尔干民歌，脑子里却一片空白。"
"The word: “Mont!” startled him.","一声“蒙特！”惊醒了他。"
"Wilfrid was standing just below.","威尔弗里德就站在他下面。"
"Mont?","蒙特？"
"He had not been that to Wilfrid for two years!","他有两年没听到威尔弗里德这样叫他了！"
"“Come down here.”","“下来。”"
"On that half-landing was a bust of Lionel Charwell, K.C., by Boris Strumolowski, in the genre he had cynically adopted when June Forsyte gave up supporting his authentic but unrewarded genius.","在楼梯中间的平台上，摆有一尊前王室法律顾问莱昂内尔·查韦尔的半身雕塑，这是鲍里斯·斯特拉莫洛斯基的作品。当琼·福赛特不再支持他创作那种反映现实却无利可图的作品后，他就玩世不恭地进入了这一艺术流派。"
"It had been almost indistinguishable from any of the other busts in that year’s Academy, and was used by the young Charwells to chalk moustaches on.","这尊塑像几乎同当年在皇家艺术学院里展出的其他作品没什么区别，现在却成了查韦尔家孩子们的玩具了，他们在上面乱画胡须。"
"Beside this object Desert leaned against the wall with his eyes closed.","德赛特站在这尊雕像旁，靠墙倚着，眼睛闭着。"
"His face was a study to Michael.","他的表情让迈克尔捉摸不透。"
"“What’s wrong, Wilfrid?”","“什么事，威尔弗里德？”"
"Desert did not move.","德赛特一动不动。"
"“You’ve got to know—I’m in love with Fleur.”","“我必须告诉你——我爱上弗勒了。”"
"“What!”","“你说什么？”"
"“I’m not going to play the snake.","“我不想偷偷摸摸。"
"You’re up against me.","我是你的情敌。"
"Sorry, but there it is!","很抱歉，可情况就是这样！"
"You can let fly!”","你尽管骂我吧！”"
"His face was death-pale, and its muscles twitched.","他脸色惨白，面部肌肉抽搐着。"
"In Michael, it was the mind, the heart that twitched.","听到这些话，迈克尔头脑混乱，心乱如麻。"
"What a very horrible, strange, “too beastly” moment!","这一刻太可怕、太诡异、“太让人恶心”了！"
"His best friend—his best man!","这就是他的最好朋友——他的伴郎！"
"Instinctively he dived for his cigarette case—instinctively handed it to Desert.","他下意识地掏出烟盒，又下意识地递给德赛特。"
"Instinctively they both took cigarettes, and lighted each other’s.","两人都不由自主地取出香烟，互相点着了。"
"Then Michael said:","然后，迈克尔说："
"“Fleur—knows?”","“弗勒——知道吗？”"
"Desert nodded: “She doesn’t know I’m telling you—wouldn’t have let me.","德赛特点点头，说道：“她不知道我会和你讲——她肯定不让我告诉你。"
"You’ve nothing against her—yet.”","她没有对不起你的地方——到目前为止。”"
"And, still with closed eyes, he added: “I couldn’t help it.”","然后，他继续闭着眼睛，又加了一句，“我可忍不住了。”"
"It was Michael’s own subconscious thought!","这正符合迈克尔的猜测！"
