"Fool not to see how natural!","傻瓜才看不出来这有多自然呢！"
"Then something shut-to within him, and he said: “Decent of you to tell me; but—aren’t you going to clear out?”","接着，他内心一阵疼痛，说：“你告诉我，还算个正人君子，但——你不觉得你现在应该马上离开吗？”"
"Desert’s shoulders writhed against the wall.","德赛特倚着墙，肩膀微动了一下。"
"“I thought so; but it seems not.”","“我之前也这样想，可现在我好像不想这样了。”"
"“Seems?","“好像是什么意思？"
"I don’t understand.”","我听糊涂了。”"
"“If I knew for certain I’d no chance—but I don’t,” and he suddenly looked at Michael: “Look here, it’s no good keeping gloves on.","“如果我知道我没有一点儿机会的话，我当然会离开——可我知道情况并非如此。”这时，他突然看着迈克尔，说道，“你看，咱们都别再伪装了。"
"I’m desperate, and I’ll take her from you if I can.”","我豁出去了，如果可行的话，我会从你身边抢走她。”"
"“Good God!” said Michael.","“上帝啊！”迈克尔说，"
"“It’s the limit!”","“太过分了！”"
"“Yes!","“好！"
"Rub it in!","你尽管嘀咕吧！"
"But, I tell you, when I think of you going home with her, and of myself,” he gave a dreadful little laugh, “I advise you NOT to rub it in.”","但是，我告诉你，当想到你和她一起回家，而我却孤独一人，”他发出一声可怕的笑声，“奉劝你还是别嘀咕的好。”"
"“Well,” said Michael, “as this isn’t a Dostoievsky novel, I suppose there’s no more to be said.”","“嗯，”迈克尔说道，“既然这不是陀思妥耶夫斯基的小说，我也没什么好说的了。”"
"Desert moved from the wall and laid his hand on the bust of Lionel Charwell.","德赛特离开墙壁，把手放在那尊莱昂内尔·查韦尔的半身塑像上。"
"“You realise, at least, that I’ve gone out of my way—perhaps dished myself—by telling you.","“至少，你应该知道我把事情告诉你，我已经无路可走了——也可能完全把路堵死了。"
"I’ve not bombed without declaring war.”","我向来不干不宣而战的事。”"
"“No,” said Michael dully.","“可不是。”迈克尔呆呆地说。"
"“You can chuck my books over to some other publisher.”","“你可以把我的书转给别的出版商。”"
"Michael shrugged.","迈克尔只是耸了耸肩。"
"“Good-night, then,” said Desert.","“那么，晚安。”德赛特说，"
"“Sorry for being so primitive.”","“很抱歉，失礼了。”"
"Michael looked straight into his ‘best man’s’ face.","迈克尔的目光直视着他的“伴郎”。"
"There was no mistaking its expression of bitter despair.","他的表情的确痛苦而绝望。"
"He made a half-movement with his hand, uttered half the word “Wilfrid,” and, as Desert went down, he went upstairs.","他做了半个手势，“威尔弗里德，”这几个字只说了一半，然后，德赛特下楼了，他就上楼了。"
"Back in his place against the balustrade, he tried to realise that life was a laughing matter, and couldn’t.","迈克尔继续回到原来的位子，倚在栏杆旁，努力让自己相信人生不过是场玩笑，可他做不到。"
"His position required a serpent’s cunning, a lion’s courage, a dove’s gentleness: he was not conscious of possessing such proverbial qualities.","他目前的处境需要像蛇一样狡猾、狮子一样的勇猛、鸽子一样的温柔，可是他知道自己并不具备这么高的品质。"
"If Fleur had loved him as he loved her, he would have had for Wilfrid a real compassion.","如果弗勒也能像他爱她那样深爱着他，他的确会同情威尔弗里德。"
"It was so natural to fall in love with Fleur!","爱上弗勒是再自然不过的事情！"
"But she didn’t—oh! no, she didn’t!","但是她不爱他——哦！不爱，她不爱他！"
"Michael had one virtue—if virtue it be—a moderate opinion of himself, a disposition to think highly of his friends.","迈克尔有个优点——如果这个算是优点的话——他对自己评价很谦虚，对朋友评价很高。"
"He had thought highly of Desert; and—odd!—he still did not think lowly of him.","他曾经对德赛特评价很高，而且——说来也怪！——一直到现在，他对德赛特的看法也还没有改变。"
"Here was his friend trying to do him mortal injury, to alienate the affection—more honestly, the toleration—of his wife; and yet he did not think him a cad.","他的这个朋友企图给他致命的一击，挑拨他们夫妻的感情——说得更明白点——煽动他妻子出轨，可他并不认为他是个无赖。"
"Such leniency, he knew, was hopeless; but the doctrines of free-will, and free contract, were not to him mere literary conceptions, they were part of his nature.","他知道这种宽宏大量是无济于事的。但是，对他而言，意志自由和婚姻自由的原则不只是文学上的概念，也是他天性的一部分。"
"To apply duress, however desirable, would not be on his cards.","无论强硬的办法多有用，都不符合他的原则。"
"And something like despair ravaged the heart of him, watching Fleur’s ingratiating little tricks with the great Gerald Chalfont.","当看着弗勒正对那个了不起的杰拉尔德·查尔方特施展一些小花招时，迈克尔的心被一种类似于绝望的情感蹂躏着。"
"If she left him for Wilfrid!","万一她离开他，去找威尔弗里德呢！"
"But surely—no—her father, her house, her dog, her friends, her—her collection of—of—she would not—could not give THEM up?","但是，肯定——不会——她的父亲、她的房子、她的狗、她的朋友，她——她的收藏——她不会——她无法放弃这些吧？"
"But suppose she kept everything, Wilfrid included!","可是她如果既要这些，也要威尔弗里德呢！"
"No, no!","不，不！"
"She wouldn’t!","她不会这样的！"
"Only for a second did that possibility blur the natural loyalty of his mind.","在他天性忠诚的头脑里，这种揣测只是一闪而过。"
"Well, what to do?","那么，怎么办呢？"
"Tell her—talk the thing out?","告诉她——把事情讲清楚？"
"Or wait and watch?","还是静观事态发展？"
"For what?","观望什么呢？"
"Without deliberate spying, he could not watch.","没有周密的监视，他就无从观察。"
"Desert would come to their house no more.","德赛特不会再来他们家了。"
"No!","不行！"
"Either complete frankness; or complete ignoring—and that meant living with the sword of Damocles above his head!","要么开诚布公地讲出来，要么假装什么也没发生——但这就意味着今后头上要悬着一把剑，像达摩克里斯那样生活！"
"No!","不行！"
"Complete frankness!","还是应该开诚布公地讲出来！"
"And not do anything that seemed like laying a trap!","不做背地里捣鬼的事情！"
"He passed his hand across a forehead that was wet.","他用手抹了下湿漉漉的额头。"
"If only they were at home, away from that squalling and these cultivated jackanapes!","他们要是在家里，远离这种嘈杂的世界和这些自命不凡的家伙，该有多好！"
"Could he go in and hook her out?","他能进去把她哄出来吗？"
"Impossible without some reason!","没有正当理由，肯定不行！"
"Only his brain-storm for a reason!","他努力思考，想找出个理由！"
"He must just bite on it.","他必须找个理由。"
"The singing ceased.","歌唱结束了。"
"Fleur was looking round.","弗勒在四处张望。"
"Now she would beckon!","现在，她可能要招呼他了！"
"On the contrary, she came towards him.","相反，弗勒朝他这边走了过来。"
"He could not help the cynical thought: ‘She’s hooked old Chalfont!’","他的脑子里不由得出现了一个恶意的想法：“她一定勾引了老查尔方特！”"
"He loved her, but he knew her little weaknesses.","他爱她，也了解她的小缺点。"
"She came up and took hold of his sleeve.","她走到他面前，拽住他的袖子。"
"“I’ve had enough, Michael, let’s slip off; d’you mind?”","“我玩够了，迈克尔，咱们撤吧，行吗？”"
"“Quick!” he said, “before they spot us!”","“赶快！”他说，“别让他们发现我们！”"
"In the cold air outside he thought: ‘Now?","走在寒冷的室外，他在想：“现在说吗？"
"Or in her room?’","还是回家再说？”"
"“I think,” said Fleur, “that Mr. Chalfont is overrated—he’s nothing but a mental yawn.","“我认为，”弗勒说，“人们对查尔方特先生的评价太高了——他只不过是个酸腐的文人。"
"He’s coming to lunch tomorrow week.”","他下周的明天会来吃午饭。”"
"Not now—in her room!","现在不说——回家再说！"
"“Whom do you think to meet him, besides Alison?”","“除了艾莉森，你还想请谁与他共进午餐呢？”"
"“Nothing jazzy.”","“爵士派的一个也不请。”"
"“Of course not; but it must be somebody intriguing, Michael.","“当然不请，但也必须请些有魅力的人，迈克尔。"
"Bother! sometimes I think it isn’t worth it.”","真讨厌！有时我觉得这么做真没劲。”"
"Michael’s heart stood still.","迈克尔的心差点儿就不跳了。"
"Was that a portent—sign of ‘the primitive’ rising within his adored practitioner of social arts?","这该不会是凶兆吧？难道他所崇拜的这位社会艺术实践家的心里萌生了原始情感了？"
"An hour ago he would have said:","如果是一小时以前，他会这么说："
"“You’re right, my child; it jolly well isn’t!”","“宝贝，你说得对，这么做确实没什么乐趣而言！”"
"But now—any sign of change was ominous!","可现在——任何变化都不是好兆头！"
"He slipped his arm in hers.","他挽住她的手臂。"
"“Don’t worry, we’ll snare the just-right cuckoos, somehow.”","“别担心，不管怎样，我们总会找到合适的人来。”"
"“A Chinese Minister would be perfect,” mused Fleur, “with Minho and Bart—four men—two women—cosy.","“要是有位中国公使就太好了。”弗勒沉思着，“加上明霍和准爵爷——四位男士，两位女士——刚刚好。"
"I’ll talk to Bart.”","我去和准爵爷说。”"
"Michael had opened their front door.","迈克尔打开他们家的前门。"
"She passed him; he lingered to see the stars, the plane trees, a man’s figure motionless, collared to the eyes, hatted down to them.","弗勒从他身边进去。他在外面徘徊了一会儿，望着天空中的点点繁星和一排排法国梧桐树。这时，他看到树边站着一个一动不动的人影，那人衣领遮到眼睛下面，用帽子盖住了眼睛。"
"‘Wilfrid!’ he thought: ‘Spain!","“威尔弗里德!”他想，“西班牙式的！"
"Why Spain?","为何是西班牙式的？"
"And all poor devils who are in distress—the heart—oh! darn the heart!’","所有挣扎着的可怜人——爱情——该死的爱情！”"
"He closed the door.","他关上了门。"
"But soon he had another to open, and never with less enthusiasm.","可是，随后他要打开另一扇窗，再没有比这更提不起劲的事了。"
"Fleur was sitting on the arm of a chair, in the dim lavender pyjamas she sometimes wore just to keep in with things, staring at the fire.","弗勒坐在椅子扶手上，凝望着壁炉。她身穿那件淡紫色的睡衣，有时她只是为了配合屋内的色调才穿这件睡衣。"
"Michael stood, looking at her and at his own reflection beyond in one of the five mirrors—white and black, the pierrot pyjamas she had bought him.","迈克尔站在那里，看看她，再看看其中一面墙镜中的自己——穿着她给买的那件黑白相间、丑角似的睡衣。"
"‘Figures in a play,’ he thought, ‘figures in a play!","“戏剧中的人物，”他想道，“戏剧中的人物！"
"Is it real?’","这一切是真的吗？”"
"He moved forward and sat on the chair’s other arm.","他走过去，坐在椅子另一边的扶手上。"
"“Hang it!” he muttered.","“该死！”他喃喃自语道，"
"“Wish I were Antinous!”","“我要是安提诺乌斯就好了！”"
"And he slipped from the arm into the chair, to be behind her face, if she wanted to hide it from him.","于是，他从扶手滑进椅子里，坐在她身后，万一她不想让自己看到她的脸呢。"
"“Wilfrid’s been telling me,” he said, quietly.","“威尔弗里德已经告诉我了。”他平静地说。"
"Off his chest!","总算把憋在心里的话说出来了！"
"What now?","现在是什么状况？"
"He saw the blood come flushing into her neck and cheek.","他看到弗勒的脖子和脸涨得通红。"
"“Oh!","“哦！"
"What business—how do you mean ‘telling you’?”","什么事——‘他告诉你’是什么意思？”"
"“Just that he’s in love with you—nothing more—there’s nothing more to tell, is there?”","“就是说他爱上你了——没说别的——没别的事可说了，是吗？”"
"And drawing his feet up on to the chair, he clasped his hands hard round his knees.","说着，他把脚缩到椅子里，用双手抱着膝盖。"
"Already—already he had asked a question!","他已经——已经问了一个问题了！"
"Bite on it!","稳住！"
"Bite on it!","稳住！"
"And he shut his eyes.","然后他闭上了眼睛。"
"“Of course,” said Fleur, very slowly, “there’s nothing more.","“当然。”弗勒慢条斯理地说，“当然没别的事了。"
"If Wilfrid chooses to be so silly.”","如果威尔弗里德愿意这样犯傻的话。”"
"Chooses!","愿意！"
"The word seemed unjust to one whose own ‘silliness’ was so recent—so enduring!","这个词听着这么接近“愚蠢”，似乎对一个如此执著于你的人很不公平！"
"And—curious! his heart wouldn’t bound.","而且——奇怪的是，他的心情并没因此而好起来。"
"Surely it ought to have bounded at her words!","听到这话，他本应该高兴起来的！"
"“Is that the end of Wilfrid, then?”","“那么，这就是威尔弗里德的结局了吗？”"
"“The end?","“结局?"
"I don’t know.”","我不清楚。”"
"Ah!","啊！"
"Who knew anything—when passion was about?","当激情奔放之时，谁知道会发生什么呢？"
"“Well,” he said, holding himself hard together, “don’t forget I love you awfully!”","“嗯。”他一边紧紧抱住自己，一边说，“别忘了我非常爱你！”"
"He saw her eyelids flicker, her shoulders shrugging.","他看到她眼睛眨了一下，肩膀耸了耸。"
"“Am I likely to?”","“我像是会忘记吗？”"
"Bitter, cordial, simple—which?","痛苦、热忱、简单——究竟是哪一种？"
"Suddenly her hands came round and took him by the ears.","突然间，她把双手伸过来，抓住他的耳朵。"
"Holding them fast she looked down at him, and laughed.","她一边紧紧捏住他的耳朵，一边低头向下看着他，哈哈一笑。"
"And again his heart WOULD not bound.","可是，他的心还是没有高兴起来。"
"If she did not lead him by the nose, she—!","如果她不是牵着他的鼻子走，她——！"
"But he clutched her to him in the chair.","但他还是一把把她搂进椅子里。"
"Lavender and white and black confused—she returned his kiss.","淡紫色和黑白相间的颜色混在一起——她回应着他的吻。"
"But from the heart?","可这是不是发自内心的？"
"Who knew?","谁知道？"
"Not Michael.","反正迈克尔不知道。"

"Chapter X","第十章"
"Passing of a Sportsman","一个运动家过世了"
"Soames, disappointed of his daughter, said: “I’ll wait,” and took his seat in the centre of the jade green settee, oblivious of Ting-a-ling before the fire, sleeping off the attentions of Amabel Nazing, who had found him ‘just too cunning.’","见女儿不在家，索姆斯有些失落，他说道：“我等等吧。”随后，他坐在那张翠绿色长椅的中间，全然没有注意到火炉前的小叮铃。此时，它正在打盹，将阿玛贝尔·内津的那句“太机灵”的恭维给忘到脑后去了。"
"Grey and composed, with one knee over the other, and a line between his eyes, he thought of Elderson and the condition of the world, and of how there was always something.","索姆斯头发灰白，神情自若。他跷起二郎腿，双目间蹙起一道皱纹。他心里想着埃尔德森、世界局势以及为何总有事情发生。"
"And the more he thought, the more he wondered why he had ever been such a flat as to go on to a Board which had anything to do with foreign contracts.","他越想就越觉得奇怪，自己怎么会傻到加入一个与外国有合同往来的董事会。"
"All the old wisdom that in the nineteenth century had consolidated British wealth, all the Forsyte philosophy of attending to one’s own business, and taking no risks, the close-fibred national individualism which refused to commit the country to chasing this wild goose or that, held within him silent demonstration.","所有为巩固英国财富做出贡献的19世纪的古老智慧、一切摒弃冒险主义、专注个人事业的福赛特哲学以及反对国家采取任何徒劳无益之举的民族利己主义精神，都在他心里静静翻腾着。"
"Britain was on the wrong tack politically to try and influence the Continent, and the P.P.R.S. on the wrong tack monetarily to insure business outside Britain.","就政治而言，英国企图影响欧洲大陆，这是犯了方针性错误；同样，就经济而言，天佑再保险公司扩展海外业务，也是犯了方针性错误。"
"The special instinct of his breed yearned for resumption of the straight and private path.","福赛特家的人都渴望延续有条不紊的个人发展道路。"
"Never meddle with what you couldn’t control!","千万别干自己无法控制的事情！"
"‘Old Mont’ had said: “Keep the ring!”","“老蒙特”曾说过：“保持中立！”"
"Nothing of the sort: Mind one’s own business!","根本没那么回事：管好自己的事！"
"That was the real ‘formula.’","这才是真正的“法则”。"
"He became conscious of his calf—Ting-a-ling was sniffing at his trousers.","他突然觉得小腿那里有什么东西在动——小叮铃正在闻他的裤子。"
"“Oh!” said Soames.","“哦！”索姆斯说，"
"“It’s you!”","“是你啊！”"
"Placing his forepaws against the settee, Ting-a-ling licked the air.","小叮铃吐着舌头，前爪搭在椅背上。"
"“Pick you up?” said Soames.","“要抱你起来吗？”索尔斯说，"
"“You’re too long.”","“你太大了。”"
"And again he felt that faint warmth of being liked.","他顿时有种被喜欢的感觉，丝丝暖意涌上了他的心头。"
"‘There’s something about me that appeals to him,’ he thought, taking him by the scruff and lifting him on to a cushion.","“我身上一定有什么吸引它的地方。”他一边想，一边抓着他的后颈，把它拎到坐垫上。"
"“You and I,” the little dog seemed saying with his stare—Chinese little object!","这小东西盯着他，似乎在说：“只有你和我。”——这条可爱的中国狗！"
"‘I shall resign,’ thought Soames.","“我应该辞职。”索姆斯想。"
"But what about Winifred, and Imogen, and some of the Rogers and Nicholases who had been putting money into this thing because he was a director?","可是，威妮弗雷德、伊莫金以及罗杰家族和尼古拉斯家族中的一些人怎么办？因为他当董事，这些人才把资金投进来的。"
"He wished they wouldn’t follow him like a lot of sheep!","他希望他们可别像一群羊似的跟在他后面。"
"He rose from the settee.","他从长椅上站起来。"
"It was no good waiting, he would walk on to Green Street and talk to Winifred at once.","没什么好等的了，他得马上去格林街找威妮弗雷德谈谈。"
"She would have to sell again, though the shares had dropped a bit.","尽管股票已经跌了一点儿，她必须再次抛出。"
"And without taking leave of Ting-a-ling, he went out.","然后，没与小叮铃告别，他就出去了。"
"All this last year he had almost enjoyed life.","去年整整一年，他都在享受人生。"
"Having somewhere to come and sit and receive a certain sympathy once at least a week, as in old days at Timothy’s, was of incalculable advantage to his spirit.","他会去某个地方走走、坐坐，总能收获某种安慰，至少一周一次。就像从前在蒂莫西家一样，这对他保持良好的精神状态大有益处。"
"In going from home Fleur had taken most of his heart with her; but Soames had found it almost an advantage to visit his heart once a week rather than to have it always about.","弗勒的出嫁，让他感觉心里空落落的。可是索姆斯发现，每周看一次心肝宝贝，要比她总在自己身边更好些。"
"There were other reasons conducing to light-heartedness.","还有一些其他事情也让他感觉很轻松。"
"That diabolical foreign chap, Prosper Profond, had long been gone he didn’t know where, and his wife had been decidedly less restive and sarcastic ever since.","那个可恶的外国佬——普罗斯珀·普罗芳——早就不知跑到什么地方去了。自那以后，他的妻子明显比以前安分多了，也很少嘲笑别人了。"
"She had taken up a thing they called Coue, and grown stouter.","她迷上了一种叫做“库埃”的东西，身体变得结实起来。"
"She used the car a great deal.","她经常开车。"
"Altogether she was more domestic.","总之，她比以前更爱呆在家里了。"
"Then, too, he had become reconciled to Gauguin—a little slump in that painter had convinced him that he was still worth attention, and he had bought three more.","之后，他和画家高更和解了。高更的画作市价稍有下跌，但索姆斯认为他的作品依然值得关注，所以他又买了3幅。"
"Gauguin would rise again!","高更的画会再次升值！"
"Soames almost regretted his intuition of that second coming, for he had quite taken to the chap.","索姆斯对自己追逐涨价的念头感到遗憾，自己欣赏他就可以了。"
"His colour, once you got used to it, was very attractive.","他画中的色彩，你一旦看习惯了，就非常具有吸引力。"
"One picture, especially, which meant nothing so far as he could see, had a way of making you keep your eyes on it.","特别是有一幅画，高更自己认为没什么，但却有一种让人流连其中的感觉。"
"He even felt uneasy when he thought of having to part with the thing at an enhanced price.","当索姆斯想到价格一涨他就得转手时，心里挺不是滋味的。"
"But, most of all, he had been feeling so well, enjoying a recrudescence of youth in regard to Annette, taking more pleasure in what he ate, while his mind dwelt almost complacently on the state of money.","但最重要的是，索姆斯一直感觉很好，安妮特给他带来了重返青春般的乐趣，食物也给他带来了极大的快乐，他全心享受着金钱带来的满足感。"
"The pound going up in value; Labour quiet!","英镑升值了；工党很安静！"
"And now they had got rid of that Jack-o’-lantern, they might look for some years of solid Conservative administration.","现在劳合·乔治下台了，保守党即将稳稳地掌几年权了。"
"And to think, as he did, stepping across St. James’ Park towards Green Street, that he had gone and put his foot into a concern which he could not control, made him feel—well, as if the devil had been in it!","他一边穿过圣詹姆斯公园，朝格林街的方向走去，一边在想，他怎么会涉足一个自己无法掌控的公司——唉，真是见鬼了！"
"In Piccadilly he moused along on the Park side, taking his customary look up at the ‘Iseeum’ Club.","在皮卡迪利大街，他沿着公园一边蹑手蹑脚地向前走，习惯性地瞧一眼“伊昔姆”俱乐部。"
"The curtains were drawn, and chinks of light glowed, long and cosy.","俱乐部拉着窗帘，帘缝间透出狭长而舒缓的灯光。"
"And that reminded him—some one had said George Forsyte was ill.","这时，他想起——有人说乔治·福赛特病了。"
"Certainly he had not seen him in the bay window for months past.","是啊，他有几个月没见到他坐在这里的飘窗边了。"
"Well, George had always eaten and drunk too much.","唉，乔治总是能吃能喝。"
"He crossed over and passed beneath the Club; and a sudden feeling—he didn’t know what—a longing for his own past, a sort of nostalgia—made him stop and mount the steps.","他穿过马路，朝俱乐部下面走去。他突然很怀念过去，自己也莫名其妙，像是患上思乡病了——他不由地停住脚步，登上俱乐部的台阶。"
"“Mr. George Forsyte in the Club?”","“乔治·福赛特在俱乐部里吗？”"
"The janitor stared, a grey-haired, long-faced chap, whom he had known from away back in the ‘eighties.","头发灰白的长脸门卫瞪着他看。索姆斯早在上世纪80年代就见过他了。"
"“Mr. Forsyte, sir,” he said, “is very ill indeed.","他说：“先生，福赛特先生的确病得很重。"
"They say he won’t recover, sir.”","他们都说他的病不会好了。”"
"“What?” said Soames.","“什么？”索姆斯说，"
"“Nobody told me that.”","“没人和我提过啊。”"
"“He’s very bad—VERY bad indeed.","“他病得很重——的确很严重。"
"It’s the heart.”","是心脏病。”"
"“The heart!","“心脏病！"
"Where is he?”","他在哪儿？”"
"“At his rooms, sir; just round the corner.","“在他家，先生。转过那个拐角就是了。"
"They say the doctors have given him up.","他们都说，医生已经宣布放弃了。"
"He WILL be missed here.","俱乐部的人都会想念他。"
"Forty years I’ve known him.","我认识他40年了。"
"One of the old school, and a wonderful judge of wine and horses.","他是老派人，一名了不起的品酒师和评马师。"
"We none of us last for ever, they say, but I never thought to see HIM out.","人们常说，没有人会永远活着，可是我从来没想过会看到他离开。"
"Bit too full-blooded, sir, and that’s a fact.”","因为他一直精力非常旺盛，先生，可这就是事实。”"
"With a slight shock Soames realised that he had never known where George lived, so utterly anchored had he seemed to that bay window above.","索姆斯微微一惊，他竟然不知道乔治住在哪里，他一直以为他就安居在俱乐部上面的飘窗旁。"
"“Just give me the number of his rooms,” he said.","“请把他寓所的门牌号告诉我。”他说。"
"“Belville Row—No. 11, sir; I’m sure I hope you’ll find him better.","“贝尔维尔街11号，先生。我真希望您能看到他好一些。"
"I shall miss his jokes—I shall, indeed.”","我真想听他讲笑话——真的很想听。”"
"Turning the corner into Belville Row, Soames made a rapid calculation.","转过街角，进入贝尔维尔街，索姆斯快速地算了一下。"
"George was sixty-six, only one year younger than himself!","乔治今年66岁，只比他小一岁！"
"If George was really in extremis it would be quite unnatural!","如果乔治真的快不行了，那太不合常理了！"
"‘Comes of not leading a careful life,’ he thought; ‘always rackety—George!","“是生活不节制的结果。”他想，“乔治总是寻欢作乐！"
"When was it I made his will?’","我什么时候给他立的遗嘱来着？”"
"So far as he remembered, George had left his money to his brothers and sisters—no one else to leave it to.","就他所知，乔治把钱都留给兄弟姐妹了——他也没别人可给了。"
"The feeling of kinship stirred in Soames, the instinct of family adjustment.","骨肉亲情在索姆斯心里激荡着，这是一种家人的本能。"
"George and he had never got on—opposite poles of temperament—still he would have to be buried, and who would see to it if not Soames, who had seen to so many Forsyte burials in his time?","乔治和他向来不和——两人性格相反——可是总得为他料理后事啊，除了索姆斯，谁会做这些事呢？他一生中不是已经料理过那么多福赛特家的丧事了吗？"
"He recalled the nickname George had once given him, ‘the undertaker!’","他想起乔治曾给他起过一个绰号——“殡仪事务承办人”！"
"H’m!","哼！"
"Here was poetical justice!","这是因果报应！"
"Belville Row!","贝尔维尔街！"
"Ah!"
"No. 11—regular bachelor-looking place!","11号——真像是单身汉的住所！"
"And putting his hand up to the bell, he thought: ‘Women!’","他一边按门铃，一边在想：“女人们！”"
"What had George done about women all his life?","乔治一生在女人方面做了些什么？"
"His ring was answered by a man in a black cut-away coat with a certain speechless reticence.","一个男子出来开门，他身着黑色燕尾服，十分沉默。"
"“My cousin, Mr. George Forsyte?","“我堂弟乔治·福赛特先生呢？"
"How is he?”","他怎么样？”"
"The man compressed his lips.","那人抿了抿嘴唇，说："
"“Not expected to last the night, sir.”","“恐怕过不了今晚了，先生。”"
"Soames felt a little clutch beneath his Jaeger vest.","索姆斯感觉自己的心好像被人抓了一把。"
"“Conscious?”","“神志清醒吗？”"
"“Yes, sir.”","“清醒，先生。”"
"“Could you show him my card?","“你能把我的名片给他看看吗？"
"He might possibly like to see me.”","也许他会想见我。”"
"“Will you wait in here, sir?”","“先生，您能在这儿稍等一会儿吗？”"
"Soames passed into a low room panelled up to the level of a man’s chest, and above that line decorated with prints.","索姆斯走进一间低矮的房间。那房间的护墙板镶到齐胸那么高，板线以上挂着一幅幅版画。"
"George—a collector!","乔治是个收藏家！"
"Soames had never supposed he had it in him!","索姆斯从来没想过他还有这个爱好！"
"On those walls, wherever the eye roved, were prints coloured and uncoloured, old and new, depicting the sports of racing and prize-fighting!","放眼望去，四面墙壁上既有色彩画也有黑白画，既有旧画也有新作。画的是赛马运动和职业拳击运动。"
"Hardly an inch of the red wall space visible!","整个红色墙壁上，几乎没有一处是空的！"
"About to examine them for marks of value, Soames saw that he was not alone.","正当索姆斯想仔细看看标价时，他发现房间里不只他一个人。"
"A woman—age uncertain in the shaded light—was sitting in a very high-backed chair before the fire with her elbow on the arm of it, and a handkerchief held to her face.","一位女子正坐在火炉前面一张靠背很高的椅子里。由于灯光微弱，他看不出她的年龄。她一只手撑在椅子的扶手上，一只手拿手帕贴着脸。"
"Soames looked at her, and his nostrils moved in a stealthy sniff.","索姆斯看着她，偷偷地抽了一下鼻子。"
"‘Not a lady,’ he thought.","“肯定不是女主人。”他想，"
"‘Ten to one but there’ll be complications.’","“十之八九有什么关系。”"
"The muffled voice of the cut-away man said:","这时，那个穿礼服的男子低声说："
"“I’m to take you in, sir.”","“我带您进去，先生。”"
"Soames passed his hand over his face and followed.","索姆斯抹了一把脸，跟在后面。"
"The bedroom he now entered was in curious contrast.","他现在走进的卧室和刚才那间形成了鲜明的对比。"
"The whole of one wall was occupied by an immense piece of furniture, all cupboards and drawers.","一个大柜占据了整整一面墙，柜上只有碗厨和抽屉。"
"Otherwise there was nothing in the room but a dressing-table with silver accoutrements, an electric radiator alight in the fireplace, and a bed opposite.","此外，房间里只有一个摆着银制品的梳妆台、一个放在壁炉里的、开着的电暖炉，还有对面的一张床。"
"Over the fireplace was a single picture, at which Soames glanced mechanically.","壁炉上只有一幅画，索姆斯有意无意地瞥了一眼。"
"What!","什么？"
"Chinese!","中国画！"
"A large whitish sidelong monkey, holding the rind of a squeezed fruit in its outstretched paw.","画中有一只侧坐着的白毛猴子，伸出一只爪子捏着一块挤碎的水果皮。"
"Its whiskered face looked back at him with brown, almost human eyes.","猴子的脸上带着胡须，正用它那棕褐色的、类似于人类的眼睛回头望着。"
"What on earth had made his inartistic cousin buy a thing like that and put it up to face his bed?","他这位不懂艺术的堂弟，为什么会买这件东西，还挂在正对着床的位置？"
"He turned and looked at the bed’s occupant.","他转身看了看床上躺着的病人。"
"“The only sportsman of the lot,” as Montague Dartie in his prime had called him, lay with his swollen form outlined beneath a thin quilt.","蒙塔古·达尔蒂这样称赞过当时正值盛年的他：“他是这群人里唯一的运动健将。”而今，他却只能盖着薄被躺在那里，浮肿的身体在薄被下显现出来。"
"It gave Soames quite a turn to see that familiar beef-coloured face pale and puffy as a moon, with dark corrugated circles round eyes which still had their japing stare.","那张熟悉的牛肉色的脸变得像月亮一般苍白且浮肿。那双眼睛依稀带着嘲弄人的眼神，却已是皱纹密布、黑圈重重。这一切让索姆斯大吃一惊。"
"A voice, hoarse and subdued, but with the old Forsyte timbre, said:","这时，床上传来一个声音，嘶哑而低沉，仍旧带有老福赛特家的特质，说道："
"“Hallo, Soames!","“你好，索姆斯！"
"Come to measure me for my coffin?”","你来给我量棺材尺寸吗？”"
"Soames put the suggestion away with a movement of his hand; he felt queer looking at that travesty of George.","索姆斯摆了摆手，让这句话过去了。看着乔治硬装出滑稽的神情，他心里很不是滋味。"
"They had never got on, but—!","他们一直合不来，但是——！"
"And in his flat, unemotional voice he said:","他平缓而不动声色地说道："
"“Well, George!","“好了，乔治！"
"You’ll pick up yet.","你会好起来的。"
"You’re no age.","你还没老呢。"
"Is there anything I can do for you?”","我能为你做些什么吗？”"
"A grin twitched George’s pallid lips.","乔治苍白的嘴唇挤出一丝笑容。"
"“Make me a codicil.","“给我立份遗嘱附录。"
"You’ll find paper in the dressing table drawer.”","梳妆台的抽屉里有纸。”"
"Soames took out a sheet of ‘Iseeum’ Club notepaper.","索姆斯取出一张“伊昔姆”俱乐部的信纸。"
"Standing at the table, he inscribed the opening words of a codicil with his stylographic pen, and looked round at George.","他站在桌边，用尖头钢笔把遗嘱附录的开头写好，然后回头望着乔治。"
"The words came with a hoarse relish.","乔治的声音虽然嘶哑，却独具吸引力。"
"“My three screws to young Val Dartie, because he’s the only Forsyte that knows a horse from a donkey.”","“我那3匹老马给小瓦尔·达尔蒂，因为他是福赛特家族里唯一懂得区分马和驴的人。”"
"A throaty chuckle sounded ghastly in the ears of Soames.","他发出一阵沙哑而低沉的笑声，在索姆斯听来很是瘆人。"
"“What have you said?”","“你是怎么写的？”"
"Soames read: “I hereby leave my three racehorses to my kinsman, Valerius Dartie, of Wansdon, Sussex, because he has special knowledge of horses.”","索姆斯读道：“兹将我3匹赛马赠予我的亲戚瓦勒列斯·达尔蒂，萨塞克斯郡沃斯顿人，因他深谙识马之术。”"
"Again the throaty chuckle.","又一阵沙哑低沉的笑声。"
"“You’re a dry file, Soames.","“你真是一个冷冰冰的家伙，索姆斯。"
"Go on.","继续。"
"To Milly Moyle, of 12, Claremont Grove, twelve thousand pounds, free of legacy duty.”","给住在克莱尔蒙特林荫街12号的米利·莫伊尔12，000镑，免付遗产税。”"
"Soames paused on the verge of a whistle.","索姆斯差点儿停下来吹口哨。"
"The woman in the next room!","就是隔壁房间里的那个女人！"
"The japing in George’s eyes had turned to brooding gloom.","乔治那捉弄人的眼神变得阴郁忧愁起来。"
"“It’s a lot of money,” Soames could not help saying.","索姆斯禁不住说了一句：“这是一大笔钱啊。”"
"George made a faint choleric sound.","乔治病弱的声音显得很生气。"
"“Write it down, or I’ll leave her the lot.”","“照这样写，否则我全都留给她。”"
"Soames wrote.","索姆斯写下了。"
"“Is that all?”","“就这些吗？”"
"“Yes.","“是的。"
"Read it!”","念一下！”"
"Soames read.","索姆斯念了。"
"Again he heard that throaty chuckle.","他又听到一阵低沉而嘶哑的笑声。"
"“That’s a pill.","“这是一桩自作自受的事。"
"You won’t let THAT into the papers.","你可别把这句也写进遗嘱里。"
"Get that chap in, and you and he can witness.”","叫那家伙进来，就由你俩做见证人吧。”"
"Before Soames reached the door, it was opened and the man himself came in.","还没等索姆斯开门，门就开了，那个男子走了进来。"
"“The—er—vicar, sir,” he said in a deprecating voice, “has called.","“先生，那位——嗯——牧师来了。”他语气轻蔑地说，"
"He wants to know if you would like to see him.”","“您愿意见他吗？”"
"George turned his face, his fleshy grey eyes rolled.","乔治回过头，灰色的大眼睛转来转去。"
"“Give him my compliments,” he said, “and say I’ll see him at the funeral.”","“替我问候他。”他说，“告诉他，我们葬礼上见。”"
"With a bow the man went out, and there was silence.","男子鞠了一躬，出去了，屋里一片寂静。"
"“Now,” said George, “get him in again.","乔治说：“现在，把他叫进来。"
"I don’t know when the flag’ll fall.”","我不知道什么时候就走了。”"
"Soames beckoned the man in.","于是索姆斯招呼那人进来。"
"When the codicil was signed and the man gone, George spoke:","当遗嘱附录签好字，男子出去了以后，乔治说道："
"“Take it, and see she gets it.","“遗嘱附录放你那里，务必确保她拿到这笔钱。"
"I can trust you, that’s one thing about you, Soames.”","我相信你，索姆斯，你就是这一点好。”"
"Soames pocketed the codicil with a very queer sensation.","索姆斯把遗嘱附录放进口袋里，心里很不是滋味。"
"“Would you like to see her again?” he said.","“你想再见见她吗？”他说。"
"George stared up at him a long time before he answered.","乔治抬头看着他，过了很久才回答："
"“No. What’s the good?","“不必了。有什么用呢？"
"Give me a cigar from that drawer.”","抽屉里有雪茄，递给我一支吧。”"
"Soames opened the drawer.","索姆斯打开抽屉。"
"“Ought you?” he said.","“你可以抽烟吗？”他说。"
"George grinned.","乔治咧嘴笑了笑。"
"“Never in my life done what I ought; not going to begin now.","“我平生没做过什么该做的事，现在也不打算做。"
"Cut it for me.”","帮我把烟头剪掉吧。”"
"Soames nipped the end of the cigar.","索姆斯剪掉烟头。"
"‘Shan’t give him a match,’ he thought.","他心想：“不能给他火柴。"
"‘Can’t take the responsibility.’","我可负不起这个责任啊。”"
"But George did not ask for a match.","可是乔治没朝他要火柴。"
"He lay quite still, the unlighted cigar between his pale lips, the curved lids down over his eyes.","他静静地躺着，苍白的嘴唇含着那支没有点着的雪茄，眼睑弯成了一道弧形。"
"“Good-bye,” he said, “I’m going to have a snooze.”","“再见。”他说，“我要打个盹。”"
"“Good-bye,” said Soames.","“再见。”索姆斯说，"
"“I—I hope—you—you’ll soon—”","“我——我希望——你——你很快就——”"
"George reopened his eyes—fixed, sad, jesting, they seemed to quench the shams of hope and consolation.","乔治又睁开那双眼睛——眼神定定的，忧伤而戏谑，它们似乎把希望和慰藉一扫而光。"
"Soames turned hastily and went out.","索姆斯急忙转身离开了。"
"He felt bad, and almost unconsciously turned again into the sitting-room.","他感到很不舒服，不知不觉走进了刚才那间起居室。"
"The woman was still in the same attitude; the same florid scent was in the air.","那个女人依然那个姿势坐着；空气里依旧弥漫着浓重的香气。"
"Soames took up the umbrella he had left there, and went out.","索姆斯拿起留在那里的雨伞，走了出去。"
"“This is my telephone number,” he said to the servant waiting in the corridor; “let me know.”","“这是我的电话号码。”他对等在走廊里的仆人说，“有事通知我。”"
"The man bowed.","那个男子鞠了一躬。"
"Soames turned out of Belville Row.","索姆斯走出贝尔维尔街。"
"Never had he left George’s presence without the sense of being laughed at.","每次与乔治分手，总是有种被嘲笑的感觉。"
"Had he been laughed at now?","今天又被他嘲笑了吗？"
"Was that codicil George’s last joke?","那个遗嘱附录是他开的最后一次玩笑吗？"
"If he had not gone in this afternoon, would George ever have made it, leaving a third of his property away from his family to that florid woman in the high-backed chair?","如果今天下午他没去，乔治还会立遗嘱附录吗？把1/3的遗产留给那个高背椅子里坐着的香艳女子，而不是留给家人？"
"Soames was beset by a sense of mystery.","索姆斯越想越觉得奇怪。"
"How could a man joke at death’s door?","一个将死之人还会开玩笑吗？"
"It was, in a way, heroic.","从某种程度上说，这也算是英雄所为吧。"
"Where would he be buried?","他会葬在哪里呢？"
"Somebody would know—Francie or Eustace.","总会有人安排的——弗朗西或是尤斯塔斯。"
"And what would they think when they came to know about that woman in the chair—twelve thousand pounds!","而当他们最终得知那个坐在椅子里的女人得到12，000镑，他们会作何感想呢!"
"‘If I can get hold of that white monkey, I will,’ he thought suddenly.","“如果能得到那幅白猿，我一定要搞到手。”他突然想到，"
"‘It’s a good thing.’","“那是件好东西。”"
"The monkey’s eyes, the squeezed-out fruit—was life all a bitter jest and George deeper than himself?","那只白猿的眼睛，那个干瘪的水果——人的一生就是一个布满心酸的玩笑吗？乔治真的比我更深刻吗？"
"He rang the Green Street bell.","他按响了格林街的门铃。"
"Mrs. Dartie was very sorry, but Mrs. Cardigan had called for her to dine and make a fourth at the play.","达尔蒂夫人表示很抱歉，因为卡迪盖夫人刚请她去一起吃晚饭，而且牌戏四缺一，她会去凑个局。"
"Soames went in to dinner alone.","索姆斯独自一人吃晚饭。"
"At the polished board below which Montague Dartie had now and again slipped, if not quite slept, he dined and brooded.","他坐在那张擦得锃亮的餐桌旁，边吃边想。每到吃饭的时候，蒙塔古·达尔蒂不是在楼下睡觉，就是悄悄地溜出去了。"
"“I can trust you, that’s one thing about you, Soames.”","“我相信你，索姆斯，你就是这一点好。”"
"The words flattered and yet stung him.","这话听着很舒服，同时也刺痛了他。"
"The depths of that sardonic joke!","那个讥讽的玩笑开得多深刻啊！"
"To give him a family shock and trust him to carry the shock out!","这会是一件震惊家族的事件，而且他还受托执行此事！"
"George had never cared twelve thousand pounds for a woman who smelled of patchouli.","乔治居然在一个浑身散发着薄荷香气的女人身上花了12，000镑。"
"No!","不！"
"It was a final gibe at his family, the Forsytes, at Soames himself!","这是对福赛特家族以及索姆斯本人的最后一次嘲弄！"
"Well! one by one those who had injured or gibed at him—Irene, Bosinney, old and young Jolyon, and now George, had met their fates.","哼！曾经伤害或嘲笑过他的人——艾琳、波辛尼、老乔利恩和小乔利恩以及现在的乔治，一个个都完蛋了。"
"Dead, dying, or in British Columbia!","去世的、快要去世的，或是在英属哥伦比亚的！"
"He saw again his cousin’s eyes above that unlighted cigar, fixed, sad, jesting—poor devil!","他仿佛又看见了他堂弟的眼睛，那双在未点着的雪茄上方的定定的、忧郁的、戏弄人的眼睛——可怜的家伙！"
"He got up from the table, and nervously drew aside the curtains.","他站起身来，惴惴不安地拉开窗帘。"
"The night was fine and cold.","夜色美好却寒冷。"
"What happened to one—after?","人死后会怎样呢？"
"George used to say that he had been Charles the Second’s cook in a former existence!","乔治过去经常说他自己前世是查理二世的厨师！"
"But reincarnation was all nonsense, weak-minded theorising!","可是灵魂再生说全是胡说，是无稽之谈！"
"Still, one would be glad to hold on if one could, after one was gone.","不过，如果人去世后能继续存在的话，人们是很乐意继续存在的。"
"Hold on, and be near Fleur!","继续存在，在弗勒身边！"
"What noise was that?","那是什么声音？"
"Gramophone going in the kitchen!","厨房里开着留声机！"
"When the cat was away, the mice—!","猫不在家，老鼠就嚣张——！"
"People were all alike—take what they could get, and give as little as they could for it.","人都一样——尽其所能去得到，付出的越少越好。"
"Well! he would smoke a cigarette.","好吧！他想吸根烟。"
"Lighting it at a candle—Winifred dined by candle-light, it was the ‘mode’ again—he thought: ‘Has he still got that cigar between his teeth?’","他借着蜡烛点着了香烟——威妮弗雷德喜欢在烛光下吃饭，这又是一种“时尚”——他又想到：“他嘴里还含着那根雪茄吗？”"
"A funny fellow, George—all his days a funny fellow!","乔治，滑稽的家伙——一生都这样滑稽！"
"He watched a ring of smoke he had made without intending to—very blue, he never inhaled!","他看着一个无意形成的烟圈——颜色很蓝，他从不把烟吸进去！"
"Yes!","没错！"
"George had lived too fast, or he would not have been dying twenty years before his lime—too fast!","乔治活得太放荡了，否则他一定可以再多活20年——太放荡了！"
"Well, there it was, and he wished he had a cat to talk to!","嗯，它在那里，他正希望有只猫能陪他聊聊天！"
"He took a little monster off the mantelboard.","他从壁炉上拿下一只小怪物。"
"Picked up by his nephew Benedict in an Eastern bazaar the year after the War, it had green eyes—’Not emeralds,’ thought Soames, ‘some cheap stone!’","这是战后那年，他的外甥贝内迪克特在一个东方市场上买的。它有一双绿眼睛——“不是祖母绿，”索姆斯想，“就是块不值钱的石头！”"
"“The telephone for you, sir.”","“先生，您的电话。”"
"He went into the hall and took up the receiver.","他进入门厅，拿起听筒。"
"“Yes?”","“喂？”"
"“Mr. Forsyte has passed away, sir—in his sleep, the doctor says.”","“福赛特先生去世了，先生——医生说他是在睡梦中走的。”"
"“Oh!” said Soames: “Had he a cig—?","“哦！”索姆斯说，“他嘴里有没有一支雪——？"
"Many thanks.”","非常感谢。”"
"He hung up the receiver.","他挂断了电话。"
"Passed away!","去世了！"
"And, with a nervous movement, he felt for the codicil in his breast pocket.","于是，他心神不安地摸了摸胸口衣袋里的那封遗嘱附录。"

"Chapter XI","第十一章"
"Venture","冒险"
"For a week Bicket had seen ‘the job,’ slippery as an eel, evasive as a swallow, for ever passing out of reach.","一周来，比克特眼睁睁地瞅着“他要找的工作”像鳗鱼一样从他面前溜走，又像燕子一样从他面前翩翩飞过，永远可望而不可即。"
"A pound for keep, and three shillings invested on a horse, and he was down to twenty-four bob.","在这7天时间里，他花了一英镑维持生计，3个先令赌马，就剩下24先令了。"
"The weather had turned sou’-westerly and Victorine had gone out for the first time.","外面刮的已经是西南风了，并且维多琳也已经出了一次门了。"
"That was something off his mind, but the cramp of the unemployed sensation, that fearful craving for the means of mere existence, a protesting, agonising anxiety, was biting into the very flesh of his spirit.","这两件事使他放心了些，但是失业的感觉紧紧地束缚着他，单纯只是想活下去的渴望强烈得令人害怕，还有一种由于发自内心的抗争而产生的焦虑正折磨着他，啃噬着他的脑细胞。"
"If he didn’t get a job within a week or two, there would be nothing for it but the workhouse, or the gas.","如果一周或是两周之内他还找不到工作，那就只能去济贫院或是开煤气自杀了。"
"‘The gas,’ thought Bicket, ‘if she will, I will.","“煤气，”比克特想道，“要是她愿意的话，我也没问题。"
"I’m fed up.","我已经受够了。"
"After all, what is it?","毕竟，也没什么大不了的。"
"In her arms I wouldn’t mind.’","要是能死在她的怀里，我死而无憾。”"
"Instinct, however, that it was not so easy as all that to put one’s head under the gas, gave him a brainwave that Monday night.","然而，他本能地觉得把脑袋放在煤气灶下不是那么容易，于是在周一的晚上他脑中闪过一丝灵光。"
"Balloons—that chap in Oxford Street today!","气球——今天在牛津街看到的那个卖气球的家伙！"
"Why not?","为什么不呢？"
"He still had the capital for a flutter in them, and no hawker’s licence needed.","小赌一把的资本他还是有的，而且卖气球也不需要申请小贩许可证。"
"His brain, working like a squirrel in the small hours, grasped the great, the incalculable advantage of coloured balloons over all other forms of commerce.","后半夜，他的大脑像松鼠一样活跃，想的全都是卖彩色气球能获得的极大的、无法估量的好处，这些好处是其他生意比不了的。"
"You couldn’t miss the man who sold them—there he was for every eye to see, with his many radiant circumferences dangling in front of him!","你肯定不会错过那卖气球的人的——他就在那里，谁都能看得到，面前飘荡着许多颜色亮丽的气球！"
"Not much profit in them, he had gathered—a penny on a sixpenny globe of coloured air, a penny on every three small twopenny globes; still their salesman was alive, and probably had pitched him a poor tale for fear of making his profession seem too attractive.","利润不会太高，他已经算过了——一个六便士的彩色气球可以赚一个便士，三个两便士的小气球也能赚一个便士。可是卖气球的人还活着，也许他还会给别人讲述他的悲惨故事，以免让人眼红他的生意。"
"Over the Bridge, just where the traffic—no, up by St. Paul’s!","是站在桥上，还是在交通要道上——不，还是上圣保罗教堂去！"
"He knew a passage where he could stand back a yard or two, like that chap in Oxford Street!","他知道那里有一条小路，可以让他退后一两码，就像那个站在牛津街的家伙那样！"
"But to the girl sleeping beside him he said nothing.","但是，对睡在他身边的妻子，他什么也没说。"
"No word to her till he had thrown the die.","等事情有眉目了再告诉她。"
"It meant gambling with his last penny.","这意味着拿最后一点儿小钱去赌一把。"
"For a bare living he would have to sell—why, three dozen big and four dozen small balloons a day would only be twenty-six shillings a week profit, unless that chap was kidding.","为了能够活下去，他每天得卖掉——3打大气球和4打小气球，一周也就赚26先令，除非那个卖气球的家伙骗他。"
"Not much towards ‘Austrylia’ out of that!","靠这些钱是去不了“澳大利亚”的！"
"And not a career—Victorine would have a shock!","再说，这也算不上是一种职业——维多琳会大吃一惊的！"
"But it was neck or nothing now—he must try it, and in off hours go on looking for a job.","但是现在成败在此一举——他必须试试，然后利用空余时间继续找工作。"
"Our thin capitalist, then, with four dozen big and seven dozen small on a tray, two shillings in his pocket, and little in his stomach, took his stand off St. Paul’s at two o’clock next day.","于是，在第二天下午2点的时候，我们这位体格单薄的资本家，带着一个盛着4打大气球和7打小气球的盘子，站在了圣保罗教堂外面。他的肚子里空空如也，口袋里只剩下两先令。"
"Slowly he blew up and tied the necks of two large and three small, magenta, green and blue, till they dangled before him.","他慢慢地吹起两个大气球和三个小气球，把气球口扎紧了，让这些紫红色、绿色和蓝色的气球在自己面前飘荡。"
"Then with the smell of rubber in his nostrils, and protruding eyes, he stood back on the kerb and watched the stream go by.","然后，他满嘴都是橡胶的味道，两眼突出，靠后站在人行道边石上，瞅着川流不息的过往人群。"
"It gratified him to see that most people turned to look at him.","看到大多数路人都会转身看看自己，他感到很是满意。"
"But the first person to address him was a policeman, with:","但是，第一个和他说话的却是一个警察，他说："
"“I’m not sure you can stand there.”","“我想你不能站在这儿。”"
"Bicket did not answer, his throat felt too dry.","比克特没有回答，他觉得自己的嗓子很干。"
"He had heard of the police.","他听人说过警察。"
"Had he gone the wrong way to work?","难道他选错了做生意的地方？"
"Suddenly he gulped, and said: “Give us a chance, constable; I’m right on my bones.","他猛吸了一大口气，然后说：“给我们一个机会吧，警官。我已经一贫如洗了。"
"If I’m in the way, I’ll stand anywhere you like.","要是我挡着道了，您让我站哪儿都行。"
"This is new to me, and two bob’s all I’ve got left in the world besides a wife.”","我头一次干这个买卖。我在这个世上就剩下一个老婆和两个先令了。”"
"The constable, a big man, looked him up and down.","这位大个子警察上上下下地打量了他一番。"
"“Well, we’ll see.","“好吧。我们看着办吧。"
"I shan’t make trouble for you if no one objects.”","如果没有人反对的话，我也不会找你麻烦的。”"
"Bicket’s gaze deepened thankfully.","比克特满怀感激之情地望着那位警官。"
"“I’m much obliged,” he said; “tyke one for your little girl—to please me.”","“太谢谢您了。”他说，“拿一个给您的小孩玩去吧——让我高兴一下。”"
"“I’ll buy one,” said the policeman, “and give you a start.","“我会买一个的，”那警察说，“就算给你开张了。"
"I go off duty in an hour, you ‘ave it ready—a big one, magenta.”","再过一个小时我就下班了，到时候你给我准备好就行——一个大气球，要紫红色的。”"
"He moved away.","说完，他就走开了。"
"Bicket could see him watching.","比克特能看见他值勤。"
"Edging into the gutter, he stood quite still; his large eyes clung to every face that passed; and, now and then, his thin fingers nervously touched his wares.","比克特静静地站在排水沟的旁边，用那双大眼睛盯着每一位过路人的脸，还时不时紧张地用他那瘦削的手指去碰碰他的货品。"
"If Victorine could see him!","要是维多琳能看见他就好了！"
"All the spirit within him mounted.","他的精神为之一振。"
"By Golly! he would get out of this somehow into the sun, into a life that was a life!","天哪！他得设法摆脱这种生活，到阳光下去，过真正的生活！"
"He had been standing there nearly two hours, shifting from foot to unaccustomed foot, and had sold four big and five small—sixpenny worth of profit—when Soames, who had changed his route to spite those fellows who couldn’t get past William Gouldyng Ingerer, came by on his way to the P.P.R.S. board.","他已经站了将近两个小时了，重心从一只脚换到另一只脚，卖掉了四个大气球和五个小气球——赚了六个便士——这时，索姆斯刚好路过这里。他改走这条道去天佑再保险公司董事会，是为了去教训一下那些连威廉·古尔丁·英格勒家族都不知道的家伙。"
"Startled by a timid murmur: “Balloon, sir, best quality,” he looked round from that contemplation of St. Paul’s which had been his lifelong habit, and stopped in sheer surprise.","他这辈子有个习惯，每逢路过圣保罗教堂，总要看上两眼。这时，一个怯生生的低语吓了他一跳：“气球，先生，最好的气球。”他四下看了看，十分惊奇地停下了脚步。"
"“Balloon!” he said.","“气球！”他说道，"
"“What should I want with a balloon?”","“我要气球干什么？”"
"Bicket smiled.","比克特笑了。"
"Between those green and blue and orange globes and Soames’ grey self-containment there was incongruity which even he could appreciate.","那些绿色、蓝色、橙色的气球和索姆斯那副阴沉的表情实在有点儿不相称，这一点连他都能感觉出来。"
"“Children like ‘em—no weight, sir, waistcoat pocket.”","“孩子们喜欢它们——不占分量，先生，放在您的马甲口袋里就行。”"
"“I daresay,” said Soames, “but I’ve no children.”","“也许吧，”索姆斯说，“可我没有小孩。”"
"“Grandchildren, sir.”","“孙儿孙女也行啊，先生。”"
"“Nor any grandchildren.”","“也没有孙儿孙女。”"
"“Thank you, sir.”","“那谢谢您了，先生。”"
"Soames gave him one of those rapid glances with which he was accustomed to gauge the character of the impecunious.","索姆斯迅速地瞥了他一眼，他惯于以此评定那些穷人的品性。"
"‘A poor, harmless little rat!’ he thought “Here, give me two—how much?”","“一个可怜的、没有恶意的小东西！”他想，“喂，给我两个气球——多少钱？”"
"“A shilling, sir, and much obliged.”","“一个先令，先生，非常感谢。”"
"“You can keep the change,” said Soames hurriedly, and passed on, astonished.","“不用找零了。”索姆斯一边说，一边匆忙地走了过去。他自己也很吃惊。"
"Why on earth he had bought the things, and for more than double their price, he could not conceive.","他不明白自己究竟为什么会买这样的东西，还付了两倍以上的价钱。"
"He did not recollect such a thing having happened to him before.","他记得以前自己从没做过这样的事情。"
"Extremely peculiar!","太奇怪了！"
"And suddenly he realised why.","可是他突然明白自己为什么这样做了。"
"The fellow had been humble, mild—to be encouraged, in these days of Communistic bravura.","那个人谦卑、温驯——在共产主义大行其道的今天，这样的人值得鼓励。"
"After all, the little chap was—was on the side of Capital, had invested in those balloons!","这小家伙毕竟是——站在资本主义这边的，他把钱投资在这些气球上了！"
"Trade!","做买卖了！"
"And, raising his eyes towards St. Paul’s again, he stuffed the nasty-feeling things down into his overcoat pocket.","然后，他再次抬眼向圣保罗大教堂望去，把那邋遢东西塞进外衣口袋里。"
"Somebody would be taking them out, and wondering what was the matter with him!","有人会把这东西拿出来的，还会奇怪他怎么会有这样的东西！"
"Well, he had other things to think of!...","得了，他还有别的事情要考虑呢！……"
"Bicket, however, stared after him, elated.","而比克特则兴高采烈地目送他离开。"
"Two hundred and fifty odd percent. profit on those two—that was something like.","这两只气球获利250%以上——这感觉好极了。"
"The feeling, that not enough women were passing him here, became less poignant—after all, women knew the value of money, no extra shillings out of them!","由于从他这里路过的妇女不多，他一度有些泄气，现在则不那么难过了——毕竟，女人懂得钱的价值，她们是一个先令也不会多给的！"
"If only some more of these shiny-hatted old millionaires would come along!","要是能多来几个像这样帽子锃亮的老百万富翁就好了！"
"At six o’clock, with a profit of three and eightpence, to which Soames had contributed just half, he began to add the sighs of deflating balloons to his own; untying them with passionate care he watched his coloured hopes one by one collapse, and stored them in the drawer of his tray.","到6点钟的时候，比克特一共赚了3先令零8便士，其中有一半是索姆斯贡献的。他开始一边叹气一边给气球放气。他小心翼翼地把这一只只气球解开，看着这些彩色的希望一个个瘪下去，然后把它们收进托盘的抽屉里。"
"Taking it under his arm, he moved his tired legs in the direction of the Bridge.","他把托盘夹在腋下，拖着疲惫的双腿，朝大桥方向走去。"
"In a full day he might make four to five shillings—Well, it would just keep them alive, and something might turn up!","要是干上一整天的话，该能挣四五个先令的——嗯，刚好够他们活下去，也许会时来运转！"
"He was his own master, anyway, accountable neither to employer nor to union.","不管怎样，他现在是自己的主人了，无需再为老板或是工会做什么。"
"That knowledge gave him a curious lightness inside, together with the fact that he had eaten nothing since breakfast.","想到这一点，再加上他早饭过后就什么也没吃，他心里感到一阵莫名的轻松感。"
"‘Wonder if he was an alderman,’ he thought; ‘they say those aldermen live on turtle soup.’","“不知道他是不是个市议员，”他想，“据说那些市议员都是喝甲鱼汤的。”"
"Nearing home, he considered nervously what to do with the tray?","快到家的时候，他为不知如何处理这个托盘而紧张起来。"
"How prevent Victorine from knowing that he had joined the ranks of Capital, and spent his day in the gutter?","怎么才能不让维多琳知道他已经加入了资本家的队伍，还在排水沟旁站了一天呢？"
"Ill luck!","真倒霉！"
"She was at the window!","她就站在窗口！"
"He must put a good face on it.","他必须得装成一副高高兴兴的样子。"
"And he went in whistling.","于是，他吹着口哨走了进去。"
"“What’s that, Tony?” she said, pointing to the tray.","“那是什么，托尼？”她指着那个托盘问道。"
"“Ah! ha!","“啊哈！"
"Great stunt—this!","精彩的表演——看这个！"
"Look ‘ere!”","看这里！”"
"Taking a balloon out from the tray, he blew.","他从托盘里拿出一个气球，吹了起来。"
"He blew with a desperation he had not yet put into the process.","他从来没使过这么大的劲，拼命地吹着。"
"They said the things would swell to five feet in circumference.","据说这东西可以吹到周长五英尺那么大。"
"He felt somehow that if he could get it to attain those proportions, it would soften everything.","不知为什么，他觉得只要能把球吹成那么大，就能让事情缓和下来。"
"Under his breath the thing blotted out Victorine, and the room, till there was just the globe of coloured air.","他吹着吹着，气球已经大到遮住了维多琳，挡住了房间，直到眼前能看到的只有这个彩色的气球。"
"Nipping its neck between thumb and finger, he held it up, and said:","他用拇指和食指捏住气球口，把它举起来，对维多琳说："
"“There you are; not bad value for sixpence, old girl!” and he peered round it.","“你瞧，六个便士不算贵吧，大姑娘！”说着，他从气球一侧探头望去。"
"Lord, she was crying!","天啊，她哭了！"
"He let the ‘blymed’ thing go; it floated down, the air slowly evaporating till a little crinkled wreck rested on the dingy carpet.","他撒手放掉了那个“该死的”东西。它缓缓飘落，里面的空气慢慢漏出来，直到缩成皱巴巴的一团，落在脏兮兮的地毯上。"
"Clasping her heaving shoulders, he said desperately:","他抓住她哭得一耸一耸的肩膀，拼命地说道："
"“Cheerio, my dear, don’t quarrel with bread and butter.","“亲爱的，振作起来，别再为了生计吵架了。"
"I shall get a job, this is just to tide us over.","我会找到工作的，这只是暂时的过渡罢了。"
"I’d do a lot worse than that for you.","为了你，比这更糟糕的事，我也愿意做。"
"Come on, and get my tea, I’m hungry, blowin’ up those things.”","好啦，好啦，把我的茶点拿来吧。一直吹这些东西，我都饿了。”"
"She stopped crying, looked up, said nothing—mysterious with those big eyes!","她不哭了，抬起头来看看，什么也没说——那双大眼睛太神秘了！"
"You’d say she had thoughts!","看得出来，她肯定有心事！"
"But what they were Bicket could not tell.","但是那是什么心事，比克特却说不出来。"
"Under the stimulus of tea, he achieved a certain bravado about his new profession.","在茶点的刺激下，他对自己的新营生有了夸夸其谈的勇气了。"
"To be your own master!","做自己的主人！"
"Go out when you liked, come home when you liked—lie in bed with Vic if he jolly well pleased.","想什么时候出去就什么时候出去，想什么时候回家就什么时候回家——要是特别开心的话，就和维躺在床上不必起来。"
"A lot in that!","好处可多了！"
"And there rose in Bicket something truly national, something free and happy-go-lucky, resenting regular work, enjoying a spurt, and a laze-off, craving independence—something that accounted for the national life, the crowds of little shops, of middlemen, casual workers, tramps, owning their own souls in their own good time, and damning the consequences—something inherent in the land, the race, before the Saxons and their conscience and their industry came in-something that believed in swelling and collapsing coloured air, demanded pickles and high flavours without nourishment—yes, all that something exulted above Bicket’s kipper and his tea, good and strong.","于是，比克特心里涌起了一些真正英国式的想法——想要自由自在、随遇而安；不喜欢规律性的工作，喜欢拼命努力一阵子，然后懒散消闲一阵子；渴望独立自主——这可就是英国人的生活。你看那成群的小商铺、经纪人、临时工和流浪汉，随心所欲地消磨自己美好的时光，管他什么后果——这种想法是这片土地、这个民族所特有的，在撒克逊人来之前，在产生良知和勤勉之前就有了——这种想法就是相信彩色气球会先膨胀后萎缩，就是能吃到那些腌制品和味道很重但毫无营养的东西就够了——比克特享用着可口的腌鱼和浓茶时，这些想法就在他心中欢腾着。"
"He would rather sell balloons than be a packer any day, and don’t let Vic forget it!","他宁可卖气球，也不愿意再做一天的包装工人，可不能让维忘记这一点！"
"And when she was able to take a job, they would get on fine, and not be long before they’d saved enough to get out of it to where those blue butterflies came from.","然后等她也能工作的时候，他们的生活就会好起来。再然后，用不了多久，他们就能攒够钱，摆脱这种生活，到蓝蝴蝶飞来的那个地方去。"
"And he spoke of Soames.","他还谈到了索姆斯。"
"A few more aldermen without children—say two a day, fifteen bob a week outside legitimate trade.","要是再来几个没有子女的市议员——比方说，一天来两个吧，一周就能多挣15先令的外快了。"
"Why, in under a year they’d have the money!","哦，用不了一年的工夫，他们就能弄到那笔钱了！"
"And once away, Vic would blow out like one of those balloons; she’d be twice the size, and a colour in her cheeks to lay over that orange and magenta.","只要离开这里，维就会像那些气球一样丰满起来。她的身体会是现在的两倍那么大，脸蛋也会红润起来，比橙色和紫红的气球还要红。"
"Bicket became full of air.","比克特变得神采飞扬。"
"And the girl, his wife, watched with her large eyes and spoke little; but she did not cry again, or, indeed, throw any water, warm or cold, on him who sold balloons.","而那位姑娘，他的妻子，则睁着大大的眼睛看着他，什么话也没说。但是，她没有再哭。或者说，确实没有再向他——这个卖气球的——泼热水或是泼冷水。"

"Chapter XII","第十二章"
"Figures and Facts","数字与事实"
"With the exception of old Fontenoy—in absence as in presence ornamental—the Board was again full; Soames, conscious of special ingratiation in the manner of ‘that chap’ Elderson, prepared himself for the worst.","除了老福坦诺——他出不出席都是个摆设——董事会成员再次全体莅会。索姆斯注意到埃尔德森“那家伙”的一举一动都是在刻意地讨好别人，于是为自己作了最坏的打算。"
"The figures were before them; a somewhat colourless show, appearing to disclose a state of things which would pass muster, if within the next six months there were no further violent disturbances of currency exchange.","数字就摆在董事们的面前，这种展示有点儿无趣，看起来就像是要说明这么一个状况：如果未来六个月里外汇市场没有发生剧烈震荡的话，那么公司的情况就还不错。"
"The proportion of foreign business to home business was duly expressed in terms of two to seven; German business, which constituted the bulk of the foreign, had been lumped—Soames noted—in the middle section, of countries only half bankrupt, and taken at what might be called a conservative estimate.","公司的国内业务和国外业务的比例是七比二，看起来很合理。索姆斯发现，占据国外业务绝大比例的德国业务被并入到中间部分，即与半破产国家归在一起，而且这“半破产”还是保守的估计。"
"During the silence which reigned while each member of the Board digested the figures, Soames perceived more clearly than ever the quandary he was in.","会场里安静极了。董事会的每个成员都在琢磨着那些数字，而索姆斯却更清楚地觉得自己陷入了两难的境地。"
"Certainly, these figures would hardly justify the foregoing of the dividend earned on the past year’s business.","的确，很难以这些数字为理由要求公司按照去年的业绩发放红利。"
"But suppose there were another Continental crash and they became liable on the great bulk of their foreign business, it might swamp all profits on home business next year, and more besides.","但是，如果欧洲大陆再次发生经济危机，而他们又要对公司绝大部分对外业务承担责任的话，那么下一年度国内业务的盈利很可能会全赔进去，也许还不止如此。"
"And then his uneasiness about Elderson himself—founded he could not tell on what, intuitive, perhaps silly.","此外，埃尔德森这个人也令索姆斯感到不安——至于为什么不安，他也说不清楚。也许是出于直觉，也许有些杞人忧天。"
"“Well, Mr. Forsyte,” the chairman was speaking; “there are the figures.","“嗯，福赛特先生，”董事长说话了，“这就是那些数字。"
"Are you satisfied?”","您觉得满意吗？”"
"Soames looked up; he had taken a resolution.","索姆斯抬起头来，下定了决心："
"“I will agree to this year’s dividend on condition that we drop this foreign business in future, lock, stock and barrel.”","“我同意发放今年的红利，但条件是从此放弃这种对外业务——完全放弃。”"
"The manager’s eyes hard and bright, met his, then turned towards the chairman.","那位经理的眼神冷峻而机警，和索姆斯对视一眼，而后转向了董事长。"
"“That appears to savour of the panicky,” he said; “the foreign business is responsible for a good third of our profit this year.”","“这听起来让人觉得恐慌，”他说道，“国外业务占到今年公司利润的三分之一之多呢。”"
"The chairman seemed to garner the expressions of his fellow-directors, before he said:","董事长貌似环顾了一下各位董事的表情，然后才说："
"“There is nothing in the foreign situation at the moment, Mr. Forsyte, which gives particular cause for alarm.","“福赛特先生，眼下国外业务没有出现可以引起恐慌的状况。"
"I admit that we should watch it closely—”","我承认我们应该密切关注这方面——”"
"“You can’t,” interjected Soames.","“您不能这么做。”索姆斯插话说，"
"“Here we are four years from the Armistice, and we know no more where we stand than we did then.","“停战至今已经四年了，而我们对自己处境的了解并没有增加。"
"If I’d realised our commitment to this policy, I should never have come on the Board.","要是我早意识到我们为这个业务承担的风险，我是绝对不会加入董事会的。"
"We must drop it.”","我们必须放弃这一业务方针。”"
"“Rather an extreme view.","“这是相当极端的看法。"
"And hardly a matter we can decide in a moment.”","而且这件事也不是一时半会儿就能决定的。”"
"The murmur of assent, the expression, faintly ironical, of ‘that chap’s’ lips, jolted the tenacity in Soames.","赞同者小声嘀咕起来，再加上“那家伙”嘴上略带讽刺的表情，让索姆斯的决心动摇了。"
"“Very well!","“很好！"
"Unless you’re prepared to tell the shareholders in the report that we are dropping foreign business, you drop me.","除非你们准备好在报告里告知股东，说我公司将放弃国外业务，否则你们就得放弃我。"
"I must be free to raise the question myself at the general meeting.”","我一定会亲自在全体股东大会上提出这个问题的。我有这个自由。”"
"He did not miss the shift and blink in the manager’s eyes.","他没有错过那位经理躲躲闪闪的眼神。"
"That shot had gone home!","这一下可击中要害了！"
"The Chairman said:","董事长说："
"“You put a pistol to our heads.”","“你这是拿枪指着我们的脑袋啊。”"
"“I am responsible to the shareholders,” said Soames, “and I shall do my duty by them.”","“我这是对股东们负责，”索姆斯说，“我也会依靠他们履行我的职责。”"
"“So we all are, Mr. Forsyte; and I hope we shall all do our duty.”","“我们都是这样的，福赛特先生，而且我希望大家都能尽到自己的职责。”"
"“Why not confine the foreign business to the small countries—their currency is safe enough?”","“为什么不把国外业务限定在那些小国家内呢——他们的货币不是很稳定的吗？”"
"‘Old Mont,’ and his precious ‘ring!’","“老蒙特”和他那宝贝“圈子”！"
"“No,” said Soames, “we must go back to safety.”","“不行，”索姆斯说，“我们必须退到安全线内。”"
"“Splendid isolation, Forsyte?”","“辉煌的孤立吗，福赛特？”"
"“Meddling was all very well in the war, but in peace—politics or business—this half-and-half interference is no good.","“在战争时期，干预是非常管用的，但是在和平年代——不论是政治还是经济——这种一手经济、一手政治的干涉是没有用的。"
"We can’t control the foreign situation.”","我们无法掌控英国以外的形势。”"
"He looked around him, and was instantly conscious that with those words he had struck a chord.","他环顾四周，马上意识到自己的话已经触动大家的心弦了。"
"‘I’m going through with this!’ he thought.","“在这个问题上我要坚持到底！”他想道。"
"“I should be glad, Mr. Chairman”—the manager was speaking—“if I might say a word.","“董事长先生，”——那位经理说道——“请允许我说几句，我将不胜感激。"
"The policy was of my initiation, and I think I may claim that it has been of substantial benefit to the Society so far.","那个方针是我提议的，而且我想我可以断言，到目前为止，这一方针为本公司带来的收益是很可观的。"
"When, however, a member of the Board takes so strong a view against its continuance, I certainly don’t press the Board to continue it.","但是，如果董事会的成员里有人如此强烈地反对继续这一方针，我当然不会强迫董事会继续推行这一方针。"
"The times ARE uncertain, and a risk, of course, is involved, however conservative our estimates.”","由于时局是不确定的，就算我们的估计再怎么保守，风险依然是存在的。”"
"‘Now why?’ thought Soames: ‘What’s he ratting for?’","“他这是怎么了？”索姆斯想，“怎么突然变词了？”"
"“That’s very handsome of you, Elderson; Mr. Chairman, I think we may say that is very handsome of our manager.”","“你真是太大度了，埃尔德森。董事长先生，我觉得我们这位经理可以说是太大度了。”"
"Old Dosey Cosey!","老混蛋！"
"Handsome!","大度！"
"The old woman!","这个老妖婆！"
"The Chairman’s rather harsh voice broke a silence.","董事长那相当刺耳的声音打破了会场的沉默。"
"“This is a very serious point of policy.","“这是一个十分严肃的方针问题。"
"I should have been glad to have Lord Fontenoy present.”","我觉得如果福坦诺勋爵在场的话，就太好了。”"
"“If I am to endorse the report,” said Soames shortly, “it must be decided today.","“如果想要我在这份报告上签名的话，”索姆斯立刻说，“今天就得定下来。"
"I have made up my mind.","我已经拿定主意了。"
"But please yourselves.”","你们想怎么办，随便。”"
"He threw in those last three words from a sort of fellow feeling—it was unpleasant to be dragooned!","他之所以说最后这句话，是念在大家同事一场的情分上——被逼无奈的感觉让人很不愉快！"
"A moment’s silence, and then discussion assumed that random volubility which softens a decision already forced on one.","大家沉默了片刻，然后讨论起来，就好像这种人人畅所欲言的讨论缓和了此前被迫做出决定的气氛。"
"A quarter of an hour thus passed before the Chairman said:","就这么过了一刻钟之后，董事长宣布："
"“We are agreed then, gentlemen, that the report shall contain the announcement that, in view of Continental uncertainty, we are abandoning foreign risks for the present.”","“那么，诸位，我们都同意在这份报告中写入这样一份声明，即鉴于欧洲大陆局势的不确定性，我公司将暂时放弃国外保险业务。”"
"Soames had won.","索姆斯获胜了。"
"Relieved and puzzled, he walked away alone.","他觉得既轻松又困惑，独自离开了。"
"He had shown character; their respect for him had gone up, he could see; their liking for him down, if they’d ever had any—he didn’t know!","他让他们见识了自己的个性，他们对他的尊敬程度增加了，这他看得出来；但是，他们对他的好感却降低了，他们对他有没有过好感呢？——这他就不知道了！"
"But why had Elderson veered round?","但是埃尔德森为什么突然改词了呢？"
"He recalled the shift and blink of the fellow’s steely eyes at the idea of the question being raised at the general meeting.","他回想起来，就在他说要将此事提交股东大会时，那家伙冷峻的眼神突然闪烁不定起来。"
"That had done it!","他就是为这个改口的！"
"But why?","可是，为什么呢？"
"Were the figures faked?","是因为数字作假了吗？"
"Surely not!","当然不是！"
"That would be too difficult, in the face of the accountants.","在那些会计师的眼皮子底下作假，那可太难了。"
"If Soames had faith, it was in chartered accountants.","如果说索姆斯还相信什么的话，那就是相信那些持有皇家特许状的会计师了。"
"Sandis and Jevon were tip-top people.","桑迪斯和杰文两人都是最棒的会计师。"
"It couldn’t be that!","捏造数字是不可能的！"
"He glanced up from the pavement.","他站在人行道上抬头望去。"
"The dome of St. Paul’s was dim already in evening sky—nothing to be had out of it!","圣保罗教堂的圆顶在夜幕下已经模糊不清——什么都看不清了！"
"He felt badly in need of some one to talk to; but there was nobody; and he quickened his pace among the hurrying crowd.","他迫切地想找个人聊聊，但是身边连个说话的人都没有，于是他在匆忙的人群中加快了脚步。"
"His hand, driven deep into his overcoat pocket, came into sudden contact with some foreign sticky substance.","他把手深深地插入外衣的口袋，突然碰到了一种异样的、黏糊糊的东西。"
"‘Gracious!’ he thought: ‘those things!’","“啊呀！”他想道，“是那些东西！”"
"Should he drop them in the gutter?","该把它们扔进水沟里吗？"
"If only there were a child he could take them home to!","要是家里有孩子的话，就能把它们带回去了！"
"He must get Annette to speak to Fleur.","他得让安妮特跟弗勒谈谈了。"
"He knew what came of bad habits from his own experience of long ago.","他自己多年前的亲身经历让他清楚地知道陋习会产生什么样的恶果。"
"Why shouldn’t he speak to her himself?","为什么他不自己去跟她谈呢？"
"He was staying the night there!","今晚他就住在她那里呀！"
"But there came on him a helpless sense of ignorance.","但是他觉得很无助，不知道该怎么做。"
"These young people!","这些年轻人啊！"
"What did they really think and feel?","他们究竟是怎么想的，有什么样的感觉？"
"Was old Mont right?","老蒙特是对的吗？"
"Had they given up interest in everything except the moment, abandoned all belief in continuity, and progress?","难道他们除了眼前的事，对其他任何事都不感兴趣了吗，对繁衍和进化全都不相信了吗？"
"True enough that Europe was in Queer Street.","的确，欧洲如今负债累累。"
"But look at the state of things after the Napoleonic Wars.","但是看看经历过拿破仑战争后的情况。"
"He couldn’t remember his grandfather ‘Superior Dosset,’ the old chap had died five years before he was born, but he perfectly remembered how Aunt Ann, born in 1799, used to talk about “that dreadful Bonaparte—we used to call him Boney, my dear;” of how her father could get eight or ten per cent. for his money; and of what an impression ‘those Chartists’ had made on Aunts Juley and Hester, and that was long afterwards.","他记不得自己的祖父“高傲的多塞特”，那个老头早在他出生前5年就去世了。但是，他却清清楚楚地记得生于1799年的安姑妈。她以前总是说：“那个可怕的波拿巴——我们总是叫他博尼，亲爱的。”她会说他的父亲怎么为他自己的钱挣到8%或是10%的利息，还会说“那些宪章运动者”给朱莉姑姑和赫斯特姑姑留下了怎样深刻的印象。这都是很久之后的事情了。"
"Yet, in spite of all that, look at the Victorian era—a golden age, things worth collecting, children worth having!","然而，尽管经历了上述种种情况，但是看看维多利亚时代——一个黄金时代，有值得收藏的器物，也有值得养育的儿女！"
"Why not again!","为什么不再来一个这样的时代呢？"
"Consols had risen almost continuously since Timothy died.","蒂莫西死后，统一公债几乎是接连不断地一涨再涨。"
"Even if Heaven and Hell had gone, they couldn’t be the reason; none of his uncles had believed in either, and yet had all made fortunes, and all had families, except Timothy and Swithin.","就算是天堂和地狱都不存在了，都不能成为这么做的理由。他的叔叔伯伯们没有谁相信有天堂或是地狱的存在，但是他们却都发了财，也都成了家，就只有蒂莫西和斯威森没有家小。"
"No!","不！"
"It couldn’t be the want of Heaven and Hell!","这不可能是因为缺少天堂和地狱造成的！"
"What, then, was the reason of the change—if change there really were?","那么，什么才是造成这种变化的原因呢——如果真的有变化的话？"
"And suddenly it was revealed to Soames.","索姆斯突然明白了。"
"They talked too much—too much and too fast!","他们说话太多了——太多而且太快！"
"They got to the end of interest in this and that and the other.","他们失去了对这个、那个或是其他事物的兴趣。"
"They ate life and threw away the rind, and—and—.","他们吞噬了人生，丢掉了人生的果皮，然后——然后——"
"By the way, he must buy that picture of George’s!...","顺便说一下，他一定要把乔治那幅画买下来！……"
"Had these young folk more mind than his own generation?","难道这些年轻人比他们这代人想的更多吗？"
"And if so—why?","如果是这样的话——又是为什么呢？"
"Was it diet?","是饮食造成的吗？"
"That lobster cocktail Fleur had given him the Sunday before last.","就是上上周日弗勒给他吃的那个龙虾冷盘。"
"He had eaten the thing—very nasty!","他居然把那东西吃了——那么恶心的东西！"
"But it hadn’t made him want to talk.","但这东西并没有使得他想要说话。"
"No!","不！"
"He didn’t think it could be diet.","他认为不可能是饮食造成的。"
"Besides—Mind!","何况——还有头脑！"
"Where were the minds now that equalled the Victorians—Darwin, Huxley, Dickens, Disraeli, even old Gladstone?","现在哪里有能媲美维多利亚时代的人——达尔文、赫胥黎、狄更斯、迪斯累里，甚至老格莱斯顿？"
"Why, he remembered judges and advocates who seemed giants compared with those of the present day, just as he remembered that the judges of James his father’s youth had seemed giants to James compared with those of Soames’ prime.","唉，他想起以前的那些法官和律师，同现在这些同行相比，那些都是巨人了。就像他记得在他父亲詹姆斯看来，詹姆斯年轻时的那些法官和儿子索姆斯年轻时的那些法官相比的话，也是巨人一般的。"
"According to that, mind was steadily declining.","照此看来，大脑的确是逐渐退化了。"
"It must be something else.","但是，一定还有别的什么缘故。"
"There was a thing they called psycho-analysis, which so far as he could understand attributed people’s action not to what they ate at breakfast, or the leg they got out of bed with, as in the good old days, but to some shock they had received in the remote past and entirely forgotten.","有一种被称为心理分析的东西，根据他的理解，并没有像过去那样，把人们的行动归结为早餐吃的什么或是早晨起床时先迈出的是哪条腿，而是归结为人们已经忘却的、很早以前曾受过的精神冲击。"
"The subconscious mind!","潜意识！"
"Fads!","时尚！"
"Fads and microbes!","流行和微生物！"
"The fact was this generation had no digestion.","事实就是，这一代人根本没有消化能力。"
"His father and his uncles had all complained of liver, but they had never had anything the matter with them—no need of any of these vitamins, false teeth, mental healing, newspapers, psycho-analysis, spiritualism, birth control, osteopathy, broadcasting, and what not.","他的父亲、他的叔叔伯伯们都曾经抱怨说自己的肝脏不好，但是他们从来没得过什么大毛病——不需要什么维生素、假牙、精神治疗、报纸、精神分析、招魂术、计划生育、整骨疗法、广播等等。"
"‘Machines!’ thought Soames.","“机器！”索姆斯想道，"
"‘That’s it—I shouldn’t wonder!’","“就是这个——这就不足为奇了！”"
"How could you believe in anything when everything was going round so fast?","如果一切都这么快速地运转的话，你还怎么能相信什么东西呢？"
"When you couldn’t count your chickens—they ran about so?","如果你养的小鸡四下乱跑，你又怎么去数它们的数目呢？"
"But Fleur had got a good little head on her!","但是，弗勒有一个很棒的小脑瓜！"
"‘Yes,’ he mused, ‘and French teeth, she can digest anything.","“是啊，”他默默地想着，“她还有一副法国牙齿，能消化任何东西。"
"Two years!","两年了！"
"I’ll speak to her before she gets the habit confirmed.","我得在她还没有养成这个习惯之前，和她谈谈。"
"Her mother was quick enough about it!’","她妈妈在这件事上可是够快的！”"
"And perceiving the Connoisseurs’ Club in front of him, he went in.","这时，他发现自己走到了鉴赏家俱乐部前，于是就走了进去。"
"The hall porter came out of his box.","俱乐部的看门人从他的小隔间里走出来。"
"A gentleman was waiting.","他告诉索姆斯，有位先生在等他。"
"“What gentleman?” said Soames, sidelong.","“哪位先生？”索姆斯侧着身问道。"
"“I think he’s your nephew, sir, Mr. Dartie.”","“先生，我想他是您的外甥，达尔蒂先生。”"
"“Val Dartie!","“瓦尔·达尔蒂！"
"H’m!","哦！"
"Where?”","他人呢？”"
"“In the little room, sir.”","“在小房间里，先生。”"
"The little room—all the accommodation considered worthy of such as were not Connoisseurs—was at the end of a passage, and in no taste at all, as if the Club were saying: “See what it is not to be one of us!”","那个小房间在走廊的末端——只有非会员才配呆在那种地方。那里毫无品味，就好像是这家俱乐部在说：“瞧瞧，非会员就是这么个待遇！”"
"Soames entered it, and saw Val Dartie smoking a cigarette and gazing with absorption at the only object of interest, his own reflection in the glass above the fire.","索姆斯走了进去，看到瓦尔·达尔蒂正在一边抽烟一边全神贯注地盯着这里唯一有趣的东西——壁炉上方的镜子，看镜中的自己。"
"He never saw his nephew without wondering when he would say: “Look here, Uncle Soames, I’m up a stump.”","他每次看见自己的外甥，总免不了要想到他又要跟自己说：“索姆斯舅舅，你瞧，我又遇上麻烦了。”"
"Breeding race horses!","养赛马的！"
"There could only be one end to that!","他们就只会有那么一个下场！"

"The face in the glass turned round, and became the back of a clipped sandyish head.","镜子里的那张脸转了过来，镜中映出了一个留着金黄色短发的后脑勺。"
"“Oh! bobbish, thanks!","“哦！我很好，谢谢您！"
"YOU look all right, Uncle Soames.","您看起来气色很好，索姆斯舅舅。"
"I just wanted to ask you: Must I take these screws of old George Forsyte’s?","我只是想问问您：我非得接受老乔治·福赛特的那几匹驽马吗？"
"They’re dashed bad.”","它们真的很糟。”"
"“Gift horse in the mouth?” said Soames.","“对礼物不满意吗？”索姆斯问道。"
"“Well,” said Val, “but they’re SO dashed bad; by the time I’ve paid legacy duty, boxed them to a sale, and sold them, there won’t be a sixpence.","“哎呀，”瓦尔说道，“可是它们实在太糟糕了，就算等我付完遗产税，把它们装在箱子里运出去卖的话，三匹加在一起也卖不了六便士。"
"One of them falls down when you look at it.","其中一匹马，一见人就会摔倒。"
"And the other two are broken-winded.","另外两匹都有气喘病。"
"The poor old boy kept them, because he couldn’t get rid of them.","那个可怜的老头子养着它们，是因为他甩不掉它们。"
"They’re about five hundred years old.”","它们差不多都有五百岁了。”"
"“Thought you were fond of horses,” said Soames.","“我还以为你喜欢马呢。”索姆斯说道，"
"“Can’t you turn them out?”","“你就不能把它们放了？”"
"“Yes,” said Val, drily; “but I’ve got my living to make.","“我是喜欢马，”瓦尔淡淡地说，“但是我也得养家糊口啊。"

"She was the daughter of his enemy, young Jolyon.","她是他的仇人——小乔利恩的女儿。"
"That fellow was dead, but the fact remained.","虽然那家伙死了，他们之间的敌对关系却没变。"
"“I will, then,” said Val.","“那么，就这么办了。”瓦尔说，"
"“How did his funeral go off?”","“他的葬礼办得怎么样了？”"
"“Very simple affair—I had nothing to do with it.”","“非常简单——我没管这事。”"
"The days of funerals were over.","办葬礼的日子已经过去了。"
"No flowers, no horses, no plumes—a motor hearse, a couple of cars or so, was all the attention paid nowadays to the dead.","没有鲜花，没有马匹，没有羽饰——就只有一辆机动灵车和两三辆小汽车，这就是现今人们对死者的全部关照。"
"Another sign of the times!","这个时代的又一项标志！"
"“I’m staying the night at Green Street,” said Val.","“我今天晚上住在格林大街。”瓦尔说道，"

"“Why?","“为什么？"

"Exchanging a chilly hand-shake, he watched his nephew withdraw.","两人冷冷地握了握手，然后索姆斯看着外甥退了出去。"
"So long!","再见！"
"An expression, old as the Boer war, that he had never got used to—meant nothing so far as he could see!","这个词像布尔战争一样古老，可他就是不习惯这个词——他看不出这个词有什么意义！"
"He entered the reading-room.","他走进了阅览室。"
"A number of Connoisseurs were sitting and standing about, and Soames, least clubbable of men, sought the solitude of an embrasured window.","那里有几个会员，有的站着，有的坐着，索姆斯则是其中最不善交际的，于是他找了个僻静的地方，坐在一扇斜面窗户前。"
"He sat there polishing the nail of one forefinger against the back of the other, and chewing the cud of life.","他坐在那里，一边用一根食指擦亮另一根食指的指甲，一边细细地品味人生。"
"After all, what was the point of anything.","人这辈子究竟有什么意义呢？"
"There was George!","看看乔治！"
"He had had an easy life—never done any work!","他安逸地过了一辈子——什么活也没干！"
"And here was himself, who had done a lot of work!","再看看他自己，做了那么多事情！"
"And sooner or later they would bury him too, with a motor hearse probably!","早晚有一天，他们也会为他送葬的，很可能也是用一辆机动的灵车！"
"And there was his son-inlaw, young Mont, full of talk about goodness knew what—and that thin-cheeked chap who had sold him the balloons this afternoon.","看看他的女婿——小蒙特，满口胡言乱语——还有今天下午卖气球给他的那个脸颊瘦瘦的家伙。"
"And old Fontenoy, and that waiter over there; and the out-of-works and the inworks; and those chaps in Parliament, and the parsons in their pulpits—what were they all for?","老福坦诺、那边那个侍者、有工作的和没工作的人、议会里的那些议员以及教堂里的牧师——他们为了什么而活着呢？"
"There was the old gardener down at Mapledurham pushing his roller over and over the lawn, week after week, and if he didn’t, what would the lawn be like?","在梅普尔达勒姆那个地方有一个老园丁，日复一日地推着车修剪草坪，要是他不修剪的话，草坪会变成什么样子？"
"That was life—gardener rolling lawn!","这就是人生——就像园丁修剪草坪一样！"
"Put it that there was another life—he didn’t believe it, but for the sake of argument—that life must be just the same.","假如说有另外一种人生的话——他是不会信的，但是作为讨论的基础，姑且这样假设——那种生活也一定是一样的。"

"Conscious of pessimism, he rose.","他觉得自己想得太悲观了，于是站了起来。"

"He supposed there was something in dressing for dinner, but it was like lawn—you came unrolled—undressed again, and so it went on!","他想，穿礼服吃晚餐总会有什么原因的吧，但是就像草坪一样——有时不修剪——有时脱下礼服，就这么循环下去！"
"Over and over and over to keep up to a pitch, that was—ah! what WAS the pitch for?","一遍又一遍地做同样的事只是为了保持一个高度，那就是——哎呀！这些高度又是为了什么呀？"
"Turning into South Square, he cannoned into a young man, whose head was craned back as if looking after some one he had parted from.","他拐进南广场的时候，突然和一个年轻人撞在了一起。那个年轻人正在扭着脖子朝后看，像是在看着某个刚刚和他分手的什么人。"
"Uncertain whether to apologise or to wait for an apology, Soames stood still.","索姆斯不知道自己是该道歉还是应该等着接受别人的道歉，于是索性站在那里，不动了。"

"“Now you’ve been married two years, my child, I suppose you’ll be looking towards the future.","“孩子，现在你结婚都两年了，我觉得你得为将来考虑一下了。"

"If there was point in anything, it was in perpetuation of oneself, though, of course, that begged the question.","如果有什么事情是真正有意义的话，那就是传宗接代了。当然了，这件事情尚无定论。"
