"Off it flew—purple and extravagant, alighting on his bed.","它飞起来了——紫红色的，那么大，飘到了他的床上。"
"H’m!","嗯！"
"He took up the other, and did the same to it.","他把另一个气球也拿起来，同样地吹了起来。"
"Purple and green!","紫色的和绿色的！"
"The deuce!","糟了！"
"If any one came in and saw!","要是有人走进来看见怎么办！"
"He threw up the window, batted them, balloon after balloon, into the night, and shut the window down.","他打开窗户，把气球一只一只地拍了出去，拍进黑暗里，然后关上了窗户。"
"There they’d be in the dark, floating about.","气球将在黑暗中四处飘荡。"
"His lips contracted in a nervous grin.","他扯动嘴角，不安地做出一个笑脸。"
"People would see them in the morning.","早上，人们就会看见它们了。"
"Well!","唉！"
"What else could you do with things like that?","这样的东西，还能怎么处置它们？"

"Chapter XIII","第十三章"
"Tenterhooks","焦虑不安"
"Michael had gone to the Labour candidate’s meeting partly because he wanted to, and partly out of fellow feeling for ‘old Forsyte,’ whom he was always conscious of having robbed.","迈克尔之所以去参加工党候选人的集会，一部分是因为他自己想去，一部分是出于对“老福赛特”的同情，他总是觉得他夺了“老福赛特”的心头爱。"
"His father-in-law had been very decent about Fleur, and he liked the ‘old man’ to have her to himself when he could.","他的岳父一向对弗勒很好，因此只要他能办到，他就让这位“老人”单独和她呆在一起。"
"In a constituency which had much casual and no trades-union labour to speak of, the meeting would be one of those which enabled the intellectuals of the Party to get it ‘off their chests.’","在一个有许多临时工而且完全没有工会会员的选区里，这次集会将令党内知识分子们能够“直抒胸臆”。"
"Sentiment being ‘slop,’ and championship mere condescension, one might look for sound economic speeches which left out discredited factors, such as human nature.","由于可以“滔滔不绝”地抒发情感，获胜时也可以尽情展现优越感，人们可以在这里听到纯经济意义上的演讲。这种演讲摒弃了诸如人性之类的不可信的因素。"
"Michael was accustomed to hearing people disparaged for deprecating change because human nature was constant; he was accustomed to hearing people despised for feeling compassion; he knew that one ought to be purely economic.","迈克尔听惯了诽谤那些由于坚持人性永恒论而反对变革的人的话，他也听惯了鄙视那些富有同情心的人的话。他知道，这种演讲应该是纯经济意义上的。"
"And anyway that kind of speech was preferable to the tub-thumpings of the North or of the Park, which provoked a nasty underlying class spirit in himself.","不管怎样，这种演讲比北方的或者公园里的大吹大擂的演讲要好得多，因为那些演讲只会在他心中激起一种潜在的肮脏的阶级意识。"
"The meeting was in full swing when he arrived, the candidate pitilessly exposing the fallacies of a capitalism which, in his view, had brought on the war.","当迈克尔到达的时候，集会正热火朝天地进行着，那个候选人正在毫不客气地揭露资本主义的种种弊端，在他看来，正是资本主义导致了这场战争。"
"For fear that it should bring on another, it must be changed for a system which would ensure that nations should not want anything too much.","为了避免它引起另一场战争，就必须用另一种制度取代它——一种能够保证各个国家都不会贪得无厌的制度。"
"The individual—said the candidate—was in every respect superior to the nation of which he formed a part; and the problem before them was to secure an economic condition which would enable the individual to function freely in his native superiority.","每一个人——这个候选人说——在每一个方面都比他所属的民族要优越，摆在他们面前的问题就是要获得一种经济条件，来让每一个人自由地发挥他与生俱来的优越性。"
"In that way alone, he said, would they lose those mass movements and emotions which imperilled the sanity of the world.","他认为，只有这样，人们才能摆脱危害人类理智的群众运动和大众情绪。"
"He spoke well.","他讲得很精彩。"
"Michael listened, purring almost audibly, till he found that he was thinking of himself, Wilfrid and Fleur.","迈克尔一直听着，忍不住啧啧称赞，直到他发现他想到了自己、威尔弗里德和弗勒。"
"Would he ever function so freely in a native superiority that he did not want Fleur too much?","他能否非常自由地发挥他与生俱来的优越性，从而使自己不太需要弗勒呢？"
"And did he wish to?","他是否愿意这样做呢？"
"He did not.","他不愿意。"
"That seemed to introduce human nature into the speaker’s argument.","那样似乎就把人性引入到了那个演讲者的观点里了。"
"Didn’t everybody want something too much?","每一个人不都是贪得无厌的吗？"
"Wasn’t it natural?","这不是很自然的吗？"
"And if so, wouldn’t there always be a collective wanting too much—poolings of primary desire, such as the desire of keeping your own head above water?","如果是这样，那岂不是始终存在一种共同的贪得无厌——诸如使自己免遭灭顶之灾的这类基本欲望的集合呢？"
"The candidate’s argument seemed to him suddenly to leave out heat, to omit friction, to be that of a man in an armchair after a poor lunch.","他突然觉得那个候选人的言论忽视了问题的症结，忽略了矛盾，变成了一个吃了一顿糟糕的午餐的男人坐在扶手椅上发表的言论。"
"He looked attentively at the speaker’s shrewd, dry, doubting face.","他聚精会神地看着演讲者那张精明的、冷漠的、令人质疑的脸。"
"‘No juice!’ he thought.","“毫无意义！”他想。"
"And when ‘the chap’ sat down, he got up and left the hall.","于是当“那个家伙”坐下之后，他就起身离开了大厅。"
"This Wilfrid business had upset him horribly.","威尔弗里德这件事让他非常心烦意乱。"
"Try as he had to put it out of his mind, try as he would to laugh it off, it continued to eat into his sense of security and happiness.","虽然他试着将这件事抛诸脑后，虽然他试着对这件事一笑而过，但是这件事仍然不断地侵蚀着他的安全感和幸福感。"
"Wife and best friend!","妻子和最好的朋友！"
"A hundred times a day he assured himself that he trusted Fleur.","他每天说服自己一百次，让自己确信他是信任弗勒的。"
"Only, Wilfrid was so much more attractive than himself, and Fleur deserved the best of everything.","只是，威尔弗里德比自己更有吸引力，而弗勒应该得到一切最好的。"
"Besides, Wilfrid was going through torture, and it was not a pleasant thought!","不仅如此，想到威尔弗里德正在遭受着折磨，这也令他很难过。"
"How end the thing, restore peace of mind to himself, to him, to her?","如何了结这件事，让他自己、他和她都恢复内心的平静呢？"
"She had told him nothing; and it simply was impossible to ask.","她什么也没有对他说，他也绝不可能去问她。"
"No way even of showing his anxiety!","他甚至不能表现出焦虑！"
"The whole thing was just ‘dark,’ and, so far as he could see, would have to stay so; nothing to be done but screw the lid on tighter, be as nice as he could to her, try not to feel bitter about him.","整个这件事“不能挑明”，而且在他看来，这件事不得不继续保持现有的状态。除了控制住自己的脾气，尽可能地对她好，尽量不去记恨他，没有别的办法。"
"Hades!","真见鬼！"
"He turned down Chelsea Embankment.","他转过弯，沿着切尔西堤岸走着。"
"Here the sky was dark and wide and streaming with stars.","这里的天空黑暗而宽广，繁星点点。"
"The river wide, dark and gleaming with oily rays from the Embankment lamps.","河面很宽阔，黑暗的河水在堤岸灯的映照下闪烁着油亮的波光。"
"The width of it all gave him relief.","这一切广阔的景象让他感到解脱。"
"Dash the dumps!","去他的忧郁！"
"A jolly, queer, muddled, sweet and bitter world; an immensely intriguing game of chance, no matter how the cards were falling at the moment!","一个愉快的、奇怪的、混乱的、甜蜜的和痛苦的世界，一种极其有趣的赌博游戏，无论当时是怎样出的牌！"
"In the trenches he had thought: ‘Get out of this, and I’ll never mind anything again!’","当年在战壕里他曾经想过：“只要能从这里出去，以后什么事情我都不在乎了！”"
"How seldom now he remembered thinking that!","现在他很少能记起当时想过这个了！"
"The human body renewed itself—they said—in seven years.","据说，人的身体每七年更新一次。"
"In three years’ time his body would not be the body of the trenches, but a whole-time peace body with a fading complex.","再过三年，他的身体就不是战壕里的那个身体了，而是逐渐没了恐惧、永远安宁的身体。"
"If only Fleur would tell him quite openly what she felt, what she was doing about Wilfrid, for she must be doing something!","要是弗勒能把她对威尔弗里德的看法和她对威尔弗里德所做的事情都坦白地告诉他就好了，她一定在做着什么事情！"
"And Wilfrid’s verse?","还有威尔弗里德的诗呢？"
"Would his confounded passion—as Bart suggested—flow in poetry?","他那该死的热恋会不会——如准爵爷所说——化为诗歌呢？"
"And if so, who would publish it?","如果会，那么谁会将它出版呢？"
"A miserable business!","真是一件痛苦的事情！"
"Well the night was beautiful, and the great thing not to be a pig.","唉，夜晚是美丽的，而重要的是，不要做一个贪婪的人。"
"Beauty and not being a pig!","美丽而不贪婪！"
"Nothing much else to it—except laughter—the comic side!","乐观处之——除了大笑——再也没有别的什么了！"
"Keep one’s sense of humour, anyway!","无论如何，要保持幽默感！"
"And Michael searched, while he strode beneath plane trees half-stripped of leaves and plume-like in the dark, for the fun in his position.","于是迈克尔一边大步走在那树叶落了一半、在黑暗中像羽毛一样的法国梧桐树下，一边寻找着他的处境的可笑之处。"
"He failed to find it.","他找不出来。"
"There seemed absolutely nothing funny about love.","似乎爱情是完全没有什么可笑之处的。"
"Possibly he might fall out of love again some day, but not so long as she kept him on her tenterhooks.","也许有朝一日他会再次放弃爱情，但是只要她一直令他焦虑不安，他就还是放弃不了。"
"Did she do it on purpose?","她是故意这样做的吗？"
"Never!","绝对不是！"
"Fleur simply could not be like those women who kept their husbands hungry and fed them when they wanted dresses, furs, jewels.","弗勒绝对不像那些女人。她们一直吊着丈夫的胃口，当她们想要衣服、皮草和珠宝的时候才满足他们一下。"
"Revolting!","真令人恶心！"
"He came in sight of Westminster.","他来到能看见威斯敏斯特的地方。"
"Only half-past ten!","刚刚10点半！"
"Suppose he took a cab to Wilfrid’s rooms, and tried to have it out with him.","他可以乘出租车到威尔弗里德的住处，然后设法把这件事向他摊牌。"
"It would be like trying to make the hands of a clock move backwards to its ticking.","这就像是企图让钟表的指针滴滴答答地倒着走一样。"
"What use in saying: “You love Fleur—well, don’t!” or in Wilfrid saying it to him.","假如他对威尔弗里德说：“你爱弗勒——唉，别爱她了！”或者是威尔弗里德这样对他说，又有什么用呢？"
"‘After all, I was first with Fleur,’ he thought.","“毕竟，我是第一个和弗勒好的人。”他想。"
"Pure chance, perhaps, but fact!","也许这纯属运气，但这也是事实！"
"Ah!","啊！"
"And wasn’t that just the danger?","这不正是危险所在吗？"
"He was no longer a novelty to her—nothing unexpected about him now!","对于她来说，他已经不再新奇了——现在她对他已经了如指掌！"
"And he and she had agreed times without number that novelty was the salt of life, the essence of interest and drama.","而且他和她曾经无数次地一致认为，新奇是生活的调味剂，是兴趣和戏剧的本质。"
"Novelty now lay with Wilfrid!","现在威尔弗里德才是新奇的！"
"Lord!","上帝啊！"
"Lord!","上帝啊！"
"Possession appeared far from being nine points of the law!","占有者似乎在诉讼中远远不占上风！"
"He rounded-in from the Embankment towards home—jolly part of London, jolly Square; everything jolly except just this infernal complication.","他从堤岸绕了一圈，朝家走去——堤岸是伦敦的一个愉快的地方、一个愉快的广场，除了这该死的感情纠葛，一切都是愉快的。"
"Something, soft as a large leaf, tapped twice against his ear.","有个像大树叶一样柔软的东西轻轻地碰了他的耳朵两下。"
"He turned, astonished; he was in empty space, no tree near.","他回过头去，吃了一惊，他是在一片空地上，周围没有一棵树。"
"Floating in the darkness, a round thing—he grabbed, it bobbed.","一个圆圆的东西在黑暗中飘荡着——他伸手去抓，它上下摆动。"
"What?","那是什么？"
"A child’s balloon!","一只小孩子玩的气球！"
"He secured it between his hands, took it beneath a lamp-post—green, he judged.","他双手把它抓住，拿到路灯下去看——他看到是绿色的。"
"Queer!","奇怪！"
"He looked up.","他抬头看去。"
"Two windows lighted, one of them Fleur’s!","两个窗户里有灯光，其中一个是弗勒房间的窗户！"
"Was this the bubble of his own happiness expelled?","这气球是不是就是他自己幸福的气泡，被人驱赶出来了呢？"
"Morbid!","神经病！"
"Silly ass!","大笨蛋！"
"Some gust of wind—a child’s plaything lodged and loosened!","几阵风吹来的——一件小孩子的玩具，原本系着，后来松脱了！"
"He held the balloon gingerly.","他小心翼翼地拿着这只气球。"
"He would take it in and show it to her.","他要把它带回家去给她看。"
"He put his latch-key in the door.","他把弹簧锁的钥匙插进门里。"
"Dark in the hall—gone up!","门厅里一片漆黑——她已经上楼去了！"
"He mounted, swinging the balloon on his finger.","他一边上楼，一边用手指将气球晃来晃去。"
"Fleur was standing before a mirror.","弗勒正站在镜子前。"
"“What on earth’s that?” she said.","“那是什么东西啊？”她问道。"
"The blood returned to Michael’s heart.","血又流回到迈克尔的心里。"
"Curious how he had dreaded its having anything to do with her!","真奇怪，他刚才多么担心这个东西会和她有关系啊！"
"“Don’t know, darling; fell on my hat—must belong to heaven.”","“不知道，亲爱的，它落在了我的帽子上——一定是从天上掉下来的。”"
"And he batted it.","说着他把它拍了起来。"
"The balloon floated, dropped, bounded twice, wobbled and came to rest.","气球飘上去，落下来，弹了两下，晃了一会儿，就停住不动了。"
"“You ARE a baby, Michael.","“你真是个孩子，迈克尔。"
"I believe you bought it.”","我相信是你买的。”"
"Michael came closer, and stood quite still.","迈克尔向她走近了些，就站住不动了。"
"“My hat!","“天啊！"
"What a misfortune to be in love!”","爱上一个人是多么不幸啊！”"
"“You think so!”","“你是这样想的！”"
"“Il y a toujours un qui baise, et l’autre qui ne tend pas la joue.”","“既有吻别人的人，也有不肯把脸给人吻的人。”"
"“But I do.”","“但是我愿意。”"
"“Fleur!”","“弗勒！”"
"Fleur smiled.","弗勒笑了。"
"“Baise away.”","“尽情地吻吧。”"
"Embracing her, Michael thought: ‘She holds me—does with me what she likes; I know nothing of her!’","迈克尔抱着她，心里想：“她征服了我——她喜欢对我怎样就怎样吧，我一点儿也弄不懂她！”"
"And there arose a small sound—from Ting-a-ling smelling the balloon.","这时响起了一阵轻微的声音——小叮铃正在嗅那只气球。"

"Part II","第二卷"
"Chapter I","第一章"
"The Mark Falls","马克贬值"
"The state of the world had been getting more and more on Soames’ nerves ever since the general meeting of the P. P. R. S. It had gone off with that fatuity long associated by him with such gatherings—a watertight rigmarole from the chairman; butter from two reliable shareholders; vinegar from shareholders not so reliable; and the usual ‘gup’ over the dividend.","自从天佑再保险公司召开股东大会以来，索姆斯对世界局势越来越感到不安。长期以来他一直把愚蠢和这种会议联系在一起，这次大会进行过程中也充满了愚蠢的言论——董事长的无懈可击的冗长废话、两位可靠的股东的奉承话、几位不太可靠的股东的尖酸刻薄的话以及关于红利的惯常的“闲谈”。"
"He had gone there glum, come away glummer.","他去开会时闷闷不乐，离开时更是愁容满面。"
"From a notion once taken into his head Soames parted more slowly than a cheese parts from its mites.","一旦一个想法在索姆斯脑中形成，再要他放弃它，简直比小虫子离开奶酪还要慢。"
"Two-sevenths of foreign business, nearly all German!","七分之二的国外业务，几乎全部都是德国的！"
"And the mark falling!","而马克正在贬值！"
"It had begun to fall from the moment that he decided to support the dividend.","从他决定支持分红的那个时候起，马克就开始贬值了。"
"And why?","是什么原因呢？"
"What was in the wind?","会发生什么事情呢？"
"Contrary to his custom, he had taken to sniffing closely the political columns of his paper.","他一反平日的习惯，开始密切注意他读的那份报纸的政治专栏。"
"The French—he had always mistrusted them, especially since his second marriage—the French were going to play old Harry, if he was not greatly mistaken!","法国人——他向来不信任他们，尤其是从他第二次婚姻之后——除非他大错特错，法国人又要兴风作浪了！"
"Their papers, he noticed, never lost a chance of having a dab at English policy; seemed to think they could always call the tune for England to pipe to!","他注意到，他们的报纸从来不放过任何一个抨击英国政策的机会，他们似乎认为总能对英国发号施令！"
"And the mark and the franc, and every other sort of money, falling.","而马克和法郎以及其他各种货币，都在贬值。"
"And, though in Soames was that which rejoiced in the thought that one of his country’s bits of paper could buy a great quantity of other countries’ bits of paper, there was also that which felt the whole thing silly and unreal, with an ever-growing consciousness that the P. P. R. S. would pay no dividend next year.","虽然索姆斯一想到自己国家的一张纸可以买到其他国家的许多张纸就感到高兴，但是他也觉得整件事情既愚蠢又虚幻，而且他越来越清楚地知道，天佑再保险公司明年不会分红了。"
"The P. P. R. S. was a big concern; no dividend would be a sign, no small one, of bad management.","天佑再保险公司是一家大公司，不分红是经营不善的标志，还是一个不小的标志。"
"Assurance was one of the few things on God’s earth which could and should be conducted without real risk.","普天之下，能够而且应该经营得毫无实际风险的事业屈指可数，保险业就是其中之一。"
"But for that he would never have gone on the Board.","要不是这个原因，当初他是绝不会加入这个董事会的。"
"And to find assurance had not been so conducted and that by himself, was—well!","如今保险业并非经营得毫无实际风险，而发现这一点的人正是他自己，这真是——唉！"
"He had caused Winifred to sell, anyway, though the shares had already fallen slightly.","不管怎样，他已经让威妮弗雷德把股票卖掉了，虽然股票已经略微下跌了一些。"
"“I thought it was such a good thing, Soames,” she had said plaintively: “it’s rather a bore, losin’ money on the shares.”","“我以为它是件好东西呢，索姆斯，”她伤心地说，“在股票上赔了钱，真讨厌！”"
"He had answered without mercy: “If you don’t sell, you’ll lose more.”","他毫不留情地回答说：“如果不卖掉，你会赔更多。”"
"And she had done it.","于是她把股票卖掉了。"
"If the Rogers and Nicholases who had followed him into it hadn’t sold too—well, it was their look out!","如果之前跟着他买进的罗杰和尼古拉斯两家人至今还没有卖掉股票——呃，那就是他们自己的事情了！"
"He had made Winifred warn them.","他已经让威妮弗雷德提醒过他们了。"
"As for himself, he had nothing but his qualifying shares, and the missing of a dividend or two would not hurt one whose director’s fees more than compensated.","至于他自己，除了取得董事资格所必需的股份外，他一无所有，少拿一两次分红对他也没有什么损害，因为他的董事酬劳足以弥补损失，而且绰绰有余。"
"It was not, therefore, private uneasiness so much as resentment at a state of things connected with foreigners and the slur on his infallibility.","因此，与其说这是他个人的不安，还不如说是对与外国人有关的事态以及对他一贯正确的破灭所产生的愤恨。"
"Christmas had gone off quietly at Mapledurham.","圣诞节在梅普尔达勒姆汉静悄悄地过去了。"
"He abominated Christmas, and only observed it because his wife was French, and her national festival New Year’s Day.","他非常不喜欢圣诞节，因为他的妻子是法国人，而她的民族节日是元旦，所以他只能过圣诞节。"
"One could not go so far as to observe that, encouraging a foreign notion.","他总不至于要过元旦，以助长外国人的观念吧。"
"But Christmas with no child about—he still remembered the holly and snapdragons of Park Lane in his own childhood—the family parties; and how disgusted he had been if he got anything symbolic—the thimble, or the ring—instead of the shilling.","但是过圣诞节却没有孩子在身边——他还记得自己小时候公园巷里的冬青树和金鱼草——那些家庭聚会；如果他得到的只是象征性的东西——顶针或者戒指——而不是先令，他是多么厌烦。"
"They had never gone in for Santa Claus at Park Lane, partly because they could see through the old gentleman, and partly because he was not at all a late thing.","在公园巷，他们从来就不喜欢圣诞老人，一部分是因为他们看穿了这位老先生，一部分是因为圣诞老人一点儿也不新奇。"
"Emily, his mother, had seen to that.","他的母亲埃米莉注意到了那一点。"
"Yes; and, by the way, that William Gouldyng, Ingerer, had so stumped those fellows at the Heralds’ College, that Soames had dropped the enquiry—it was just encouraging them to spend his money for a sentimental satisfaction which did not materialise.","的确如此。顺便提一下，威廉·古尔丁·英格勒这个名字，竟然难住了纹章院的那帮家伙，使索姆斯放弃了追查——继续查下去只不过是鼓励他们花他的钱，使他获得一种无法实现的感情上的满足而已。"
"That narrow-headed chap, ‘Old Mont,’ peacocked about his ancestry; all the more reason for having no ancestry to peacock about.","“老蒙特”，这个心胸狭窄的家伙，炫耀着他的祖宗家世；越是没有祖宗家世可炫耀的人，越有理由这样做。"
"The Forsytes and the Goldings were good English country stock—that was what mattered.","福赛特家族和戈尔丁家族都是英国乡村的名门望族——这才是最关键的。"
"And if Fleur and her child, if one came, had French blood in them—well, he couldn’t help it now.","如果弗勒和她的孩子，假如她生一个孩子，身上有法国血统——唉，现在他也无能为力啦。"
"In regard to the coming of a grandchild, Soames knew no more than in October.","关于是否会有一个外孙出生，索姆斯并不比10月份那时更有把握。"
"Fleur had spent Christmas with the Monts; she was promised to him, however, before long, and her mother must ask her a question or two!","弗勒是和蒙特一家人一起过圣诞节的，但是她已经答应他，不久就会要孩子，她妈妈必须去问问情况了！"
"The weather was extremely mild; Soames had even been out in a punt fishing.","天气非常暖和，索姆斯甚至乘坐方头平底船出去游钓。"
"In a heavy coat he trailed a line for perch and dace, and caught now and then a roach—precious little good, the servants wouldn’t eat them, nowadays!","他穿了件厚厚的外套，拖着一根钓线，去钓鲈鱼和鲦鱼，偶尔还能钓到一条拟鲤——这种鱼毫无用处，如今连仆人都不吃了！"
"His grey eyes would brood over the grey water under the grey sky; and in his mind the mark would fall.","他那双灰色的眼睛注视着灰色天空下那灰色的水面，脑子里却想着马克要贬值。"
"It fell with a bump on that eleventh of January when the French went and occupied the Ruhr.","1月11日那天，当法国人出兵攻占了鲁尔区的时候，马克突然贬值了。"
"He said to Annette at breakfast: “Your country’s cracked!","他在吃早餐时对安妮特说：“你的国家疯了！"
"Look at the mark now!”","看看现在的马克！”"
"“What do I care about the mark?” she had answered over her coffee.","“我干吗要关心马克呢？”她边喝咖啡边回答，"
"“I care that they shall not come again into my country.","“我只关心德国人不要再闯入我的国家。"
"I hope they will suffer a little what we have suffered.”","我希望他们也受一点儿我们以前受过的苦！”"
"“You,” said Soames; “you never suffered anything.”","“你，”索姆斯说，“你从来没有受过什么苦。”"
"Annette put her hand where Soames sometimes doubted the existence of a heart.","安妮特把手放在心口上，索姆斯有时怀疑那地方是否真的有一颗心。"
"“I suffered here,” she said.","“我这儿受过苦。”她说。"
"“I didn’t notice it.","“我没有发现过。"
"You never went without butter.","你从来没有缺少过黄油。"
"What do you suppose Europe’s going to be like now for the next thirty years!","你认为在今后的30年里欧洲会变成什么样子！"
"How about British trade?”","英国的贸易又会怎样？”"
"“We French see before our noses,” said Annette with warmth.","“我们法国人只管眼前的事。”安妮特激动地说，"
"“We see that the beaten must be kept the beaten, or he will take revenge.","“我们明白要让战败国始终处于战败国的地位，否则他们就会进行报复。"
"You English are so sloppy.”","你们英国人太多愁善感了。”"
"“Sloppy, are we?” said Soames.","“我们多愁善感？”索姆斯说，"
"“You’re talking like a child.","“你说话就像个小孩一样。"
"Could a sloppy people ever have reached our position in the world?”","一个多愁善感的民族能达到我们在世界上的地位吗？”"
"“That is your selfishness.","“那是因为你们自私自利。"
"You are cold and selfish.”","你们既冷酷无情又自私自利。”"
"“Cold, selfish and sloppy—they don’t go together.","“冷酷无情、自私自利和多愁善感——这有些互相矛盾啊。"
"Try again.”","继续说。”"
"“Your slop is in your thought and your talk; it is your instinct that gives you your success, and your English instinct is cold and selfish, Soames.","“你们的多愁善感在你们的思想和言论里。给你们带来成功的是你们的本能，而你们英国人的本能就是冷酷无情和自私自利，索姆斯。"
"You are a mixture, all of you, of hypocrisy, stupidity and egoism.”","你和你们所有人都是虚伪、愚蠢和自私的混合体。”"
"Soames took some marmalade.","索姆斯拿了些果酱。"
"“Well,” he said, “and what are the French?—cynical, avaricious and revengeful.","“那么，”他说，“法国人又怎样呢？——愤世嫉俗、贪得无厌和睚眦必报。"
"And the Germans are sentimental, heady and brutal.","德国人则是感情用事、顽固任性和野蛮残忍。"
"We can all abuse each other.","我们都可以互相辱骂。"
"There’s nothing for it but to keep clear.","除了避免接触之外别无他法。"
"And that’s what you French won’t do.”","但这正是你们法国人不愿意做的。”"
"Annette’s handsome person stiffened.","安妮特挺直了漂亮的身躯。"
"“When you are tied to a person, as I am tied to you, Soames, or as we French are tied to the Germans, it is necessary to be top dog, or to be bottom dog.”","“当你和一个人联系在一起的时候，就像我和你联系在一起一样，索姆斯，或者像我们法国人和德国人联系在一起一样，你必须处于支配地位，否则就处于被支配地位。”"
"Soames stayed his toast.","索姆斯放下了他的烤面包。"
"“Do you suppose yourself top dog in this house?”","“你认为你自己在这个家里处于支配地位吗？”"
"“Yes, Soames.”","“是的，索姆斯。”"
"“Oh!","“哦！"
"Then you can go back to France tomorrow.”","那么你明天可以回法国去了。”"
"Annette’s eyebrows rose quizzically.","安妮特嘲弄般地扬起了眉毛。"
"“I would wait a little longer, my friend; you are still too young.”","“我还要再等一段时间，我的朋友，你还很年轻呢。”"
"But Soames had already regretted his remark; he did not wish any such disturbance at his time of life, and he said more calmly:","但是索姆斯已经后悔刚才说过的话了，他不希望在他这把年纪的时候还发生这样的争吵，于是他较为平静地说："
"“Compromise is the essence of any reasonable existence between individuals or nations.","“妥协是人与人或国与国之间合理生存的要素。"
"We can’t have the fat thrown into the fire every few years.”","我们不能每隔几年就闹一次。”"
"“That is so English,” murmured Annette.","“这就是典型的英国人。”安妮特喃喃地说，"
"“We others never know what you English will do.","“我们外国人从来不知道你们英国人要做什么。"
"You always wait to see which way the cat jumps.”","你们总是见风使舵。”"
"However deeply sympathetic with such a reasonable characteristic, Soames would have denied it at any ordinary moment—to confess to temporising was not, as it were, done.","无论索姆斯多么认同这种合情合理的特性，若在平时，他一定不会承认的——承认自己见风使舵，可以说那是绝对不行的。"
"But, with the mark falling like a cartload of bricks, he was heated to the point of standing by his nature.","但是，随着马克像一车砖块跌落似的贬值，他已经被激怒到出于本性地挺身而出了。"
"“And why shouldn’t we?","“我们为什么不能这样做呢？"
"Rushing into things that you’ll have to rush out of!","难道非要我们卷入那些你们必须摆脱的事情里去吗！"
"I don’t want to argue.","我不想争论。"
"French and English never did get on, and never will.”","法国人和英国人从来没有和睦相处过，而且永远不会和睦相处。”"
"Annette rose.","安妮特站了起来。"
"“You speak the truth, my friend.","“你说的是事实，我的朋友。"
"Entente, mais pas cordiale.","协商，但并不友好。"
"What are you doing today?”","你今天打算做什么？”"
"“Going up to town,” said Soames glumly.","“到城里去。”索姆斯闷闷不乐地说，"
"“Your precious Government has put business into Queer Street with a vengeance.”","“你的宝贝政府的复仇行为已经把经济逼入绝境了。”"
"“Do you stay the night?”","“你在那儿过夜吗？”"
"“I don’t know.”","“不知道。”"
"“Adieu, then, jusqu’ au revoir!”","“再会，那么，以后再见！”"
"And she got up.","说完她就上楼去了。"
"Soames remained brooding above his marmalade—with the mark falling in his mind—glad to see the last of her handsome figure, having no patience at the moment for French tantrums.","索姆斯仍然看着他的果酱沉思——心里想着马克贬值——他很高兴看到她那漂亮的身躯离开，因为此刻他实在是不能容忍她那法国式的坏脾气。"
"An irritable longing to say to somebody “I told you so” possessed him.","他现在急切地渴望对某个人说“我早警告过你了”。"
"He would have to wait, however, till he found somebody to say it to.","但是，他现在只能等，直到找到这么个人之后才能对他说。"
"A beautiful day, quite warm; and, taking his umbrella as an assurance against change, he set out for the station.","天气晴朗，非常暖和。他带着雨伞，以防变天，动身去了车站。"
"In the carriage going up they were talking about the Ruhr.","在进城去的车厢里，人们正在谈论着鲁尔区的事情。"
"Averse from discussion in public, Soames listened from behind his paper.","索姆斯不喜欢当众议论，他就用报纸遮住脸听着。"
"The general sentiment was surprisingly like his own.","大家的态度和他的态度惊人地相似。"
"In so far as it was unpleasant for the Huns—all right; in so far as it was unpleasant for British trade—all wrong; in so far as love of British trade was active and hate of Huns now passive—more wrong than right.","只要是对德国佬不利的——都对；只要是对英国贸易不利的——都错；只要对英国贸易的爱是积极的，对德国佬的恨是消极的——错多对少。"
"A Francophil remark that the French were justified in making themselves safe at all costs, was coldly received.","一个亲法派的人说法国人不惜一切代价确保自身安全的做法是合情合理的，大家听了都反应冷淡。"
"At Maidenhead a man got in whom Soames connected automatically with disturbance.","在梅登黑德站上来一个人，索姆斯自然而然地把他和骚乱联系在了一起。"
"He had much grey hair, a sanguine face, lively eyes, twisting eyebrows, and within five minutes had asked in a breezy voice whether anyone had heard of the League of Nations.","他的头发斑白，面色红润，眼神活跃，眉毛弯曲。还不到五分钟，他就用一种轻松愉快的声音发话了，问是否有人听说过国际联盟。"
"Confirmed in his estimate, Soames looked round the corner of his paper.","索姆斯觉得自己的判断得到了证实，他从报纸的一角向外看去。"
"Yes, that chap would get off on some hobby-horse or other!","是的，那个家伙要开始鼓吹自己喜欢的话题了。"
"And there he went!","他果然开始了！"
"The question—said the newcomer—was not whether the Germans should get one in the eye, the British one in the pocket, or the French one in the heart, but whether the world should get peace and goodwill.","问题——这个新来的家伙说——不在于德国人是不是应该当头挨一棒，英国人是不是应该在口袋里大捞一把，或者法国人是不是应该在情感上宣泄一下，而在于这个世界是不是应该获得和平与友好。"
"Soames lowered his paper.","索姆斯放下了报纸。"
"If—this fellow said—they wanted peace, they must sink their individual interests, and think in terms of collective interest.","如果——这个家伙说——他们想要和平，就必须放下个人利益，而去考虑集体利益。"
"The good of all was the good of one!","集体的利益就是个人的利益！"
"Soames saw the flaw at once.","索姆斯一眼就看出了破绽。"
"That might be, but the good of one was not the good of all.","这话也许是对的，但是个人的利益不一定是集体的利益。"
"He felt that if he did not take care he would be pointing this out.","他觉得如果自己一不小心就会指出这一点的。"
"The man was a perfect stranger to him, and no good ever came of argument.","他和这个人素不相识，跟这种人争论毫无意义。"
"Unfortunately his silence amid the general opinion that the League of Nations was ‘no earthly,’ seemed to cause the newcomer to regard him as a sympathiser; the fellow kept on throwing his eyebrows at him!","不幸的是，在大家都认为国际联盟“毫无希望”的时候，索姆斯的沉默似乎使那个新来的家伙把他当成了一个同情者，从而不断地向他使眼色！"
"To put up his paper again seemed too pointed, and his position was getting more and more false when the train ran in at Paddington.","他若再拿起报纸来，就似乎显得太有针对性了，正当他的处境越来越容易让人误会的时候，火车驶入了帕丁顿车站。"
"He hastened to a cab.","他急忙下车，走向一辆出租车。"
"A voice behind him said:","一个声音在他背后说："
"“Hopeless lot, sir, eh!","“一群无药可救的人，先生，唉！"
"Glad to see YOU saw my point.”","很高兴看到您能理解我的观点。”"
"“Quite!” said Soames.","“没错！”索姆斯说，"
"“Taxi!”","“出租车！”"
"“Unless the League of Nations functions, we’re all for Gehenna.”","“除非国际联盟发挥作用，否则我们全都得下地狱。”"
"Soames turned the handle of the cab door.","索姆斯转动出租车的门把手。"
"“Quite!” he said again.","“没错！”他又说了一句，"
"“Poultry!” and got in.","“家禽街！”然后就上了车。"
"He was not going to be drawn.","他不想被人纠缠。"
"The fellow was clearly a firebrand!","那个家伙显然是个煽动者！"
"In the cab the measure of his disturbance was revealed.","在出租车里，他的烦躁程度显现出来了。"
"He had said ‘Poultry,’ an address that ‘Forsyte, Bustard and Forsyte’ had abandoned two-and-twenty years ago when, merged with ‘Cuthcott, Holliday and Kingson,’ they became ‘Cuthcott, Kingson and Forsyte.’","他刚才说的“家禽街”，早在22年前，“福赛特、巴斯塔德和福赛特”公司就已经放弃不用这个地址了。那时他们和“卡斯考特、霍利迪和金森”公司合并，变成了“卡斯考特、金森和福赛特”公司。"
"Rectifying the error, he sat forward, brooding.","纠正了地址的错误之后，他朝前坐好，心里沉思着。"
"Fall of the mark!","马克贬值！"
"The country was sound about it, yes—but when they failed to pay the next dividend, could they rely on resentment against the French instead of against the directors?","国家对此有着充分的准备，是的——但是下次当他们不能分红的时候，他们能指望人们对法国人的怨恨会代替对董事们的怨恨吗？"
"Doubtful!","不大可能！"
"The directors ought to have seen it coming!","董事们应该预见到会发生这样的事情！"
"That might be said of the other directors, but not of himself—here was a policy that he personally never would have touched.","对其他的董事也许可以这样说，但是对他自己却不能这么说——这种政策是他本人从来没有接触过的。"
"If only he could discuss the whole thing with some one—but old Gradman would be out of his depth in a matter of this sort.","要是他能把整个事情和某人探讨一下就好了——但是这种问题不是老格雷德曼力所能及的。"
"And, on arrival at his office, he gazed with a certain impatience at that changeless old fellow, sitting in his swivel chair.","于是，他一到自己的办公室，就有点儿不耐烦地注视着那个坐在转椅中的一成不变的老家伙。"
"“Ah!","“啊！"
"Mr. Soames, I was hopin’ you might come in this morning.","索姆斯先生，我正盼着您今天早上能来呢。"
"There’s a young man been round to see you from the P. P. R. S. Wouldn’t give his business, said he wanted to see you privately.","有一个天佑再保险公司的年轻人来看您。他不肯说明来意，只说要单独和您见一面。"
"Left his number on the ‘phone.”","他留下了电话号码。”"
"“Oh!” said Soames.","“哦！”索姆斯说。"
"“Quite a young feller—in the office.”","“一个非常年轻的小伙子——在办公室工作。”"
"“What did he look like?”","“他长得什么样子？”"
"“Nice, clean young man.","“文雅、干净的年轻人。"
"I was quite favourably impressed—name of Butterfield.”","给我的印象非常不错——名叫巴特菲尔德。”"
"“Well, ring him up, and let him know I’m here.”","“那么，给他打电话，告诉他我在这儿。”"
"And going over to the window, he stood looking out on to a perfectly blank wall.","说完他走到窗前，站在那里望着窗外一面光秃秃的墙壁。"
"Suited to a sleeping partner, his room was at the back, free from disturbance.","为了适合他匿名合伙人的身份，他的房间设在后面，不受打扰。"
"Young man!","年轻人！"
"The call was somewhat singular!","这次拜访有些非同寻常！"
"And he said over his shoulder: “Don’t go when he comes, Gradman, I know nothing of him.”","他回过头说：“等他来了，你不要走开，格雷德曼，我一点儿也不了解他。”"
"The world changed, people died off, the mark fell, but Gradman was there—embodiment, faithful and grey, of service and integrity—an anchor.","世界改变了，逝者已逝，马克贬值了，但是格雷德曼还在那里——他是贡献与正直的化身，忠诚而又老练——一个可以依靠的人。"
"Gradman’s voice, grating, ingratiating, rose.","格雷德曼那刺耳而讨好的声音响了起来。"
"“This French news—it’s not nice, Mr. Soames.","“这条法国新闻——可不太妙啊，索姆斯先生。"
"They’re a hasty lot.","他们是一帮轻率的家伙。"
"I remember your father, Mr. James, coming into the office the morning the Franco-Prussian war was declared—quite in his prime then, hardly more than sixty, I should say.","我记得在普法战争宣战那天早上，您的父亲詹姆斯先生走进办公室——那时他正值壮年，还不到60岁，我记得。"
"Why, I recall his very words: ‘There,’ he said, ‘I told them so.’","哦，我想起了他的原话。‘你瞧，’他说，‘我早就告诉过他们要打仗了。’"
"And here they are—at it still.","现在他们——仍然要打。"
"The fact is, they’re cat and dog.”","事实就是，他们是猫狗不相容。”"
"Soames, who had half turned, resumed his contemplation of a void.","索姆斯半转过身，继续凝视着那一片空白处，沉思开了。"
"Poor old Gradman dated!","可怜的老格雷德曼落伍了！"
"What would he say when he heard that they had been insuring foreign business?","如果他听到他们一直在给外国生意做保险，他会怎么说呢？"
"Stimulated by the old-time quality of Gradman’s presence, his mind ranged with sudden freedom.","由于受到格雷德曼身上的往日情怀的感染，他的思绪突然自由翱翔起来。"
"He himself had another twenty years, perhaps.","或许他自己还能再活20年吧。"
"What would he see in that time?","到那时他会看到些什么呢？"
"Where would old England be at the end of it?","古老的英国最后会变成什么样子？"

"“Mr. Butterfield, sir.”","“巴特菲尔德先生来了，先生。”"
"H’m!","嗬！"
"The young man had been very spry.","这个年轻人来得可真快。"
"Covered by Gradman’s bluff and greasy greeting, he “took a lunar,” as his Uncle Roger used to call it.","在格雷德曼那既直率又圆滑的招呼的掩护之下，他可以像他叔叔罗杰过去常说的那样“观察一下”。"
"The young fellow, in a neat suit, a turndown collar, with his hat in his hand, was a medium modest-looking chap.","这个小伙子穿着一套整洁的翻领西服，手里拿着帽子，身材中等，态度谦恭。"
"Soames nodded.","索姆斯点点头。"
"“You want to see me?”","“你想要见我？”"
"“Alone, if I might, sir.”","“我想单独见您，如果可以的话，先生。”"
"“Mr. Gradman here is my right-hand man.”","“这位格雷德曼先生是我的得力助手。”"
"Gradman’s voice purred gratingly: “You can state your business.","格雷德曼的声音刺耳地响了起来：“你尽管说明你的来意。"
"Nothing goes outside these walls, young man.”","任何事情都不会传出去的，年轻人。”"
"“I’m in the office of the P.P.R.S., sir.","“我在天佑再保险公司的办公室工作，先生。"
"The fact is, accident has just put some information in my hands, and I’m not easy in my mind.","事情是这样的，我意外地得到了一些消息，我感到心里不安。"
"Knowing you to be a solicitor, sir, I preferred to come to you, rather than go to the chairman.","因为我知道您是一名律师，先生，所以我宁愿来找您，也不愿去找董事长。"
"As a lawyer, would you tell me: Is my first duty to the Society, being in their employ?”","作为一名律师，请您告诉我：作为公司的雇员，我的首要职责是不是要对它负责？”"
"“Certainly,” said Soames.","“当然。”索姆斯说。"
"“I don’t like this job, sir, and I hope you’ll understand that I’m not here for any personal motive—it’s just because I feel I ought to.”","“我不喜欢这份工作，先生，而且我希望您能明白我到这里来不是出于任何个人目的——而是因为我觉得我应该这样做。”"
"Soames regarded him steadily.","索姆斯一直注视着他。"
"Though large and rather swimming, the young man’s eyes impressed him by their resemblance to a dog’s.","虽然这个年轻人的眼睛又大又水灵，但是给他的印象却像是一条忠实的狗的眼睛。"
"“What’s it all about?” he said.","“究竟是什么事情？”他说。"
"The young man moistened his lips.","这个年轻人舔了舔嘴唇。"
"“The insurance of our German business, sir.”","“是我们在德国的保险业务，先生。”"
"Soames pricked his ears, already slightly pointed by Nature.","索姆斯那双天生就稍微有点儿尖的耳朵竖已经了起来。"
"“It’s a very serious matter,” the young man went on, “and I don’t know how it’ll affect me, but the fact is, this morning I overheard a private conversation.”","“这件事非常严重，”这个年轻人接着说，“我不知道这件事会对我产生什么影响，但事实是，今天早上我无意间听到一段私人谈话。”"
"“Oh!” said Soames.","“哦！”索姆斯说。"
"“Yes, sir.","“是的，先生。"
"I quite understand your tone, but the very first words did it.","我非常理解您的反应，但是第一句话就让我忍不住偷听下去。"
"I simply couldn’t make myself known after hearing them.","我不能让他们知道我听到了他们的谈话。"
"I think you’ll agree, sir.”","我想您会同意的，先生。”"
"“Who were the speakers?”","“谈话的人是谁？”"
"“The manager, and a man called Smith—I fancy by his accent his name’s a bit more foreign—who’s done most of the agenting for the German business.”","“经理和一个叫做史密斯的人——听他的口音，我猜想他的名字更像是个外国人的——他代理绝大部分的德国业务。”"
"“What were the words?” said Soames.","“他们谈了些什么？”索姆斯说。"
"“Well, sir, the manager was speaking, and then this Smith said: ‘Quite so, Mr. Elderson, but we haven’t paid you a commission on all this business for nothing; if the mark goes absolutely phut, you will have to see that your Society makes it good for us!’”","“嗯，先生，当时经理正在说话，然后这个史密斯说：‘的确如此，埃尔德森先生，但是在整个业务中我们不是白给你们佣金的，如果马克彻底完蛋了，你就得设法让你的公司赔偿我们的损失！’”"
"The intense longing, which at that moment came on Soames to emit a whistle, was checked by sight of Gradman’s face.","那一刻，索姆斯十分渴望吹个口哨，但是一看到格雷德曼脸上的表情，他抑制住了这种强烈的渴望。"
"The old fellow’s mouth had opened in the nest of his grizzly short beard; his eyes stared puglike, he uttered a prolonged: “A-ow!”","那个老家伙的嘴在他那灰白的鸟巢似的短须里张开了，他的眼睛瞪得像哈巴狗一样，发出一声拖长的“啊——呦！”"
"“Yes,” said the young man, “it was a knock-out!”","“是的，”年轻人说，“真是耸人听闻！”"
"“Where were you?” asked Soames, sharply.","“当时你在哪儿？”索姆斯厉声问道。"
"“In the lobby between the manager’s room and the board room.","“在经理室和董事会会议室之间的走廊里。"
"I’d just come from sorting some papers in the boardroom, and the manager’s door was open an inch or so.","我刚在会议室整理完一些文件，出来的时候，经理室的门开着一英寸左右的缝。"
"Of course I know the voices well.”","当然我非常熟悉他们的声音。”"
"“What after?”","“后来呢？”"

"I’d had more than enough, sir, I assure you.”","我听到的已经够多了，先生，我向您保证。”"
"Suspicion and surmise clogged Soames’ thinking apparatus.","怀疑和猜测充斥着索姆斯的大脑。"
"Was this young fellow speaking the truth?","这个小伙子说的是真话吗？"
"A man like Elderson—the risk was monstrous!","像埃尔德森这样的人——居然冒这样大的风险！"
"And, if true, what was the directors’ responsibility?","那么，如果是真的，董事们的责任是什么？"
"But proof—proof?","但是证据——证据呢？"
"He stared at the young man, who looked upset and pale enough, but whose eyes did not waver.","他盯着这个年轻人。年轻人看起来焦虑不安，脸色很苍白，但他的目光却很坚定。"
"Shake him if he could!","想办法诈一诈他！"
"And he said sharply:","于是他厉声说："
"“Now mind what you’re saying!","“你得注意你所说的话！"
"This is most serious!”","这是非常严重的！”"
"“I know that, sir.","“我知道，先生。"
"If I’d consulted my own interest, I’d never have come here.","如果考虑到我个人的利益，我绝不会到这来。"
"I’m not a sneak.”","我不是一个告密的人。”"
"The words rang true, but Soames did not drop his caution.","这些话听起来是真的，但是索姆斯没有放松警惕。"
"“Ever had any trouble in the office?”","“你以前在办公室出过什么问题吗？”"
"“No, sir, you can make enquiry.","“没有，先生，您可以去查问。"

"Soames thought suddenly: ‘Good heavens!","索姆斯突然想到：“天哪！"
"He’s shifted it on to me, and in the presence of a witness!","他把这件事推到我身上了，而且还有一个证人在场！"
"And I supplied the witness!’","而这个证人又是我提供的！”"
"“Have you any reason to suppose,” he said, “that they became aware of your being there?”","“依你看，”他说，“他们是不是发现了你当时在那里呢？”"
"“They couldn’t have, I think.”","“他们不会知道的，我想。”"
"The implications of this news seemed every second more alarming.","这个消息的含义似乎每一秒钟都让人更加担忧。"
"It was as if Fate, kept at bay all his life by clever wrist-work, had suddenly slipped a thrust under his guard.","就像命运之神，一生都以巧妙的腕力使对手无法近身，却突然被对手趁其不备刺了一剑。"
"No good to get rattled, however—must think it out at leisure!","不管怎样，惊慌失措毫无用处——必须从容不迫地把它想清楚！"
"“Are you prepared, if necessary, to repeat this to the Board?”","“如果有必要，你是否准备把这件事向董事会再说一遍？”"

"“Well, sir, I’d much rather have held my tongue; but if you decide it’s got to be taken up, I suppose I must go through with it now.","“哦，先生，我倒宁愿保持沉默，但如果您决定必须这么做的话，我想我一定会奉陪到底。"
"I’m sure I hope you’ll decide to leave it alone; perhaps it isn’t true—only why didn’t Mr. Elderson say: ‘You ruddy liar!’?”","我是真的希望您会决定要不要管它，或许这件事不是真的——只是为什么埃尔德森先生不说：‘你这个大骗子！呢？’”"
"Exactly!","的确如此！"
"Why didn’t he?","他为什么不说呢？"
"Soames gave a grunt of intense discomfort.","索姆斯非常不安地咕哝了一声。"
"“Anything more?” he said.","“还有别的吗？”他说。"
"“No, sir.”","“没有了，先生。”"
"“Very well.","“很好。"

"No satisfaction whatever in this sudden fulfilment of his prophetic feeling about Elderson.","虽然他对埃尔德森的预感突然得到了证实，但是他一点儿也不感到满意。"

"When Gradman said a thing was delicate, it meant that it was the sort of matter on which he was accustomed to wait for orders—presumptuous even to hold opinion!","当格雷德曼说一件事情很微妙的时候，就意味着对于这类事情他向来是惟命是从的——就连有想法都是很冒昧的！"
"But had he got one?","但是他有没有想法呢？"
"Well, one would never know!","哦，没有人会知道！"
"The old chap would sit and rub his nose over it till Kingdom Come.","这个老家伙会一直坐在那里对着这件事擦鼻子，直到上西天。"
"“I shan’t act in a hurry,” he said, almost angrily: “I can’t see to the end of this.”","“我不能贸然行事，”他几乎生气地说，“我还没有摸透这件事。”"
"Every hour confirmed that statement.","那句话每时每刻都在得到证实。"
"At lunch the tape of his city club showed the mark still falling—to unheard-of depths!","午餐时，城市俱乐部的行情收录带上显示马克仍然在贬值——跌到了一种闻所未闻的程度！"
"How they could talk of golf, with this business on his mind, he could not imagine!","心里装着这件事，他简直无法想象他们怎么还能谈论高尔夫球！"
"“I must go and see that fellow,” he said to himself.","“我要去见见那个家伙，”他自言自语道，"
"“I shall be guarded.","“我要保持警惕。"
"He may throw some light.”","或许他会露出一些破绽。”"
"He waited until three o’clock and repaired to the P. P. R. S. ","一直等到3点钟，他才到天佑再保险公司去。"
"Reaching the office, he sought the Board room.","一到公司，他就找到董事会会议室。"
"The chairman was there in conference with the manager.","董事长正在那里和经理开会。"
"Soames sat down quietly to listen; and while he listened he watched that fellow’s face.","索姆斯静静地坐下来听着，一边听一边注视着那家伙的脸。"
"It told him nothing.","从他脸上看不出什么。"
"What nonsense people talked when they said you could tell character from faces!","有人说你能从脸上看出人的性格，这简直是胡说八道！"
"Only a perfect idiot’s face could be read like that.","只有纯粹的白痴才能让人从脸上看出来。"
"And here was a man of experience and culture, one who knew every rope of business life and polite society.","而眼下这个人却是一个有经验有文化的人，他熟悉商业生活和上流社会的一切规则。"
"The hairless, neat features exhibited no more concern than the natural mortification of one whose policy had met with such a nasty knock.","他那光秃秃的头顶和整洁的面容所表现出来的忧虑，只不过是一个经营方针遭到了严重打击的人自然而然的窘迫感而已。"
"The drop of the mark had already wiped out any possible profit on the next half-year.","马克贬值已经彻底抵消了下半年所有潜在的利润。"
"Unless the wretched thing recovered, they would be carrying a practically dead load of German insurance.","除非那该死的东西能恢复原状，否则他们就会背上一笔名存实亡的德国保险。"
"Really it was criminal that no limit of liability had been fixed!","之前竟没有确定责任限额，这真是犯罪！"
"How on earth could he ever have overlooked that when he came on the Board?","他加入董事会的时候怎么会忽略了这一点呢？"
"But he had only known of it afterwards.","但是他也是后来才知道这件事的。"
"And who could have foreseen anything so mad as this Ruhr business, or realised the slack confidence of his colleagues in this confounded fellow?","而且谁能预见到像鲁尔事件这么疯狂的事情呢，谁又能意识到他的同事们会对这个糊涂的家伙盲目信任呢？"
"The words “gross negligence” appeared ‘close up’ before his eyes.","“严重失职”这几个字像“特写镜头”一样浮现在他的眼前。"
"What if an action lay against the Board!","假如有人控告董事会怎么办！"
"Gross negligence!","严重失职！"
"At his age and with his reputation!","以他的年龄，凭他的声望！"
"Why!","唉！"
"The thing was plain as a pikestaff; for omitting a limit of liability this chap had got his commission!","这件事再明显不过了，由于忽略了责任限额，那家伙才拿到了他的佣金！"
"Ten per cent, probably, on all that business—he must have netted thousands!","可能有10%，在整个那笔生意上——他一定已经净赚了几千镑！"
"A man must be in Queer Street indeed to take a risk like that!","一个敢于冒那样风险的人，一定是走投无路了！"
"But conscious that his fancy was running on, Soames rose, and turned his back.","索姆斯意识到自己的想象没完没了，于是他站了起来，转过身去。"
"The action suggested another.","这个动作使他想到了另一个动作。"
"Simulate anger, draw some sign from that fellow’s self-control!","假装生气，从那个家伙的自我控制中找出一些迹象！"
"He turned again, and said pettishly: “What on earth were you about, Mr. Manager, when you allowed these contracts to go through without limit of liability?","他又回过身来，怒气冲冲地说：“你到底是怎么搞的，经理先生，没有制定责任限额就通过了这些合同？"
"A man of your experience!","像你这么有经验的人，居然干出这种事！"
"What was your motive?”","你的动机是什么？”"
"A slight narrowing of the eyes, a slight compression of the lips.","那家伙眼睛稍稍一眯，嘴唇微微一抿。"
"He had relied on the word ‘motive,’ but the fellow passed it by.","他原指望“动机”这个词会起作用，但那个家伙却把它避开了。"
"“For such high premiums as we have been getting, Mr. Forsyte, a limited liability was not possible.","“对于我们一直以来收取的如此高的保险费而言，福赛特先生，要设定责任限额是不太可能的。"
"This is a most outrageous development, and I’m afraid it must be considered just bad luck.”","这是十分异常的发展情况，恐怕只能把它归结于坏运气。”"
"“Unfortunately,” said Soames, “there’s no such thing as luck in properly regulated assurance, as we shall find, or I’m much mistaken.","“不幸的是，”索姆斯说，“我们将会发现，在管理得当的保险业中是不存在运气这类东西的，否则就是我大错特错了。"
"I shouldn’t be surprised if an action lay against the Board for gross negligence!”","如果有人控告董事会严重失职，我一点儿也不感到意外！”"
"That had got the chairman’s goat!—Got his goat?","这下倒把董事长惹怒了！——把他惹怒了？"
"What expressions they used nowadays!","如今他们用的都是些什么词啊！"
"Or did it mean the opposite?","或者这是正话反说？"
"One never knew!","谁知道呢！"
"But as for Elderson—he seemed to Soames to be merely counterfeiting a certain flusteration.","但是至于埃尔德森——在索姆斯看来，他只是在假装一副紧张不安的样子。"
"Futile to attempt to spring anything out of a chap like that.","试图从他那样的家伙身上套出些什么来，是白费劲了。"
"If the thing were true, the fellow must be entirely desperate, prepared for anything and everything.","如果这件事是真的，那个家伙一定彻底绝望了，肯定会铤而走险。"
"And since from Soames the desperate side of life—the real holes, the impossible positions which demand a gambler’s throw—had always been carefully barred by the habits of a prudent nature, he found it now impossible to imagine Elderson’s state of mind, or his line of conduct if he were guilty.","由于对索姆斯来说，人生绝望的一面——那些迫使赌徒孤注一掷的真实的困境和难以忍受的境地——一直都被他那谨慎的天性小心翼翼地隔绝了，如果埃尔德森有罪的话，他现在简直无法想象他的心理状态和行为方式会是什么样子。"
"For all he could tell, the chap might be carrying poison about with him; might be sitting on a revolver like a fellow on the film.","因为他现在能感觉到的是，那家伙可能随身带着毒药，也可能像电影里的人一样，屁股下坐着一把左轮手枪。"
"The whole thing was too unpleasant, too worrying for words.","整个这件事太让人不悦，太让人焦虑了，非言语所能表达。"
"And without saying any more he went away, taking nothing with him but the knowledge that their total liability on this German business, with the mark valueless, was over two hundred thousand pounds.","于是，他没有再说什么就离开了，他没有带走任何东西，只是得知了一条消息，由于马克变得一文不值，他们在德国业务上的负债总计超过20万英镑。"
"He hastily reviewed the fortunes of his co-directors.","他匆匆地估算了一下那些和他共事的董事们的财产。"
"Old Fontenoy was always in low water; the chairman a dark horse; Mont was in land, land right down in value, and mortgaged at that; old Cosey Mothergill had nothing but his name and his director’s fees; Meyricke must have a large income, but light come, light go, like most of those big counsel with irons in many fires and the certainty of a judgeship.","老福坦诺向来手头拮据；董事长的财产难以猜测；蒙特的财产是地皮，地皮正在贬值，并且都抵押出去了；老柯赛·莫德吉尔除了他的虚名和董事酬劳金外一无所有；迈里克一定有一大笔收入，但是来得快，去得也快，就像大多数的那些大律师，业务繁忙，而且肯定能当上法官。"
"Not a really substantial man among the lot, except himself!","这些人之中，除了他自己，没有一个是真正富裕的人！"
"He ploughed his way along, head down.","他低着头，脚步沉重地向前走着。"
"Public companies!","上市公司！"
"Preposterous system!","荒谬的制度！"
"You had to trust somebody, and there you were!","你不得不信任某一个人，然后你就落到了今天的境地！"
"It was appalling!","这可真可怕！"
"“Balloons, sir—beautiful colours, five feet circumference.","“气球，先生——漂亮的颜色，可以吹出五英尺的周长。"
"Take one, gentleman!”","买一个吧，先生！”"
"“Good gad!” said Soames.","“上帝啊！”索姆斯说。"
"As if the pricked bubble of German business were not enough!","好像戳破了德国业务的气泡还不够似的！"

"Chapter II","第二章"
"Victorine","维多琳"
"All through December balloons had been slack—hardly any movement about them, even in Christmas week, and from the Bickets Central Australia was as far as ever.","进入十二月以来，气球生意一直萧条——即使在圣诞节的那一周，生意也没什么起色。对于比克特夫妇来说，移居澳大利亚中部的梦想还是那么遥不可及。"
"The girl Victorine, restored to comparative health, had not regained her position in the blouse department of Messrs.Boney Blayds & Co.","维多琳的身体已经恢复得差不多了，但还是没有如期到博尼·布莱兹公司的女衬衣部报到。"
"They had given her some odd sewing, but not of late, and she had spent much time trying to get work less uncertain.","他们给过她一些琐碎的针线活，但是最近没有什么零活。她花了很长时间，就是想要找一份相对稳定的工作。"
"Her trouble was—had always been—her face.","她的问题出在——一直出在——她的脸上。"
"It was unusual.","她的脸与众不同。"
"People did not know what to make of a girl who looked like that.","人们不知道是什么使一个女孩出落成这样的。"
"Why employ one who without qualification of wealth, rank, fashion, or ability (so far as they knew) made them feel ordinary?","为什么非要雇佣一个没有财富、地位和品味，还缺乏能力（在他们看来），但又使他们相形见绌的员工呢？"
"For—however essential to such as Fleur and Michael—dramatic interest was not primary in the manufacture or sale of blouses, in the fitting-on of shoes, the addressing of envelopes, making-up of funeral wreaths, or the other ambitions of Victorine.","因为在制作或销售衬衣时，在试穿皮鞋时，在填写信封时，在做殡仪的花圈时，或者是在维多琳感兴趣的其他行当中，兴趣爱好不是她首要考虑的——尽管它对于弗勒和迈克尔那类人是不可或缺的。"
"Behind those large dark eyes and silent lips, what went on?","在那双黑黑的大眼睛和沉默的双唇后面，究竟发生过什么事情呢？"
"It worried Boney Blayds & Co., and the more wholesale firms of commerce.","这一切使博尼·布莱兹公司和更多的商业批发公司感到一丝不安。"
"The lurid professions—film-super, or mannequin—did not occur to one, of self-deprecating nature, born in Putney.","但是对于出生在帕特尼镇而且生来自卑的维多琳来说，像那种需要浓妆艳抹的职业——例如电影演员或者服装模特——都是从来没有想过的。"
"When Bicket had gone out of a morning with his tray and his balloons not yet blown up, she would stand biting her finger, as though to gnaw her way to some escape from this hand-to-mouth existence which kept her husband thin as a rail, tired as a rook, shabby as a tailless sparrow, and, at the expense of all caste feeling, brought them in no more than just enough to keep them living under a roof.","每天早晨，当比克特带着托盘和那些还没充气的气球离开家时，她就会站在那里一直咬着自己的手指，似乎要咬出一条摆脱这贫困生活的出路。贫困生活已经使她的丈夫骨瘦如柴，累得像只白嘴鸦，寒酸得像只秃尾巴的麻雀，而且，就算以丢掉自己社会地位为代价，也只能勉强不流落街头而已。"
"It had long been clear to them both that there was no future in balloons, just a cadging present.","他们两个人心里早就明白，气球只不过是一件贩卖的礼物，靠它是没有前途的。"
"And there smouldered in the silent, passive Victorine a fierce resentment.","所以维多琳沉默地压抑着，消极地积聚着一股愤恨之情。"
"She wanted better things for herself, for him, chiefly for him.","她要为自己，为他，主要是为他，争取更好的生活。"
"On the morning when the mark was bumping down, she was putting on her velveteen jacket and toque (best remaining items of her wardrobe), having taken a resolve.","在马克惨跌的那个清晨，她穿上短款棉绒上衣，戴上那顶小圆帽（这两件可是她衣橱里剩下的最好的东西了），心里已经做了决定。"
"Bicket never mentioned his old job, and his wife had subtly divined some cause beyond the ordinary for his loss of it.","比克特对之前那份工作只字未提，但是她已经能敏感地猜测到，他失业可能另有隐情。"
"Why not see if she could get him taken back?","为什么不再尝试一下呢，也许她能让比克特复职？"
"He had often said: “Mr. Mont’s a gent and a sort o’ socialist; been through the war, too; no high-and-mighty about HIM.”","他总是说：“蒙特先生可是个好人，是社会主义者那种类型的，还参加过大战，一点儿架子也没有，平易近人。”"
"If she could ‘get at’ this phenomenon!","要是她能和这位非凡人物“交流”就好了！"
"With the flush of hope and daring in her sallow cheeks, she took stock of her appearance from the window-glasses of the Strand.","蜡黄的脸上涌起了希望和勇敢带来的红晕，她不禁在斯特兰德大街的橱窗玻璃中打量着自己。"
"Her velveteen of jade-green always pleased one who had an eye for colour, but her black skirt—well, perhaps the wear and tear of it wouldn’t show if she kept behind the counter.","喜欢色彩艳丽的人总是喜欢她那件翠绿色的短棉绒上衣，但是她的黑裙子嘛——嗯，假如她站在柜台后面的话，就不会看出它的破旧了。"
"Had she brass enough to say that she came about a manuscript?","她有足够的胆量和勇气说她是因为书稿来的吗？"

"Yes! and then would come the question: “What name, please?”","对了！可能接待人会发问：“请问您贵姓？”"

"Really, her sallow, large-eyed face, with its dead-black, bobbed, frizzy-ended hair, was extraordinarily interesting—a little too refined and anaemic for the public; but, dash it all! the public couldn’t always have its Reckitt’s blue eyes, corn-coloured hair, and poppy cheeks.","她那张长着一双大眼睛的蜡黄色脸蛋，再配上乌黑、发梢卷曲的短发，的确引人注目——在一般大众看来，这副长相有些太过优雅和苍白了，但是，管他呢！人们眼前不能总是那种利洁时广告女郎的蓝眼睛、淡黄色的头发和红彤彤的脸颊。"
