"That girl’s figure wasn’t usual either, was it?","那位女士的身材挺出众的，是不是？"
"She’s thin, but she stands up straight.","她很瘦，但是站得笔直。"
"There’s a question I always want to ask, Miss Perren: Why do modern girls walk in a curve with their heads poked forward?","佩伦小姐，有个问题我一直想问，为什么那些时髦女性走路时总喜欢把头往前伸，让身子形成一条曲线呢？"
"They can’t all be built like that.”","她们不可能都长成那个模样。”"
"The secretary’s cheeks brightened.","女秘书脸红了。"
"“There IS a reason, Mr. Mont.”","“蒙特先生，这是有原因的。”"
"“Good!","“真的！"
"What is it?”","什么原因？”"
"The secretary’s cheeks continued to brighten.","女秘书的脸继续红着。"
"“I don’t really know whether I can—”","“我实在不知道我是否能——”"
"“Oh! sorry.","“哦！对不起。"
"I’ll ask my wife.","我问我妻子好了。"
"Only she’s quite straight herself.”","不过她的身板也挺得笔直。”"
"“Well, Mr. Mont, it’s this, you see: They aren’t supposed to have anything be—behind, and, of course, they have, and they can’t get the proper effect unless they curve their chests in and poke their heads forward.","“嗯，蒙特先生，是这样的，您看：她们不喜欢有东西在——后面，但是，当然，她们后面肯定是有东西的，所以除非她们把胸部收进去，把头伸在前面，她们不可能达到预计效果。"
"It’s the fashion-plates and mannequins that do it.”","穿着时髦的人和模特都这样。＂"
"“I see,” said Michael; “thank you, Miss Perren; awfully good of you.","“我明白了，”迈克尔说，“谢谢你，佩伦小姐，你真是太好了。"
"It’s the limit, isn’t it?”","那样子让人难以接受，是不是？”"
"“Yes, I don’t hold with it, myself.”","“是，我自己不那样。”"
"“No, quite!”","“不，你一点儿也不那样！”"
"The secretary lowered her eyelids and withdrew.","女秘书低下眼皮，走了出去。"
"Michael sat down and drew a face on his blotting-paper.","迈克尔坐下，在那张吸墨水纸上画了一张脸。"
"It was not Victorine’s....","那不是维多琳的脸……"
"Armed with the note to Aubrey Greene, Victorine had her usual lunch, a cup of coffee and a bit of heavy cake, and took the tube towards Chelsea.","维多琳拿着写给奥布里·格林的那张便条，像往常一样，用一杯咖啡和一点儿油酥蛋糕当午餐，就乘地铁去了切尔西。"
"She had not succeeded, but the gentleman had been friendly and she felt cheered.","虽然比克特复职的事没办成，但是那位先生和蔼可亲，使她受到鼓舞。"
"At the studio door was a young man inserting a key—very elegant in smoke-grey Harris tweeds, a sliding young man with no hat, beautifully brushed-back bright hair, and a soft voice.","画室门口，一个年轻人正把钥匙插进门锁里——一个没戴帽子、看着挺机灵的小伙子，穿着一身烟灰色哈里斯粗花呢制服，显得很雅致，光亮的头发漂亮地朝后梳着，声音非常柔和。"
"“Model?” he said.","“是模特吗？”他说。"
"“Yes, sir, please.","“是的，先生。"
"I have a note for you from Mr. Mont.”","蒙特先生让我捎一张便条。”"
"“Michael?","“迈克尔？"
"Come in.”","进来吧。”"
"Victorine followed him in.","维多琳随他走进去。"
"It was ‘not half’ sea-green in there; a high room with rafters and a top light, and lots of pictures and drawings on the walls, and as if they had slipped off on to the floor.","屋内是一片海绿色，房子很高，屋顶有许多椽子和一扇天窗，墙上挂着许多素描和画像，而且看起来它们就像要滑落到地板上了。"
"A picture on an easel of two ladies with their clothes sliding down troubled Victorine.","画架上的一幅画令维多琳感到不安，画的是两位裸体妇人，她们的衣服滑落在一旁。"
"She became conscious of the gentleman’s eyes, sea-green like the walls, sliding up and down her.","此时，她注意到那位先生正用像墙壁一样的海绿色的眼睛上下打量着自己。"
"“Will you sit for anything?” he asked.","“我要开始画了，您可以坐好吗？”他问。"
"Victorine answered mechanically: “Yes, sir.”","维多琳机械地回答：“可以，先生。”"
"“Do you mind taking your hat off?”","“您不介意把帽子摘了吧？”"
"Victorine took off the toque, and shook out her hair.","维多琳摘下帽子，把头发抖开。"
"“Ah!” said the gentleman.","“啊！”先生说道，"
"“I wonder.”","“我觉得奇怪。”"
"Victorine wondered what.","维多琳不知道他奇怪什么。"
"“Just sit down on the dais, will you?”","“坐在台子上，好吗？”"
"Victorine looked about her, uncertain.","维多琳迟疑地朝四周环顾。"
"A smile seemed to fly up his forehead and over his slippery bright hair.","一丝微笑好像飞过他的前额，掠过他那光亮的头发。"
"“This is your first shot, then?”","“这是您第一次试画吗？”"
"“Yes, sir.”","“是的，先生。”"
"“All the better.”","“那更好。”"
"And he pointed to a small platform.","说着他用手指指那个小平台。"
"Victorine sat down on it in a black oak chair.","维多琳坐在平台上的一把黑色橡木椅子上。"
"“You look cold.”","“您看上去感觉好像有些冷。”"
"“Yes, sir.”","“是的，先生。”"
"He went to a cupboard and returned with two small glasses of a brown fluid.","他朝橱柜走去，拿了两个盛着棕色液体的小杯回来。"
"“Have a Grand Marnier?”","“喝杯柑曼怡吧？”"
"She noticed that he tossed his off in one gulp, and did the same.","她看他一饮而尽，于是自己也喝干了。"
"It was sweet, strong, very nice, and made her gasp.","这酒甘甜浓郁，很好喝，让她大吸一口气。"
"“Take a cigarette.”","“抽支烟。”"
"Victorine took one from a case he handed, and put it between her lips.","维多琳从他递过来的烟盒里拿了一支，把它放在嘴里。"
"He lit it.","他点着烟。"
"And again a smile slid up away over the top of his head.","又是一个微笑掠过他的前额。"
"“You draw it in,” he said.","“您抽吧，”他说，"
"“Where were you born?”","“您是哪里人？”"
"“In Putney, sir.”","“帕特尼人，先生。”"
"“That’s very interesting.","“很有意思。"
"Just sit still a minute.","只要静静地坐那儿一会。"
"It’s not as bad as having a tooth out, but it takes longer.","不像拔牙那么糟，只是坐的时间有些长。"
"The great thing is to keep awake.”","关键是要保持清醒。”"
"“Yes, sir.”","“好的，先生。”"
"He took a large piece of paper and a bit of dark stuff, and began to draw.","他拿了一张大纸和一块黑颜色的东西，开始画了起来。"
"“Tell me,” he said, “Miss—”","“告诉我，”他说，“您贵姓——”"
"“Collins, sir—Victorine Collins.”","“柯林斯，先生，——维多琳·柯林斯。”"
"Some instinct made her give her maiden name.","她本能地说出了自己结婚之前的名字。"
"It seemed somehow more professional.","这个习惯倒是很符合职业化的要求。"
"“Are you at large?”","“您没有固定工作？”"
"He paused, and again the smile slid up over his bright hair: “Or have you any other occupation?”","他停顿了一下，微笑再一次掠过光亮的头发，“还是您有其他职业？”"
"“Not at present, sir.","“目前没有，先生。"
"I’m married, but nothing else.”","我已经结婚了，就这些。”"
"For some time after that the gentleman was silent.","从这之后，那位先生沉默了许久。"
"It was interesting to see him, taking a look, making a stroke on the paper, taking another look.","她看着他看一眼自己，在纸上画一笔，然后再看一眼，觉得很有意思。"
"Hundreds of looks, hundreds of strokes.","看了有几百次，就画了几百笔。"
"At last he said: “All right!","最后他说：“好了！"
"Now we’ll have a rest.","现在我们歇会儿吧。"
"Heaven sent you here, Miss Collins.","柯林斯小姐，是上帝派您来到这儿的。"
"Come and get warm.”","过来暖暖身子吧。”"
"Victorine approached the fire.","维多琳走到壁炉旁。"
"“Do you know anything about expressionism?”","“您了解表现主义吗？”"
"“No, sir.”","“不，先生。”"
"“Well, it means not troubling about the outside except in so far as it expresses the inside.","“嗯，表现主义就是不考虑外在事物，除非外在事物能够表现出内心的东西。"
"Does that convey anything to you?”","您明白了吗？”"
"“No, sir.”","“不明白，先生。”"
"“Quite!","“没关系！"
"I think you said you’d sit for the—er—altogether?”","我记得您曾经说过，愿意坐着让我给您画一张裸身像？”"
"Victorine regarded the bright and sliding gentleman.","维多琳注视着面前这位既聪明又圆滑的先生。"
"She did not know what he meant, but she felt that he meant something out of the ordinary.","她没理解他的意思，但是她隐约感觉他指的是某种不同寻常的东西。"
"“Altogether what, sir?”","“先生，裸身像是什么？”"
"“Nude.”","“就是裸体画。”"
"“Oh!”","“哦！”"
"She cast her eyes down, then raised them to the sliding clothes of the two ladies.","她垂下眼睛，然后抬头朝两位妇人滑落的衣服望去。"
"“Like that?”","“跟那种一样？”"
"“No, I shouldn’t be treating you cubistically.”","“不是，我不想用立体派的手法来画您。”"
"A slow flush was burning out the sallow in her cheeks.","她那张蜡黄色的脸上慢慢地泛起了一丝红晕。"
"She said slowly:","她慢吞吞地说："
"“Does it mean more money?”","“这样的画法是不是能挣更多的钱？”"
"“Yes, half as much again—more perhaps.","“是啊，最起码翻一倍——或更多。"
"I don’t want you to if you’d rather not.","我不勉强您。"
"You can think it over and let me know next time.”","您自己认真考虑一下，下次来的时候告诉我。”"
"She raised her eyes again, and said: “Thank you, sir.”","她再次抬起眼睛，说：“谢谢您，先生。”"
"“Righto!","“好！"
"Only please don’t ‘sir’ me.”","就是别再叫我‘先生’了。”"
"Victorine smiled.","维多琳笑了。"
"It was the first time she had achieved this functional disturbance, and it seemed to have a strange effect.","这是她第一次做出这么反常的表情，却似乎产生了奇特的功效。"
"He said hurriedly: “By George!","他匆忙地说：“上帝啊！"
"When you smile, Miss Collins, I see you impressionistically.","柯林斯小姐，当您微笑时，我就从印象派角度来观察您。"
"If you’ve rested, sit up there again.”","如果您感觉休息得差不多了，请再坐回那里。”"
"Victorine went back.","维多琳走了回去。"
"The gentleman took a fresh piece of paper.","年轻人又拿了一张新的画纸。"
"“Can you think of anything that will keep you smiling?”","“您能不能想一些高兴的事，使您一直保持微笑呢？”"
"She shook her head.","她摇摇头。"
"That was a fact.","确实如此。"
"“Nothing comic at all?","“一件高兴的事都没有？"
"I suppose you’re not in love with your husband, for instance?”","打个比方，我猜，您不爱您的丈夫吧？”"
"“Oh! yes.”","“哦！爱呀。”"
"“Well, try that.”","“对呀，就想想这些。”"
"Victorine tried that, but she could only see Tony selling his balloons.","维多琳试着那样做，但她眼前只是浮现出托尼卖气球的场景。"
"“That won’t do,” said the gentleman.","“感觉不对，”年轻人说，"
"“Don’t think of him!","“别想他了。"
"Did you ever see ‘L’apres midi d’un Faune’?”","您看没看过《牧神的午后》？”"
"“No, sir.”","“没有，先生。”"
"“Well, I’ve got an idea.","“嗯，我有个主意。"
"‘L’apres midi d’une Dryade.’","《林中仙女的午后时光》。"
"About the nude you really needn’t mind.","关于裸体画的事您不必在意。"
"It’s quite impersonal.","它跟个人完全无关。"
"Think of art, and fifteen bob a day.","想想那是艺术，想想一天15个先令。"
"Shades of Nijinsky, I see the whole thing!”","尼金斯基的每个角度，我都画过！”"
"All the time that he was talking his eyes were sliding off and on to her, and his pencil off and on to the paper.","他说话这段时间，他的眼睛一直在她身上不停打量，他手里的铅笔在纸上忽上忽下。"
"A sort of infection began to ferment within Victorine.","一种影响力开始在维多琳心中起了作用。"
"Fifteen shillings a day!","一天15个先令。"
"Blue butterflies!","蓝色蝴蝶！"
"There was a profound silence.","一阵沉默。"
"His eyes and hand slid off and on.","他的眼睛和手一起一落地忙着。"
"A faint smile had come on Victorine’s face—she was adding up the money she might earn.","维多琳脸上浮现出一抹淡淡的微笑——此时此刻她心里正盘算着自己能挣多少钱呢。"
"At last his eyes and hand ceased moving, and he stood looking at the paper.","终于，他的手和眼睛不再移动了，之后他站在那里端详着那幅画。"
"“That’s all for today, Miss Collins.","“柯林斯小姐，今天就到这里吧。"
"I’ve got to think it out.","我得再仔细酝酿一下。"
"Will you give me your address?”","您给我留下您的地址好吗？”"
"Victorine thought rapidly.","维多琳脑子快速转动了一下。"
"“Please, sir, will you write to me at the post office.","“不好意思，先生，还是请您把信寄到邮局，我自己去领。"
"I don’t want my husband to know that I’m—I’m—”","我不想让我丈夫知道我在——我在——”"
"“Affiliated to art?","“与艺术打交道？"
"Well!","嗯！"
"Name of post office?”","邮局的名字？”"
"Victorine gave it and resumed her hat.","维多琳把邮局名称给了他，然后戴上帽子。"
"“An hour and a half, five shillings, thank you.","“一个半小时，五个先令，谢谢您。"
"And tomorrow, at half-past two, Miss Collins—not ‘sir.’”","明天两点半，柯林斯小姐——别再叫我先生了。”"
"“Yes, s—, thank you.”","“是，先——，谢谢您。”"
"Waiting for her ‘bus in the cold January air, the altogether appeared to Victorine improbable.","维多琳在一月的寒风中等着公共汽车。在她看来，裸体似乎是不太可能实现的。"
"To sit in front of a strange gentleman in her skin!","赤身裸体地坐在一位陌生男人面前！"
"If Tony knew!","要是托尼知道了！"
"The slow flush again burned up the sallow in her cheeks.","她那蜡黄的脸颊上又泛起了一丝红晕。"
"She climbed into the ‘bus.","她上了公共汽车。"
"But fifteen shillings!","但是15个先令啊！"
"Six days a week—why, it would be four pound ten!","一周六天——啊，那就是四镑十先令啊！"
"In four months she could earn their passage out.","只要四个月就能赚到他们去澳大利亚的路费了。"
"Judging by the pictures in there, lots must be doing it.","从放在那里的那些画像来看，肯定有不少人在干这一行。"
"Tony must know nothing, not even that she was sitting for her face.","绝不能让托尼知道，就连别人给她画脸这件事也不能让他知道。"
"He was all nerves, and that fond of her!","他异常敏感，而且很爱她！"
"He would imagine things; she had heard him say those artists were just like cats.","他会胡思乱想的，她曾经听他说过，那些艺术家就像猫一样。"
"But that gentleman had been very nice, though he did seem as if he were laughing at everything.","不过画画的那位年轻人倒是很正派，虽然他看起来对任何事情都不屑一顾。"
"She wished he had shown her the drawing.","她真希望他把那幅画给自己看看。"
"Perhaps she would see herself in an exhibition some day.","也许有一天，她能在展览会上看见自己的画像。"
"But without—oh!","但是不穿衣服——哦！"
"And suddenly she thought: ‘If I ate a bit more, I’d look nice like that, too!’","这时她突然想到：“我要是再多吃点儿，我也会像那幅画上的女子那样漂亮的！”"
"And as if to escape from the daring of that thought, she stared up into the face opposite.","似乎是要躲避这个大胆的想法，她抬起头，望着对面的那张脸。"
"It had two chins, was calm and smooth and pink, with light eyes staring back at her.","那张脸双下巴、冷静、光滑、红润，一双灵敏的眼睛也在注视着她。"
"People had thoughts, but you couldn’t tell what they were!","人们都在思考，但你说不出他们都在思考什么！"
"And the smile which Aubrey Greene desired crept out on his model’s face.","于是奥布里·格林渴望的那种微笑悄悄浮上他模特的脸庞。"

"Chapter III","第三章"
"Michael Walks and Talks","迈克尔的游历和言论"
"The face Michael drew began by being Victorine’s, and ended by being Fleur’s.","迈克尔画的那张脸从描绘维多琳开始，到以描绘弗勒收尾。"
"If physically Fleur stood up straight, was she morally as erect?","假如弗勒身体站得笔直，那她在道德上又是否同样正直呢？"
"This was the speculation for which he continually called himself a cad.","这种想法一出现，总是让他觉得自己很龌龊。"
"He saw no change in her movements, and loyally refrained from enquiring into the movements he could not see.","他丝毫看不出弗勒有什么改变，同时他在极力避免自己去追问那些他不知道的事情。"
"But his aroused attention made him more and more aware of a certain cynicism, as if she were continually registering the belief that all values were equal and none of much value.","但是他那被激发的注意力愈发使他感觉到某种不屑一顾的态度，好像它已成了弗勒一贯信奉的信仰——所有价值观都是平等的，也没有什么价值观是有价值的。"
"Wilfrid, though still in London, was neither visible nor spoken of.","虽然威尔弗里德还在伦敦，但是看不见他的人影，大家也不提他。"
"“Out of sight and hearing, out of mind,” seemed to be the motto.","“眼不见，耳不闻，心不烦。”好像已经成为了至理名言。"
"It did not work with Michael—Wilfrid was constantly in his mind.","但是这句至理名言对迈克尔丝毫不起作用——他的心中总是有威尔弗里德的影子。"
"If Wilfrid were not seeing Fleur, how could he bear to stay within such tantalising reach of her?","假如威尔弗里德见不到弗勒，那他怎么能忍受那种可望而不可即的痛苦？"
"If Fleur did not want Wilfrid to stay, why had she not sent him away?","假如弗勒不想让威尔弗里德留下，那么为什么不打发他走呢？"
"He was finding it difficult, too, to conceal from others the fact that Desert and he were no longer pals.","如果对旁人隐瞒自己和德赛特已经不是好友了，他觉得也很难。"
"Often the impetus to go and have it out with him surged up and was beaten back.","好几次他都冲动地想找他说个清楚，但都克制住了。"
"Either there was nothing beyond what he already knew, or there was something—and Wilfrid would say there wasn’t.","可能确实没有什么他不知道的事情，也可能是有事情——并且威尔弗里德还是会说没有。"
"Michael accepted that without cavil; one did not give a woman away!","迈克尔无可奈何，一个男人是不会把自己的女人拱手相让的！"
"But he wanted to hear no lies from a War comrade.","但他想从一起打过仗的战友那里打听实情。"
"Between Fleur and himself no word had passed; for words, he felt, would add no knowledge, merely imperil a hold weak enough already.","弗勒和他之间没有发生过口角，他觉得吵架并不会加深对事情的了解，反而使原本脆弱的关系变得更糟。"
"Christmas at the ancestral manor of the Monts had been passed in covert-shooting.","圣诞节是在蒙特家祖传的庄园里度过的，人们在那里进行丛林打猎。"
"Fleur had come and stood with him at the last drive on the second day, holding Ting-a-ling on a lead.","第二天最后一次驱车外出打猎时，弗勒来了，站在他身旁，手里牵着小叮铃。"
"The Chinese dog had been extraordinarily excited, climbing the air every time a bird fell, and quite unaffected by the noise of guns.","这只中国犬特别兴奋，每次有鸟被打落时，它总是一跃而起，丝毫不受枪声的干扰。"
"Michael, waiting to miss his birds—he was a poor shot—had watched her eager face emerging from grey fur, her form braced back against Ting-a-ling.","迈克尔一边等待着他的猎物——他的技术不怎样——一边看着她那露在灰色皮毛领子外的充满渴望的脸颊。她的身子朝后倾，使劲拉着小叮铃。"
"Shooting was new to her; and under the stimulus of novelty she was always at her best.","打猎对她来说可是件新鲜事，而每当有新鲜刺激的事情时，她总是处在最佳的精神状态。"
"He had loved even her “Oh, Michaels!” when he missed.","当他没打中时，就连她的“哎呀，迈克尔，迈克尔！”他都愿意听。"
"She had been the success of the gathering, which meant seeing almost nothing of her except a sleepy head on a pillow; but, at least, down there he had not suffered from lurking uneasiness.","她是这次聚会的成功之处，除了晚上看见她头枕枕头香甜地睡着，白天几乎看不到她的人影。不过，至少在那里，他感觉不到潜在的痛苦。"
"Putting a last touch to the bobbed hair on the blotting paper, he got up.","他在吸水画纸上给短发加了最后一笔之后，就站了起来。"
"St. Paul’s, that girl had said.","那位女子说过，圣保罗大教堂。"
"He might stroll up and have a squint at Bicket.","他可以散步到那里，去看看比克特。"
"Something might occur to him.","他可能想起了什么。"
"Tightening the belt of his blue overcoat round his waist, he sallied forth, thin and sprightly, with a little ache in his heart.","他系好蓝色大衣的腰带，看起来很精干。然后，他带着一丝忐忑动身了。"
"Walking east, on that bright, cheerful day, nothing struck him so much as the fact that he was alive, well, and in work.","天气晴朗宜人，他朝东走去，心中竟涌起从未有过的感慨，感慨如今自己活着，活得还很好，并且拥有一份不错的工作。"
"So very many were dead, ill, or out of a job.","而有那么多的人已经离世、生病，或失业。"
"He entered Covent Garden.","他走进了科芬园。"
"Amazing place!","这是个令人惊异的地方！"
"A human nature which, decade after decade, could put up with Covent Garden was not in danger of extinction from its many ills.","尽管人性有许多弱点，人们数十年以来对科芬园的喜爱却没有濒临灭绝的危险。"
"A comforting place—one needn’t take anything too seriously after walking through it.","这是一个给人慰藉的地方——人们但凡在这里走上一圈，就会对世间万事看淡许多。"
"On this square island were the vegetables of the earth and the fruits of the world, bounded on the west by publishing, on the cast by opera, on the north and south by rivers of mankind.","广场西起出版社，东至歌剧院，南北两则是川流不息的人群。这里汇集了来自世界各地的蔬菜和水果。"
"Among discharging carts and litter of paper, straw and men out of drawing, Michael walked and sniffed.","迈克尔行走在卸货的大车、乱丢的纸屑和麦秆中，走在和周围景致不相协调的人群中间，边走边嗅闻着。"
"Smell of its own, Covent Garden, earthy and just not rotten!","科芬园有股特殊的泥土气味，但又不是泥土腐烂的气味！"
"He had never seen—even in the War—any place that so utterly lacked form.","即使是在大战中，他也从未见过如此凌乱不堪的地方。"
"Extraordinarily English!","非凡的英国人！"
"Nobody looked as if they had anything to do with the soil—drivers, hangers-on, packers, and the salesmen inside the covered markets, seemed equally devoid of acquaintanceship with sun, wind, water, earth or air—town types all!","似乎没人关心这片土壤——赶车的、不务正业的、打包工，还有在遮蔽的货摊里的小贩们——他们也跟阳光、风、水、大地，或者空气——跟这里的一切都毫不相干！"
"And—Golly!—how their faces jutted, sloped, sagged and swelled, in every kind of featural disharmony.","而且——上帝！——他们的脸怪模怪样、形态各异——向前伸着的、歪向一边的、下垂的、肿胀的。"
"What was the English type amongst all this infinite variety of disproportion?","在这么多不正常的模样中，哪一类才算是典型的英国脸呢？"
"There just wasn’t one!","一个也没有！"
"He came on the fruits, glowing piles, still and bright—foreigners from the land of the sun—globes all the same size and colour.","他来到水果摊前，一堆堆色彩鲜艳、表面光亮的水果静静地摆在那里——来自阳光充足地方的进口货——堆成了同样大小、同样颜色的圆圈。"
"They made Michael’s mouth water.","这些水果令迈克尔垂涎三尺。"
"‘Something in the sun,’ he thought; ‘there really is.’","“那才是真正产自阳光充足地方的水果。”他心想。"
"Look at Italy, at the Arabs, at Australia—the Australians came from England, and see the type now!","看看意大利、阿拉伯、澳大利亚——澳大利亚人来自英格兰，看看现在他们的模样！"
"Nevertheless—a Cockney for good temper!","不过——伦敦佬脾气好！"
"The more regular a person’s form and features, the more selfish they were!","一个人的体型和外貌越匀称正常，这个人越自私！"
"Those grape-fruit looked horribly self-satisfied, compared with the potatoes!","与土豆相比，那些葡萄柚就自负得多！"
"He emerged still thinking about the English.","他走出广场，脑子里还在想着英国人。"
"Well!","对！"
"They were now one of the plainest and most distorted races of the world; and yet was there any race to compare with them for good temper and for ‘guts’?","现在的英国人是世界上最平庸、最畸形的民族了，可是还有哪个民族能跟他们较量脾气和“厚颜无耻”呢？"
"And they needed those in their smoky towns, and their climate—remarkable instance of adaptation to environment, the modern English character!","但是对于他们而言，在那烟雾弥漫和多变的气候环境中，恰恰需要这种性格——适应环境，现代英国性格的一个典型例子！"
"‘I could pick out an Englishman anywhere,’ he thought, ‘and yet, physically, there’s no general type now!’","“我可以在任何一个地方认出英国人，”他心想，“但是，从外表体征上来讲，现在可没有一个通用类型了！”"
"Astounding people!","令人震惊的民族！"
"So ugly in the mass, yet growing such flowers of beauty, and such strange sprigs—like that little Mrs. Bicket; so unimaginative in bulk, yet with such a blooming lot of poets!","整体看是那么丑陋，却能培养出绝世美人，还有一群与众不同的佳人——就像小巧玲珑的比克特夫人那样；即使大多数人缺乏想象力，但是还是有着数不胜数的诗人才子！"
"How would old Danby like it, by the way, when Wilfrid took his next volume to some other firm; or rather what should he—Wilfrid’s particular friend!—say to old Danby?","顺便提一下，威尔弗里德把自己下一卷诗作拿给其他出版社时，不知老丹比会有何感想？换言之，他——这位威尔弗里德的特殊朋友——该如何向老丹比开口？"
"Aha!","啊哈！"
"He knew what he should say:","他知道他应该这么说："
"“Yes, sir, but you should have let that poor blighter off who snooped the ‘Copper Coins.’","“对了，先生，您应该宽恕那个偷了《铜币》的年轻人。"
"Desert hasn’t forgotten your refusal.”","德赛特可一直记着您拒绝了他。”"
"One for old Danby and his eternal inthe-rightness!","这是对老丹比和他那永远认为自己正确的想法的有力回击！"
"‘Copper Coin’ had done uncommonly well.","《铜币》销路很好。"
"Its successor would probably do uncommonly better.","接下来的书可能销路会更好。"
"The book was a proof of what he—Michael—was always saying: The ‘cockyolly-bird period’ was passing.","这本书就印证了他——迈克尔——一直说的话：“雏鸟时期”已经过去。"
"People wanted life again.","人们重新寻找生活的真谛。"
"Sibley, Walter Nazing, Linda—all those who had nothing to say except that they were superior to such as had—were already measured for their coffins.","西布莉、沃尔特·内津、琳达——只会自视清高却言之无物的人们——已经是气息奄奄了。"
"Not that they would know when they were in them; not blooming likely!","这并不意味着他们躺在棺材里的时候会明白这一切，这根本是不可能的！"
"They would continue to wave their noses and look down them!","他们会继续得意忘形，看不起那些人！"
"‘I’M fed-up with them,’ thought Michael.","“我十分厌恶他们，”迈克尔心想，"
"‘If only Fleur would see that looking down your nose is a sure sign of inferiority!’","“要是弗勒能明白看不起别人是自卑的表现，那该多好！”"
"And, suddenly, it came to him that she probably did.","于是，他突然想到，可能她已经明白了。"
"Wilfrid was the only one of the whole lot she had ever been thick with; the others were there because—well, because she was Fleur, and had the latest things about her.","在弗勒曾经密切交往的一群人中，威尔弗里德只是其中的一个。其他的人与她交往一则是因为——嗯，因为她是弗勒，还有就是弗勒身边总是汇集着时髦的事情。"
"When, very soon, they were no longer the latest things, she would drop them.","不久之后，当他们不再时髦时，弗勒自然而然就会抛弃他们。"
"But Wilfrid she would not drop.","但是她绝不会抛弃威尔弗里德的。"
"No, he felt sure that she had not dropped, and would not drop Wilfrid.","不，他肯定弗勒绝没有抛弃而且也绝不会放弃威尔弗里德的。"
"He looked up.","他抬头看看。"
"Ludgate Hill!","来到了拉德盖特山街！"
"“Near St. Paul’s—sells balloons?”","“在圣保罗大教堂附近——卖气球？”"
"And there—sure enough—the poor beggar was!","在那里——果然是他——那个可怜的家伙！"
"Bicket was deflating with a view to going off his stand for a cup of cocoa.","比克特为了到别处去喝一杯可可，正在把气球里的空气放掉。"
"Remembering that he had come on him by accident, Michael stood for a moment preparing the tones of surprise.","迈克尔想到他要装作偶然遇见，就故意站了一会儿，准备装出诧异的口气。"
"Pity the poor chap couldn’t blow himself into one of those coloured shapes and float over St. Paul’s to Peter.","令人遗憾的是，这个可怜的家伙不可能把自己吹到一个五颜六色的气球里，使他从圣保罗大教堂的上空一直飞到彼得那里去。"
"Mournful little cuss he looked, squeezing out the air!","他看上去的确像一只可怜虫，使劲地把气球里的空气挤出去。"
"Memory tapped sharply on his mind.","回忆强烈地涌上他的心头。"
"Balloon—in the square—November the first—joyful night!","气球——在广场上——11月1号——令人愉快的夜晚！"
"Special!","特别的！"
"Fleur!","弗勒！"
"Perhaps they brought luck.","也许它们带来了好运。"
"He moved and said in an astounded voice: “YOU, Bicket?","他走过去，用吃惊的语气说：“比克特，是你吗？"
"Is this your stunt now?”","你现在做这个生意吗？”"
"The large eyes of Bicket regarded him over a puce-coloured sixpennyworth.","比克特瞪着那双大眼睛，将目光从一个价值六便士的深褐色气球转移到他身上。"
"“Mr. Mont!","“蒙特先生！"
"Often thought I’d like to see you again, sir.”","我经常想着再能遇见您，先生。”"
"“Same here, Bicket.","“我也是啊，比克特。"
"If you’re not doing anything, come and have some lunch.”","你现在没什么生意的话，咱俩一起吃午饭吧。”"
"Bicket completed the globe’s collapse, and, closing his tray-lid, said: “Reelly, sir?”","比克特弄瘪了那个气球，随手关上了托盘的盖子，说道：“您说的是真的吗，先生？”"
"“Rather!","“当然啦！"
"I was just going into a fish place.”","我正想去一家海鲜餐馆。”"
"Bicket detached his tray.","比克特拿下托盘。"
"“I’ll leave this with the crossing-sweeper.”","“我把这个放在路口清洁工那儿。”"
"He did so, and followed at Michael’s side.","他交给清洁工后，就跟在迈克尔身后的一侧走着。"
"“Any money in it, Bicket?”","“比克特，这生意赚钱吗？”"
"“Bare livin’, sir.”","“勉强维持，先生。”"
"“How about this place?","“这环境怎么样？"
"We’ll have oysters.”","我们吃点儿生蚝吧。”"
"A little saliva at the corner of Bicket’s mouth was removed by a pale tongue.","比克特用苍白的舌头舔了一下嘴角的唾沫。"
"At a small table decorated with white oilcloth and a cruet stand, Michael sat down.","迈克尔坐在了一张铺着白色油布和放着调味瓶架的小桌旁。"
"“Two dozen oysters, and all that; then two good soles, and a bottle of Chablis.","“两打生蚝，全套的佐料；另外再来两条新鲜的鳎目鱼，和一瓶夏布利酒。"
"Hurry up, please.”","麻烦快一些。”"
"When the white-aproned fellow had gone about it, Bicket said simply:","当系着白围裙的服务员拿着菜单去准备的时候，比克特迟钝地说了句："
"“My Gawd!”","“我的上帝啊！”"
"“Yes, it’s a funny world, Bicket.”","“是啊，比克特，这是个可笑的世界。”"
"“It is, and that’s a fact.","“是啊，是这样。"
"This lunch’ll cost you a pound, I shouldn’t wonder.","这顿午饭要花费您一镑钱吧。"
"If I take twenty-five bob a week, it’s all I do.”","假如我一周挣25先令，那肯定要全花上了。”"
"“You touch it there, Bicket.","“比克特，你说到了痛处。"
"I eat my conscience every day.”","我每天都在泯灭自己的良心。”"
"Bicket shook his head.","比克特摇摇头。"
"“No, sir, if you’ve got money, spend it.","“不是的，先生，如果您有钱，那就花吧。"
"I would.","要是我有钱我也会花的。"
"Be ‘appy if you can—there yn’t too many that are.”","及时行乐吧——能行乐的人不多啊。”"
"The white-aproned fellow began blessing them with oysters.","那个系白围裙的服务员端上来生蚝，请他们享用。"
"He brought them fresh-opened, three at a time.","他把那些新剖开的端上来，一次三只。"
"Michael bearded them; Bicket swallowed them whole.","迈克尔把鳃去掉，而比克特则狼吞虎咽地吞了下去。"
"Presently above twelve empty shells, he said:","过了一会儿，看着桌上12只空壳，他说："
"“That’s where the Socialists myke their mistyke, sir.","“先生，这是社会主义者的错误。"
"Nothing keeps me going but the sight of other people spendin’ money.","除去看到别人花钱之外，没有什么可以激励我继续活下去。"
"It’s what we might all come to with a bit of luck.","只要是有点儿运气，我们大家都能获得这种生活。"
"Reduce the world to a level of a pound a dy—and it won’t even run to that, they sy!","把世界的生活水平降低到一天一镑钱的水平——他们说，也许还不到一镑钱呢！"
"It’s not good enough, sir.","这还不够好，先生。"
"I’d rather ‘ave less with the ‘ope of more.","我宁愿现在少拿点儿，将来多得点儿。"
"Take awy the gamble, and life’s a frost.","没有冒险刺激，生活就平淡无趣了。"
"Here’s luck!”","祈求好运！”"
"“Almost thou persuadest me to be a capitalist, Bicket.”","“比克特，你这一席话就像是在劝我当一个资本家。”"
"A glow had come up in the thin and large-eyed face behind the greenish Chablis glass.","在浅绿色的夏布利酒杯后面，那张有着一双大眼睛的瘦削的脸上泛起了一片红晕。"
"“I wish to Gawd I had my wife here, sir.","“先生，我从内心希望我妻子能在这里。"
"I told you about her and the pneumonia.","我跟您说过我妻子和她得肺炎的事情。"
"She’s all right agyne now, only thin.","她现在康复了，只是很瘦弱。"
"She’s the prize I drew.","她是我亲手描绘出来的理想。"
"I don’t want a world where you can’t draw prizes.","我不希望拥有一个不能描绘理想的世界。"
"If it were all bloomin’ conscientious an’ accordin’ to merit, I’d never have got her.","假如当初一切全凭良心和依照个人成就办事的话，我现在肯定不会娶到我的妻子。"
"See?”","您明白吗？”"
"‘Me, too,’ thought Michael, mentally drawing that face again.","“我也一样啊。”迈克尔心想，又在心里勾勒着那张脸。"
"“We’ve all got our dreams; mine’s blue butterflies—Central Austrylia.","“我们每个人都有梦想，我的愿望是得到那只蓝蝴蝶——去澳大利亚中部。"
"The Socialists won’t ‘elp me to get there.","社会主义者是不会帮助我去那里的。"
"Their ideas of ‘eaven don’t run beyond Europe.”","他们设想的天堂从未超出欧洲。”"
"“Cripes!” said Michael.","“谁知道呢！”迈克尔说，"
"“Melted butter, Bicket?”","“要融化的黄油吗，比克特？”"
"“Thank you, sir.”","“谢谢您，先生。”"
"Silence was not broken for some time, but the soles were.","一阵沉默，两人只是默默地吃着鳎目鱼。"
"“What made you think of balloons, Bicket?”","“比克特，你是怎么想起做气球生意的？”"
"“You don’t ‘ave to advertise, they do it for you.”","“你不必做广告，他们自己就给你做广告了。”"
"“Saw too much of advertising with us, eh?”","“你看了许多我们做的广告，嗯？”"
"“Well, sir, I did use to read the wrappers.","“嗯，先生，我确实经常欣赏书的封面。"
"Astonished me, I will sy—the number of gryte books.”","我想说——著作的数量真让人震惊。”"
"Michael ran his hands through his hair.","迈克尔用手快速捋了捋头发。"
"“Wrappers!","“书的封面！"
"The same young woman being kissed by the same young man with the same clean-cut jaw.","总是用一个胡子刮得干净的年轻男士吻年轻女子当封面。"
"But what can you do, Bicket?","比克特，可是又有什么办法呢？"
"They WILL HAVE IT. I tried to make a break only this morning—I shall see what comes of it.","他们一定就要这个。今天早晨我还想破除惯例——我想看看结果如何。”"
"“‘And I hope YOU won’t!’ he thought: ‘Fancy coming on Fleur outside a novel!’","“我真心希望你别这样做！”他心想，“要是弗勒上了小说封面，效果如何呢！”"
"“I did notice a tendency just before I left,” said Bicket, “to ‘ave cliffs or landskips and two sort of dolls sittin’ on the sand or in the grass lookin’ as if they didn’t know what to do with each other.”","“就在我离开之前，我的确看出了倾向，”比克特说，“悬崖或者峭壁与两个坐在沙滩上或者草地上的漂亮姑娘画在一起，看起来似乎不知道该如何相处。”"
"“Yes,” murmured Michael, “we tried that.","“是啊，”迈克尔低声说，“我们这样试过了。"
"It was supposed not to be vulgar.","本来以为那样做会避免落入俗套。"
"But we soon exhausted the public’s capacity.","但人们很快就厌烦了。"
"What’ll you have now—cheese?”","现在你要点儿什么呢——奶酪？”"
"“Thank you, sir; I’ve had too much already, but I won’t say ‘No.’”","“谢谢您，先生，我饱了，但是我也不会说不要的。”"
"“Two Stiltons,” said Michael.","“来两块斯蒂尔顿奶酪。”迈克尔说。"
"“How’s Mr. Desert, sir?”","“先生，德赛特先生好吗？”"
"Michael reddened.","迈克尔脸红了。"
"“Oh!","“哦！"
"He’s all right.”","他很好。”"
"Bicket had reddened also.","比克特脸也红了。"
"“I wish—I wish you’d let him know that it was quite a—an accident my pitchin’ on his book.","“我希望——希望您能告诉他，我拿他的书纯粹是一件——一件意外。"
"I’ve always regretted it.”","对于这件事我一直感到愧疚。”"
"“It’s usually an accident, I think,” said Michael slowly, “when we snoop other people’s goods.","“我想，通常这是偶然发生的，”迈克尔缓慢地说，“当我们拿别人东西时。"
"We never WANT to.”","我们从来都没想过要这么做。”"
"Bicket looked up.","比克特抬起了头。"
"“No, sir, I don’t agree.","“不是的，先生，我不同意。"
"‘Alf mankind’s predytory—only, I’m not that sort, meself.”","有半数的人是偷窃成性——只是，我自己绝不是那种人。”"
"In Michael loyalty tried to stammer “Nor is he.”","迈克尔忠厚老实，他也尝试结结巴巴地说：“他也不是那种人。”"
"He handed his cigarette case to Bicket.","他把烟盒递给比克特。"
"“Thank you, sir, I’m sure.”","“对此我确信无疑，谢谢您，先生。”"
"His eyes were swimming, and Michael thought: ‘Dash it!","他的眼里噙着泪水，迈克尔心里想：“该死的！"
"This is sentimental.","这真是多愁善感。"
"Kiss me good-bye and go!’","吻别之后就分手再见吧！”"
"He beckoned up the white-aproned fellow.","他示意那系着白围裙的服务员过来。"
"“Give us your address, Bicket.","“给我留个地址，比克特。"
"If integuments are any good to you, I might have some spare slops.”","如果你需要衣服的话，我那里富余几件，可以送给你。”"
"Bicket backed the bill with his address and said, hesitating: “I suppose, sir, Mrs. Mont wouldn’t ‘ave anything to spare.","比克特在账单背面写下地址，然后吞吞吐吐地说：“我想蒙特太太不会有什么富余的衣服吧。"
"My wife’s about my height.”","我妻子的身高跟我相仿。”"
"“I expect she would.","“我想她会有的。"
"We’ll send them along.”","我们会把衣服送来的。”"
"He saw the ‘little snipe’s’ lips quivering, and reached for his overcoat.","他看着这个“小人物”嘴唇颤抖，然后就去拿他的大衣了。"
"“If anything blows in, I’ll remember you.","“如果碰巧有工作机会的话，我会记着你的。"
"Goodbye, Bicket, and good luck.”","再见了，比克特，祝你好远。”"
"Going east, because Bicket was going west, he repeated to himself the maxim: “Pity is tripe—pity is tripe!”","因为比克特朝西走，所以迈克尔往东走去，心里反复想着那句名言：“怜悯是扯淡——怜悯是扯淡！”"
"Then getting on a ‘bus, he was borne back past St. Paul’s.","接着他坐上了公共汽车，车往回开，路过了圣保罗大教堂。"
"Cautiously ‘taking a lunar’—as old Forsyte put it—he SAW Bicket inflating a balloon; little was visible of his face or figure behind that rosy circumference.","他仔细“观察一番”——就像老福赛特说过的那样——发现比克特正在吹气球，他的脸和身体几乎被那只玫瑰色气球遮住了。"
"Nearing Blake Street, he developed an invincible repugnance to work, and was carried on to Trafalgar Square.","车快到布莱克大街时，他对工作突然产生了一种不可阻挡的反感情绪，索性就一直坐到了特拉瓦尔加广场。"
"Bicket had stirred him up.","比克特让他思绪起伏。"
"The world was sometimes almost unbearably jolly.","这个世界有时简直是太有趣了。"
"Bicket, Wilfrid, and the Ruhr!”","比克特、威尔弗里德，还有鲁尔区！"
"Feeling is tosh!","感情是胡言乱语！"
"Pity is tripe!”","怜悯是扯淡！"
"He descended from his ‘bus, and passed the lions towards Pall Mall.","他下了公共汽车，经过蓓尔美尔街的两座狮子。"
"Should he go into ‘Snooks’ and ask for Bart?","他有必要去“轻蔑”俱乐部找准爵爷吗？"
"No use—he would not find Fleur there.","没用——他不会在那里找到弗勒的。"
"That was what he really wanted—to see Fleur in the daytime.","那其实才是他真正的目的——在白天看见弗勒。"
"But—where?","但是——弗勒在哪儿呢？"
"She was everywhere to be found, and that was nowhere.","她有可能在任何地方，也就是说，有可能哪里都找不到她。"
"She was restless.","她闲不住。"
"Was that his fault?","那是他的过错吗？"
"If he had been Wilfrid—would she be restless?","如果他是威尔弗里德——那她会闲不住吗？"
"‘Yes,’ he thought stoutly, ‘Wilfrid’s restless, too.’","“是的，”他肯定地想着，“威尔弗里德也闲不住。”"
"They were all restless—all the people he knew.","他们都闲不住——所有他熟识的那些人都如此。"
"At least all the young ones—in life and in letters.","至少是那些年轻作家们——无论是在生活中还是在文学作品中。"
"Look at their novels!","看看他们写的小说！"
"Hardly one in twenty had any repose, any of that quality which made one turn back to a book as a corner of refuge.","20部作品里，几乎没有一本能带给人安静之感，缺少让人视书为避风港湾的品质。"
"They dashed and sputtered and skidded and rushed by like motor cycles—violent, oh! and clever.","他们犹如摩托车般冲撞，发出巨响、打滑和飞奔——啊！极为猛烈和娴熟。"
"How tired he was of cleverness!","他是多么厌恶这种娴熟！"
"Sometimes he would take a manuscript home to Fleur for her opinion.","有时他会给弗勒带一份原稿，征求一下她的意见。"
"He remembered her saying once: “This is exactly like life, Michael, it just rushes—it doesn’t dwell on anything long enough to mean anything anywhere.","他记得有一次她曾说过：“迈克尔，这跟生活一模一样，急速行进——不会为了表明什么而在任何地方、在任何事情上喋喋不休地做过久的停留。"
"Of course the author didn’t mean it for satire, but if you publish it, I advise you to put: ‘This awful satire on modern life’ outside the cover.”","当然，作者并不打算把它写成讽刺作品，但是如果你要出版，我建议你在封面上写下一句话：‘此书是对现代生活的强烈讽刺。’”"
"And they had.","他们这样做了。"
"At least, they had put: “This wonderful satire on modern life.”","至少他们写了一句话：“此书是对现代生活的绝妙讽刺。”"
"Fleur WAS like that!","弗勒就像这样！"
"She could see the hurry, but, like the author of the wonderful satire, she didn’t know that she herself veered and hurried, or—did she know?","她知道自己闲不住，但就像那部绝妙讽刺作品的作者一样，她丝毫不知道自己正在追逐着、忙碌着，又或者——她已经知道了？"
"Was she conscious of kicking at life, like a flame at air?","她是否意识到自己正在生活中冲撞，就像空气中的火焰一样？"
"He had reached Piccadilly, and suddenly he remembered that he had not called on her aunt for ages.","他已经到了皮卡迪利大街。突然间，他想起自己已经很久没有去看望她的姑姑了。"
"That was a possible draw.","那倒是可行的。"
"He bent his steps towards Green Street.","于是他向格林街走去。"
"“Mrs. Dartie at home?”","“达尔蒂夫人在家吗？”"
"“Yes, sir.”","“在家，先生。”"
"Michael moved his nostrils.","迈克尔吸了一下鼻子。"
"Fleur used—but he could catch no scent, except incense.","是弗勒用过的味道，但是他闻不到香水味，只是闻到了燃香的味道。"
"Winifred burnt joss-sticks when she remembered what a distinguished atmosphere they produced.","威妮弗雷德燃起线香，通常是因为她想起线香会制造出一种高雅气氛。"
"“What name?”","“您贵姓啊？”"
"“Mr. Mont.","“蒙特先生。"
"My wife’s not here, I suppose?”","我猜我的妻子不在这里吧？”"
"“No, sir.","“不在，先生。"
"Only Mrs. Val Dartie.”","屋里只有瓦尔·达尔蒂夫人。”"
"Mrs. Val Dartie!","瓦尔·达尔蒂夫人！"
"Yes, he remembered, nice woman—but not a substitute for Fleur!","嗯，他记起来了，是个长相标致的女人——但是无法取代弗勒！"
"Committed, however, he followed the maid.","既然已经通报了，不管怎样，他都得跟着女仆进去了。"
"In the drawing-room Michael found three people, one of them his father-in-law, who had a grey and brooding aspect, and, from an Empire chair, was staring at blue Australian butterflies’ wings under glass on a round scarlet table.","迈克尔在客厅见到了三个人，其中一位是他的岳父。他一副忧郁沉思的模样，坐在一张帝国时期的椅子上，凝视着压在绯红色圆桌玻璃下的澳大利亚的蓝蝴蝶翅膀。"
"Winifred had jazzed the Empire foundations of her room with a superstructure more suitable to the age.","威妮弗雷德已经在房间原有的帝国时期风格的基础上，增添了一些更适合当今时代特征的装饰，使房间看起来更加活泼动感一些。"
"She greeted Michael with fashionable warmth.","她用上流社会习惯的热情方式欢迎迈克尔。"
"It was good of him to come when he was so busy with all these young poets.","他每天忙于和青年诗人打交道，能抽空来作客，真是好极了。"
"“I thought ‘Copper Coin,’” she said—“what a NICE title!—such an intriguing little book.","“我想到《铜币》，”她说，“多好的书名啊！——让人着迷的小册子。"
"I do think Mr. Desert is clever!","我从内心认为德赛特先生智慧非凡！"
"What is he doing now?”","他现在忙什么呢？”"
"Michael said: “I don’t know,” and dropped on to a settee beside Mrs. Val.","迈克尔说：“我不太清楚。”说完便坐在瓦尔夫人旁边的长靠椅上。"
"Ignorant of the Forsyte family feud, he was unable to appreciate the relief he had brought in with him.","由于他之前丝毫不知道福赛特家族长期的矛盾，所以也根本不清楚因为自己的到来而使得气氛有所缓和。"
"Soames said something about the French, got up, and went to the window; Winifred joined him—their voices sounded confidential.","索姆斯说了一些关于法国人的事，就起身朝窗边走去；威妮弗雷德也跟着过去——他们说话声音很小，似乎很神秘。"
"“How is Fleur?” said Michael’s neighbour.","“弗勒好吗？”迈克尔的邻座问道。"
"“Thanks, awfully well.”","“谢谢您，她很好。”"
"“Do you like your house?”","“您喜欢您的房子吗？”"
"“Oh, fearfully.","“哦，很喜欢。"
"Won’t you come and see it?”","您不来看看吗？”"
"“I don’t know whether Fleur would—?”","“我不知道弗勒会不会——”"
"“Why not?”","“怎么会不呢？”"
"“Oh!","“哦！"
"Well!”","好吧！”"
"“She’s frightfully accessible.”","“她是很容易亲近的。”"
"She seemed to be looking at him with more interest than he deserved, to be trying to make something out from his face, and he added:","她似乎异常兴致勃勃地看着他，试图想从他的脸上看出什么。他接着说："
"“You’re a relation—by blood as well as marriage, aren’t you?”","“无论是从血缘还是从婚姻角度来说，您都是我们的亲戚，是不是？”"
"“Yes.”","“是的。”"
"“Then what’s the skeleton?”","“那么有什么不可以来的呢？”"
"“Oh! nothing.","“哦！没有啊。"
"I’ll certainly come.","我当然要来了。"
"Only—she has so many friends.”","只不过——她的朋友太多了。”"
"Michael thought: ‘I like this woman!’","迈克尔心想：“我喜欢这个女人！”"
"“As a matter of fact,” he said, “I came here this afternoon thinking I might find Fleur.","“事实上，”他说，“我今天下午来这儿，原以为弗勒在这儿呢。"
"I should like her to know you.","我希望她能和您多聊聊天。"
"With all the jazz there is about, she’d appreciate somebody restful.”","现在处处都是爵士音乐，她一定会喜欢文静的人。”"
"“Thank you.”","“谢谢您。”"
"“You’ve never lived in London?”","“您从来没在伦敦居住过吗？”"
"“Not since I was six.”","“我六岁之前在这里住过。”"
"“I wish she could get a rest—pity there isn’t a d-desert handy.”","“我希望她能休息一下——可惜这附近没有沙——沙漠。”"
"He had stuttered; the word was not pronounced the same—still!","他结巴起来，这个词的发音虽然有所不同——但仍然刺痛了他的心！"
"He glanced, disconcerted, at the butterflies.","他有些窘迫，看着那些蝴蝶。"
"“I’ve just been talking to a little Cockney whose S. O. S. is ‘Central Austrylia.’","“我刚才正好跟一个小伦敦佬说话，他的救赎地就是澳大利亚中部。"
"But what do you say—Have we got souls to save?”","但您说——咱们有需要拯救的灵魂吗？”"
"“I used to think so, but now I’m not so sure—something’s struck me lately.”","“我以前一直这样认为，但现在我不敢肯定了——最近有些事触动了我。”"
"“What was that?”","“是什么事呢？”"
"“Well, I notice that any one at all out of proportion, or whose nose is on one side, or whose eyes jut out, or even have a special shining look, always believes in the soul; people who are in proportion, and have no prominent physical features, don’t seem to be really interested.”","“嗯，我注意到，任何一个五官不端正的人，要么鼻子歪的，要么眼睛突出的，要么样子与众不同的人，他们总是相信灵魂；而那些五官端正、外貌没有明显缺陷的人，似乎就不关心他们的灵魂。”"
"Michael’s ears moved.","迈克尔的耳朵动了动。"
"“By Jove!” he said; “some thought!","“上帝啊！”他说，“有道理！"
"Fleur’s beautifully proportioned—SHE doesn’t seem to worry.","弗勒长得漂亮——所以她无忧无虑。"
"I’m not—and I certainly do.","而我长得不好看——所以我忧心忡忡。"
"The people in Covent Garden must have lots of soul.","那些在科芬园的人一定有很多灵魂。"
"You think ‘the soul’s’ the result of loose-gearing in the organism—sort of special consciousness from not working in one piece.”","您想‘灵魂’是生物体连接松散的结果——一种因为不能进行整体活动而产生的特殊感觉。”"
"“Yes, rather like that—what’s called psychic power is, I’m almost sure.”","“是啊，的确如此——我几乎可以断言，就是所谓的通灵能力。”"
"“I say, is your life safe?","“问一下，您的生活安全吗？"
"According to your theory, though, we’re in a mighty soulful era.","按照您的理论，我们正处于一个灵魂极其兴盛的时代。"
"I must think over my family.","我必须仔细考虑一下我的家庭。"
"How about yours?”","您的家庭怎么样？”"
"“The Forsytes!","“福赛特家族！"
"Oh, they’re quite too well-proportioned.”","哦，他们五官再端正不过了。”"
"“I agree, they haven’t any special juts so far as I’ve seen.","“我同意，在我看来，他们没有什么长相特殊的地方。"
"The French, too, are awfully close-knit.","法国人的长相也是很紧凑的。"
"It really is an idea, only, of course, most people see it the other way.","这的确是一种说法，只不过，当然了，大多数人不这样认为。"
"They’d say the soul produces the disproportion, makes the eyes shine, bends the nose, and all that; where the soul is small, it’s not trying to get out of the body, whence the barber’s block.","他们可能会说，灵魂导致了五官不端正——眼睛发亮、鼻子弯曲以及等等一系列说法。如果一个人的灵魂渺小，它是不会妄图摆脱肉体的，那些理发师的头型由此而来。"
"I’ll think about it.","我要思考一下这个问题。"
"Thanks for the tip.","感谢您的提示。"
"Well, do come and see us.","嗯，一定要到我家来。"
"Good-bye!","再见！"
"I don’t think I’ll disturb them in the window.","我想我就不去打扰窗边的两位了。"
"Would you mind saying I had to scoot?”","劳烦您替我跟他们说一声，我得赶紧走了。”"
"Squeezing a slim, gloved hand, receiving and returning a smiling look, he slid out, thinking: ‘Dash the soul, where’s her body?’","他紧握着那只纤细的戴手套的手，她微笑着答应了。他悄悄溜了出去，心想：“该死的灵魂，她的肉体在哪儿啊？”"

"Chapter IV","第四章"
"Fleur’s Body","弗勒的肉体"
"Fleur’s body, indeed, was at the moment in one of those difficult positions which continually threaten the spirit of compromise.","的确，此刻弗勒的肉体处境很困难，这困难的处境正在不断地威胁着她妥协的内心。"
"It was in fact in Wilfrid’s arms; sufficiently, at least, to make her say:","此时，她正在威尔弗里德的怀抱中。至少，这一举动足以让她说："
"“No, Wilfrid—you promised to be good.”","“别这样，威尔弗里德——你答应过我会守规矩的。”"
"It was a really remarkable tribute to her powers of skating on thin ice that the word ‘good’ should still have significance.","“守规矩”一词现在竟然还有意义，她如履薄冰的本事确实令人佩服。"
"For eleven weeks exactly this young man had danced on the edge of fulfilment, and was even now divided from her by two clenched hands pressed firmly against his chest, and the word ‘good’; and this after not having seen her for a fortnight.","整整11周了，这个年轻人一直在欲望的边缘垂死挣扎。即使是现在，弗勒仍然握紧双手挡在他的胸前，还让他“守规矩”，可是他已经两周没见到她了。"
"When she said it, he let her go, with a sort of violence, and sat down on a piece of junk.","她说完这句话后，他就放开了她，一副凶神恶煞的样子，坐在一堆废旧杂物上。"
"Only the sense of damnable iteration prevented him from saying: “It can’t go on, Fleur.”","只是因为他不想再重复了，才忍住没说：“不能这样下去了，弗勒。”"
"She knew that!","她何尝不知道呢！"
"And yet it did!","可是情况就是这样！"
"This was what perpetually amazed him.","这一点始终让他感到诧异。"
"How a poor brute could hang on week after week saying to her and to himself: “Now or never!” when it wasn’t either.","一个可怜虫怎么能每周都对她、对自己说：“现在不做就断绝关系！”而其实这两点他都办不到。"
"Subconsciousness, that, until the word ‘now’ had been reached, Fleur would not know her own mind, alone had kept him dancing.","他下意识地感觉到在所谓的“现在”实现之前，弗勒自己都不清楚她自己的心思，只有先晾着他了。"
"His own feelings were so intense that he almost hated her for indecision.","他对她的感情如此强烈，以至于他快受不了她的犹豫不决了。"
"And he was unjust.","但他错了。"
"It was not exactly indecision.","并不完全是犹豫不决。"
"Fleur wanted the added richness and excitement which Wilfrid’s affection gave to life, but without danger and without loss.","弗勒需要威尔弗里德的爱情给她的生活带来额外的丰富和刺激，而不会带来风险和损失。"
"How natural!","多自然的事啊！"
"His frightful passionateness was making all the trouble.","而他可怕的热情正是所有麻烦的根源。"
"Neither by her wish, nor through her fault, was he passionate!","他那热情既不是出于她的愿望，也不是由于她的过错！"
"And yet—it was both nice and proper to inspire passion; and, of course, she had the lurking sense that she was not ‘in the mode’ to cavil at a lover, especially since life owed her one.","不过——热情总能给人愉快和美好的感觉。当然，她还隐隐觉得，对情人过于挑剔有悖“时尚”，更何况她的生活缺少一个情人呢。"
"Released, she smoothed herself and said: “Talk of something sensible; what have you been writing?”","威尔弗里德放开手后，她整理了一下自己，说道：“谈点儿有意思的事吧，你最近在写些什么？”"
"“This.”","“这个。”"
"Fleur read.","弗勒翻了几页。"
"Flushing and biting her lips, she said:","她涨红了脸，咬着嘴唇，然后说道："
"“It’s frightfully bitter.”","“这个读起来让人很痛苦。”"
"“It’s frightfully true.","“却非常真实。"
"Does HE ever ask you now whether you see me?”","他现在还问你，你是否和我见面吗？”"
"“Never.”","“从来不问。”"
"“Why?”","“为什么？”"
"“I don’t know.”","“我也不知道。”"
"“What would you answer if he did?”","“如果他问起，你怎么作答？”"
"Fleur shrugged her shoulders.","弗勒耸了耸肩。"
"Desert said quietly: “Yes, that’s your attitude.","德赛特平静地说：“不错，这就是你的态度。"
"It can’t last, Fleur.”","不能这样下去了，弗勒。”"
"He was standing by the window.","此时，他正站在窗边。"
"She put the sheets down on his desk and moved towards him.","她把稿子放到书桌上，然后朝他走去。"
"Poor Wilfrid!","可怜的威尔弗里德！"
"Now that he was quiet she was sorry.","现在他平静了，她反倒难过起来。"
"He said suddenly: “Stop!","他突然说：“站住!"
"Don’t move!","别动！"
"HE’S down there in the street.”","他就在对面街上。”"
"Recoiling, she gasped: “Michael!","她一边后退，一边喘着气说：“迈克尔!"
"Oh!","哦！"
"But how—how could he have known?”","但是怎么——他怎么知道的呢？”"
"Desert said grimly: “Do you only know him as little as that?","德赛特冷冷地说：“你对他的了解就这么少吗？"
"Do you suppose he’d be there if he knew you were here?”","你觉得如果他知道你在这里，他还会站在那儿吗？”"
"Fleur winced.","弗勒畏缩了一下。"

"He had waited for the flippant; but he recognised in the tone something reverential, if not aghast.","他本以为会听到一句轻率无礼的话，可是，从那口气中他却听出了一种介于敬畏和惊奇之间的意思来。"

"When I was a youngster in Switzerland with my people, two of my sisters had some black cherries.","我小时候，一次和家人在瑞士玩，我的两个妹妹不知从哪里得到了一些黑樱桃。"

"An English climber there saw how upset they were, and ate the whole of the rest of the cherries—about two pounds—maggots, stones and all, just to show them.","当时在场的一个英国登山者见她们不舒服，就把剩下的樱桃全吃了——大约有两磅——蛆虫和果核也都吃了，就是吃给她们看的。"

"Tea, Ting?” and, turning up the lights, she rang the bell.","喝茶吗，叮铃？”于是她扭亮灯，按了按铃。"
"When her unexpected visitor had gone, she sat very still before the fire.","当这位不速之客离开后，她非常安静地坐在壁炉前。"
"To-day, when she had been so very nearly Wilfrid’s!","今天，她差一点儿就成为威尔弗里德的人了。"
"So Jon was not married!","原来乔恩还没结婚！"
"Not that it made any odds!","这样也并不意味着就有什么机会！"
"Things did not come round as they were expected to in books.","事情的发展并不像书里写的那样。"
"And anyway sentiment was swosh!","可是不管怎样，感情已经过去了！"
"Cut it out!","断了吧！"
"She tossed back her hair; and, getting hammer and nail, proceeded to hang the white monkey.","她把头发往后一捋，拿起榔头和钉子，动手去挂那幅白猿。"
"Between the two tea-chests with their coloured pearl-shell figures, he would look his best.","把它挂在两只彩色珍珠贝图案的茶具中间，会显得非常出色。"
"Since she couldn’t have Jon, what did it matter—Wilfrid or Michael, or both, or neither?","既然她得不到乔恩，那么无论得到威尔弗里德还是迈克尔，或者两个都得到，或者两个都失去，又有什么关系呢？"
"Eat the orange in her hand, and throw away the rind!","吃掉手里的橙子，把果皮扔掉！"
"And suddenly she became aware that Michael was in the room.","突然间，她发现迈克尔已经在房间里了。"
"He had come in very quietly and was standing before the fire behind her.","他静静地走到壁炉前面，站在她的身后。"
"She gave him a quick look and said:","她迅速瞥了他一眼，说道："
"“I’ve had Aubrey Greene here about a model you sent him, and Holly—Mrs. Val Dartie—she said she’d seen you.","“刚才奥布里·格林来过，提起你送过去的一个模特，还有霍莉——瓦尔·达尔蒂夫人——她说她见过你了。"
"Oh! and father’s brought us this.","哦！爸爸给我们带来了这个。"
"Isn’t it perfect?”","不错吧？”"
"Michael did not speak.","迈克尔没说话。"
"“Anything the matter, Michael?”","“有什么事吗，迈克尔？”"
"“No, nothing.”","“没有，没什么。”"
"He went up to the monkey.","他走到那幅画跟前。"
"From behind him now Fleur searched his profile.","弗勒审视着他的背影。"
"Instinct told her of a change.","她的直觉告诉她，一定有什么事情。"
"Had he, after all, seen her going to Wilfrid’s—coming away?","难道他最终还是看到她到威尔弗里德家去了——又从那里出来离开了？"
"“Some monkey!” he said.","“是只猴子！”他说，"
"“By the way, have you any spare clothes you could give the wife of a poor snipe—nothing too swell?”","“顺便问一句，你有什么多余的衣服可以送给一个可怜人的妻子吗——不用太漂亮？”"
"She answered mechanically: “Yes, of course!” while her brain worked furiously.","她机械地答道：“有，当然有！”她的脑子却在拼命地转着。"
"“Would you put them out, then?","“那么，把它们找出来好吗？"
"I’m going to make up a bunch for him myself—they could go together.”","我自己也打算给他凑几件——一起送过去。”"
"Yes!","不错！"
"He was quite unlike himself, as if the spring in him had run down.","他今天完全变了个人，好像他身上的发条已经坏了。"
"A sort of malaise overcame her.","她感觉浑身不舒服。"
"Michael not cheerful!","迈克尔不高兴了！"
"It was like the fire going out on a cold day.","这就像是冬日里的火炉熄灭了一样。"
"And, perhaps for the first time, she was conscious that his cheerfulness was of real importance to her.","可是，这或许是她第一次感觉到，他的快乐对她而言意义重大。"
"She watched him pick up Ting-a-ling and sit down.","她看着他抱起小叮铃，坐了下来。"
"And going up behind him, she bent over till her hair was against his cheek.","她走到他的背后，弯下身子，直到头发碰触到他的脸颊。"
"Instead of rubbing his cheek on hers, he sat quite still, and her heart misgave her.","可是，他并没有用脸去碰触她的面颊，而是在那里一动不动地坐着，于是她不安起来。"
"“What is it?” she said, coaxing.","“怎么了？”她撒娇地说。"
"“Nothing!”","“没事！”"
"She took hold of his ears.","她捏着他的耳朵。"
"“But there is.","“但是，是有点儿事。"
"I suppose you know somehow that I went to see Wilfrid.”","我猜你大概知道我去找过威尔弗里德了。”"
"He said stonily: “Why not?”","他面无表情地说：“为什么不呢？”"
"She let go, and stood up straight.","她放开手，站得直直的。"
"“It was only to tell him that I couldn’t see him again.”","“我只是去告诉他，以后都不见他了。”"
"That half-truth seemed to her the whole.","她觉得这句半真半假的话全是真的。"
"He suddenly looked up, a quiver went over his face; he look her hand.","他突然抬起头，脸上一阵颤抖。他抓住了她的手。"
"“It’s all right, Fleur.","“好了，弗勒。"
"You must do what you like, you know.","你喜欢怎么样就怎么样吧。"
"That’s only fair.","这样才公平。"
"I had too much lunch.”","我只是午饭吃多了。”"
"Fleur withdrew to the middle of the room.","弗勒退到房间中央。"
"“You’re rather an angel,” she said slowly, and went out.","“你真是个善人。”她缓缓地说，然后出去了。"
"Upstairs she looked out garments, confused in her soul.","她上楼找衣服去了，感情一片混乱。"

"Chapter VI","第六章"
"Michael Gets ‘What-For’","迈克尔受到“惩罚”"
"After his Green Street quest Michael had wavered back down Piccadilly, and, obeying one of those impulses which make people hang around the centres of disturbance, on to Cork Street.","在格林大街探究无果，迈克尔摇摇晃晃地沿着皮卡迪利大街走了回去。他顺从了内心的冲动，想要流连于混乱的中心，于是就走到了科克大街上。"
"He stood for a minute at the mouth of Wilfrid’s backwater.","他在威尔弗里德家的后街口站了一会儿。"
"‘No,’ he thought, at last, ‘ten to one he isn’t in; and if he is, twenty to one that I get any change except bad change!’","“还是算了吧，”他最后想道，“十有八九他不在家，就算他在家，对我而言，这件事好转的可能性也低于5%！”"
"He was moving slowly on to Bond Street, when a little light lady, coming from the backwater, and reading as she went, ran into him from behind.","他正慢慢地向邦德大街走着，这时一位身材小巧的女士迈着轻快的步子从后街里走了出来。她一边走路一边阅读，一下子就撞上了迈克尔的后背。"
"“Why don’t you look where you’re going!","“你怎么都不看路的！"
"Oh!","哦！"
"You?","是你？"
"Aren’t you the young man who married Fleur Forsyte?","你不就是和弗勒·福赛特结婚的那个年轻人吗？"
"I’m her cousin, June.","我是她的表姐，琼。"
"I thought I saw her just now.”","我想我刚才还看见她了呢。”"
"She waved a hand which held a catalogue with a gesture like the flirt of a bird’s wing.","她扬了扬手里的目录，那姿势就像是只小鸟在扇动翅膀。"
"“Opposite my gallery.","“就在我画廊的对面。"
"She went into a house, or I should have spoken to her—I’d like to have seen her again.”","她走进一幢房子里去了。我都来不及和她打招呼呢——我还挺想再见见她呢。”"
"Into a house!","走进一幢房子里去了！"
"Michael dived for his cigarette-case.","迈克尔伸手去取他的烟盒。"
"Hard-grasping it, he looked up.","他紧紧地抓着烟盒，抬起头来。"
"The little lady’s blue eyes were sweeping from side to side of his face with a searching candour.","这位小巧的女士正用她那双蓝色的眼睛在他脸上来回打量，毫不掩饰地探究着。"
"“Are you happy together?” she said.","“你们在一起幸福吗？”她问道。"
"A cold sweat broke out on his forehead.","他的额头上冒出了冷汗。"
"A sense of general derangement afflicted him—hers, and his own.","一时间他心乱如麻——她的生活乱了，他的生活也乱了，这让他很痛苦。"
"“I beg your pardon?” he gasped.","“您刚才说什么？我没听清楚。”他喘着气说。"
"“I hope you are.","“我希望你们幸福。"
"She ought to have married my little brother—but I hope you are.","她本来应该和我弟弟结婚的——不过我希望你们俩能幸福。"
"She’s a pretty child.”","她是个漂亮姑娘。”"
"In the midst of a dull sense of stunning blows, it staggered him that she seemed quite unconscious of inflicting them.","面对这一连串迎头痛击，他懵了。更令他惊讶的是，貌似她根本没有意识到这些话会使他痛苦。"
"He heard his teeth gritting, and said dully: “Your little brother, who was he?”","他咬着牙，沮丧地问道：“你弟弟是谁？”"
"“What!","“怎么？"
"Jon—didn’t you know Jon?","乔恩——你不认识乔恩吗？"
"He was too young, of course, and so was she.","那时他还小，当然她也还小。"
"But they were head over—the family feud stopped that.","虽然他们深爱着对方——但是鉴于两家的世仇，他们断了关系。"
"Well! it’s all past.","唉！都过去了。"
"I was at your wedding.","我参加你的婚礼了。"
"I hope you’re happy.","我希望你们幸福。"
"Have you seen the Claud Brains show at my gallery?","你看过克劳德·布雷恩斯在我们画廊办的画展吗？"
"He’s a genius.","他是个天才。"
"I was going to have a bun in here; will you join me?","我打算到这儿吃些点心，你也来好吗？"
"You ought to know his work.”","你应该去看看他的作品的。”"
"She had paused at the door of a confectioner’s.","她在一家甜点店门口停住了。"
"Michael put his hand on his chest.","迈克尔把一只手放在胸口。"
"“Thank you,” he said, “I have just had a bun—two, in fact.","“谢谢，”他说，“可是我刚吃过甜点了——实际上吃了两个呢。"
"Excuse me!”","抱歉了！”"
"The little lady grasped his other hand.","那位小巧的女士握着他的另一只手。"
"“Well, good-bye, young man!","“好吧，再见，年轻人！"
"Glad to have met you.","很高兴见到你。"
"You’re not a beauty, but I like your face.","你长得虽然不漂亮，但是我喜欢你这张脸。"
"Remember me to that child.","代我向那姑娘问好。"
"You should go and see Claud Brains.","你真应该去看看克劳德·布雷恩斯的作品。"
"He’s a real genius.”","他真的是个天才。”"
"Stock-still before the door, he watched her turn and enter, with a scattered motion, as of flying, and a disturbance among those seated in the pastry-cook’s.","他一动不动地站在店门前，看着她转身走进店里去了。她的动作轻盈，像在飞一样，在那些已经坐在甜点店里的客人中引起了一阵骚动。"
"Then he moved on, the cigarette unlighted in his mouth, dazed, as a boxer from a blow which knocks him sideways, and another which knocks him straight again.","然后他继续朝前走，嘴里叼着根没有点燃的香烟，神情恍惚，就像是一个拳击手——先是侧面挨了一记，接着正面又吃了一拳。"
"Fleur visiting Wilfrid—at this moment in his rooms up there—in his arms, perhaps!","弗勒去找威尔弗里德了！——此刻就在楼上，在他的房间里！——也许，在他的怀里！"
"He groaned.","他痛苦地呻吟着。"
"A well-fed young man in a new hat skipped at the sound.","一个戴着新帽子的胖乎乎的年轻人听到这声音连忙走开了。"
"Never!","不可能！"
"He could never stick that!","他绝对无法容忍这件事！"
"He would have to clear out!","他要离开这里！"
"He had believed Fleur honest!","他以前居然相信弗勒是忠诚的！"
"A double life!","两面派！"
"The night before last she had smiled on him.","前天晚上她还对他笑呢。"
"Oh!","啊！"
"God!","上帝啊！"
"He dashed across into Green Park.","他飞快地跑过马路，冲进了格林公园。"
"Why hadn’t he stood still and let something go over him?","刚才过马路的时候，怎么就不站住让车撞死算了？"
"And that lunatic’s little brother—John—family feud?","还有刚才那疯女人的弟弟——乔恩——家族世仇？"
"Himself—a pis aller, then—taken without love at all—a makeshift!","而自己呢——一个备胎，那时——她选择和他结婚时根本就不爱他——不过是一项权宜之计罢了！"
"He remembered now her saying one night at Mapledurham: “Come again when I know I can’t get my wish.”","他现在想起有天晚上在梅普尔达勒姆她说过的话：“等我知道我不能如愿以偿时，你再来吧。”"
"So that was the wish she couldn’t get!","原来这就是她那无法实现的愿望！"
"A makeshift!","拿我当临时替代品！"
"‘Jolly,’ he thought: ‘Oh! jolly!’","“好，”他想道，“哦！好极了！”"
"No wonder, then!","这就难怪了！"
"What could she care?","她还有什么好在乎的？"
"One man or another!","不是这个男人就是那个男人！"
"Poor little devil!","可怜的小家伙！"
"She had never let him know—never breathed a word!","她从来没有告诉过他——连一个字都没提过！"
"Was that decent of her—or was it treachery?","她这么做是为了保全她的体面——还是对他的背叛？"
"‘No,’ he thought, ‘if she HAD told me, it wouldn’t have made any difference—I’d have taken her at any price.","“不，”他心里想，“就算她之前告诉我了，事情也不会有什么变化——我还是会不惜一切代价把她娶回家。"
"It was decent of her not to tell me.’","她不告诉我还是对的。”"
"But how was it he hadn’t heard from some one?","但是怎么别人也没对他说过呢？"
"Family feud?","家族世仇？"
"The Forsytes!","福赛特家族？"
"Except ‘Old Forsyte,’ he never saw them; and ‘Old Forsyte’ was closer than a fish.","除了“老福赛特”，他没见过其他的人，可是“老福赛特”却守口如瓶。"
"Well! he had got what-for!","得啦！他已经受到惩罚了！"
"And again he groaned, in the twilight spaces of the Park.","黄昏时分，在公园的空地上，他又痛苦地呻吟了一声。"
"Buckingham Palace loomed up unlighted, huge and dreary.","白金汉宫隐约可见，因为没有点灯，这庞然大物看起来阴沉可怕。"
"Conscious of his cigarette at last, he stopped to strike a match, and drew the smoke deep into his lungs with the first faint sense of comfort.","他终于想起自己的烟了，于是停下来划火柴点烟。等他把烟深深地吸进肺里，他才开始觉得舒服了一点儿。"
"“You couldn’t spare us a cigarette, Mister?”","“您能不能给我一支烟，先生？”"
"A shadowy figure with a decent sad face stood beside the statue of Australia, so depressingly abundant!","一个模糊的人影出现在澳大利亚雕像旁边，那张很正派的脸上写满忧郁，衬得那雕像丰满得令人沮丧！"
"“Of course!” said Michael; “take the lot.”","“当然可以！”迈克尔说，“都给你吧。”"
"He emptied the case into the man’s hand.","他把烟盒里的烟都倒在那人的手上。"
"“Take the case too—‘present from Westminster’—you’ll get thirty bob for it.","“这烟盒也给你好了——‘威斯敏斯特大教堂赠’——你拿它能换30先令。"
"Good luck!”","祝你好运！”"
"He hurried on.","他匆匆忙忙地走开了。"
"A faint: “Hi, Mister!” pursued him unavailingly.","身后传来那人微弱的声音：“您真好，先生！”"
"Pity was pulp!","同情是不值钱的！"
"Sentiment was bilge!","怜悯是无聊的！"
"Was he going home to wait till Fleur had—finished and come back?","要他回家去等弗勒——完事后再回来吗？"
"Not he!","他才不呢！"
"He turned towards Chelsea, batting along as hard as he could stride.","他朝切尔西走去，一路上使劲地迈着大步。"
"Lighted shops, gloomy great Eaton Square, Chester Square, Sloane Square, the King’s Road—along, along!","灯火通明的商店、阴森森的大伊顿广场、切斯特广场、斯隆广场、国王路——他一路走着，走着！"
"Worse than the trenches—far worse—this whipped and scorpioned sexual jealousy!","这种性嫉妒带给他的痛苦像鞭笞一般，又像蝎子蜇了一样——比在战壕里呆着还要糟糕——糟透了！"
"Yes, and he would have felt even worse, but for that second blow.","没错，要不是那第二个打击，也许他会觉得更糟糕一些呢。"
"It made it less painful to know that Fleur had been in love with that cousin, and Wilfrid, too, perhaps, nothing to her.","当他得知弗勒此前爱的是她的堂兄弟之后，他觉得不那么痛苦了。也许在她看来，威尔弗里德也一样，什么都不是。"
"Poor little wretch!","真可怜！"
"‘Well, what’s the game now?’ he thought.","“唉，现在这游戏算什么？”他心里想。"
"The game of life—in bad weather, in stress?","在这恶劣的天气中，在这种压力下——游戏人生？"
"What was it?","这是怎么了？"
"In the war—what had a fellow done?","在战时——人们是怎么做的呢？"
"Somehow managed to feel himself not so dashed important; reached a condition of acquiescence, fatalism, “Who dies if England live” sort of sob-stuff state.","人们会想方设法忽视个人的重要性，默默承受、听天由命。那是一种催人泪下的境界——“为了英格兰，虽死犹生”。"
"The game of life?","游戏人生？"
"Was it different?","有什么不同？"
"“Bloody but unbowed” might be tripe; still—get up when you were knocked down!","“流血却不屈服”或许是胡说八道，但是——在被人击倒后，你仍然会重新站起来！"
"The whole was big, oneself was little!","集体是伟大的，个人是渺小的！"
"Passion, jealousy, ought they properly to destroy one’s sportsmanship, as Nazing and Sibley and Linda Frewe would have it?","应该为了情欲、嫉妒而变得不光明正大吗？就像内津、西布莉和琳达·弗鲁那样吗？"
"Was the word ‘gentleman’ a dud?","“绅士”这个词是没有价值的吗？"
"Was it?","是吗？"
"Did one keep one’s form, or get down to squealing and kicking in the stomach?","是保持个人的精神状态呢，还是抓紧时间大声抱怨、打击报复呢？"
"‘I don’t know,’ he thought, ‘I don’t know what I shall do when I see her—I simply don’t know.’","“我不知道，”他心里想，“我不知道等我见到她时，我该怎么办——我真的不知道。”"
"Steel-blue of the fallen evening, bare plane-trees, wide river, frosty air!","深蓝的夜色降临，法国梧桐光秃秃的，河面宽广，寒气袭人！"
"He turned towards home.","他转身朝家走去。"
"He opened his front door, trembling, and trembling, went into the drawing-room....","他哆哆嗦嗦地打开前门，一路哆嗦着走进客厅……"
"When Fleur had gone upstairs and left him with Ting-a-ling he didn’t know whether he believed her or not.","等到弗勒上楼去了，就剩他和小叮铃在楼下时，他不知道自己是否还相信她。"
"If she had kept that other thing from him all this time, she could keep anything!","如果她一直对他隐瞒那件事，那么她也能隐瞒其他的事！"
"Had she understood his words: “You must do as you like, that’s only fair?”","她听明白他的话了吗：“你喜欢怎么样就怎么样吧，这样才公平。”"
"He had said them almost mechanically, but they were reasonable.","他刚才几乎是机械地说出这句话的，但这句话是有道理的。"
"If she had never loved him, even a little, he had never had any right to expect anything; he had been all the time in the position of one to whom she was giving alms.","如果她从来没有爱过他，就连一丁点儿也没有，那么他有什么权利期盼呢，他一直是在接受她的救济。"
"Nothing compelled a person to go on giving alms.","怎么能强迫一个人一直施舍下去呢？"
"And nothing compelled one to go on taking them—except—the ache of want, the ache, the ache!","又怎么能迫使一个人一直接受施舍呢——除非——出于那种要占有的痛苦，痛苦啊，痛苦！"
"“You little Djinn!","“你这个小妖精！"
"You lucky little toad!","你这个幸运的小家伙！"
"Give me some of your complacency—you Chinese atom!”","把你的得意分给我一些——你这个中国来的小家伙！”"
"Ting-a-ling turned up his boot-buttons.","小叮铃抬起它那双靴扣般的大眼睛。"

"They had just discovered his complex, and he was going to have it out.","这种变态心理被人们发现了，于是他准备把这件事说出来。"
"The rest of the manuscript no doubt would show how that was done.","这份手稿的其他部分写的肯定是那是怎么回事。"

"During dinner, as if visited by remorse for having given them advice and two pictures worth some thousands of pounds, Soames pitched a tale like those of James in his palmy days.","吃晚饭的时候，索姆斯好像懊悔起来，觉得不该给他们提建议，还把两幅价值数千英镑的画送给他们了。他编了一个故事，像是詹姆斯在他的黄金时代讲的那些故事一样。"

"His mind was too miserable and disconcerted to be known; but she would know hers.","他心里装了太多的痛苦，太乱了，已经没办法想明白了。但是她明白她自己的心。"
"She had the information which alone made decision possible about Wilfrid, that cousin, her own actions and feelings.","她所知道的情况足以让她自己下决定，怎么处理威尔弗里德和那个堂兄弟，还有她自己的行动和感情。"
