"Chapter VII","第七章"
"The Altogether","裸体画"
"Tony Bicket, replete, was in vein that fine afternoon; his balloons left him freely, and he started for home in the mood of a conqueror.","那天下午天气很好，托尼·比克特吃饱喝足之后，心情愉快。他的气球卖得很好，于是他怀着胜利的心情动身回家了。"
"Victorine, too, had colour in her cheeks.","维多琳的双颊也有了血色。"
"She requited the story of his afternoon with the story of hers.","她听他讲完下午的故事后，也把她的故事讲给他听。"
"A false tale for a true—no word of Danby and Winter, the gentleman with the sliding smile, of the Grand Marnier, or ‘the altogether.’","不过刚才听的是真故事，现在讲的是假故事——她没有提丹比&温特出版社，或是那个笑容圆滑的先生，也没有提柑曼怡酒或者“裸体画”。"
"She had no compunction.","她并没有良心不安。"
"It was her secret, her surprise; if, by sitting in or out of ‘the altogether,’ not yet decided, she could make their passage money—well, she should tell him she had won it on a horse.","这是她的秘密，她的惊人之举。如果坐在那里当模特让人作画——或是“裸体画”，这件事她还没拿定主意——能够让她赚到他们的路费的话，那她会告诉他这是她赌马赢来的钱。"
"That night she asked:","那天晚上她问道："
"“Am I so very thin, Tony?” more than once.","“托尼，我是太瘦了吗？”她不止一次提起这件事了，"
"“I do so want to get fat.”","“我真希望能胖起来。”"
"Bicket, still troubled that she had not shared that lunch, patted her tenderly, and said he would soon have her as fat as butter—he did not explain how.","比克特还在为她没能分享到那顿午餐而难过。他一边轻轻地拍着她，一边说他很快就会让她胖得像发面馒头一样——但是他没有说明怎么做到这一点。"
"They dreamed together of blue butterflies, and awoke to chilly gaslight and a breakfast of cocoa and bread-and-butter.","他们一起梦见了蓝色的蝴蝶，醒来后看到的却是煤气灯的冷光以及一顿可可和黄油面包的早餐。"
"Fog!"
"Bicket was swallowed up before the eyes of Victorine ten yards from the door.","比克特走出家门还不到十米，就在维多琳的眼前被大雾吞没了。"
"She returned to the bedroom with anger in her heart.","她回到卧室，感到愤愤不平。"
"Who would buy balloons in a fog?","谁会在雾天来买气球呢？"
"She would do anything rather than let Tony go on standing out there all the choking days!","她什么都愿意干，只要能够不让比克特在这种令人窒息的天气里一直站在外面！"
"Undressing again, she washed herself intensively, in case—!","她又把衣服脱掉了，把浑身上下洗了个干净，万一——！"
"She had not long finished when her landlady announced the presence of a messenger boy.","刚洗完不久，房东太太就告诉她，来了一个送信的。"
"He bore an enormous parcel entitled “Mr. Bicket.”","他带来了一个大大的包裹，上面写着“比克特先生收”。"
"There was a note inside.","里面有张便条。"
"She read:","她读道："
"“DEAR BICKET,—Here are the togs.","“亲爱的比克特，——这里有几件衣服。"
"Hope they’ll be useful.—Yours, MICHAEL MONT.”","希望你用得上。——迈克尔·蒙特敬礼。”"
"In a voice that trembled she said to the boy:","她用颤抖的声音对送信人说："
"“Thank you, it’s O. K. Here’s twopence.”","“谢谢，这样就行了。这是给你的两便士。”"
"When his rich whistle was heard writhing into the fog, she flung herself down before the ‘togs’ in ecstasy.","等到送信人响亮的口哨声从雾中隐隐传来的时候，她已经欣喜若狂地扑到那堆“衣服”面前了。"
"The sexes were divided by tissue paper.","男女衣服是用薄纸隔开的。"
"A blue suit, a velour hat, some brown shoes, three pairs of socks with two holes in them, four shirts only a little frayed at the cuffs, two black-and-white ties, six collars, not too new, some handkerchiefs, two vests beautifully thick, two pairs of pants, and a brown overcoat with a belt and just two or three nice little stains.","一件蓝色套装、一顶绒帽、几双棕色的鞋子、三双有两个洞的袜子、四件袖口有点儿磨损的衬衣、两条黑白相间的领带、六件不太新的硬领、几块手绢、两件漂亮的厚背心、两条裤子，还有一件棕色带腰带的大衣，上面只有两三个不难看的小污迹。"
"She held the blue suit up against her arms and legs, the trousers and sleeves would only need taking-in about two inches.","她拿起那套蓝色的衣服，在自己的胳膊和腿上比试着，裤腿和袖口只需要收进去两英寸左右就行了。"
"She piled them in a pyramid, and turned with awe to the spoil beneath the tissue paper.","她把它们叠好，堆得像个金字塔似的，然后怯生生地去翻看薄纸下面的衣服。"
"A brown knitted frock with little clear yellow buttons—unsoiled, uncreased.","一件咖啡色的针织衫，钉着透明的黄色小扣子——既不脏也不皱。"
"How could anybody spare a thing like that!","怎么会有人把这么好的一件衣服送人呢！"
"A brown velvet toque with a little tuft of goldeny-brown feathers.","一顶棕色天鹅绒无檐小帽，上面装饰着金褐色的羽毛。"
"She put it on.","她把它戴上了。"
"A pair of pink stays ever so little faded, with only three inches of bone above the waist, and five inches of bone below, pink silk ribbons, and suspenders—a perfect dream.","一件颜色稍稍褪掉一点点的粉红色紧身衣，龙骨在腰以上只有三英寸宽，腰以下五英寸宽，有粉红色的丝带，还有吊袜带——正是她梦寐以求的东西。"
"She could not resist putting them on also.","她忍不住把它们也穿上了。"
"Two pairs of brown stockings; brown shoes; two combinations, a knitted camisole.","两双棕色的长筒袜、棕色的鞋子、两件连裤内衣、一件针织短袖衬衣。"
"A white silk jumper with a hole in one sleeve, a skirt of lilac linen that had gone a little in the wash; a pair of pallid pink silk pants; and underneath them all an almost black-brown coat, long and warm and cosy, with great jet buttons, and in the pocket six small handkerchiefs.","一件袖子上有一个洞的白色丝质套头衫、一条已经洗过几次的淡紫色亚麻短裙、一条淡粉色的绸裤；在它们下面是一件深棕色的大衣，又长又暖又舒服，钉着黑色大理石般的大纽扣，口袋里还有六条小手绢。"
"She took a deep breath of sweetness—geranium!","她深深地吸了一口上面的香气——天竺葵！"
"Her mind leaped forward.","她的思绪远远地跳跃开来。"
"Clothed, trousseaued, fitted out—blue butterflies—the sun!","有了衣服，有了行头，有了装备——蓝色的蝴蝶——太阳！"
"Only the money for the tickets wanting.","现在就只差买船票的钱了。"
"And suddenly she saw herself with nothing on standing before the gentleman with sliding eyes.","突然间，她看见自己赤身裸体地站在那个先生面前，任由他用眼睛上下打量。"
"Who cared!","谁在乎这些！"
"The money!","给钱就行！"
"For the rest of the morning she worked feverishly, shortening Tony, mending the holes in his socks, turning the fray of his cuffs.","在上午剩下的时间里，她亢奋地忙碌着，给托尼把衣服改短了，把袜子上的洞补好了，把磨损的袖口翻转了过来。"
"She ate a biscuit, drank another cup of cocoa—it was fattening, and went for the hole in the white silk jumper.","她吃了一块饼干，又喝了一杯可可——这会让人发胖的，然后继续缝补那件白色的丝质套头衫。"
"One o’clock.","1点钟了。"
"In panic she stripped once more, put on a new combination, pair of stockings, and the stays, then paused in superstition.","她慌慌张张地把衣服再次脱了，穿上一件新的连裤内衣、长筒袜，还有那件紧身衣，然后呆呆地停了下来。"
"No!","不！"
"Her own dress and hat—like yesterday!","该穿她自己的衣服，戴自己的帽子——和昨天一样！"
"Keep the rest until—!","把其他的衣服都留到——！"
"She hastened to her ‘bus, overcome alternately by heat and cold.","她匆匆忙忙去赶公共汽车，觉得忽冷忽热的。"
"Perhaps he would give her another glass of that lovely stuff.","也许他会再给她来一杯那种可口的甜酒。"
"If only she could go swimmy and not care for anything!","要是她能够晕晕乎乎的，什么都不在乎就好了！"
"She reached the studio as two o’clock was striking, and knocked.","两点整的时候，她到了画室门口，敲了敲门。"
"It was lovely and warm in there, much warmer than yesterday, and the significance of this struck her suddenly.","这里既温馨又暖和，比昨天暖和多了。她突然明白这么安排的重要意义了。"
"In front of the fire was a lady with a little dog.","因为她看到在壁炉前有一位夫人，还带着一只小狗。"
"“Miss Collins—Mrs. Michael Mont; she’s lending us her Peke, Miss Collins.”","“柯林斯小姐——这位是迈克尔·蒙特夫人，她把她的哈巴狗借给我们了，柯林斯小姐。”"
"The lady—only her own age, and ever so pretty—held out her hand.","那位夫人——和她年纪相仿，非常漂亮——伸出她的手来。"
"Geranium!","天竺葵！"
"This, then, was she whose clothes—!","那么，就是她把自己的衣服——！"
"She took the hand, but could not speak.","她握住了那只手，却说不出话来。"
"If this lady were going to stay, it would be utterly impossible.","如果这位夫人呆在这里，她绝对不可能脱掉衣服的。"
"Before her—so pretty, so beautifully covered—oh! no!","在她面前——这么漂亮的人，穿着这么好看的衣服——不！她做不到！"
"“Now, Ting, be good, and as amusing as you can.","“好了，叮铃，要乖乖的，要讨人喜欢哦。"
"Goodbye, Aubrey!","再见，奥布里！"
"Good luck to the picture!","希望这幅画能成功！"
"Good-bye, Miss Collins; it ought to be wonderful.”","再见，柯林斯小姐，这幅画一定会很棒的。”"
"Gone!","走了！"
"The scent of geranium fading; the little dog snuffling at the door.","天竺葵的味道渐渐淡去了，那只小狗在门口嗅来嗅去的。"
"The sliding gentleman had two glasses in his hands.","那位眼睛转得溜溜的先生手里拿了两杯酒。"
"‘Ah!’ thought Victorine, and drank hers at a gulp.","“啊！”维多琳心里喊道，然后她把那杯酒一饮而尽。"
"“Now, Miss Collins, you don’t mind, do you!","“现在，柯林斯小姐，您不介意了吧，是吗？"
"You’ll find everything in there.","您在那儿能找到你需要的一切东西。"
"It’s really nothing.","其实这都不重要。"
"I shall want you lying on your face just here with your elbows on the ground and your head up and a little turned this way; your hair as loose as it can be, and your eyes looking at this bone.","我希望您能趴在这里，手肘撑在地上，头抬起来稍微偏向这个方向；尽量披散着头发，眼睛看着这根骨头。"
"You must imagine that it’s a faun or some other bit of all right.","您要把它想象成潘神或是诸如此类的其他形象。"
"The dog’ll help you when he settles down to it.","这只小狗等会儿开始啃骨头之后，会对您有所帮助的。"
"F-a-u-n, you know, not f-a-w-n.”","想象成潘神，明白吗，可不是鹿神哦。”"
"“Yes,” said Victorine faintly.","“明白。”维多琳无力地说。"
"“Have another little tot?”","“还要再喝点儿酒吗？”"
"“Oh! please.”","“好的！再来点儿吧。”"
"He brought it.","他把酒拿过来了。"
"“I quite understand; but you know, really, it’s absurd.","“我很了解您现在的想法，但是您明白的，其实，这种想法很可笑。"
"You wouldn’t mind with a doctor.","您在医生面前是不会介意的。"
"That’s right.","这就对了。"
"Look here, I’ll put this little cow-bell on the ground.","看这里，我把这个铃铛放在地上。"
"When you’re in position, give it a tinkle, and I’ll come out.","当您摆好姿势之后，摇摇铃铛，我就会走出来。"
"That’ll help you.”","这将会对您有所帮助的。”"
"Victorine murmured:","维多琳喃喃地说："
"“You ARE kind.”","“您真好。”"
"“Not at all—it’s natural.","“没什么——是我该做的。"
"Now will you start in?","现在可以开始了吗？"
"The light won’t last for ever.","不会一直都有阳光的。"
"Fifteen bob a day, we said.”","我们说好的，一天15个先令。”"
"Victorine saw him slide away behind a screen, and looked at the little cow-bell.","维多琳看着他悄悄走到屏障后面去，然后她又看了看那个小铃铛。"
"Fifteen bob!","15个先令！"
"And fifteen bob!","再来15个先令！"
"And fifteen bob!","再来15个先令！"
"Many, many fifteen bobs before—!","许多、许多15个先令，然后——！"
"But not more times of sitting than of Tony’s standing from foot to foot, offering balloons.","但是她坐着的次数不会比托尼站着的次数多的。他就是那样两只脚换着站在那里卖气球。"
"And as if wound up by that thought, she moved like clockwork off the dais, into the model’s room.","这样想着，她高兴起来了。她机械地离开了那个台子，走进模特的房间里去了。"
"Cosy in there, too; warm, a green silk garment thrown on a chair.","那里面也很舒服、温暖，椅子上扔着一件绿色丝绸长袍。"
"She took off her dress.","她把自己的衣服脱了。"
"The beauty of the pink stays struck her afresh.","她又为那件漂亮的粉色紧身衣着迷了。"
"Perhaps the gentleman would like—no, that would be even worse—!","也许这位先生会喜欢呢——不，那样会更糟糕的——！"
"A noise reached her—from Ting-a-ling complaining of solitude.","她听见一阵响声——是小叮铃在抱怨又没人理他了。"
"If she delayed, she never would—!","要是她拖拖拉拉地，那她就不会——！"
"Stripping hastily, she stood looking at herself in a glass.","她赶紧把衣服脱了，站在那里看着镜中的自己。"
"If only that slim, ivory-white image could move out on to the dais and she could stay here!","要是能让镜中这个苗条的、肤色雪白的人走到台子上去，而自己能留在这里，就好了！"
"Oh!","啊！"
"It was awful—awful!","这太可怕了——太可怕了！"
"She couldn’t—no! she couldn’t.","她不能——不！她不能。"
"She caught up her final garment again.","她再次抓住自己最后的一件衣服。"
"Fifteen bob!","15先令！"
"But fifteen bob!","那可是15先令啊！"
"Before her eyes, wild and mournful, came a vision: Of a huge dome, and a tiny Tony, with little, little balloons in a hand held out!","她的眼前出现了一个荒凉而又令人心伤的幻象：在一个巨大的穹顶下，渺小的托尼拿着一个个小小的气球！"
"Something cold and steely formed over her heart as icicles form on a window.","一些又冷又硬的东西在她的心里凝结，就像是冬天窗户上形成的冰柱。"
"If that was all they would do for him, she would do better!","如果他们只肯为他做这些，那么她会为他做得更好！"
"She dropped the garment; and, confused, numb, stepped forth in the ‘altogether.’","她松开了那件衣服，然后混乱而又麻木地“裸体”走了出去。"
"Ting-a-ling growled at her above his bone.","小叮铃从那根骨头上抬起头来，朝她叫着。"
"She reached the cow-bell and lay down on her face as she had been told, with feet in the air, crossed.","她拿起那个铃铛，趴在那里，就像刚才他告诉她的那样，双脚朝上，交叉着。"
"Resting her chin on one hand, she wagged the bell.","她用一只手托着下巴，摇了摇铃铛。"
"It made a sound like no bell she had ever heard; and the little dog barked—he did look funny!","它发出来的声音，和她听过的铃铛声音都不一样，那只小狗也叫起来——它看上去确实很好笑！"
"“Perfect, Miss Collins!","“太好了，柯林斯小姐！"
"Hold that!”","就这样别动！”"
"Fifteen bob! and fifteen bob!","15个先令！再来15个先令！"
"“Just point those left toes a bit more.","“左边的脚趾再往上翘起来点儿。"
"That’s right!","就是这样！"
"The flesh tone’s perfect!","皮肤的色调美极了！"
"My God, why must one walk before one runs!","上帝啊，为什么一定要先会走才能跑啊！"
"Drawing’s a bore, Miss Collins; one ought to draw with a brush only; a sculptor draws with a chisel, at least when he’s a Michelangelo.","素描是一件令人讨厌的事，柯林斯小姐，人应该只用画笔来画画，而雕塑家是用凿子作画的，至少在他是个米开朗基罗的时候。"
"How old are you?”","您今年多大了？”"
"“Twenty-one,” came from lips that seemed to Victorine quite far away.","“21了。”维多琳嘴里发出的声音在她自己听来好像来自遥远的地方。"
"“I’m thirty-two.","“我32了。"
"They say our generation was born so old that it can never get any older.","据说我们这代人生下来就很老练，因此也就不会再老了。"
"Without illusions.","没有幻想。"
"Well!","唉！"
"I never had any beliefs that I can remember.","从我记事起，我就没什么信仰。"
"Had you?”","您有吗？”"
"Victorine’s wits and senses were astray, but it did not matter, for he was rattling on:","维多琳迷迷糊糊的，理智和意识都不知所踪了。不过这也没关系，他还在喋喋不休："
"“We don’t even believe in our ancestors.","“我们连自己的祖先都不相信。"
"All the same, we’re beginning to copy them again.","尽管如此，我们又开始效仿他们了。"
"D’you know a book called ‘The Sobbing Turtle’ that’s made such a fuss?—sheer Sterne, very well done; but sheer Sterne, and the author’s tongue in his cheek.","您知不知道一本叫《啜泣的海龟》的书？它可是轰动一时的——完全斯特恩式的，写得很好，纯粹斯特恩式的写法，假情假意的。"
"That’s it in a nutshell, Miss Collins—our tongues are in our cheeks—bad sign.","简单地说，就那么回事。柯林斯小姐——要是我们都毫无诚意——那可不是个好兆头。"
"Never mind; I’m going to out-Piero Cosimo with this.","不要紧，我要用这幅画来打败皮尔洛·科西莫。"
"Your head an inch higher, and that curl out of your eye, please.","头往上抬一英寸，还有请把您眼前那绺头发拨开。"
"Thanks!","谢谢！"
"Hold that!","就这样别动！"
"By the way, have you Italian blood?","顺便问一句，您是不是有意大利血统？"
"What was your mother’s name, for instance?”","比如说，您母亲姓什么？”"
"“Brown.”","“布朗。”"
"“Ah!","“啊！"
"You can never tell with Browns.","姓布朗的人就很难说是哪儿的了。"
"It may have been Brune—or Bruno—but very likely she was Iberian.","这个姓也许本来是布龙——或者是布鲁诺——很可能是伊比利亚人。"
"Probably all the inhabitants of Britain left alive by the Saxons were called Brown.","很可能在撒克逊入侵后所有活下来的英国人都叫布朗。"
"As a fact, that’s all tosh, though.","但是，事实上，那都是胡说八道。"
"Going back to Edward the Confessor, Miss Collins—a mere thirty generations—we each of us have one thousand and seventy-four million, five hundred and seventy-three thousand, nine hundred and eighty-four ancestors, and the population of this island was then well under a million.","从忏悔者爱德华起到现在，柯林斯小姐——不过才30代——我们每个人就有10亿多个祖先，而当时这个岛上总共还不到100万人呢。"
"We’re as inbred as racehorses, but not so nice to look at, are we?","就像赛马一样，我们都是近亲繁殖的，但是长得不怎么好看，是不是？"
"I assure you, Miss Collins, you’re something to be grateful for.","我敢说，柯林斯小姐，您长得这么漂亮真该感谢上帝。"
"So is Mrs. Mont.","蒙特夫人也一样。"
"Isn’t she pretty?","她漂亮吧？"
"Look at that dog?”","看看她那只狗？”"
"Ting-a-ling, indeed, with forelegs braced, and wrinkled nose, was glaring, as if under the impression that Victorine was another bone.","没错，小叮铃伸直了前腿，皱着鼻子，正在看着她，好像觉得她也是一根骨头。"
"“He’s funny,” she said, and again her voice sounded far away.","“它很滑稽。”她说，感觉声音再一次从远方传来。"
"Would Mrs. Mont lie here if he’d asked her?","如果他向蒙特夫人提出请求，她会趴在这里吗？"
"SHE would look pretty!","如果是她的话，一定很好看！"
"But SHE didn’t need the fifteen bob!","但是她不需要这15先令！"
"“Comfortable in that position?”","“这个姿势舒服吗？”"
"In alarm, she murmured:","她吓了一跳，小声说："
"“Oh! yes, thank you!”","“哦！舒服，谢谢您！”"
"“Warm enough?”","“够暖和吗？”"
"“Oh! yes, thank you!”","“哦！暖和，谢谢您！”"
"“That’s good.","“那就好。"
"Just a little higher with the head.”","您把头再抬高一点儿。”"
"Slowly in Victorine the sense of the dreadfully unusual faded.","维多琳那种极其不自在的感觉慢慢地消失了。"
"Tony should never know.","托尼不会知道这件事的。"
"If he never knew, he couldn’t care.","只要他不知道，他就不会介意。"
"She could lie like this all day—fifteen bob, and fifteen bob!","她可以一整天都这样趴着——15先令，再来15先令！"
"It was easy.","很容易办到的。"
"She watched the quick, slim fingers moving, the blue smoke from the cigarette.","她看着那细长的手指迅速地移动着，看着香烟所散发出的青烟。"
"She watched the little dog.","她看着那只小狗。"
"“Like a rest?","“想休息一下吗？"
"You left your gown; I’ll get it for you.”","您忘记带外袍了，我去拿给您。”"
"In that green silk gown, beautifully padded, she sat up, with her feet on the floor over the dais edge.","她穿上那件有漂亮垫肩的绿色外袍，坐了起来，把脚从平台边缘伸出来放在地板上。"
"“Cigarette?","“抽烟吗？"
"I’m going to make some Turkish coffee.","我去煮些土耳其咖啡。"
"You’d better walk about.”","您最好走动走动。”"
"Victorine obeyed.","维多琳照他说的做了。"
"“You’re out of a dream, Miss Collins.","“您就像是从梦里走出来的，柯林斯小姐。"
"I shall have to do a Mathew Maris of you in that gown.”","我将来一定把您穿这件衣服的样子画成一幅马修·马里斯式的作品。”"
"The coffee, like none she had ever tasted, gave her a sense of well-being.","这种咖啡和她以前喝的咖啡都不一样，给她一种幸福的感觉。"
"She said:","她说："
"“It’s not like coffee.”","“它不像咖啡。”"
"Aubrey Greene threw up his hands.","奥布里·格林摊开双手。"
"“You have said it.","“您说对了。"
"The British are a great race—nothing will ever do them in.","英国人是很了不起的——从来没有什么能骗得了他们。"
"If they could be destroyed, they must long ago have perished of their coffee.","如果有什么能毁灭他们的话，那么他们一定早就毁在自己的咖啡里了。"
"Have some more?”","要不要再来点儿？”"
"“Please,” said Victorine.","“好的。”维多琳说。"
"There was such a little in the cup.","杯子里只有一点点了。"
"“Ready, again?”","“准备好了吗，又要开始了？”"
"She lay down, and let the gown drop off.","她躺下了，那件长袍顺势落了下来。"
"“That’s right!","“对，就是这样！"
"Leave it there—you’re lying in long grass, and the green helps me.","别动——您躺在长长的绿草丛中，这件绿衣服帮了我的大忙。"
"Pity it’s winter; I’d have hired a glade.”","可惜这是冬天，要不然我一定去树林中租一块空地。”"
"Lying in long grass—flowers, too, perhaps.","躺在长长的绿草丛中——也许还有鲜花。"
"She did love flowers.","她喜欢花。"
"As a little girl she used to lie in the grass, and make daisy-chains, in the field at the back of her grandmother’s lodge at Norbiton.","在她小的时候，在诺比顿的外婆家屋后的田野里，她常常躺在草丛里，拿雏菊编花环。"
"Her grandmother kept the lodge.","外婆守着那房子。"
"Every year, for a fortnight, she had gone down there—she had liked the country ever so.","每年她都要去那里住两周——她非常喜欢乡下。"
"Only she had always had something on.","只是那时她身上都是穿着衣服的。"
"It would be nicer with nothing.","要是什么都不穿就更美了。"
"Were there flowers in Central Australia?","澳大利亚中部有花吗？"
"With butterflies there must be!","既然那里有蓝色的蝴蝶，就一定有花！"
"In the sun—she and Tony—like the Garden of Eden!...","沐浴在阳光下——她和托尼——就像在伊甸园一样！……"
"“Thank you, that’s all for today.","“谢谢。今天就到这里吧。"
"Half a day—ten bob.","半天——十先令。"
"To-morrow morning at eleven.","明天早晨11点钟。"
"You’re a first-rate sitter, Miss Collins.”","您是一个顶级的写生模特，柯林斯小姐。”"
"Putting on the pink stays, Victorine had a feeling of elation.","维多琳穿上那件粉红色的紧身衣，心里高兴极了。"
"She had done it!","她做到了！"
"Tony should never know!","托尼绝不会知道！"
"The thought that he never would gave her pleasure.","一想到他绝不会知道，她就觉得很开心。"
"And once more divested of the ‘altogether,’ she came forth.","她再次摆脱了“裸体”的状态，走了出来。"
"Aubrey Greene was standing before his handiwork.","奥布里·格林站在他的作品前。"
"“Not yet, Miss Collins,” he said; “I don’t want to depress you.","“还没完成，柯林斯小姐，”他说，“我不想打击您。"
"That hip-bone’s too high.","髋骨太高了。"
"We’ll put it right tomorrow.","明天会把它修正过来的。"
"Forgive my hand, it’s all chalk.","原谅我不能和您握手了，我满手都是粉笔末。"
"Au revoir!","再见！"
"Eleven o’clock.","11点钟哦。"
"And we shan’t need this chap.","到时我们就不需要这个小家伙了。"
"No, you don’t!”","别，你别走啊！”"
"For Ting-a-ling was showing signs of accompanying the larger bone.","原来小叮铃正表现出想和这根大骨头一起走的样子。"
"Victorine passed out smiling.","维多琳笑着离开了。"

"Chapter VIII","第八章"
"Soames Takes the Matter up","索姆斯着手处理此事"
"Soames had concentrated, sitting before the fire in his bedroom till Big Ben struck twelve.","索姆斯坐在卧室的壁炉前，全神贯注地思考着，直到大本钟敲了12下。"
"His reflections sum-totalled in a decision to talk it over with ‘old Mont’ after all.","他的思绪始终围绕着是否要把这件事和“老蒙特”好好谈一谈。"
"Though light-brained, the fellow was a gentleman, and the matter delicate.","这个人虽然头脑简单，但却是一个通情达理的人，而且这件事又很棘手。"
"He got into bed and slept, but awoke at half-past two.","他上床去睡觉，但到了两点半就醒了。"
"There it was!","就是这件事！"
"‘I WON’T think of it,’ he thought; and instantly began to.","“我不要想它了。”他想，但是马上又开始想了。"
"In a long life of dealings with money, he had never had such an experience.","在与金钱打交道的漫长一生中，他还从未有过这种经历。"
"Perfectly straightforward conformity with the law—itself so often far from perfectly straightforward—had been the sine qua non of his career.","绝对诚实地遵守法律——法律本身常常又不是绝对诚实的——是他职业生涯的必备条件。"
"Honesty, they said, was the best policy.","有人说，诚实才是上策。"
"But was it anything else?","但是，还有别的上策吗？"
"A normally honest man couldn’t keep out of a perfect penitentiary for a week.","一个普通的诚实人要使自己一个星期不进合法的教养院是不可能的。"
"But then a perfect penitentiary had no relation to prison, or the Bankruptcy Court.","但是一个合法的教养院与监狱或破产法庭没有任何关系。"
"The business of working honesty was to keep out of those two institutions.","遵循诚实就是要远离那两个机构。"
"And so far he had never had any difficulty.","到目前为止，他还没遇到过什么困难。"
"What, besides the drawing of fees and the drinking of tea, were the duties of a director?","除了领取酬劳和喝茶之外，董事的职责是什么？"
"That was the point.","这就是问题所在。"
"And how far, if he failed in them, was he liable?","如果他没有尽到职责，他要负多大的责任呢？"
"It was a director’s duty to be perfectly straightforward.","董事的职责就是要绝对诚实。"
"But if a director were perfectly straightforward, he couldn’t be a director.","但是如果一个董事真的绝对诚实，他就做不成董事了。"
"That was clear.","这是显而易见的。"
"In the first place, he would have to tell his shareholders that he didn’t anything like earn his fees.","首先，他将不得不告诉股东们，他没有做任何应该得到酬劳的事情。"
"For what did he do on his Boards?","那么他在董事会里都做了些什么呢？"
"Well, he sat and signed his name and talked a little, and passed that which the general trend of business decided must be passed.","哦，他就坐着，签签名，发发言，以及通过那些由于业务的总趋势所决定的必须通过的事情。"
"Did he initiate?","他提过什么倡议吗？"
"Once in a blue moon.","极其罕见。"
"Did he calculate?","他进行过核算吗？"
"No, he read calculations.","没有，他只看核算的结果。"
"Did he check payments out and in?","他检查过支出和收入吗？"
"No, the auditors did that.","没有，那是审计人员做的。"
"There was policy!","还有方针政策！"
"A comforting word, but—to be perfectly straightforward—a director’s chief business was to let the existing policy alone.","这是个令人感到安慰的词，但是——绝对诚实地讲——董事的主要职责就是不要干涉现行的方针政策。"
"Take his own case!","就以他自己为例吧！"
"If he had done his duty, he would have stopped this foreign insurance business which he had instinctively distrusted the moment he heard of it—within a month of sitting on the Board, or, having failed in doing so, resigned his seat.","如果他履行了自己的职责，那么他就会停止这项国外保险业务，他在一听到这项业务时就本能地产生了怀疑——那时也就刚入董事会还不到一个月，或者，如果停止不了这项业务，他就辞职。"
"But he had not.","但是他没有这么做。"
"Things had been looking better!","情况一直在好转啦！"
"It was not the moment, and so forth!","时机还不成熟，等等！"
"If he had done his duty as a perfectly straightforward director, indeed, he would never have become a director of the P. P. R. S., because he would have looked into the policy of the Society much more closely than he had before accepting a position on the Board.","如果他真的像一个绝对诚实的董事那样履行自己的职责，那他就绝不会成为天佑再保险公司的董事，因为在接受董事会的这个职务之前，他会更加仔细地调查这家公司的方针政策。"
"But what with the names, and the prestige, and not looking a gift horse too closely in the mouth—there it had been!","但是为了名声、威望以及不能对收到的礼物吹毛求疵——事情就变成了这个样子！"
"To be perfectly straightforward, he ought now to be circularising the shareholders, saying: “My laissez-faire has cost you two hundred odd thousand pounds.","要做到绝对诚实，他现在就应该挨个通知股东们，说：“我的放任政策已经使你们损失了二十多万英镑。"
"I have lodged this amount in the hands of trustees for your benefit, and am suing the rest of the directors for their quotas of the amount.”","为了你们的利益，我已经将这笔钱放在了受托人那里，同时我正在起诉其他的董事，要求他们赔偿这笔款项中他们应负责的份额。”"
"But he was not proposing to do so, because—well—because it wasn’t done, and the other directors wouldn’t like it.","但是他不打算这么做，因为——呃——没有人这么做过，而且其他的董事不会喜欢这种做法。"
"In sum: You waited till the shareholders found out the mess, and you hoped they wouldn’t.","总而言之，你等着股东们发现这一混乱情况，而你又希望他们不会发现。"
"In fact, just like a Government, you confused the issues, and made the best case you could for yourselves.","事实上，就如同政府一样，你把问题搞乱，然后尽力为自己创造最有利的局面。"
"With a sense of comfort Soames thought of Ireland: The late Government had let the country in for all that mess in Ireland, and at the end taken credit for putting an end to what need never have been!","索姆斯想到了爱尔兰，不由得心生安慰：上一届政府让全国陷入到爱尔兰的混乱之中，最后因为结束了这种原本绝对不应该发生的情况而广受赞誉！"
"The Peace, too, and the Air Force, and Agriculture, and Egypt—the five most important issues they’d had to deal with—they had put the chestnuts into the fire in every case!","还有和平、空军、农业以及埃及——他们必须面对的五个最重要的问题——每一个问题他们都是在自找麻烦！"
"But had they confessed to it?","但是他们承认了吗？"
"Not they.","他们才不会呢。"
"One didn’t confess.","没人承认。"
"One said: “The question of policy made it imperative at the time.”","有人说：“在那时，政策问题使之势在必行。”"
"Or, better still, one said nothing; and trusted to the British character.","或者，更好的办法是，什么也不说，光指望英国人的品行。"
"With his chin resting on the sheet, Soames felt a momentary relief.","索姆斯将下巴放在床单上，感到了暂时的解脱。"
"The late Government weren’t sweating into THEIR sheets—not they—he was convinced of it!","上一届政府才不会出汗到弄湿他们自己的床单呢——他们才不会——对此他确信无疑！"
"Fixing his eyes on the dying embers in the grate, he reflected on the inequalities and injustices of existence.","他盯着壁炉里即将燃尽的余火，心中思考着现实中的不平等和不公正。"
"Look at the chaps in politics and business, whose whole lives were passed in skating on thin ice, and getting knighted for it.","看看政界和商界的那些家伙们，他们的一生都在冒险，并因此加官晋爵。"
"They never turned a hair.","他们泰然自若。"
"And look at himself, for the first time in forty years on thin ice, and suffering confoundedly.","再看看他自己，40年来第一次毛线，就痛苦得要命。"
"There was a perfect cult of hoodwinking the public, a perfect cult of avoiding the consequences of administrative acts; and here was he, a man of the world, a man of the law, ignorant of those cults, and—and glad of it.","有一种蒙蔽大众的完美的热潮，一种避免行政行为后果的完美的热潮，然而他这个深谙世故、精通法律的人，却对那些热潮一无所知，而且——而且还为此感到高兴。"
"From engrained caution and a certain pride, which had in it a touch of the fine, Soames shrank from that coarse-grained standard of honesty which conducted the affairs of the British public.","由于根深蒂固的谨慎和某种自豪感——这种性格也不无优点，索姆斯对于管理英国公众事务的粗鄙的诚实标准避而远之。"
"In anything that touched money he was, he always had been, stiff-necked, stiff-kneed.","在任何涉及金钱的问题上，他是且一向是固执己见、不肯让步的。"
"Money was money, a pound a pound, and there was no way of pretending it wasn’t and keeping your self-respect.","钱就是钱，一英镑就是一英镑，要假装钱不是钱，又要保持自尊心，那是不可能的。"
"He got up, drank some water, took a number of deep breaths, and stamped his feet.","他从床上起来，喝了点儿水，做了几次深呼吸，又跺了跺脚。"
"Who was it said the other day that nothing had ever lost him five minutes’ sleep.","前几天不知是谁说的，从来没有过什么事情能让他损失五分钟的睡眠。"
"The fellow must have the circulation of an ox, or the gift of Baron Munchausen.","那家伙一定具有像公牛一样的血液循环，或者具有吹牛大王的天赋。"
"He took up a book.","他拿起一本书。"
"But his mind would only turn over and over the realisable value of his resources.","但是他的脑子翻来覆去地想着他的财产可以变现成多少钱。"
"Apart from his pictures, he decided that he could not be worth less than two hundred and fifty thousand pounds, and there was only Fleur—and she already provided for more or less.","除了他的藏画之外，他断定他的财产不会少于25万英镑，而且只有弗勒一个孩子——她已经多少做了些准备。"
"His wife had her settlement, and could live on it perfectly well in France.","他的妻子有她自己的安置费，她可以靠这笔钱在法国生活得很好。"
"As for himself—what did he care?","至于他自己——他有什么在乎的？"
"A room at his club near Fleur—he would be just as happy, perhaps happier!","在他的俱乐部里找一个房间，离弗勒不远——他一样过得很快活，或许会更快活！"
"And suddenly he found that he had reached a way out of his disturbance and anxiety.","于是他突然发现自己已经找到了摆脱烦恼和焦虑的途径。"
"By imagining the far-fetched, by facing the loss of his wealth, he had exorcised the demon.","他想象着那些牵强附会的事情，面对着自己财产的损失，他终于驱逐了心魔。"
"The book, ‘The Sobbing Turtle,’ of which he had not read one word, dropped from his hand; he slept....","那本《啜泣的乌龟》，他一个字也没有看，从他手中掉了下来。他睡着了……"
"His meeting with ‘Old Mont’ took place at ‘Snooks’ directly after lunch.","刚一吃过午饭，他就去“轻蔑”俱乐部和“老蒙特”见面。"
"The tape in the hall, at which he glanced on going in, recorded a further heavy drop in the mark.","进去的时候，他朝大厅里的行情收录带瞥了一眼，上面记录着马克又一次大跌了。"
"Just as he thought: The thing was getting valueless!","正如他所想的那样：这东西正在变得一文不值！"
"Sitting there, sipping coffee, the baronet looked to Soames almost offensively spry.","准男爵坐在那里，小口地抿着咖啡，神情活泼地看着索姆斯，那样子简直让人反感。"
"Two to one he had realised nothing!","他肯定什么都不知道呢！"
"‘Well!’ thought Soames,’ as old Uncle Jolyon used to say, I shall astonish his weak nerves!’","“嗯！”索姆斯想，“就像乔里恩叔叔过去常说的那样，我要吓一吓他那脆弱的神经！”"
"And without preamble he began.","于是他开门见山地开始了。"
"“How are you, Mont?","“你好吗，蒙特？"
"This mark’s valueless.","马克一文不值了。"
"You realise we’ve lost the P. P. R. S. about a quarter of a million by that precious foreign policy of Elderson’s.","你知道，由于埃尔德森那宝贵的国外方针政策，我们已经使天佑再保险公司损失了大约25万英镑。"
"I’m not sure an action won’t lie against us for taking unjustifiable risk.","我不敢肯定人们不会因为我们冒了不合理的风险而起诉我们。"
"But what I’ve come to see you about is this.”","我来这里见你就是为了这件事。”"
"He retailed the interview with the clerk, Butterfield, watching the eyebrows of his listener, and finished with the words: “What do you say?”","他把和职员巴特菲尔德面谈的情况详细说了一遍，他看着倾听者的眉毛，以这样一句话结尾：“你怎么看？”"
"Sir Lawrence, whose foot was jerking his whole body, fixed his monocle.","劳伦斯爵士，从脚开始全身都在颤抖，固定好他的单片眼镜。"
"“Hallucination, my dear Forsyte!","“那一定是幻觉，我亲爱的福赛特！"
"I’ve known Elderson all my life.","我认识埃尔德森一辈子了。"
"We were at Winchester together.”","我们一起在温切斯特呆过。”"
"Again!","又来了！"
"Again!","又来了！"
"Oh!","哦！"
"Lord!","上帝啊！"
"Soames said slowly:","索姆斯慢慢地说："
"“You can’t tell from that.","“仅凭那一点你是判断不出什么的。"
"A man who was at Marlborough with me ran away with his mess fund and his colonel’s wife, and made a fortune in Chili out of canned tomatoes.","有一个和我一起在莫尔伯勒呆过的人，带着伙食团的资金和他的上校的老婆跑了，后来在智利做番茄罐头发了财。"
"The point is this: If the young man’s story’s true, we’re in the hands of a bad hat.","问题在于：如果这个年轻人说的是真的，那我们就落在了一个坏蛋的手中。"
"It won’t do, Mont.","这可不行，蒙特。"
"Will you tackle him, and see what he says to it?","你可不可以去和他交涉一下，看看他对这件事怎么说？"
"You wouldn’t like a story of that sort about yourself.","你也不希望那种事情发生在你身上。"
"Shall we both go?”","我们一起去好吗？”"
"“Yes,” said Sir Lawrence, suddenly.","“好的，”劳伦斯爵士突然说，"
"“You’re right.","“你说得对。"
"We’ll both go, Forsyte.","我们一起去，福赛特。"
"I don’t like it, but we’ll both go.","我不喜欢这种事，但是我们要一起去。"
"He ought to hear it.”","他应该听一听这件事。”"
"“Now?”","“现在就去吗？”"
"“Now.”","“现在就去。”"
"With solemnity they assumed top hats, and issued.","他们一本正经地戴上大礼帽，然后出发了。"
"“I think, Forsyte, we’ll take a taxi.”","“我想，福赛特，我们坐出租车去吧。”"
"“Yes,” said Soames.","“好的。”索姆斯说。"
"The cab ground its way slowly past the lions, then dashed on down to the Embankment.","一路上，出租车缓慢地驶过两座狮子，然后朝着堤岸疾驰而去。"
"Side by side its occupants held their noses steadily before them.","车上的两个乘客肩并肩地坐着，鼻子坚定地朝向前方。"
"“He was shooting with me a month ago,” said Sir Lawrence.","“一个月之前他还和我一起打猎呢，”劳伦斯爵士说，"
"“Do you know the hymn ‘O God, our help in ages past’?","“你知道《上帝是我们的万世救主》这首赞美诗吗？"
"It’s very fine, Forsyte.”","这首诗写得非常好，福赛特。”"
"Soames did not answer.","索姆斯没有回答。"
"The fellow was beginning to tittup!","这个家伙又开始絮叨了！"
"“We had it that Sunday,” went on Sir Lawrence.","“那个礼拜天我们就唱了这首诗，”劳伦斯爵士接着说，"
"“Elderson used to have a fine voice—sang solos.","“埃尔德森以前有一副好嗓子——唱过好几次独唱曲目。"
"It’s a foghorn now, but a good delivery still.”","现在像雾号一样又粗又哑，但是演唱的姿态依然很不错。”"
"He gave his little whinnying laugh.","他发出一阵短暂的马嘶般的笑声。"
"‘Is it possible,’ thought Soames, ‘for this chap to be serious?’ and he said:","索姆斯想：“这个家伙能严肃起来吗？”于是他说："
"“If we find this is true of Elderson, and conceal it, we could all be put in the dock.”","“如果我们发现埃尔德森这件事是真的，又把它隐瞒起来，我们都会被押上被告席。”"
"Sir Lawrence refixed his monocle.","劳伦斯爵士又夹了夹他的单片眼镜。"
"“The deuce!” he said.","“见鬼！”他说。"
"“Will you do the talking,” said Soames, “or shall I?”","“是你来谈呢，”索姆斯说，“还是我来谈呢？”"
"“I think you had better, Forsyte; ought we to have the young man in?”","“我想最好还是你来谈吧，福赛特，我们该不该把那个年轻人找来？”"
"“Wait and see,” said Soames.","“看情况再说。”索姆斯说。"
"They ascended to the offices of the P. P. R. S. and entered the Board Room.","他们爬上楼，到了天佑再保险公司的办公室，然后走进董事会会议室。"
"There was no fire, the long table was ungarnished; an old clerk, creeping about like a fly on a pane, was filling inkstands out of a magnum.","室内没有生火，那张长桌子未作任何装饰。那里有一名年老的职员，他像窗格玻璃上的苍蝇一样蹒跚地走着，正在把一只大墨水瓶里的墨水倒进墨水台里。"
"Soames addressed him:","索姆斯对他说："
"“Ask the manager to be so kind as to come and see Sir Lawrence Mont and Mr. Forsyte.”","“请经理劳驾来见一见劳伦斯·蒙特爵士和福赛特先生。”"
"The old clerk blinked, put down the magnum, and went out.","老职员眨了眨眼睛，放下大墨水瓶，走了出去。"
"“Now,” said Soames in a low voice, “we must keep our heads.","“现在，”索姆斯小声说，“我们必须保持头脑冷静。"
"He’ll deny it, of course.”","当然，他会否认这件事的。”"
"“I should hope so, Forsyte; I should hope so.","“我倒希望如此，福赛特，我倒希望如此。"
"Elderson’s a gentleman.”","埃尔德森是一个绅士。”"
"“No liar like a gentleman,” muttered Soames, below his breath.","“没有哪个骗子像绅士。”索姆斯低声咕哝道。"
"After that they stood in their overcoats before the empty grate, staring at their top hats placed side by side on the table.","之后他们就穿着大衣站在空空的壁炉前面，注视着并排放在桌上的大礼帽。"
"“One minute!” said Soames, suddenly, and crossing the room, he opened a door opposite.","“等一下！”索姆斯突然说，然后他穿过房间，打开了对面的一扇门。"
"There, as the young clerk had said, was a sort of lobby between Board Room and Manager’s Room, with a door at the end into the main corridor.","正如那个年轻的职员所说的，在董事会会议室和经理室之间有一个大厅，它的尽头是一扇通向走廊的门。"
"He stepped back, closed the door, and, rejoining Sir Lawrence, resumed his contemplation of the hats.","他退了回来，关上门，又和劳伦斯爵士站在一起，继续注视着那两顶帽子。"
"“Geography correct,” he said with gloom.","“地形是对的。”他忧郁地说。"
"The entrance of the manager was marked by Sir Lawrence’s monocle dropping on to his coat-button with a tinkle.","经理进来的时候，劳伦斯爵士的单片眼镜叮当一声掉在了他的大衣纽扣上。"
"In cutaway black coat, clean-shaven, with grey eyes rather baggy underneath, a pink colour, every hair in place on a rather bald egg-shaped head, and lips alternately pouting, compressed, or smiling, the manager reminded Soames ridiculously of old Uncle Nicholas in his middle period.","经理穿着下摆裁成圆角的黑色外套，胡子刮得很干净，一双灰色的眼睛下有着大大的眼袋，粉红色的皮肤，头发不多的鸡蛋型脑袋上，每一根头发都梳得很整齐；他嘴唇时而撅起，时而紧闭，又时而露出微笑，他的模样莫名其妙地使索姆斯联想到了当年人处中年的老尼古拉斯叔叔。"
"Uncle Nick was a clever fellow—“cleverest man in London,” some one had called him—but none had ever impugned his honesty.","尼克叔叔是个聪明人——有人称他为“伦敦最聪明的人”——但是从来没有人对他的诚实表示过怀疑。"
"A pang of doubt and disinclination went through Soames.","索姆斯感到一阵怀疑和厌恶的痛苦。"
"This seemed a monstrous thing to have to put to a man of his own age and breeding.","怀疑一个和自己年龄相仿且受过同等教育的人，这似乎是一件非常荒谬的事情。"
"But young Butterfield’s eyes—so honest and doglike!","但是年轻的巴特菲尔德的眼睛——那么真诚和忠实！"
"Invent a thing like that—was it possible?","捏造这样一件事情——可能吗？"
"He said abruptly:","他突然说："
"“Is that door shut?”","“那扇门关着吗？”"
"“Yes; do you feel a draught?” said the manager.","“关着呢，您是不是觉得有一股过堂风？”经理说，"
"“Would you like a fire?”","“要不要把火生上？”"
"“No, thank you,” said Soames.","“不用了，谢谢你，”索姆斯说，"
"“The fact is, Mr. Elderson, a young man in this office came to me yesterday with a very queer story.","“事情是这样的，埃尔德森先生。这个办公室的一个年轻人昨天来找我，并给我讲了一件非常奇怪的事情。"
"Mont and I think you should hear it.”","蒙特和我认为你应该听一下。”"
"Accustomed to watching people’s eyes, Soames had the impression of a film (such as passes over the eyes of parrots) passing over the eyes of the manager.","索姆斯习惯于观察人们的眼睛，他觉得有一层薄膜（就像鹦鹉眼睛上滑过的薄膜）掠过了经理的眼睛。"
"It was gone at once, if, indeed, it had ever been.","如果它确实存在的话，那也是一闪而过的。"
"“By all means.”","“当然可以。”"
"Steadily, with that power he had over his nerves when it came to a point, and almost word for word, Soames repeated a story which he had committed to heart in the watches of the night.","每到紧要关头，索姆斯都有控制自己情绪的能力，他沉着地几乎一字一句地把他在夜不成寐时熟记于心的事情复述了一遍。"
"He concluded with:","最后他说："
"“You’d like him in, no doubt.","“毫无疑问，你想让他进来一下吧。"
"His name is Butterfield.”","他的名字叫做巴特菲尔德。”"
"During the recital Sir Lawrence had done nothing but scrutinise his finger nails; he now said:","在索姆斯叙述这件事的过程中，劳伦斯爵士只是仔细地观察着自己的手指甲，这时他说："
"“You had to be told, Elderson.”","“我们必须告诉你这件事，埃尔德森。”"
"“Naturally.”","“当然。”"
"The manager was crossing to the bell.","经理穿过房间去按铃。"
"The pink in his cheeks looked harder; his teeth showed, they had a pointed look.","他双颊上的粉红色显得更深了，他的牙齿露了出来，看起来很尖锐的样子。"
"“Ask Mr. Butterfield to come here.”","“让巴特菲尔德先生到这儿来一下。”"
"There followed a minute of elaborate inattention to each other.","接下来的一分钟，他们故意不去注意彼此。"
"Then the young man came in, neat, commonplace, with his eyes on the manager’s face.","然后那个年轻人进来了，打扮得整洁、平凡，眼睛看着经理的脸。"
"Soames had a moment of compunction.","索姆斯一时间感到有些内疚。"
"This young fellow held his life in his hands, as it were—one of the great army who made their living out of self-suppression and respectability, with a hundred ready to step into his shoes at his first slip.","可以说，这个年轻人把他的生命掌握在他的手中——他是依靠自我克制和受人尊重来谋生的庞大人群中的一员，只要他一犯错误，就会有一百个人来接替他的位置。"
"What was that old tag of the provincial actor’s declamation—at which old Uncle Jolyon used to cackle so?","那个乡下演员朗诵的陈旧的结束语是什么——老乔里恩叔叔过去常常念叨的？"
"“Like a pale martyr with his shirt on fire.”","“就像一个衬衣着了火的面色苍白的殉道者。”"
"“So, Mr. Butterfield, you have been good enough to exercise your imagination in my regard.”","“那么，巴特菲尔德先生，你在关于我的事情上充分发挥想象力了吧。”"
"“No, sir.”","“没有，先生。”"
"“You stick to this fantastic story of eavesdropping?”","“你坚信这个偷听来的荒诞离奇的故事吗？”"
"“Yes, sir.”","“是的，先生。”"
"“We have no further use for your services then.","“那么我们再也用不着你在这里工作了。"
"Good morning!”","再见！”"
"The young man’s eyes, doglike, sought the face of Soames; a string twitched in his throat, his lips moved without a sound.","那个年轻人的眼睛像狗的眼睛一样，寻找着索姆斯的脸，他的喉咙里有根筋在抽搐，嘴唇悄无声息地动了动。"
"He turned and went out.","他转身走了出去。"
"“So much for that,” said the manager’s voice; “HE’LL never get another job.”","“这件事就到此为止吧，”经理说，“他再也找不到工作了。”"
"The venom in those words affected Soames like the smell of Russian fat.","这句话里的恶意就像俄罗斯肥肉的气味一样侵袭着索姆斯。"
"At the same moment he had the feeling: This wants thinking out.","与此同时他感到：这件事要彻底地想一想。"
"Only if innocent, or guilty and utterly resolved, would Elderson have been so drastic.","只有在无辜，或者是有罪且横下一条心的情况下，埃尔德森才会如此过激。"
"Which was he?","他属于哪一种情况呢？"
"The manager went on:","经理继续说："
"“I thank you for drawing my attention to the matter, gentlemen.","“谢谢你们让我注意到这件事，先生们。"
"I have had my eye on that young man for some time.","我注意那个年轻人已经有一段时间了。"
"A bad hat all round.”","他是个彻头彻尾的坏蛋。”"
"Soames said glumly:","索姆斯闷闷不乐地说："
"“What do you make out he had to gain?”","“你觉得他这样做对自己有什么好处呢？”"
"“Foresaw dismissal, and thought he would get in first.”","“他预料到会被解雇，于是就想要先发制人。”"
"“I see,” said Soames.","“我明白了。”索姆斯说。"
"But he did not.","但是他不明白。"
"His mind was back in his own office with Gradman rubbing his nose, shaking his grey head, and Butterfield’s: “No, sir, I’ve nothing against Mr. Elderson, and he’s nothing against me.”","他回想起在自己的办公室里，格雷德曼一边擦着鼻子，一边摇着满头白发的脑袋以及巴特菲尔德说的：“没有，先生，我没有什么针对埃尔德森先生的事情，他也没有什么针对我的事情。”"
"‘I shall require to know more about that young man,’ he thought.","“我需要了解关于那个年轻人的更多的情况。”他想。"
"The manager’s voice again cut through.","经理的声音又一次传入他的耳朵。"
"“I’ve been thinking over what you said yesterday, Mr. Forsyte, about an action lying against the Board for negligence.","“我一直在考虑您昨天说的话，福赛特先生，关于有人会控告董事会失职的问题。"
"There’s nothing in that; our policy has been fully disclosed to the shareholders at two general meetings, and has passed without comment.","这没什么可担心的，我们的方针政策已经在两次股东大会上向股东们充分说明了，而且没有任何异议就通过了。"
"The shareholders are just as responsible as the Board.”","股东们和董事会一样负有责任。”"
"“H’m!” said Soames, and took up his hat.","“呣！”索姆斯说着，拿起了帽子，"
"“Are you coming, Mont?”","“你走吗，蒙特？”"
"As if summoned from a long distance, Sir Lawrence galvanitically refixed his monocle.","仿佛听到了远方的召唤一样，劳伦斯爵士触电似的重新戴上了他的单片眼镜。"
"“It’s been very distasteful,” he said; “you must forgive us, Elderson.","“这件事非常令人不快，”他说，“你必须原谅我们，埃尔德森。"
"You had to be told.","我们不得不告诉你。"
"I don’t think that young man can be quite all there—he had a peculiar look; but we can’t have this sort of thing, of course.","我认为那个年轻人头脑不是很清醒——他的样子很奇怪，但是，当然了，我们不能允许这种事情发生。"
"Good-bye, Elderson.”","再见，埃尔德森。”"
"Placing their hats on their heads simultaneously the two walked out.","他们两个同时戴上帽子，走了出去。"
"They walked some way without speaking.","他们默默地走了一段路。"
"Then Sir Lawrence said:","然后劳伦斯爵士说："
"“Butterfield?","“巴特菲尔德？"
"My brother-inlaw has a head gardener called Butterfield—quite a good fellow.","我的姐夫有一个园丁主管叫巴特菲尔德——是一个非常好的人。"
"Ought we to look into that young man, Forsyte?”","我们是不是应该调查一下那个年轻人，福赛特？”"
"“Yes,” said Soames, “leave him to me.”","“是的，”索姆斯说，“交给我办吧。”"
"“I shall be very glad to.","“我很乐意把这件事交给你。"
"The fact is, when one has been at school with a man, one has a feeling, don’t you know.”","事实是，当一个人和另一个人当过同学以后，对这个人就会有一种感情，你是知道的。”"
"Soames gave vent to a sudden outburst.","索姆斯突然发泄起来。"
"“You can’t trust anyone nowadays, it seems to me,” he said.","“在我看来，如今你谁都不能相信，”他说，"
"“It comes of—well, I don’t know what it comes of.","“这是因为——哦，我也不知道这是因为什么。"
"But I’ve not done with this matter yet.”","但是这件事我不会就此罢手。”"

"Chapter IX","第九章"
"Sleuth","侦探"
"The Hotch-potch Club went back to the eighteen-sixties.","大杂烩俱乐部的历史可以追溯到19世纪60年代。"
"Founded by a posse of young sparks, social and political, as a convenient place in which to smoulder, while qualifying for the hearths of ‘Snooks’, The Remove, The Wayfarers, Burton’s, Ostrich Feather, and other more permanent resorts, the Club had, chiefly owing to a remarkable chef in its early days, acquired a stability and distinction of its own.","它由一群社会上的和政党中的翩翩少年们创办的，是一个韬光养晦的方便去处，以便获得加入“轻蔑”、利姆夫、旅行者、伯顿、鸵鸟羽毛以及其他更为永久的场所的资格。在俱乐部成立初期，它因为有一名非常杰出的厨师而获得了稳固的地位和名声。"
"It still, however, retained a certain resemblance to its name, and this was its attraction to Michael—all sorts of people belonged.","但是，它仍然保持着和它的名字相似的地方，这也是它吸引迈克尔的地方——各色人等一应俱全。"
"From Walter Nazing, and young semi-writers and patrons of the stage, who went to Venice, and talked of being amorous in gondolas, or of how so-and-so ought to be made love to; from such to bottle-brushed demi-generals, who had sat on courts-martial and shot men out of hand for the momentary weaknesses of human nature; from Wilfrid Desert (who never came there now) to Maurice Elderson, in the card-room, he could meet them all, and take the temperature of modernity.","这里有沃尔特·内津以及年轻的兼职作家和舞台赞助人——他们去过威尼斯，谈论着在凤尾船里的恋爱，或者应该如何向某某人求爱；还有嗜酒如命的低级将领们，他们曾坐在军事法庭上，为了人性一时的软弱而立即将人枪毙；还有威尔弗里德·德赛特（现在他再也不来这里了）和莫里斯·埃尔德森。在棋牌室里，他什么人都能见得到，而且还能感受现代事物。"
"He was doing this in the Hotch-potch smoking-room, the late afternoon but one after Fleur had come into his bed, when he was informed:","就在弗勒上了他的床的第二天下午的晚些时候，他正在大杂烩的吸烟室感受现代事物，这时有人通知他："
"“A Mr. Forsyte, sir, in the hall for you.","“先生，有一位福赛特先生在大厅里等你。"
"Not the member we had here many years before he died; his cousin, I think.”","不是生前在我们这里做了许多年会员的那个人，我想，是他的堂兄弟。”"
"Conscious that his associates at the moment would not be his father-inlaw’s ‘dream,’ nor he theirs, Michael went out, and found Soames on the weighing machine.","迈克尔很清楚，此刻他的同伴们不是他的岳父“梦想见到的人”，他的岳父也不是他的同伴们“梦想见到的人”，迈克尔走了出去，发现索姆斯正站在体重计上。"
"“I don’t vary,” he said, looking up.","“我的体重没什么变化，”他说着，抬起头来，"
"“How’s Fleur?”","“弗勒好吗？”"
"“Very well, thank you, sir.”","“很好，谢谢您，先生。”"
"“I’m at Green Street.","“我现在住在格林大街。"
"I stayed up about a young man.","因为一个年轻人，我彻夜未眠。"
"Have you any vacancy in your office for a clerk—used to figures.","你的办公室里有没有职员的空缺——他过去是做账的。"
"I want a job for him.”","我想给他找个工作。”"
"“Come in here, sir,” said Michael, entering a small room.","“请跟我来，先生。”迈克尔说着，走进了一个小房间。"
"Soames followed and looked round him.","索姆斯跟了进去，环顾四周。"
"“What do you call this?” he said.","“你们把这儿叫做什么？”他说。"
"“Well, we call it ‘the grave’; it’s nice and quiet.","“哦，我们把它叫做‘坟墓’，这里又舒服又安静。"
"Will you have a sherry?”","您要来一杯雪利酒吗？”"
"“Sherry!” repeated Soames.","“雪利酒！”索姆斯重复道，"
"“You young people think you’ve invented sherry; when I was a boy no one dreamed of dining without a glass of dry sherry with his soup, and a glass of fine old sherry with his sweet.","“你们年轻人以为雪利酒是你们发明的。在我小时候，要是喝汤的时候没有一杯干雪利酒，吃甜点的时候没有一杯上好的陈年雪利酒，那是不可想象的。"
"Sherry!”","雪利酒！”"
"“I quite believe you, sir.","“我完全相信您的说法，先生。"
"There really is nothing new.","确实没有什么新鲜的。"
"Venice, for instance—wasn’t that the fashion, too; and knitting, and royalties?","例如，威尼斯——以前不也很时尚吗，还有针织品、版税？"
"It’s all cyclic.","一切都是周期性的。"
"Has your young man got the sack?”","您的那个年轻人是不是被解雇了？”"
"Soames stared.","索姆斯盯着他。"
"“Yes,” he said, “he has.","“是的，”他说，“他被解雇了。"
"His name is Butterfield; he wants a job.”","他的名字叫做巴特菲尔德，他想要一份工作。”"
"“That’s frightfully rife; we get applications every day.","“这非常普遍，我们每天都会收到一些求职信。"
"I don’t want to be swanky, but ours is a rather specialised business.","我不想炫耀，但是我们的工作专业性很强。"
"It has to do with books.”","它和书本有关。”"
"“He strikes me as capable, orderly, and civil; I don’t see what more you want in a clerk.","“他给我的印象是有能力、有条理和有礼貌，我不知道你对一个职员还能再要求些什么。"
"He writes a good hand, and, so far as I can see, he tells the truth.”","他写得一手好字，而且，据我所知，他很诚实。”"
