"Only one book in twenty is a necessity really, the rest are luxuries.","20本书里面只有一本是真正必要的，其他的都是奢侈品。"
"Your stunt will be to make them believe the nineteen are necessaries, and the twentieth a luxury that they need.","你的绝招就是要让他们相信这19本书是必要的，而第二十本书是他们需要的一件奢侈品。"
"It’s like food or clothes, or anything else in civilisation.”","书就像是食物或衣服，或者文明世界中的任何其他的东西。”"
"“Yes, sir, I quite understand.”","“是的，先生，我非常明白。”"
"“All right, then.","“那么，很好。"
"Good-night, and good luck!”","晚安，祝你好运！”"
"Michael stood up and held out his hand.","迈克尔站起来，伸出手。"
"The young man took it with a queer reverential little bow.","年轻人握着他的手，古怪而尊敬地鞠了一小躬。"
"A minute later he was out in the street; and Michael in the hall was thinking: ‘Pity is tripe!","一分钟以后，他已经走在了街上。迈克尔在大厅里想着：“怜悯就是扯淡！"
"Clean forgot I was a sleuth!’","把我是侦探这件事忘得干干净净吧！”"

"Chapter X","第十章"
"Face","脸"
"When Michael rose from the refectory table, Fleur had risen, too.","当迈克尔从细长的餐桌旁站起来时，弗勒也跟着站了起来。"
"Two days and more since she left Wilfrid’s rooms, and she had not recovered zest.","离开威尔弗里德的公寓两天多了，她一直都无精打采。"
"The rifling of the oyster Life, the garlanding of London’s rarer flowers which kept colour in her cheeks, seemed stale, unprofitable.","打破牡蛎式的封闭生活，佩戴伦敦的奇花异草编织的花冠来保持气色红润，这些似乎都已变得乏味无益。"
"Those three hours, when from shock off Cork Street she came straight to shocks in her own drawing-room, had dislocated her so that she had settled to nothing since.","那三个小时，从科克大街到自家客厅所经历的一系列惊吓，都令她心惊肉跳，以致到现在还不能平静。"
"The wound re-opened by Holly had nearly healed again.","被霍莉重新揭开的疮疤已差不多愈合了。"
"Dead lion beside live donkey cuts but dim figure.","死在活驴身旁的狮子给人留下了丝毫没有威严的可悲印象。"
"But she could not get hold again of—what?","但她不可能再获得——什么呢？"
"That was the trouble: What?","问题就在这里：是什么呢？"
"For two whole days she had been trying.","足足两天的时间里，她一直在思索着这个问题。"
"Michael was still strange, Wilfrid still lost, Jon still buried alive, and nothing seemed novel under the sun.","迈克尔依然是那么陌生，威尔弗里德依然还是失去了，乔恩依然不能去想，天底下似乎没有一件新奇的事情。"
"The only object that gave her satisfaction during those two dreary, disillusioned days was the new white monkey.","在那郁闷、心灰意冷的两天里，唯一使她感到满足的就是那幅新送来的白猿了。"
"The more she looked at it, the more Chinese it seemed.","她越端详这幅画，这幅画就越显示出中国的风格。"
"It summed up the satirical truth of which she was perhaps subconscious, that all her little modern veerings and flutterings and rushings after the future showed that she believed in nothing but the past.","这幅画概括了也许在她下意识中也认可的具有讽刺意味的事实——除了过去，其他皆不可信——她对于未来所表现出的具有现代特点的小犹豫、不安分以及仓促行事都说明了这一点。"
"The age had overdone it and must go back to ancestry for faith.","这个时代已经过于浮夸，必须回到祖先那里去重寻信仰了。"
"Like a little bright fish out of a warm bay, making a splash in chill, strange waters, Fleur felt a subtle nostalgia.","此时，弗勒心头涌起一丝怀旧情绪，就像一条来自温暖海湾的活泼小鱼，在寒冷陌生的水域溅起水花。"
"In her Spanish room, alone with her own feelings, she stared at the porcelain fruits. They glowed, cold, uneatable!","她在西班牙式的房间里，端详着瓷水果，独自想着心事。那些果子色彩鲜艳、冰冷，不可食用。"
"She took one up.","她拿起一个。"
"Meant for a passion fruit?","把它看成激情的果实吗？"
"Alas!","啊！"
"Poor passion!","可怜的激情！"
"She dropped it with a dull clink on to the pyramid, and shuddered a little.","她把它扔回去，瓷果子落在果堆上，发出沉闷的碰撞声，这不禁使她为之一震。"
"Had she blinded Michael with her kisses?","她的吻已经蒙蔽了迈克尔吗？"
"Blinded him to—what?","蒙蔽他——什么呢？"
"To her incapacity for passion?","让他相信她已经没有激情了？"
"‘But I’m not incapable,’ she thought; ‘I’m not.","“但是我不是没有激情啊，”她想，“不是啊。"
"Some day I’ll show him; I’ll show them all.’","总有一天我让他看看，让所有人都看看。”"
"She looked up at ‘the Goya’ hanging opposite.","她抬眼看了看挂在对面的那幅戈雅的画。"
"What gripping determination in the painting—what intensity of life in the black eyes of a rather raddled dame!","画作体现了多么强的坚定决心——浓妆艳抹的贵妇，黑黑的眼眸闪烁着生活的激情！"
"SHE would know what she wanted, and get it, too!","她肯定知道自己想要什么，而且一定要得到它！"
"No compromise and uncertainty there—no capering round life, wondering what it meant, and whether it was worth while, nothing but hard living for the sake of living!","没有一丝妥协和犹豫——不游戏人生，猜测生活的意义；不论是否值得，只有为了生活而努力活着！"
"Fleur put her hands where her flesh ended, and her dress began.","弗勒把手放在裸露的那部分肉体上。"
"Wasn’t she as warm and firm—yes, and ten times as pretty, as that fine and evil-looking Spanish dame, with the black eyes and the wonderful lace?","与那有着一双黑眼眸，穿着镶满蕾丝的服饰，面容姣好而又面带邪念的西班牙女郎相比，难道她不是同样温情和坚定吗——而且比她漂亮十倍？"
"And, turning her back on the picture, she went into the hall.","是的，她转过身背对着那幅画，向门厅走去。"
"Michael’s voice and another’s!","迈克尔和另一个人的声音！"
"They were coming down!","他们正从楼上下来！"
"She slipped across into the drawing-room and took up the manuscript of a book of poems, on which she was to give Michael her opinion.","她悄悄穿过门厅，溜进客厅，拿起一本诗集原稿。她要把对这本书的意见告诉迈克尔。"
"She sat, not reading, wondering if he were coming in.","她坐在那里，并没有阅读稿子，而是猜想着迈克尔是否会进来。"
"She heard the front door close.","她听见关大门的声音。"
"No!","不会进来了！"
"He had gone out!","他已经出去了！"
"A relief, yet chilling!","一阵轻松，但又有些心寒！"
"Michael not warm and cheerful in the house—if it were to go on, it would be wearing.","迈克尔在这里感觉不到温暖和愉快——如果长此下去，一定会令人厌烦的。"
"She curled herself up and tried to read.","她蜷起身子，试图读上一点儿。"
"Dreary poems—free verse, blank, introspective, all about the author’s inside!","枯燥的诗歌——自由体、无韵、内心自省，都是描写作者内心世界的！"
"No lift, no lilt!","没有激情，没有韵律！"
"Duds!","毫无新意！"
"She seemed to have read them a dozen times before.","她似乎已经读过十几遍了。"
"She lay quite still—listening to the click and flutter of the burning logs!","她安静地躺在那里——倾听着燃烧的干柴发出的噼啪声！"
"If the light were out she might go to sleep.","要是没有灯光，她会睡着的。"
"She turned it off, and came back to the settee.","她关了灯，又回到那张长靠椅上。"
"She could see herself sitting there, a picture in the firelight; see how lonely she looked, pretty, pathetic, with everything she wished for, and—nothing!","她可以看到自己独自坐在那里的身影，犹如火光中的一幅画。她是那么孤单、漂亮、哀婉动人，拥有她想要的一切，但又——一无所有！"
"Her lip curled.","她撅起了嘴。"
"She could even see her own spoiled-child ingratitude.","她甚至可以看到自己好像被宠坏了的孩子一样忘恩负义。"
"And what was worse, she could see herself seeing it—a triple-distilled modern, so subtly arranged in life-tight compartments that she could not be submerged.","而且更加糟糕的是，她亲眼目睹这一切——一个经过反复修炼的时髦人物，却被如此巧妙地安排在犹如密闭的船舱一般的生活中，让她无法沉沦。"
"If only something would blow in out of the unkempt cold, out of the waste and wilderness of a London whose flowers she plucked.","如果伦敦——这个让她享受了荣华富贵的地方，有一种力量能够一扫凛冽的寒冷，除掉垃圾和荒野，那该多好啊。"
"The firelight—soft, uncertain—searched out spots and corners of her Chinese room, as on a stage in one of those scenes, seductive and mysterious, where one waited, to the sound of tambourines, for the next moment of the plot.","柔和、摇曳的火光照到了这间中国式的房间的一个角落，好像舞台上上演的一幕幕充满诱惑与神秘的戏剧，观众在铃鼓声中期待着剧情的发展。"
"She reached out and took a cigarette.","她伸手拿了一支香烟。"
"She could see herself lighting it, blowing out the smoke—her own half-curled fingers, her parted lips, her white rounded arm.","她可以看到自己点燃了香烟，喷出烟来——她那弯曲的手指、张开的双唇和白皙圆润的手臂。"
"She was decorative!","她就是一个装饰品！"
"Well, and wasn’t that all that mattered?","哦，难道一切问题的关键就在这里？"
"To be decorative, and make little decorations; to be pretty in a world that wasn’t pretty!","装饰，但无需装潢，要在一个不美的世界里依然保持美丽！"
"In ‘Copper Coin’ there was a poem of a flicker-lit room, and a spoiled Columbine before the fire, and a Harlequin hovering without, like ‘the spectre of the rose.’","《铜币》里有一首诗，叙述的是一间火光闪烁的房间里，一个被人宠坏了的科伦芭茵站在壁炉前，而门外徘徊着一个丑角，就像一个“玫瑰之魔”一样。"
"And suddenly, without warning, Fleur’s heart ached.","突然间，没有任何征兆，弗勒的心隐隐作痛。"
"It ached definitely, rather horribly, and, slipping down on to the floor before the fire, she snuggled her face against Ting-a-ling.","确实是心痛，很痛，她慢慢倒在壁炉前的地板上，用侧脸贴着小叮铃。"
"The Chinese dog raised his head—his black eyes lurid in the glow.","这只中国狗抬起头来——一双黑色的眼睛在火光中显得鲜红。"
"He licked her cheek, and turned his nose away.","它舔舔她的脸，然后把鼻子转过去。"
"Huf!","嘿！"
"Powder!","香粉的味道！"
"But Fleur lay like the dead.","但弗勒躺在那里，没了声息。"
"And she saw herself lying—the curve of her hip, the chestnut glow in her short hair; she heard the steady beat of her heart.","同时她看见自己躺在那里——那臀部的线条，还有闪着光泽的栗色短发。她听到自己的心跳声。"
"Get up!","起来！"
"Go out!","出去！"
"Do something!","干点儿事情！"
"But what—what was worth doing?","但是什么——什么值得去做呢？"
"What had any meaning in it?","什么事情有意义呢？"
"She saw herself doing—extravagant things; nursing sick women; tending pale babies; making a speech in Parliament; riding a steeplechase; hoeing turnips in knickerbockers—decorative.","她看到自己在做些怪诞的事情——护理生病的妇女；照料虚弱的婴儿；在议会里发表演讲；参加障碍赛马；穿着灯笼裤挖萝卜——成为装饰品。"
"And she lay perfectly still, bound by the filaments of her self-vision.","于是她安静地躺着，被自己看到的幻影束缚着。"
"So long as she saw herself she would do nothing—she knew it—for nothing would be worth doing!","只要她能看到自己，她就不会做任何事情——她清楚这一点——因为没有一件事值得去做！"
"And it seemed to her, lying there so still, that not to see herself would be worse than anything.","她静静地躺在那里，似乎对于她来讲，最糟糕的事情莫过于不去看自己。"
"And she felt that to feel this was to acknowledge herself caged for ever.","而且她意识到，体会着这种感觉就意味着承认自己将永远被囚禁在牢笼里。"
"Ting-a-ling growled, turning his nose towards the windows.","小叮铃咆哮起来，朝着窗口咆哮。"
"“In here,” he seemed to say, “we are cosy; we think of the past.","它似乎说：“我们在这里很舒服，我们怀念过去。"
"We have no use for anything outside.","我们不需要外面的任何东西。"
"Kindly go away—whoever it is out there!”","请走开吧——不论外面是谁！”"
"And again he growled—a low, continuous sound.","接着它又咆哮起来——不断地低声咆哮着。"
"“What is it, Ting?”","“怎么了，叮铃？”"
"Ting-a-ling rose on his fore-legs, with muzzle pointed at the window.","小叮铃的脸正对着窗户，前腿立起来。"
"“Do you want your walk?”","“你想要出去遛遛吗？”"
"“No,” said the growl.","“不。”它咆哮道。"
"Fleur picked him up.","弗勒把它抱起来。"
"“Don’t be so silly!”","“别傻叫！”"
"And she went to the window.","说着朝窗户走去。"
"The curtains were closely drawn; rich, Chinese, lined, they excluded the night.","窗帘拉得严严实实。这中国式窗帘很华美，还带着里衬，把夜色挡在窗外。"
"Fleur made a chink with one hand, and started back.","弗勒用一只手把窗帘拉开一条缝，大吃一惊，不由得往后退了一步。"
"Against the pane was a face, the forehead pressed against the glass, the eyes closed, as if it had been there a long time.","贴在玻璃上的是一张脸——前额紧贴着玻璃，双眼紧闭，似乎已经在那里很长时间了。"
"In the dark it seemed featureless, vaguely pale.","黑暗中，它显得面目模糊、苍白。"
"She felt the dog’s body stiffen under her arm—she felt his silence.","她感到小叮铃的身体在她的胳膊下变得僵硬了——她感到了小叮铃的沉默。"
"Her heart pumped.","她的心猛烈地跳着。"
"It was ghastly—face without body.","太可怕了——没有躯体的脸。"
"Suddenly the forehead was withdrawn, the eyes opened.","突然那前额缩了回去，睁开了双眼。"
"She saw—the face of Wilfrid.","她看清楚了——那是威尔弗里德的脸。"
"Could he see in-see her peering out from the darkened room?","他能看见里面——看见她从黑暗的屋里朝外张望吗？"
"Quivering all over, she let the curtains fall to.","她浑身颤抖，松手把窗帘合上。"
"Beckon?","打招呼？"
"Let him in?","请他进来？"
"Go out to him?","出去见他？"
"Wave him away?","还是挥手让他离开？"
"Her heart beat furiously.","她的心狂跳不止。"
"How long had he been out there—like a ghost?","他在窗外呆了多久——像个幽灵一样？"
"What did he want of her?","他对她有什么企图？"
"She dropped Ting-a-ling with a flump, and pressed her hands to her forehead, trying to clear confusion from her brain.","她砰地扔下小叮铃，双手按住前额，想要把这一切混乱全部忘记。"
"And suddenly she stepped forward and flung the curtains apart.","突然，她走上前，一把拉开窗帘。"
"No face!","没有脸！"
"Nothing!","什么都没有！"
"He was gone!","他走了！"
"The dark, draughty square—not a soul in it!","那狂风大作、黑漆漆的大街上——一个人影也没有！"
"Had he ever been—or was the face her fancy?","他到底来过没有——或者说她看到的那张脸只是幻觉？"
"But Ting-a-ling!","但是小叮铃看到了！"
"Dogs had no fancies.","狗不可能有幻觉啊。"
"He had gone back to the fire and settled down again.","它已经回到壁炉前，安静地趴在那里。"
"‘It’s not my fault,’ she thought passionately.","“这不是我的错，”她情绪激动地想着，"
"‘It’s not!","“不是！"
"I didn’t want him to love me.","我没有要他爱我。"
"I only wanted his—his—!’","我只是想要他的——他的——！”"
"Again she sank down before the fire.","她又倒在了壁炉前的地板上，"
"“Oh!","“哦！"
"Ting, have a feeling heart!”","叮铃，发发慈悲！”"
"But the Chinese dog, mindful of the flump, made no response....","但这条中国狗还记恨着刚才她把它扔下的那一幕，根本不理她……"

"Chapter XI","第十一章"
"Cocked Hat","三角帽"
"After missing his vocation with the young man Butterfield, Michael had hesitated in the hall.","由于年轻人巴特菲尔德的到访，使迈克尔未完成任务。他在门厅犹豫徘徊了一阵。"
"At last he had not gone upstairs again, but quietly out.","最后他还是决定不上楼，而是选择静悄悄地出去了。"
"He walked past the Houses of Parliament and up Whitehall.","他经过议会大厦，走在白厅大街上。"
"In Trafalgar Square, it occurred to him that he had a father.","在特拉法尔加广场上，他忽然想起自己还有个父亲。"
"Bart might be at ‘Snooks’, The Coffee House, The Aeroplane; and, with the thought, ‘He’d be restful,’ he sought the most modern of the three.","准爵爷也许在“轻蔑”俱乐部，也许在咖啡厅，或者是在飞机俱乐部。于是，抱着“他会使人心静”的念头，他找到了上述三个地方中最时髦的一个。"
"“Yes, Sir Lawrence Mont is in the lounge, sir.”","“是的，先生，劳伦斯·蒙特爵士在休息室。”"
"He was sitting with knees crossed, and a cigar between his finger-tips, waiting for some one to talk to.","他跷着二郎腿坐在那里，手指缝夹着一只雪茄，正等着和人聊天。"
"“Ah!","“啊！"
"Michael!","迈克尔！"
"Can you tell me why I come here?”","你知道我为什么来这儿吗？”"
"“To wait for the end of the world, sir?”","“是为了等待世界末日吗，先生？”"
"Sir Lawrence sniggered.","劳伦斯爵士咧嘴笑了一下。"
"“An idea,” he said.","“说得好，”他说，"
"“When the skies are wrecking civilisation, this will be the best-informed tape in London.","“当大祸临头时，恐怕这个地方是伦敦消息最灵通的地方了。"
"The wish to be in at the death is perhaps the strongest of our passions, Michael.","迈克尔，也许我们最强烈的愿望无非就是亲眼目睹猎物当场被咬死罢了。"
"I should very much dislike being blown up, especially after dinner; but I should still more dislike missing the next show if it’s to be a really good one.","我可绝不愿意被炸得粉身碎骨，尤其是在饱餐之后，但我更不愿意错过下一场演出，如果是一场精彩的演出的话。"
"The air raids were great fun, after all.”","毕竟空袭很有意思。”"
"Michael sighed.","迈克尔叹了口气。"
"“Yes,” he said, “the war got us used to thinking of the millennium, and then it went and stopped, and left the millennium hanging over us.","“是的，”他说，“大战很容易让我们联想到天下和平，但是交战几年后双方就休战了，而天下和平仍悬在我们的头顶上。"
"Now we shall never be happy till we get it.","如今我们要是不得到和平，就永远不会幸福。"
"Can I take one of your cigars, sir?”","我可以拿一支您的雪茄吗，先生？”"
"“My dear fellow!","“亲爱的年轻人！"
"I’ve been reading Frazer again.","最近我又在阅读弗雷泽的作品。"
"Extraordinary how remote all superstition seems, now that we’ve reached the ultimate truth: That enlightenment never can prevail.”","既然我们已经知道最后的真理是：启蒙运动永远不会成功，那么无论一切迷信是多么不切实际，都变得非同寻常了。”"
"Michael stopped the lighting of his cigar.","迈克尔停下来，不再点烟。"
"“Do you really think that, sir?”","“先生，您真的是这样想的吗？”"
"“What else can one think?","“除了这样，你还能想到些什么？"
"Who can have any reasonable doubt now that with the aid of mechanics the headstrong part of man must do him in?","有了机械学的帮助，刚愎自用的人类一定会自取灭亡——谁还会对此有疑问？"
"It’s an unavoidable conclusion from all recent facts.","从最近发生的所有事实来看，这是一条必然的结论。"
"‘Per ardua ad astra,’ ‘Through hard knocks we shall see stars.’”","‘力克困难获殊荣’，‘历经磨难方能见彩虹’。 ”"
"“But it’s always been like that, sir, and here we are alive?”","“先生，但是事情向来如此，我们不是还活着吗？”"
"“They say so, but I doubt it.","“别人都这么说，但是我很怀疑。"
"I fancy we’re really dead, Michael.","迈克尔，我认为我们确实完了。"
"I fancy we’re only living in the past.","我认为我们只是活在过去。"
"I don’t think—no, I don’t think we can be said to expect a future.","我不认为——不，我不认为我们可以被说成怀揣未来的梦想。"
"We talk of it, but I hardly think we hope for one.","我们现在谈未来，但我感觉我们并不希望有将来。"
"Underneath our protestations we subconsciously deduce.","在我们的各种抗议下，我们其实是在下意识地追本溯源。"
"From the mess we’ve made of it these last ten years, we can feel the far greater mess we shall make of it in the next thirty.","从近十年的混乱局面来看，我们可以感觉到，今后30年，局面可能会更加糟糕。"
"Human nature can argue the hind leg off a donkey, but the donkey will be four-legged at the end of the discussion.”","人类的本性就显现在争辩时可以说驴少了一条腿，但争到最后，驴还是四条腿齐全。”"
"Michael sat down suddenly and said:","迈克尔突然一屁股坐下，说道："
"“You’re a bad, bold Bart!”","“您真是一位胆量过人、了不起的准爵爷！”"
"Sir Lawrence smiled.","劳伦斯爵士笑了。"
"“I should be glad to think that men really believed in humanity, and all that, but you know they don’t—they believe in novelty and getting their own way.","“我倒是很愿意认为人们是相信人性的，或者是诸如此类的东西，但是你应该知道人们并不相信——他们相信新鲜奇特的事物，而且喜欢随心所欲。"
"With rare exceptions they’re still monkeys, especially the scientific variety; and when you put gunpowder and a lighted match into the paws of monkeys, they blow themselves up to see the fun.","除了少数特例外，他们仍然是猴子，尤其是从事科学研究的那种人。当你把火药和一根点燃的火柴放在那些猴子的手中时，它们会把自己炸得粉身碎骨，以看看这东西是多么有趣。"
"Monkeys are only safe when deprived of means to be otherwise.”","只有在手无寸铁的情况下，猴子们才是最安全的。”"
"“Lively, that!” said Michael.","“这话真妙！”迈克尔说。"
"“Not livelier than the occasion warrants, my dear boy.","“我亲爱的孩子，这并不比时势更妙。"
"I’ve been thinking.","我一直在想。"
"We’ve got a member here who knows a trick worth twenty of any played in the war—an extraordinarily valuable fellow.","我们这里有个会员，他的一条妙计抵得上20个参过战的战士——一个难能可贵的人才。"
"The Government have got their eye on him.","政府已经关注他了。"
"He’ll help the other valuable fellows in France and Germany and America and Russia to make history.","他正在帮助法国、德国、美国和俄国那些有价值的伙伴们去创造历史。"
"Between them, they’ll do something really proud—something that’ll knock all the other achievements of man into a cocked hat.","他们会做些令他们自己自鸣得意的事情——这些事情足以使人类的其他成就变得一文不值。"
"By the way, Michael, new device of ‘homo sapiens’—the cocked hat.”","顺便说一下，迈克尔，这可是‘智人’的新发明——三角帽。”"
"“Well,” said Michael, “what are you going to do about it?”","“那么，”迈克尔说，“您有何打算呢？”"
"Sir Lawrence’s eyebrow sought his hair.","劳伦斯爵士的眉毛高高挑起。"
"“Do, my dear fellow?","“我亲爱的年轻人，怎么办？"
"What should I do?","我该做什么？"
"Can I go out and grab him and the Government by the slack of their breeches; yes, and all the valuable fellows and Governments of the other countries?","我能出去抓住他和政府的裤脚吗？是的，那也去抓住其他国家的一切大人物和政府的？"
"No!","不能！"
"All I can do is to smoke my cigar and say: ‘God rest you, merry gentlemen, let nothing you dismay!’","我所能做的就是一边抽着雪茄，一边说：‘上帝保佑，快活的先生们，愿你们无忧无虑！’"
"By hook or crook, they will come into their own, Michael; but in the normal course of things I shall be dead before they do.”","迈克尔，他们会不择手段地中饱私囊，但按照事情发展的正常进程，在他们成功之前，我就死了。”"
"“I shan’t,” said Michael","“我不会。”迈克尔说。"
"“No, my dear; but think of the explosions, the sights, the smells.","“不会，亲爱的，但是想想爆炸的情景和那气味。"
"By Jove, you’ve got something to live for, yet.","啊，你还是有值得活下去的念想的。"
"Sometimes I wish I were your age.","有时我真希望自己还是你那样的年纪。"
"And sometimes,” Sir Lawrence relighted his cigar, “I don’t.","而有时呢，”劳伦斯爵士重新点燃了雪茄，“我又不希望。"
"Sometimes I think I’ve had enough of our pretences, and that there’s nothing left but to die like gentlemen.”","有时候我觉得我已经厌烦了我们的装腔作势，所以除了体面地死去之外，实在没有什么可挂念的了。”"
"“Some Jeremiad, Dad!”","“爸，真是悲壮啊！”"
"“Well,” said Sir Lawrence, with a twirl of his little grizzled moustache, “I hope I’m wrong.","“唉，”劳伦斯爵士捻了捻灰白色的小胡子说着，“我希望我错了。"
"But we’re driving fast to a condition of things when millions can be killed by the pressing of a few buttons.","但是我们现在正快速发展到这样的形势中，只要按下电钮，几百万人就会被杀死。"
"What reason is there to suppose that our bumps of benevolence will increase in time to stop our using these great new toys of destruction, Michael!”","但是设想一下，到底有什么原因可以增加我们的仁慈之心，去及时阻止我们使用崭新的且具有毁灭性的玩具呢，迈克尔！”"
"“‘Where you know little, place terrors.’”","“凡不了解的事情，就视为恐怖。”"
"“Very nice; where did you get that?”","“太对了，你是从哪儿看到这句话的？”"
"“Out of a life of Christopher Columbus.”","“从《克里斯托弗·哥伦布传》里看到的。”"
"“Old C. C.!","“老哥伦布！"
"I could bring myself to wish sometimes that he hadn’t been so deucedly inquisitive.","我有时还真希望他不那么好奇去发现新大陆。"
"We were snugger in the dark ages.","在黑暗时代，我们活得更安逸。"
"There was something to be said for not discovering the Yanks.”","人们有一些关于没发现美国佬的评论。”"
"“Well,” said Michael, “I think we shall pedal through, yet.","“嗯，”迈克尔说，“我认为我们还是可以跨越过去的。"
"By the way, about this Elderson stunt: I’ve just seen the clerk—he doesn’t look to me the sort that would have made that up.”","顺便说一下，关于埃尔德森耍的花招，我刚才见过那个职员，看着他不像是那种捏造事实的人。”"
"“Ah!","“啊！"
"That!","那件事！"
"But if Elderson could do such a thing, well—really, anything might happen.","但如果埃尔德森真做了那件事的话，唉——那就真是世事难料了。"
"It’s a complete stumper.","这绝对是一个难题。"
"He was such a pretty bat, always went in first wicket down.","他是一个击球能将，每当一个击球员被判出局后，总是能够轮到他上场。"
"He and I put on fifty-four against Eton.","我们俩曾经就以54分战胜了伊顿公学队。"
"I suppose old Forsyte told you?”","我猜是老福赛特告诉你的吧？”"
"“Yes, he wanted me to find the chap a job.”","“是，他让我给这个年轻人找份工作。”"
"“Butterfield.","“巴特菲尔德。"
"Ask him if he’s related to old Butterfield the gardener?","询问一下他是否跟园丁老巴特菲尔德有亲戚关系？"
"It would be something to go on.","从这儿可能获得线索。"
"D’you find old Forsyte rather trying?”","你觉得老福赛特很难对付吧？”"
"Loyal to Fleur, Michael concealed his lips.","出于对弗勒的忠诚，迈克尔抿住了嘴唇。"
"“No, I get on very well with him.”","“不，我和他相处得很好。”"
"“He’s straight, I admit that.”","“我承认他为人很正直。”"
"“Yes,” said Michael, “very straight.”","“是的，”迈克尔说，“非常正直。”"
"“But somewhat reticent.”","“就是有点儿沉默寡言。”"
"“Yes,” said Michael.","“是的。”迈克尔说。"
"On this conclusion they were silent, as though terrors had been placed beyond it.","说到这里，他们都沉默了，似乎再继续这个话题就会造成恐怖一样。"
"And soon Michael rose.","过了一会儿，迈克尔站了起来。"
"“Past ten, I’d better go home.”","“10点多了，我得回家了。”"
"Returning the way he came, he could think of nothing but Wilfrid.","他从来时的路上往回走，脑子里想的只有威尔弗里德。"
"What wouldn’t he give to hear him say: “It’s all right, old man; I’ve got over it!”—to wring him by the hand again.","他愿意付出任何代价，只要听到他说：“老朋友，一切都办妥了，我已经摆脱它了！”——同时再一次紧握他的手。"
"Why should one catch this fatal disease called love?","一个人为什么会患上一种叫爱的绝症呢？"
"Why should one be driven half crazy by it?","为什么一个人会被这种病逼得半疯半癫呢？"
"They said love was Nature’s provision against Bart’s terrors, against the valuable fellows.","人们说爱是应对准爵爷暴政的精神食粮，是对付朋友的精神支柱。"
"An insistent urge—lest the race die out.","一种强烈的欲望——以免断子绝孙。"
"Prosaic, if true!","即便是真的，也平淡无奇。"
"Not that he cared whether Fleur had children.","他并不在乎弗勒生不生孩子。"
"Queer how Nature camouflaged her schemes—leery old bird!","奇怪的是，她的本性怎会把她的计划伪装得如此天衣无缝——老滑头！"
"But overreaching herself a bit, wasn’t she?","但她伪装得有点儿过头，不是吗？"
"Children might yet go clean out of fashion if Bart was right.","如果准爵爷的话正确，那生孩子也许会变为落伍的行为。"
"A very little more would do it; who would have children for the mere pleasure of seeing them blown up, poisoned, starved to death?","很少有人愿意生孩子。有谁愿意接受生孩子仅是为了目睹他们被炸死、毒死或者饿死？"
"A few fanatics would hold on, the rest of the world go barren.","少数几个人会固执己见，但余下的世界会青黄不接。"
"The cocked hat!","三角帽！"
"Instinctively Michael straightened his own, ready for crossing under Big Ben.","迈克尔下意识地扶了扶帽子，准备从大本钟下面穿过马路。"
"He had reached the centre of Parliament Square, when a figure coming towards him swerved suddenly to its left and made in the direction of Victoria.","他刚走过议会广场的中央，一个人迎面朝他走来，突然向左转弯，向维多利亚大街的方向走去。"
"Tall, with a swing in its walk.","高高的个子，走路时身子一摇一晃的。"
"Wilfrid!","威尔弗里德！"
"Michael stood still.","迈克尔站在那里一动不动。"
"Coming from—South Square!","他从南广场走过来！"
"And suddenly he gave chase.","突然，他开始跟着威尔弗里德。"
"He did not run, but he walked his hardest.","他没有跑，只是加快了步伐。"
"The blood beat in his temples, and he felt confused to a pitch past bearing.","血涌到太阳穴，他脑子混乱到了令他难以忍受的地步。"
"Wilfrid must have seen him, or he wouldn’t have swerved, wouldn’t be legging it away like a demon.","威尔弗里德一定已经看见他了，否则他不会突然转弯的，也不会像幽灵一样飞奔。"
"Black!—black!","糟糕！——糟糕！"
"He was not gaining, Wilfrid had the legs of him—to overtake him, he must run!","他赶不上他，威尔弗里德比他走得快——想要赶上他，就得跑！"
"But there rose in Michael a sort of exaltation.","但就在此时，迈克尔心中不由产生一种得意之情。"
"His best friend—his wife!","他最好的朋友——他的妻子！"
"There was a limit.","任何事情都是有限度的。"
"One might be too proud to fight that.","一个人也许会很骄傲，而不屑与这些事情计较。"
"Let him go his ways!","随他便吧！"
"He stood still, watched the swift figure disappear, and slowly, head down under the now cocked hat, turned towards home.","他站在那里一动不动，看着那个快速行走的背影渐渐消失。此时，三角帽下的脑袋慢慢地下垂，转身回家了。"
"He walked quite quietly, and with a sense of finality.","他有一种尘埃落定的感觉，仍旧安静地走在路上。"
"No use making a song about it!","大吵大闹无济于事！"
"No fuss, but no retreat!","不吵，但也绝不退缩！"
"In the few hundred yards before he reached his Square he was chiefly conscious of the tallness of houses, the shortness of men.","在他离家门口的广场还有几百码的路上，他感觉到房屋建筑的高大和人类的渺小。"
"Such midgets to have made this monstrous pile, lighted it so that it shone in an enormous glittering heap whose glow blurred the colour of the sky!","这样渺小的人类却建造出如此辉煌高大的建筑物，让它灯火灿烂、闪闪发光，朦胧了夜晚的天空！"
"What a vast business this midget activity!","渺小的人类干了一番多么伟大的事业！"
"Absurd to think that his love for another midget mattered!","把他对另一个渺小人类的爱情看成一件至关重要的事，这是多么荒唐可笑啊！"
"He turned his key in the lock, took off his cocked hat and went into the drawing-room.","他用钥匙打开房门，摘下三角帽，走进客厅。"
"Unlighted—empty?","没有灯光——屋里没人吗？"
"No. She and Ting-a-ling were on the floor before the fire!","不对，她和小叮铃都在壁炉前的地板上！"
"He sat down on the settee, and was abruptly conscious that he was trembling and sweating as if he had smoked a too strong cigar.","他坐在长靠椅上，忽然感到自己浑身颤抖，一身冷汗，跟吸了一支味道强烈的雪茄似的。"
"Fleur had raised herself, cross-legged, and was staring up at him.","弗勒已经撑起身子，两腿交叉，正抬头注视着他。"
"He waited to get the better of his trembling.","他极力止住自己的颤抖。"
"Why didn’t she speak?","她为什么不说话？"
"Why was she sitting there, in the dark?","为什么她坐在那里，黑着灯？"
"‘She knows’; he thought: ‘we both know this is the end.","“她知道了，”他想，“我们两个人心里都清楚，这就是结局。"
"O God, let me at least be a sport!’","哦，上帝啊，起码让我像个有气度的男人吧！”"
"He took a cushion, put it behind him, crossed his legs, and leaned back.","他拿了一个靠垫，放在身后，翘着腿，往后靠着。"
"His voice surprised him suddenly:","他的声音突然使自己吓了一跳："
"“May I ask you something, Fleur?","“弗勒，我能问你一件事吗？"
"And will you please answer me quite truly?”","请诚实地回答我，好吗？”"
"“Yes.”","“好的。”"
"“It’s this: I know you didn’t love me when you married me.","“是这样的：我知道你和我结婚时并不爱我。"
"I don’t think you love me now.","我觉得现在你仍然不爱我。"
"Do you want me to clear out?”","你想让我离开吗？”"
"A long time seemed to pass.","似乎过去了很长时间。"
"“No.”","“不。”"
"“Do you mean that?”","“你说的是心里话？”"
"“Yes.”","“是的。”"
"“Why?”","“为什么呢？”"
"“Because I don’t.”","“因为我不愿意你离开。”"
"Michael got up.","迈克尔站起来。"
"“Will you answer one thing more?”","“你愿意再回答一个问题吗？”"
"“Yes.”","“愿意。”"
"“Was Wilfrid here to-night?”","“今晚威尔弗里德是不是来过这里？”"
"“Yes—no.","“是的——不是。"
"That is—”","那是——”"
"His hands clutched each other; he saw her eyes fix on them, and kept them still.","他的双手攥得很紧，他看见她的双眼盯着他的双手，就把双手停住不动。"
"“Fleur, don’t!”","“弗勒，别这样！”"
"“I’m not.","“我没有遮掩。"
"He came to the window there.","他在窗子外边。"
"I saw his face—that’s all.","我看到他的脸——仅此而已。"
"His face—it—Oh!","他的脸——它——啊！"
"Michael, don’t be unkind to-night!”","迈克尔，今晚别对我这么刻薄。”"
"Unkind!","刻薄！"
"Unkind!","刻薄！"
"Michael’s heart swelled at that strange word.","迈克尔听到这话，心里不是个滋味。"
"“It’s all right,” he stammered: “So long as you tell me what it is you want.”","“没问题，”他结结巴巴地说，“只要你告诉我你想要什么就可以了。”"
"Fleur said, without moving:","弗勒一动不动，说道："
"“I want to be comforted.”","“我需要得到安慰。”"
"Ah!","啊！"
"She knew exactly what to say, how to say it!","她完全清楚自己该说些什么，以及应用什么样的方式去说！"
"And going on his knees, he began to comfort her.","于是他跪着挪到她面前，开始安慰起她来。"

"Chapter XII","第十二章"
"Going East","到东方去"
"He had not been on his knees many minutes before they suffered from reaction.","没等他跪多久，他们彼此就都难受起来。"
"To kneel there comforting Fleur brought him a growing discomfort.","迈克尔跪在那里安慰弗勒，他感到越来越难受。"
"He believed her tonight, as he had not believed her for months past.","他今晚相信她，正如最近几个月不相信她一样。"
"But what was Wilfrid doing?","可是，威尔弗里德来这里干什么呢？"
"Where wandering?","他在哪里游荡呢？"
"The face at the window—face without voice, without attempt to reach her!","窗上的脸——无声的脸，也没试图接近她！"
"Michael ached in that illegitimate organ the heart.","想到这些，迈克尔的心隐隐作痛。"
"Withdrawing his arms, he stood up.","他抽回胳膊，站起身来。"
"“Would you like me to have a look for him?","“你希望我去看看他吗？"
"If it’s all over—he might—I might—”","如果一切都结束了——他也许——我也许——”"
"Fleur, too, stood up.","弗勒也站起身来。"
"She was calm enough now.","现在，她已经很平静了。"
"“Yes, I’ll go to bed.”","“好的，我准备睡觉了。”"
"With Ting-a-ling in her arms, she went to the door; her face, between the dog’s chestnut fur and her own, was very pale, very still.","她抱着小叮铃，向门口走去。在栗色头发和栗色狗毛的衬托下，她的脸显得非常苍白，但又十分平静。"
"“By the way,” she said, “this is my second no go, Michael; I suppose it means—”","“顺便说一下，”她说，“迈克尔，这是我第二个月没来月经了，我想这意味着——”"
"Michael gasped.","迈克尔喘息起来。"
"Currents of emotion, welling, ebbing, swirling, rendered him incapable of speech.","感情如潮水般起起伏伏、上下翻腾，他激动得说不出话来。"
"“The night of the balloon,” she said: “Do you mind?”","“就是拿气球的那天晚上。”她说，“你在乎吗？”"
"“Mind?","“在乎？"
"Good God!","天啊！"
"Mind!”","在乎！”"
"“That’s all right, then.","“那么，这就好了。"
"I don’t.","可我不在乎。"
"Good-night!”","晚安！”"
"She was gone.","她走了。"
"Without reason, Michael thought: ‘In the beginning was the Word, and the Word was with God, and the Word was God.’","迈克尔莫名其妙想到：“太初有道，道与上帝同在，道就是上帝。”"
"And he stood, as if congealed, overcome by an uncontrollable sense of solidity.","他站在那里，好像被一种难以控制的充实感给凝固了。"
"A child coming!","一个孩子要出生了！"
"It was as though the barque of his being, tossed and drifted, suddenly rode tethered—anchor down.","好像他的生命之舟经过漂泊、颠簸后，忽然被绳索拴住——停下来了。"
"He turned and tore at the curtains.","他转身拉开窗帘。"
"Night of stars!","满天星斗！"
"Wonderful world!","美妙的世界！"
"Jolly—jolly!","真开心——真开心！"
"And—Wilfrid!","可是——威尔弗里德！"
"He flattened his face against the glass.","他把脸紧紧贴在玻璃窗上。"
"Outside there Wilfrid’s had been flattened.","威尔弗里德的脸曾在这窗外紧贴着。"
"He could see it if he shut his eyes.","他一闭上眼睛，就能看到当时的情景。"
"Not fair!","不公平！"
"Dog lost—man lost!","狗失踪了——人失踪了！"
"S. O. S. He went into the hall, and from the mothless marble coffer rived his thickest coat.","紧急呼救。他走进大厅，从那不生蛀虫的大理石镶板上扯下他最厚的大衣。"
"He took the first taxi that came by.","他坐上了开来的第一辆出租车。"
"“Cork Street!","“科克大街！"
"Get along!”","走吧！”"
"Needle in bundle of hay!","真是大海捞针！"
"Quarter past eleven by Big Ben!","大本钟上显示11点15分了！"
"The intense relief of his whole being in that jolting cab seemed to him brutal.","坐在那辆颠簸的出租车里，他虽然觉得不舒服，却也非常痛快。"
"Salvation!","拯救灵魂！"
"It WAS—he had a strange certainty of that as though he saw Fleur suddenly ‘close-up’ in a very strong light, concrete beneath her graceful veerings.","的确如此——他对此深信不疑，仿佛看见弗勒突然以“特写镜头”出现在一片极强的光线中，在优美的镜头变换下，显得具体生动。"
"Family!","家庭！"
"Continuation!","传宗接代！"
"He had been unable to anchor her, for he was not of her!","他过去一直没能使她安定下来，因为他并不属于她！"
"But her child could and would!","但是孩子可以做到！"
"And, perhaps, he would yet come in with the milk.","也许，他会因此沾点儿光。"
"Why did he love her so—it was not done!","为什么他过去那么爱她——却没这么做呢！"
"Wilfrid and he were donkeys—out of touch, out of tune with the times!","威尔弗里德和他都是蠢驴——跟不上时代的步伐，不合时代的潮流！"
"“Here you are, sir—what number?”","“先生，到了——门牌号是多少？”"
"“All right!","“好！"
"Cool your heels and wait for me!","请别载客，等我一会儿！"
"Have a cigarette!”","抽支烟吧！”"
"With one between his own lips which felt so dry, he went down the backwater.","他往干得要命的嘴上夹了一支烟，向着后街走去。"
"A light in Wilfrid’s rooms!","威尔弗里德的房间还亮着灯！"
"He rang the bell.","于是他按下门铃。"
"The door was opened, the face of Wilfrid’s man looked forth.","门开了，威尔弗里德的男仆朝外张望着。"
"“Yes, sir?”","“什么事，先生？”"
"“Mr. Desert in?”","“德赛特先生在家吗？”"
"“No, sir.","“不在，先生。"
"Mr. Desert has just started for the East.","德赛特先生刚动身去东方了。"
"His ship sails tomorrow.”","船明天开。”"
"“Oh!” said Michael, blankly: “Where from?”","“啊！”迈克尔茫然地说，“从哪里出发？”"
"“Plymouth, sir.","“普利茅斯，先生。"
"His train leaves Paddington at midnight.","他夜里乘火车离开帕丁顿。"
"You might catch him yet.”","您也许还能赶上他。”"
"“It’s very sudden,” said Michael, “he never—”","“这太突然了。”迈克尔说，“他从来没有——”"
"“No, sir.","“是的，先生。"
"Mr. Desert is a sudden gentleman.”","德赛特先生是位出人意料的绅士。”"
"“Well, thanks; I’ll try and catch him.”","“好，谢谢，我试试看，去赶上他。”"
"Back in the cab with the words: “Paddington—flick her along!” he thought: ‘A sudden gentleman!’","他回到车上，说了句：“帕丁顿——开快点儿！”然后心里想着：“一位出人意料的绅士！”"
"Perfect!","妙得很！"
"He remembered the utter suddenness of that little interview beside the bust of Lionel Charwell.","他想起了在莱昂内尔·查韦尔半身塑像旁的那次完全意外的简短谈话。"
"Sudden their friendship, sudden its end—sudden even Wilfrid’s poems—offspring of a sudden soul!","他们的友谊开始得出人意料，结束得也出人意料——甚至连威尔弗里德的诗也是出人意料的——真是一个出人意料的灵魂的产物！"
"Staring from window to window in that jolting, rattling cab, Michael suffered from St. Vitus’s dance.","迈克尔坐在那辆颠簸又格格作响的出租车里，忍着圣维特舞蹈病般的痛苦，从一个窗口看到另一个窗口。"
"Was he a fool?","他是个傻瓜吗？"
"Could he not let well alone?","他不能由他去吗？"
"Pity was posh!","怜悯是没用的！"
"And yet!","然而！"
"With Wilfrid would go a bit of his heart, and in spite of all he would like him to know that.","随着威尔弗里德的离开，他的心也失去了一部分。尽管发生了这一切，他还是想让他知道这一点。"
"Upper Brook Street, Park Lane!","上溪街、公园巷！"
"Emptying streets, cold night, stark plane trees painted-up by the lamps against a bluish dark.","空寂的街道、冰冷的夜晚、光秃秃的法国梧桐——衬着深蓝色的夜幕，在街灯的照射下，这一切仿佛是一幅画。"
"And Michael thought: ‘We wander!","此时，迈克尔在想：“我们徘徊！"
"What’s the end—the goal?","结局是什么——目标又是什么？"
"To do one’s bit, and not worry!","各尽所能，不必烦恼！"
"But what is my bit?","我的能力是什么？"
"What’s Wilfrid’s?","威尔弗里德的又是什么？"
"Where will he end up, now?’","现在，他要到哪里结束呢？”"
"The cab rattled down the station slope and drew up under cover.","出租车顺着车站的斜坡格格作响地驶去，停在隐蔽处。"
"Ten minutes to twelve, and a long heavy train on platform one!","差10分钟12点，一号站台旁，一长列满载的火车停在那里。"
"‘What shall I do?’ thought Michael: ‘It’s so darned crude!","“我该怎么办？”迈克尔想，“这真是糟糕透顶！"
"Must I go down—carriage by carriage?”","我要不要走过去——一节车厢一节车厢地找？"
"Couldn’t let you go, old man, without”—blurb!’","不能让你走，老朋友，不能——废话！”"
"Bluejackets!","一群水兵！"
"If not drunk—as near as made no matter.","即使没喝醉——也跟喝醉差不多了。"
"Eight minutes still!","还剩八分钟！"
"He began slowly walking along the train.","他开始慢慢地沿着车厢走过去。"
"He had not passed four windows before he saw his quarry.","还没走过四个窗口，他就看见了要找的人。"
"Desert was sitting back to the engine in the near corner of an empty first.","德赛特坐在一节空无他人的头等车厢一个靠窗的角落里，背对着火车头。"
"An unlighted cigarette was in his mouth, his fur collar turned up to his eyes, and his eyes fixed on an unopened paper on his hip.","他嘴里含着一支没点燃的香烟，毛皮衣领一直立到眼睛下边，眼睛直直地盯着腿上没有打开的报纸。"
"He sat without movement; Michael stood looking at him.","他坐在那里，一动不动。迈克尔站在那里看着他。"
"His heart beat fast.","迈克尔心跳加快。"
"He struck a match, took two steps, and said:","他划了一根火柴，向前走了两步，说道："
"“Light, old boy?”","“点火吗，老朋友？”"
"Desert stared up at him.","德赛特抬头看着他。"
"“Thanks,” he said, and took the match.","“谢谢。”他说着接过了火柴。"
"By its flare his face was dark, thin, drawn; his eyes dark, deep, tired.","在摇曳的火光中，他脸色阴沉，面容消瘦而憔悴；他眼神阴郁、深沉而疲惫。"
"Michael leaned in the window.","迈克尔靠在窗口。"
"Neither spoke.","两个人都不说话。"
"“Take your seat, if you’re going, sir.”","“先生，请入座吧，如果您乘这班车走。”"
"“I’m not,” said Michael.","“我不走。”迈克尔说。"
"His whole inside seemed turning over.","他整个内心似乎都在翻腾着。"
"“Where are you going, old man?” he said suddenly.","“你打算去哪儿，老朋友？”他突然说。"
"“Jericho.”","“杰里科。”"
"“God, Wilfrid, I’m sorry!”","“天啊，威尔弗里德，我很抱歉！”"
"Desert smiled.","德赛特笑了。"
"“Cut it out!”","“废话少说！”"
"“Yes, I know!","“好吧，我知道！"
"Shake hands?”","握握手吗？”"
"Desert held out his hand.","德赛特伸出手。"
"Michael squeezed it hard.","迈克尔紧紧和他握手。"
"A whistle sounded.","汽笛声响了。"
"Desert rose suddenly and turned to the rack above him.","德赛特突然站起来，转向他座位上方的行李架。"
"He took a parcel from a bag.","他从旅行包里取出一包东西。"
"“Here,” he said, “these wretched things!","“这个，”他说，“这些没价值的东西！"
"Publish them if you like.”","如果你愿意，就把它们出版了吧。”"
"Something clicked in Michael’s throat.","迈克尔的喉咙哽咽了。"
"“Thanks, old man!","“谢谢，老朋友！"
"That’s great!","这太好了！"
"Good-bye!”","再见！”"
"A sort of beauty came into Desert’s face.","德赛特脸上浮现出一种美好的表情。"
"“So long!” he said.","“再见！”他说。"
"The train moved.","火车开动了。"
"Michael withdrew his elbows; quite still, he stared at the motionless figure slowly borne along, away.","迈克尔把手收回来，一动不动，凝视着那个一动不动的人被火车载向前方，渐渐远去。"
"Carriage after carriage went by him, full of bluejackets leaning out, clamouring, singing, waving handkerchiefs and bottles.","一节节载满水兵的车厢从他身旁经过，他们从车窗探出身体，叫嚷着，歌唱着，挥舞着手帕和酒瓶。"
"Guard’s van now—the tail light—all spread—a crimson blur—setting East—going—going—gone!","现在是列车员的车厢了——尾灯亮着——一切伸展开去——一片模糊的绯红色——向着东方——去了——去了——驶去了！"
"And that was all—was it?","事情就这样了结了——是吗？"
"He thrust the parcel into his coat pocket.","他把那包东西塞进大衣口袋里。"
"Back to Fleur, now!","现在，回到弗勒身边去吧！"
"Way of the world—one man’s meat, another’s poison!","世上的事情——一个人的美食，却是另一个人的毒药！"
"He passed his hand over his eyes.","他用手揉了一下眼睛。"
"The dashed things were full of—blurb!","这些飞驰而去的东西充斥着——废话！"

"Part III","第三卷"
"Chapter I","第一章"
"Bank Holiday","公休日"
"Whitsuntide Bank Holiday was producing its seasonal invasion of Hampstead Heath, and among the ascending swarm were two who meant to make money in the morning and spend it in the afternoon.","在降灵节公休日期间，汉普斯蒂荒地的游人络绎不绝。在蜂拥而至的人群中，有两个人打算上午赚一笔，下午就把它花掉。"
"Tony Bicket, with balloons and wife, embarked early on the Hampstead Tube.","托尼·比克特带着妻子和气球，一早就踏上去汉普斯蒂的地铁了。"
"“You’ll see,” he said, “I’ll sell the bloomin’ lot by twelve o’clock, and we’ll go on the bust.”","“你会看到的，”他说，“到12点，我就会把这些好东西全部卖光，然后我们就可以去痛痛快快地玩一把了。”"
"Squeezing his arm, Victorine fingered, through her dress, a slight swelling just above her right knee.","维多琳紧紧握着他的胳膊，同时隔着衣服摸摸右膝上方微微鼓起的地方。"
"It was caused by fifty-four pounds fastened in the top of her stocking.","这是因为在她长筒袜的上端捆有54镑钞票。"
"She had little feeling, now, against balloons.","现在，她对气球几乎没什么抵触情绪了。"
"They afforded temporary nourishment, till she had the few more pounds needful for their passage-money.","气球生意可以暂时补贴家用，直到她再赚几镑凑足他们的路费。"
"Tony still believed he was going to screw salvation out of his blessed balloons: he was ‘that hopeful—Tony,’ though their heads were only just above water on his takings.","托尼始终认为他将从这些神赐的气球上得到拯救，他是那个“怀有希望的——托尼”，尽管他的收入只够他们勉强维持生计。"
"And she smiled.","她笑了。"
"With her secret she could afford to be indifferent now to the stigma of gutter hawking.","她有自己的秘密，所以现在她可以承受站在街头叫卖的耻辱，对之抱以无所谓的态度了。"
"She had her story pat.","她已经把她的故事编好了。"
"From the evening paper, and from communion on ‘buses with those interested in the national pastime, she had acquired the necessary information about racing.","从晚报上，从公共汽车上同那些对全民娱乐方式感兴趣的人们的交谈中，她获取了赛马方面的必要信息。"
"She even talked of it with Tony, who had street-corner knowledge.","她甚至还和托尼谈起过此事，而托尼是有些街头赛马常识的人。"
"Already she had prepared chapter and verse of two imaginary coups; a sovereign made out of stitching imaginary blouses, invested on the winner of the Two Thousand Guineas, and the result on the dead-heater for the Jubilee at nice odds; this with a third winner, still to be selected, would bring her imaginary winnings up to the needed sixty pounds odd she would so soon have saved now out of ‘the altogether.’","她已经设计了两个有理有据的说辞：代人缝制罩衫赚到了一个金币，于是便将它压在“两千几尼马赛”的优胜马身上，结果在狂欢节那天的双头马上，中彩了；这笔钱再加上一匹跑了第三名的马，具体哪匹有待选择，这样她那笔虚构的赢钱就凑够了他们所需的60镑，这笔钱她能从那种“裸体生意”中非常迅速地积蓄起来。"
"This tale she would pitch to Tony in a week or two, reeling off by heart the wonderful luck she had kept from him until she had the whole of the money.","一两周后，等她得到整笔钱，她就把这个虚构的故事讲给托尼听，她已经烂熟于心，可以滔滔不绝地讲述这个幸运的故事。"
"She would slip her forehead against his eyes if he looked at her too hard, and kiss his lips till his head was no longer clear.","如果他起疑心，她就悄悄地用额头顶着他的眼睛，接着亲吻他的双唇，直到他昏头昏脑为止。"
"And in the morning they would wake up and take their passages.","第二天一早，他们就动身启程。"
"Such was the plan of Victorine, with five ten-pound and four one-pound notes in her stocking, attached to the pink silk stays.","这就是维多琳的计划，在她的长筒袜里藏着五张十镑和四张一镑的钞票，长筒袜就吊在那件粉红色的丝质紧身胸衣下面。"
"‘Afternoon of a Dryad’ had long been finished, and was on exhibition at the Dumetrius Gallery, with other works of Aubrey Greene.","《林中仙女的午后》早已完成，同奥布里·格林的其他作品一起在杜梅特里斯画廊展出了。"
"Victorine had paid a shilling to see it; had stood some furtive minutes gazing at that white body glimmering from among grass and spikey flowers, at the face, turned as if saying: “I know a secret!”","维多琳花了一先令去看了一下。她偷偷地站了几分钟，凝视着那个闪烁在青草和穗状花朵之间、微微发亮的白皙身体，凝视着那张脸，那张脸转过去仿佛在说：“我知道一个秘密！”"
"“Bit of a genius, Aubrey Greene—that face is jolly good!”","“奥布里·格林有点儿天赋——那张脸画得非常好！”"
"Scared, and hiding the face, Victorine had slipped away.","维多琳惊慌地掩着脸，悄悄地溜走了。"
"From the very day when she had stood shivering outside the studio of Aubrey Greene she had been in full work.","从她颤抖着站在奥布里·格林画室外面那天起，她一直是全日工作。"
"He had painted her three times—always nice, always polite, quite the gentleman!","他画过她三次——始终保持正派有礼的风范，是个十足的绅士！"
"And he had given her introductions.","而他还给她做过引见。"
"Some had painted her in clothes, some half-draped, some in that ‘altogether,’ which no longer troubled her, with the money swelling her stocking and Tony without suspicion.","有的画她穿着衣服的，有的画她半遮半裸的，有的画那种“裸体”的，她现在对裸体已不再感到不安了，这样她那长筒袜里的钱日渐增多，而托尼也没生疑。"
"Not every one had been ‘nice’; advances had been made to her, but she had nipped them in the bud.","不是每个人都是“正派的”；曾经就有人要跟她发生进一步关系，她一开始就给拒绝了。"
"It would have meant the money quicker, but—Tony!","要不然，钱会来得更快些，可是——她爱托尼！"
"In a fortnight now she could snap her fingers at it all.","再过两周，她就可以完全不在乎地摆脱这一切了。"
"And often on the way home she stood by that plate-glass window, before the fruits, and the corn, and the blue butterflies...","回家的路上，她常常会站在那个厚玻璃橱窗旁，看着那些水果、谷物和蓝色的蝴蝶……"
"In the packed railway carriage they sat side by side, Bicket, with tray on knee, debating where he had best stand.","在那挤得密密麻麻的车厢里，他们并排坐着，比克特把托盘放在膝盖上，盘算着一会儿最好站在哪里叫卖。"
"“I fyvour the mokes,” he said at last, “up by the pond.","“我赞成那些笨驴，”他最后说，“就站在池子边上。"
"People’ll have more money than when they get down among the swings and cocoanuts; and you can go and sit in a chair by the pond, like the seaside—I don’t want you with me not till I’ve sold out.”","那个位置，人们身上的钱会比荡过秋千、吃过椰子出来的时候更多一些。而你还可以像在海边一样，坐在池塘边的椅子上——在我没把气球卖光之前，我不想你和我呆在一起。”"
"Victorine pressed his arm.","维多琳紧紧握了握他的手臂。"
"Along the top and over on to the heath to north and south the holiday swarms surged, in perfect humour, carrying paper bags.","休假的人群手拿纸袋，兴高采烈地沿着石楠丛生的荒地走去，翻过山顶，人群向南北散去。"
"Round the pond children, with thin, grey-white, spindly legs, were paddling and shrilly chattering, too content to smile.","在池塘周围的孩子们，一个个小腿瘦弱、细长而灰白，他们一面戏水，一面喋喋不休地尖叫，欢声笑语不断。"
"Elderly couples crawled slowly by, with jutting stomachs, and faces discoloured by the unaccustomed climb.","年纪大一些的夫妇们步伐缓慢，身材有些臃肿，由于不习惯爬高，脸色也变了。"
"Girls and young men were few, for they were dispersed already on the heath, in search of a madder merriment.","年轻男女却很少，因为他们早已跑到石南丛生的荒地去寻找更疯狂的欢乐去了。"
"On benches, in chairs of green canvas or painted wood, hundreds were sitting, contemplating their feet, as if imagining the waves of the sea.","长凳上、绿帆布椅和油漆木椅上，都坐满了人，他们静静凝视着脚面，仿佛想象着大海的波涛。"
"Now and again three donkeys would start, urged from behind, and slowly tittup their burdens along the pond’s margin.","时而出现被主人赶着的几头驴，它们驮着重物，沿池塘边慢慢地向前跑着。"
"Hawkers cried goods.","小贩们叫卖着。"
"Fat dark women told fortunes.","几个身材丰腴的黑人女子在占卜。"
"Policemen stood cynically near them.","在她们附近的警察们玩世不恭地站在那里。"
"A man talked and talked and took his hat round.","一个男人讲了又讲，然后拿着帽子四处要钱。"
"Tony Bicket unslung his tray.","托尼·比克特取下托盘。"
"His cockney voice, wheedling and a little husky, offered his coloured airs without intermission.","他操着一口伦敦音，带着谄媚和略带欺哄的口吻，用那沙哑的声音在分秒不停地叫卖着。"
"This was something like!","这才有点儿像样呢！"
"It was brisk!","这才叫生意兴隆呢！"
"And now and again he gazed through the throng away across the pond, to where Victorine would be seated in a canvas chair, looking different from every one—he knew.","他还不时地从人群中朝池塘对面望去，在那里维多琳会坐在一张帆布椅子上，与众不同地看着他——他是知道的。"
"“Fine balloons—fine balloons!","“好看的气球——好看的气球！"
"Six for a bob!","一只六便士！"
"Big one, Madam?","来一个大的吗，夫人？"
"Only sixpence.","只要六便士。"
"See the size!","瞧瞧它的大小！"
"Buy, buy!","买一个吧，买一个吧！"
"Tyke one for the little boy!”","给小男孩买一个吧！”"
"No ‘aldermen’ up here, but plenty in the mood to spend their money on a bit of brightness!","“市参议员”不来这里，但是有许多人都愿意花些钱来买一点儿欢快！"
"At five minutes before noon he snapped his tray to—not a bally balloon left!","还差五分钟才到正午时，他就合上了托盘——一只气球都没剩！"
"With six Bank Holidays a week he would make his fortune!","如果一周有六天公休日，他就发财了！"
"Tray under arm, he began to tour the pond.","他把托盘夹在手臂下，向着池塘走过来。"
"The kiddies were all right, but—good Lord—how thin and pale!","孩子们都不错，可是——天啊——他们的身体太瘦弱，脸色太苍白了！"
"If he and Vic had a kid—but not they—not till they got out there!","如果他和维有个孩子——但是他们不能——除非他们离开此地到达那里！"
"A fat brown kid, chysin’ blue butterflies, and the sun oozin’ out of him!","一个胖胖的棕色皮肤的小孩正追着蓝色的蝴蝶跑，阳光穿过他的身体照射出来。"
"Rounding the end of the pond, he walked slowly along the chairs.","绕过池塘的尽头，他慢慢地沿着椅子走过去。"
"Lying back, elegant, with legs crossed, in brown stockings showing to the knees, and neat brown shoes with the flaps over—My! she looked a treat—in a world of her own, like that!","身体靠后倚着，姿态优美，双腿自然交叉，褐色的长筒袜里显露着膝盖，带鞋边的棕色皮鞋十分整洁——啊！她的样子美极了——她沉浸在自己世界的样子，好看极了！"
"Something caught Bicket by the throat.","比克特的喉咙像被什么东西卡住了。"
"Gosh!"
"He wanted things for her!","他要为她弄些东西！"
"“Well, Vic!","“喂，维！"
"Penny!”","想什么呢！”"
"“I was thinkin’ of Australia.”","“我在想澳大利亚。”"
"“Ah!","“啊！"
"It’s a gaudy long wait.","这真是异想天开的漫长等待啊。"
"Never mind—I’ve sold the bally lot.","不管怎样——我已经把这批货全卖光了。"
"Which shall we do, go down among the trees, or get to the swings, at once?”","我们现在去哪里，是向下走到树林里去，还是去荡秋千的地方呢？”"
"“The swings,” said Victorine.","“荡秋千去。”维多琳说。"
"The Vale of Health was in rhapsodic mood.","健康谷正处在狂欢中。"
"The crowd flowed here in a slow, speechless stream, to the cries of the booth-keepers, and the owners of swings and cocoanuts.","人群像缓慢而无声的河流一般涌到了这里，涌向货摊主的叫喊声处，涌向秋千和椰子摊边。"
"“Roll—bowl—or pitch!","“滚啊——投啊——掷啊！"
"Now for the milky ones!","试试椰汁吧！"
"Penny a shy!...","一便士投一次！……"
"Who’s for the swings?...","谁来荡秋千啊？……"
"Ices... Ices... Fine bananas!”","冰淇淋……冰淇淋……上好的香蕉！”"
"On the giant merry-go-round under its vast umbrella the thirty chain-hung seats were filled with girls and men.","在大伞底下的巨大旋转木马上，30只用链条悬挂着的座位挤满了男男女女。"
"Round to the music—slowly—faster—whirling out to the full extent of the chain, bodies bent back, legs stuck forward, laughter and speech dying, faces solemn, a little lost, hands gripping the chains hard.","伴着乐声旋转——缓缓地——逐渐快起来——旋转到链条所能到达的最大幅度。大家身体后仰，双腿前伸，欢声笑语渐渐减弱，大家脸色严肃起来，有点儿茫然失措，都用手紧紧握住链条。"
"Faster, faster; slowing, slowing to a standstill, and the music silent.","更快了，更快了，慢下来，慢慢停下来了，这时音乐也停住了。"
"“My word!” murmured Victorine.","“我的天啊！”维多琳喃喃地说，"
"“Come on, Tony!”","“来呀，托尼！”"
"They entered the enclosure and took their seats.","他们走进围栏，坐在位置上。"
"Victorine, on the outside, locked her feet, instinctively, one over the other, and tightening her clasp on the chains, curved her body to the motion.","维多琳在外面，用带子绑住脚，她本能地一边将一只脚叠在另一只脚上，一边双手紧紧握住链条，并将身体弯起来以适应转动。"
"Her lips parted:","她张嘴喊道："
"“Lor, Tony!”","“天啊，托尼！”"
"Faster, faster—every nerve and sense given to that motion!","越来越快，越来越快——所有神经和触感都集中到转动上！"
"O-o-h!","哦——哦——啊！"
"It WAS a feeling—flying round like that above the world!","真有一种在世界上空飞行的感觉！"
"Faster—faster!","越来越快——越来越快！"
"Slower—slow, and the descent to earth.","慢下来了——慢下来了，又落到了地面。"
"“Tony—it’s ‘eaven!”","“托尼——这感觉真像上天了！”"
"“Queer feelin’ in yer inside, when you’re swung right out!”","“当你向外荡出去时，身体里就有一种奇怪的感觉！”"
"“I’d like it level with the top.","“我喜欢转到高处的感觉。"
"Let’s go once more!”","我们再荡一次吧！”"
"“Right-o!”","“好！”"
"Twice more they went—half his profit on balloons!","他们又荡了两次——他卖气球挣的钱花了一半！"
"But who cared?","但谁计较这些呢？"
"He liked to see her face.","他喜欢看她的脸。"
"After that, six shies at the milky ones without a hit, an ice apiece: then arm-inarm to find a place to eat their lunch.","之后，他们来到椰汁摊旁，投了六次，可是一次都没击中，每次都只得到一块冰激凌。然后，两人手挽着手去吃午饭了。"
"That was the time Bicket enjoyed most, after the ginger-beer and sandwiches; smoking his fag, with his head on her lap, and the sky blue.","他们喝了姜汁啤酒，又吃了三明治，那是比克特最快活的时刻。他抽着香烟，头枕在她的腿上，望着蓝蓝的天空。"
"A long time like that; till at last she stirred.","他这样躺了很久，直到最后她动弹了一下。"
"“Let’s go and see the dancin’!”","“咱们去看看跳舞吧！”"
"In the grass enclosure ringed by the running path, some two dozen couples were jigging to a band.","在围有跑道的草地围场上，大约有二十几对舞者伴着乐队快步跳着。"
"Victorine pulled at his arm.","维多琳拉拉他的手臂。"
"“I WOULD love a turn!”","“我真想来一圈！”"
"“Well, let’s ‘ave a go,” said Bicket.","“好啊，我们试试。”比克特说，"
"“This one-legged bloke’ll ‘old my tray.”","“这位一条腿的人会帮我拿托盘。”"
"They entered the ring.","他们走进舞池里。"
"“Hold me tighter, Tony!”","“搂紧我，托尼！”"
"Bicket obeyed.","比克特照做了。"
"Nothing he liked better; and slowly their feet moved—to this side and that.","没有比这更让他高兴的事了。他们的脚步慢慢移动起来——从这头移向那头。"
"They made little way, revolving, keeping time, oblivious of appearances.","他们移动的距离很小，合着节拍旋转着，不怕旁人笑话。"
"“You dance all right, Tony.”","“你跳得不赖，托尼。”"
"“YOU dance a treat!” gasped Bicket.","“你跳得才棒呢！”比克特气喘吁吁地说。"
"In the intervals, panting, they watched over the one-legged man; then to it again, till the band ceased for good.","在间歇时间里，他们喘着气，望着那个一条腿的男人，接着再跳，一直跳到乐队完全停止演奏。"
"“My word!” said Victorine.","“我的天！”维多琳说，"
"“They dance on board ship, Tony!”","“人家在船上跳舞，托尼！”"
"Bicket squeezed her waist.","比克特捏捏她的腰。"
"“I’ll do the trick yet, if I ‘ave to rob the Bank.","“我一定要达到这个目的，即使去抢银行也行。"
"There’s nothin’ I wouldn’t do for you, Vic.”","为了你，我什么事都肯做，维。”"
"But Victorine smiled.","维多琳只是笑了笑。"
"She had done the trick already.","她就要达到这个目标了。"
"The crowd with parti-coloured faces, tired, good-humoured, frowsily scented, strolled over a battlefield thick-strewn with paper bags, banana peel, and newspapers.","路面满是纸袋、香蕉皮和报纸，空气中弥漫着难闻的气味，他们就走在形形色色的人群中，人们虽面带疲惫却又十分欢喜。"
"“Let’s ‘ave our tea, and one more swing,” said Bicket; “then we’ll get over on the other side among the trees.”","“我们去吃茶点，然后再荡一次秋千吧。”比克特说，“之后，我们再去那边树林里溜溜。”"
"Away over on the far side were many couples.","远处有许多情侣。"
"The sun went very slowly down.","太阳慢慢下山了。"
"Those two sat under a bush and watched it go.","他们二人坐在一丛灌木下，看着落日。"
"A faint breeze swung and rustled the birch leaves.","一阵微风吹动着白桦树叶，沙沙作响。"
"There was little human sound out here.","这里寂无人声。"
"All seemed to have come for silence, to be waiting for darkness in the hush.","所有人似乎都是为了寻求宁静来到这里的，似乎都在寂静中等待夜幕的降临。"
"Now and then some stealthy spy would pass and scrutinise.","不时会有行动诡异的暗探经过这里，仔细查看着。"
"“Foxes!” said Bicket.","“狡猾的狐狸！”比克特说，"
"“Gawd!","“天啊！"
"I’d like to rub their noses in it!”","我真想揭他们的老底！”"
"Victorine sighed, pressing closer to him.","维多琳叹息了一声，同他贴得更紧了。"
"Some one was playing on a banjo now; a voice singing.","这时有人弹起了班卓琴，还有一个附唱的声音。"
"It grew dusk, but a moon was somewhere rising, for little shadows stole out along the ground.","天色渐渐暗下来，一轮明月却正从某处升起，因为影子悄然从地面露了出来。"
"They spoke in whispers.","他们低声耳语。"
"It seemed wrong to raise the voice, as though the grove were under a spell.","此时提高嗓门似乎是不合适的，仿佛这片小树林被施了魔法。"
"Even their whisperings were scarce.","连耳语声也难得出现。"
"Dew fell, but they paid no heed to it.","露水掉下来，他们却毫不在乎。"
"With hands locked, and cheeks together, they sat very still.","他们紧握着手，贴着脸，一动不动地坐在那里。"
"Bicket had a thought.","比克特有种想法。"
"This was poetry—this was!","这就是诗——就是诗！"
"Darkness now, with a sort of faint and silvery glow, a sound of drunken singing on the Spaniard’s Road, the whirr of belated cars returning from the north—and suddenly an owl hooted.","现在已经一片漆黑了，带着一丝微弱的、银白色的光，一个醉汉唱着《西班牙人之路》，汽车从北面姗姗来迟，还带着呼呼声——突然间，一只猫头鹰的叫声划破寂静。"
"“My!” murmured Victorine, shivering: “An owl!","“哎呀！”维多琳，颤抖着喃喃低语，“一只猫头鹰！"
"Fancy!","真想不到！"
"I used to hear one at Norbiton.","我在诺比顿常常听到这种声音。"
"I ‘ope it’s not bad luck!”","我希望这不是厄运！”"
"Bicket rose and stretched himself,","比克特站起身来，伸了个懒腰。"
"“Come on!” he said: “we’ve ‘ad a dy.","“走吧！”他说，“我们玩了一天了。"
"Don’t you go catchin’ cold!”","你别着凉了！”"
"Arm-inarm, slowly, through the darkness of the birch-grove, they made their way upwards—glad of the lamps, and the street, and the crowded station, as though they had taken an overdose of solitude.","他们互挽着臂，慢慢穿过那片白桦小树林，向上走去——他们看着路灯、街道和车站附近拥挤的人群而感到开心，仿佛服下一剂过量的寂寞药。"
"Huddled in their carriage on the Tube, Bicket idly turned the pages of a derelict paper.","在地铁车厢里，他们挤在一起，比克特懒散地翻阅着一份被人丢弃的报纸。"
"But Victorine sat thinking of so much, that it was as if she thought of nothing.","而维多琳坐在那里，好像在想很多事，又好像什么都没想。"
"The swings and the grove in the darkness, and the money in her stocking.","秋千、幽暗的小树林，还有长筒袜里的钱。"
"She wondered Tony hadn’t noticed when it crackled—there wasn’t a safe place to keep it in!","她感到奇怪，当这些钞票发出沙沙声响时，托尼怎么会没注意到——没有一个存钱的安全地方！"
"What was he looking at, with his eyes so fixed?","他在看什么呢，眼睛一动不动？"
"She peered, and read: “‘Afternoon of a Dryad.’","她偷看了一眼，读道：“《林中仙女的午后》。"
"The striking picture by Aubrey Greene, on exhibition at the Dumetrius Gallery.”","奥布里·格林创作的惊人画作，在杜梅特里斯画廊展出。”"
"Her heart stopped beating.","她的心霎时停止了跳动。"
"“Cripes!” said Bicket.","“见鬼！”比克特说，"
"“Ain’t that like you?”","“这不像你吗？”"
"“Like me?","“像我？"
"No!”","不会！”"
"Bicket held the paper closer.","比克特把报纸拿得更近些。"
"“It IS. It’s like you all over.","“的确。从头到脚都像你。"
"I’ll cut that out.","我要把它剪下来。"
"I’d like to see that picture.”","我喜欢看那张画。”"
"The colour came up in her cheeks, released from a heart beating too fast now.","现在，她的脸涨红了，心跳也加快了。"
"“‘Tisn’t decent,” she said.","“这真不像。”她说。"
"“Dunno about that; but it’s awful like you.","“我不那么认为，它像极了。"
"It’s even got your smile.”","甚至连你的笑容也画进去了。”"
"Folding the paper, he began to tear the sheet.","他把报纸折起来，动手把这页撕下来。"
"Victorine’s little finger pressed the notes beneath her stocking.","维多琳用小手指按了按长筒袜下的钞票。"
"“Funny,” she said, slowly, “to think there’s people in the world so like each other.”","“真好笑，”她缓缓地说，“想不到这世上竟会有如此相像的人。”"
"“I never thought there could be one like you.","“我从未想到有人像你。"
"Charin’ Cross; we gotta change.”","查林十字广场到了。我们得换车了。”"
"Hurrying along the rat-runs of the Tube, she slipped her hand into his pocket, and soon some scraps of torn paper fluttered down behind her following him in the crush.","在他们沿着地铁狭窄的过道匆匆朝前走去的时候，她在拥挤的人群中跟在他后面，偷偷地把手伸进他的口袋里，不一会儿，几片报纸碎片在她背后飘落下来。"
"If only he didn’t remember where the picture was!","但愿他记不得这幅画放在什么地方了！"
"Awake in the night, she thought:","夜里醒来，她心想："
"‘I don’t care; I’m going to get the rest of the money—that’s all about it.’","“我不管。我要把其余的钱弄到手——这才是重要的事。”"
"But her heart moved queerly within her, like that of one whose feet have trodden suddenly the quaking edge of a bog.","可是她的内心却一阵悸动，好像一个人走在随时会突然塌陷的泥沼边缘似的。"

"Chapter II","第二章"
"Office Work","办公室工作"
"Michael sat correcting the proofs of ‘Counterfeits’—the book left by Wilfrid behind him.","迈克尔坐在那里校对着《赝品》的样张——就是威尔弗里德留下来的那本书。"
"“Can you see Butterfield, sir?”","“您可以接见巴特菲尔德吗，先生？”"
"“I can.”","“可以。”"
"In Michael the word Butterfield excited an uneasy pride.","在迈克尔心里，巴特菲尔德这个词激起了一阵令人不安的自豪感。"
"The young man fulfilled with increasing success the function for which he had been engaged, on trial, four months ago.","这个年轻人四个月前得到试用，此后不断成功地履行了他的职责。"
"The head traveller had even called him “a find.”","那个首席旅行推销员还称他是“一个人才”。"
"Next to ‘Copper Coin’ he was the finest feather in Michael’s cap.","他是迈克尔仅次于《铜币》的最骄人的成就。"
"The Trade were not buying, yet Butterfield was selling books, or so it was reported; he appeared to have a natural gift of inspiring confidence where it was not justified.","同行中人都不买进了，可是据称巴特菲尔德还在卖书。看起来，他有一种天分，可以获得别人无法获得的信任。"
"Danby and Winter had even entrusted to him the private marketing of that vellum-bound ‘Limited’ of ‘A Duet,’ by which they were hoping to recoup their losses on the ordinary edition.","丹比&温特出版社甚至委托他私下销售那本《二重唱》的皮面精装限量版，希望借此弥补平装本的损失。"
"He was now engaged in working through a list of names considered likely to patronise the little masterpiece.","他眼下正忙着拟定一份名单，名单中人都有望为这部小杰作捧场。"
"This method of private approach had been suggested by himself.","这种私下买卖的方式也是他建议的。"
"“You see, sir,” he had said to Michael: “I know a bit about Coue.","“您看，先生，”他对迈克尔说道，“我对库埃的心理暗示理论有所了解。"
"Well, you can’t work that on the Trade—they’ve got no capacity for faith.","可是，对业界同行您不能使用这一理论——因为他们根本没有信仰。"
"What can you expect?","你还能指望什么呢？"
"Every day they buy all sorts of stuff, always basing themselves on past sales.","他们一直以过去的销售情况为依据，每天买进各种各样的东西。"
"You can’t find one in twenty that’ll back the future.","他们20个人里也不会有一个人为未来投资。"
"But with private gentlemen, and especially private ladies, you can leave a thought with them like Coue does—put it into them again and again that day by day in every way the author’s gettin’ better and better; and ten to one when you go round next, it’s got into their subconscious, especially if you take ‘em just after lunch or dinner, when they’re a bit drowsy.","但是，私下向那些有钱人推销，尤其是向有钱的夫人们推销的时候，你可以像库埃那样对他们作心理暗示——并且向他们反复灌输这一观点：这位作家在各个方面的声望会越来越好。这样一来，等你下一次走访的时候，十有八九这一理念已经渗入他们的潜意识中了，尤其是在吃完午餐或是晚餐之后，因为那时候人们的头脑不是那么清醒。"
"Let me take my own time, sir, and I’ll put that edition over for you.”","先生，就让我慢慢地进行吧，我一定会为您把这一版的书都卖出去的。”"
"“Well, Michael had answered, “if you can inspire confidence in the future of my governor, Butterfield, you’ll deserve more than your ten per cent.”","“好吧，”迈克尔答道，“要是你能让人们相信我老板的将来，那么，巴特菲尔德，你应得的就不止百分之十了。”"
"“I can do it, sir; it’s just a question of faith.”","“这我能办到，先生，这只是一个信念问题。”"
"“But you haven’t any, have you?”","“但是你自己是没有信仰的，对吗？”"
"“Well, not, so to speak, in the author—but I’ve got faith that I can give THEM faith in him; that’s the real point.”","“嗯，没错，可以这么说，我不相信作者——但是我相信我可以使人们相信作者。这才是真正的关键所在。”"
"“I see—the three-card stunt; inspire the faith you haven’t got, that the card is there, and they’ll take it.","“我明白了——原来是那种三张纸牌的把戏，你不信但却让别人相信，牌就在那儿，然后他们就会上当的。"
"Well, the disillusion is not immediate—you’ll probably always get out of the room in time.","还好，不会马上就穿帮——你大概总能及时抽身，逃避责任。"
"Go ahead, then!”","那么，就这么做吧！”"
"The young man Butterfield had smiled....","年轻的巴特菲尔德笑了……"
"The uneasy part of the pride inspired in Michael now by the name was due to old Forsyte’s continually saying to him that he didn’t know—he couldn’t tell—there was that young man and his story about Elderson, and they got no further....","现在，这个名字令迈克尔在自豪之余产生不安，是因为老福赛特不停地对他说他不知道——他说不出来——那个年轻人，还有他所说的那个关于埃尔德森的故事是怎么回事，他们没有任何进展……"
