"The words stirred something deep in Soames; but, far from giving it away, he continued to gaze at the white monkey.","这句话触动了索姆斯内心的某些东西，但是，他丝毫没有表露出来，他依旧凝视着白猿。"
"The restless, inhuman, and yet so human, angry sadness of the creature’s eyes!","这畜生的双眼不安定，无人性，却又如此通人情，愤怒而悲哀！"
"‘No whites to them!’ thought Soames: ‘that’s what does it, I expect!’","“那双眼睛一点儿眼白也没有！”索姆斯心想，“原因就在于此吧，我想！”"
"And George had liked that picture to hang opposite his bed!","而乔治却喜欢把这幅画挂在床的对面！"
"Well, George had grit—joked with his last breath: very English, George!","嗯，乔治有勇气——临死还讲笑话：十足的英国人，乔治！"
"Very English, all the Forsytes!","所有福赛特家的人都是十足的英国人！"
"Old Uncle Jolyon, and his way with shareholders; Swithin, upright, puffy, huge in a too little arm-chair at Timothy’s: ‘All these small fry!’ he seemed to hear the words again; and Uncle Nicholas, whom that chap Elderson reproduced as it were unworthily, spry and all-there, and pretty sensual, but quite above suspicion of dishonesty.","老乔里恩叔叔和他对付股东们的办法；斯悦辛，笔挺地坐在蒂莫西家的那把小扶手椅里，这使他的身材显得更加臃肿，嘴里说着：“所有这些小娃娃们！”他仿佛又听到了这句话；还有尼古拉叔叔，埃尔德森那家伙就像是他的翻版，其实他不配，因为尼古拉机敏、好色，但绝没有一点儿不诚实。"
"And old Roger, with his crankiness, and German mutton!","还有老罗杰和他那古怪的脾气，以及德国羊肉！"
"And his own father, James—how he had hung on, long and frail as a reed, hung on and on!","还有他的父亲，詹姆士——他是多么能坚持，尽管他身材瘦弱得像一根芦秆，但还是一再坚持了！"
"And Timothy, preserved in Consols, dying at a hundred!","还有蒂莫西，靠统一公债维持生活，活了一百岁呢！"
"Grit and body in those old English boys, in spite of their funny ways.","在老一辈英国人的身上，尽管有些可笑的作风，但是他们拥有勇气和身体。"
"And there stirred in Soames a sort of atavistic will-power.","这时，似乎唤起了索姆斯体内隔代遗传的意志力。"
"He would see, and they would see—and that was all about it!","他想看看，他们也想看看——事情就是如此！"
"The grinding of a taxi’s wheels brought him back from reverie.","一辆出租车的刹车声使他从沉思中惊醒。"
"Here came ‘Old Mont,’ tittuppy, and light in the head as ever, no doubt.","“老蒙特”大摇大摆地走进来，毋庸置疑，他还和以前一样头脑简单。"
"And, instead of his hand, Soames held out Elderson’s letter.","索姆斯没有把手伸过去，而是把埃尔德森的那封信递给他。"
"“Your precious schoolfellow’s levanted,” he said.","“你的那位宝贝同学举债出逃了。”他说。"
"Sir Lawrence read it through, and whistled.","劳伦斯爵士把信读了一遍，吹了声口哨。"
"“What do you think, Forsyte—Constantinople?”","“你怎么想，福赛特——君士坦丁堡吗？”"
"“More likely Monte Carlo,” said Soames gloomily.","“更可能是蒙特卡洛。”索姆斯沮丧地说，"
"“Secret commission—it’s not an extraditable offence.”","“秘密佣金——这不是一个可引渡的罪名。”"
"The odd contortions of that baronet’s face were giving him some pleasure—the fellow seemed to be feeling it, after all.","准男爵古怪别扭的样子溢于言表，这让他有了一点儿快感。——毕竟，这家伙也感觉到这事情的严重性了。"
"“I should think he’s really gone to escape his women, Forsyte.”","“我倒认为他是想避开那两个女人才出走的，福赛特。”"
"The chap was incorrigible!","这家伙真是不可救药！"
"Soames shrugged his shoulders almost violently.","索姆斯使劲耸了耸肩膀。"
"“You’d better realise,” he said, “that the fat is in the fire.”","“你最好能明白。”他说，“事情已经被搞糟了。”"
"“But surely, my dear Forsyte, it’s been there ever since the French occupied the Ruhr.","“不过可以肯定，我亲爱的福赛特，自从法国人侵占了鲁尔之后，局势一直就是这样。"
"Elderson has cut his lucky; we appoint some one else.","埃尔德森已经出逃了，我们再任命其他人吧。"
"What more is there to it?”","此外还有什么呢？”"
"Soames had the peculiar feeling of having overdone his own honesty.","索姆斯有一种感觉，自己好像老实过头了。"
"If an honourable man, a ninth baronet, couldn’t see the implications of Elderson’s confession, were they really there?","如果一个正派的人，第九代准男爵，都看不出埃尔德森自白中的暗示，那么是不是真的有暗示这回事呢？"
"Was any fuss and scandal necessary?","任何混乱或绯闻都有必要吗？"
"Goodness knew, HE didn’t want it!","老天为证，他不希望这样！"
"He said heavily:","他悲伤地说："
"“We now have conclusive evidence of a fraud; we KNOW Elderson was illegally paid for putting through business by which the shareholders have suffered a dead loss.","“我们现在已经掌握了一个诈骗犯的确凿证据，我们还了解到埃尔德森在成交生意中获得了非法佣金，然而股东们却因此蒙受了极大损失。"
"How can we keep this knowledge from them?”","我们怎么能瞒住这个事实不让大家知道呢？”"
"“But the mischief’s done, Forsyte.","“但是损失已经造成了，福赛特。"
"How will the knowledge help them?”","他们知道了又有什么用呢？”"
"Soames frowned.","索姆斯皱起了眉头。"
"“We’re in a fiduciary position.","“我们处于受信托的地位。"
"I’m not prepared to run the risks of concealment.","我不准备冒隐瞒不报的风险。"
"If we conceal, we’re accessory after the fact.","如果我们隐瞒不报，我们就是这件事的从犯了。"
"The thing might come out at any time.”","这件事随时都有可能被泄露出去。”"
"If that was caution, not honesty, he couldn’t help it.","如果只是出于谨慎，而不是忠诚，那他也没辙了。"
"“I should be glad to spare Elderson’s name.","“我觉得如果能保全埃尔德森的名誉是最好了。"
"We were at—”","我们曾经在——”"
"“I’m aware of that,” said Soames, drily.","“这我知道。”索姆斯冷冷地说。"
"“But what risk is there of its coming out, Forsyte?","“可是这件事有什么泄露出去的危险呢，福赛特？"
"Elderson won’t mention it; nor young Butterfield, if you tell him not to.","埃尔德森不会提的，如果你不提小巴特菲尔德的话，他也不会说的。"
"Those who paid the commission certainly won’t.","那些付佣金的人当然更不会提的。"
"And beyond us three here, no one else knows.","这样，除了我们三人之外，再没人知道了。"
"It’s not as if we profited in any way.”","不管怎样，我们似乎不会从这件事上得到好处吧。”"
"Soames was silent.","索姆斯沉默不语了。"
"The argument was specious.","这个论据有点儿似是而非。"
"Entirely unjust, of course, that he should be penalised for what Elderson had done!","当然，要他为埃尔德森做的事受罚，完全不合情理！"
"“No,” he said, suddenly, “it won’t do.","“不。”他突然说，“这样不行。"
"Depart from the law, and you can’t tell where it’ll end.","违反了法律，那你就不知道将来会落到什么下场了。"
"The shareholders have suffered this loss, and they have the right to all the facts within the directors’ knowledge.","股东们已经蒙受了损失，他们有权知道董事们知道的一切事实。"
"There might be some means of restitution they could avail themselves of.","或许会有能为他们做出赔偿的办法。"
"We can’t judge.","我们无法判断。"
"It may be they’ve a remedy against ourselves.”","说不定他们会提出一个补救的办法。”"
"“If that’s so, Forsyte, I’m with you.”","“如果是那样的话，福赛特，我和你站在一起。”"
"Soames felt disgust.","索姆斯感到很厌烦。"
"Mont had no business to put it with a sort of gallantry that didn’t count the cost; when the cost, if cost there were, would fall, not on Mont, whose land was heavily mortgaged, but on himself, whose property was singularly realisable.","蒙特根本不配摆出一副豪侠的样子，却不去计算一下损失，如果有损失，需要为此负担的话，也不会落在蒙特身上，因为他的土地已经被抵押了，反而债务会落在自己的身上，因为他的财产很容易变成现款。"
"“Well,” he said, coldly, “remember that tomorrow.","“好吧。”他冷冷地说，“明天可要记住这件事。"
"I’m going to bed.”","我准备上床睡觉了。”"
"At his open window upstairs he felt no sense of virtue, but he enjoyed a sort of peace.","在楼上，他站在打开的窗子旁，他并未感到自己做了一件善事，但是他享受着安宁带来的快乐。"
"He had taken his line, and there it was!","他采取了自己的方针，就照这样去办！"

"Chapter IX","第九章"
"Soames Doesn’t Give a Damn","索姆斯毫不在乎"
"During the month following the receipt of Elderson’s letter, Soames aged more than thirty days.","收到埃尔德森那封信后的一个月里，索姆斯老了不少。"
"He had forced his policy of disclosure on a doubting Board, the special meeting had been called, and, just as, twenty-three years ago, pursuing divorce from Irene, he had to face the public eye, so now he suffered day and night in dread of that undiscriminating optic.","他已经迫使充满怀疑的董事会接受了他提出的揭露事实真相的方针，同时还发出了召开特别会议的通知。正如23年前，为了争取与伊琳离婚，他不得不在大庭广众面前颜面扫地一样，这一回他寝食难安，害怕众人是非不分的目光。"
"The French had a proverb: “Les absents ont toujours tort!” but Soames had grave doubts about it.","法国人有一句谚语：“不在场的人总是错的！”但是，索姆斯对这句话持怀疑态度。"
"Elderson would be absent from that meeting of the shareholders, but—unless he was much mistaken—he himself, who would be present, would come in for the blame.","埃尔德森不会出席这次股东大会了，但是——除非是他犯了很大错误——即便是他亲自出席，也会备受责备。"
"The French were not to be relied on.","法国人靠不住。"
"What with his anxiety about Fleur, and his misgiving about the public eye, he was sleeping badly, eating little, and feeling below par.","他为弗勒的担忧，同时为公众的看法感到不安，吃不好，睡不好，感觉很不舒服。"
"Annette had recommended him to see a doctor.","安妮特曾经劝他去看看医生。"
"That was probably why he did not.","大概就是因为这个，他才不去的。"
"Soames had faith in doctors for other people; but they had never—he would say—done anything for HIM, possibly because, so far, there had not been anything to do.","索姆斯对医生给别人看病很有信心，但是医生们从来没有——他说——为他做过任何事，可能因为到目前为止，还没有什么事情可做。"
"Failing in her suggestion, and finding him every day less sociable, Annette had given him a book on Coue.","安妮特由于自己的建议未被接受，同时又发现他越来越难以接近，就给了他一本论述库埃的书。"
"After running it through, he had meant to leave it in the train, but the theory, however extravagant, had somehow clung to him.","他匆匆看过后，本想把这本书丢在火车上，可这个理论，不管它如何不合理，不知为什么总是缠着他。"
"After all, Fleur was doing it; and the thing cost you nothing: there might be something in it!","毕竟，弗勒正在用此疗法，而且这又没花你一分钱，这里面讲的或许有点儿道理！"
"There was.","或许有道理。"
"After telling himself that night twenty-five times that he was getting better and better, he slept so soundly that Annette, in the next room, hardly slept at all.","那天夜里，他默念了25遍自己会越来越好之后，竟然睡得酣畅淋漓，他的鼾声甚至打扰了隔壁房间里的安妮特，让她无法入睡。"
"“Do you know, my friend,” she said at breakfast, “you were snoring last night so that I could not hear the cock crow.”","“你知道吗，我的朋友。”吃早饭时，她说，“昨天夜里你的鼻鼾声很响，我连鸡叫声都没听见。”"
"“Why should you want to?” said Soames.","“你为什么要听见鸡叫声呢？”索姆斯说。"
"“Well, never mind—if you had a good night.","“好了，没关系——只要你晚上睡得好就行。"
"Was it my little Coue who gave you that nice dream?”","是不是我给你的那本小书《库埃》让你睡得那么香呢？”"
"Partly from fear of encouraging Coue, and partly from fear of encouraging her, Soames avoided a reply; but he had a curious sense of power, as if he did not care what people said of him.","索姆斯怕鼓励《库埃》，也怕鼓励她，所以他避而不答。然而好像有种神奇的力量，他好像并不介意别人说什么了。"
"‘I’ll do it again to-night,’ he thought.","“今天晚上接着这么干。”他心想。"
"“You know,” Annette went on, “you are just the temperament for Coue, Soames.","“你知道，”安妮特接着说，“你的性格恰好适合库埃疗法，索姆斯。"
"When you cure yourself of worrying, you will get quite fat.”","等你治好了忧虑的老毛病，你的身体就会胖起来。”"
"“Fat!” said Soames, looking at her curves.","“胖！”索姆斯看了看她的曲线，"
"“I’d as soon grow a beard.”","“我宁可留一把胡子。”"
"Fatness and beards were associated with the French.","肥胖和胡须总是与法国人联系在一起。"
"He would have to keep an eye on himself if he went on with this—er—what was one to call it?","他必须得好好照顾自己，如果他继续练这个——呃——人们会叫它什么呢？"
"Tomfoolery was hardly the word to conciliate the process, even if it did require you to tie twenty-five knots in a bit of string: very French, that, like telling your beads!","无聊的玩意一词实在不足以表达这一过程，甚至书中还要求你在一小段绳子上打25个结，这是地道的法国式做法，就像数念珠祷告似的！"
"He himself had merely counted on his fingers.","他只用手指来计数。"
"The sense of power lasted all the way up to London; he had the conviction that he could sit in a draught if he wanted to, that Fleur would have her boy all right; and as to the P. P. R. S.—ten to one he wouldn’t be mentioned by name in any report of the proceedings.","他深信自己的力量，这种感觉一路维持到伦敦。他深信，只要他愿意，即使他坐在风口浪尖也无所谓，他也深信弗勒一定会母子平安的，至于在天佑再保险公司里——十之八九他的名字不会再出现在大会的任何报告中。"
"After an early lunch and twenty-five more assurances over his coffee, he set out for the city.","早午饭之后，他在喝咖啡时又做了25次祈祷，便动身到城里去了。"
"This Board, held just a week before the special meeting of the shareholders, was in the nature of a dress rehearsal.","这次董事会，刚好在股东特别大会前一周举行，实际上是一场预演。"
"The details of confrontation had to be arranged, and Soames was chiefly concerned with seeing that a certain impersonality should be preserved.","对质的种种细节必须安排好，索姆斯主要关注保护那些与个人无关的方针。"
"He was entirely against disclosure of the fact that young Butterfield’s story and Elderson’s letter had been confided to himself.","他完全反对公开以下事实，即年轻人巴特菲尔德的告发和埃尔德森的那封信都是透露给他本人的。"
"The phrase to be used should be a “member of the Board.”","应该采用措辞“一个董事会成员”。"
"He saw no need for anything further.","他认为没必要进一步声明了。"
"As for explanations, they would fall, of course, to the chairman and the senior director, Lord Fontenoy.","至于解释，当然应该向董事长和资格最老的董事福坦诺勋爵询问了。"
"He found, however, that the Board thought he himself was the right person to bring the matter forward.","然而，他却发现董事会却认为他是提出这件事最适合的人选。"
"No one else—they said—could supply the personal touch, the necessary conviction; the chairman should introduce the matter briefly, then call on Soames to give the evidence within his knowledge.","他们说——除了他之外，没人具有和他们接触的机会以及提供具有说服力的证据；董事长会简要介绍一下此事，然后请索姆斯提供他所知的证据。"
"Lord Fontenoy was emphatic.","福坦诺勋爵强烈要求这样做。"
"“It’s up to you, Mr. Forsyte.","“这事全仰仗您了，福赛特先生。"
"If it hadn’t been for you, Elderson would be sitting there today.","要不是您的话，埃尔德森今天还坐在这里呢。"
"From beginning to end you put the wind up him; and I wish the deuce you hadn’t.","从开始到现在，他一直都害怕您，我希望您没做什么。"
"The whole thing’s a confounded nuisance.","这真是一件麻烦事儿。"
"He was a very clever fellow, and we shall miss him.","他是个聪明人，我们会想他的。"
"Our new man isn’t a patch on him.","我们的新经理可比不上他。"
"If he did take a few thou. under the rose, he took ‘em off the Huns.”","如果他私下里确实捞了几千镑，那也是从德国佬那拿的。”"
"Old guinea-pig!","这只老豚鼠！"
"Soames replied, acidly:","索姆斯尖声说道："
"“And the quarter of a million he’s lost the shareholders, for the sake of those few thou.?","“难道他为了这几千镑可以让股东们失掉25万镑吗？"
"Bagatelle, I suppose?”","请问这是小事吗？”"
"“Well, it might have turned out a winner; for the first year it did.","“嗯，说不定它会变成一笔赚钱的生意呢，第一年就是这样的。"
"We all back losers sometimes.”","我们都会把赌注压在输者的身上。”"
"Soames looked from face to face.","索姆斯一一打量他们的面孔。"
"They did not support this blatant attitude, but in them all, except perhaps ‘Old Mont’s,’ he felt a grudge against himself.","他们并不赞成把此事闹大，而且从他们的表情来看，除了“老蒙特”之外，他感觉到每个人都对他有怨恨之情。"
"Their expressions seemed to say: ‘Nothing of this sort ever happened till you came on the Board.’","他们的表情似乎在说：“你没来董事会之前，从没发生过这类事情。”"
"He had disturbed their comfort, and they disliked him for it.","他扰乱了他们的安逸，所以他们并不喜欢他。"
"They were an unjust lot!","他们是一帮不公道的家伙！"
"He said doggedly:","他固执地说："
"“You leave it to me, do you?","“你们都把这件事踢给我，是不是？"
"Very well!”","很好！”"
"What he meant to convey—or whether he meant to convey anything, he did not know; but even that ‘old guinea-pig’ was more civil afterwards.","他这句话要表达什么意思——或者他是否有什么意思要表达，他自己也不清楚，不过之后，就连那只“老豚鼠”也客气些了。"
"He came away from the Board, however, without any sense of power at all.","然而，从董事会出来以后，他已经感觉不到任何力量了。"
"There he would be on Tuesday next, bang in the public eye.","下周二，他就要在公众面前现眼了。"
"After calling to enquire after Fleur, who was lying down rather poorly, he returned home with a feeling of having been betrayed.","弗勒因为不舒服一直躺在床上，他去看过她之后，就直接回家了，心里有种被出卖的感觉。"
"It seemed that he could not rely, after all, on this fellow with his twenty-five knots.","看来，这种打25个结的心理疗法不适合他。"
"However much better he might become, his daughter, his reputation, and possibly his fortune, were not apparently at the disposition of his subconscious self.","不管他现在的状态变得有多好，他的女儿、他的名誉，可能还有他的财产，显然都不是那个下意识所能控制的。"
"He was silent at dinner, and went up afterwards to his picture gallery, to think things over.","吃晚饭时，他默不作声，吃完就到楼上的画廊去了，仔细考虑一下整件事情。"
"For half an hour he stood at the open window, alone with the summer evening; and the longer he stood there, the more clearly he perceived that the three were really one.","他在打开的窗前，站了半个小时，在这夏日的傍晚，独自一人。在窗前站的时间越长，他就越意识到这三件事其实是一回事、。"
"Except for his daughter’s sake, what did he care for his reputation or his fortune?","如果不是为了女儿，他还计较什么名誉和财产呢？"
"His reputation!","他的名誉！"
"Lot of fools—if they couldn’t see that he was careful and honest so far as had lain within his reach—so much the worse for them!","这帮蠢货——如果他们看不出他在力所能及的范围内表现出来的谨慎和诚实——那他们就无药可救了！"
"His fortune—well, he had better make another settlement on Fleur and her child at once, in case of accidents; another fifty thousand.","他的财产——嗯，他最好还是马上再给弗勒和她的孩子一笔财产，以防意外。再给五万镑。"
"Ah! if she were only through her trouble!","啊！只要她能顺利分娩就好！"
"It was time Annette went up to her for good; and there was a thing they called twilight sleep.","现在是时候让安妮特进城到她那里去了，还有一种人们称作半麻醉无痛分娩的方法。"
"To have her suffering was not to be thought of!","可千万不能让她受苦啊！"
"The evening lingered out; the sun went down behind familiar trees; Soames’ hands, grasping the window-ledge, felt damp with dew; sweetness of grass and river stole up into his nostrils.","夜晚悄悄降临，太阳隐没在熟悉的树林后。索姆斯紧紧握着窗框的双手已被露水打湿了，他闻到了青草伴着河水的香气。"
"The sky had paled, and now began to darken; a scatter of stars came out.","此刻，苍茫的天色逐渐暗淡，天空中繁星点点。"
"He had lived here a long time, through all Fleur’s childhood—best years of his life; still, it wouldn’t break his heart to sell.","他在这里住过很长一段时间，陪弗勒度过整个童年时光——这是他一生中最美好的时光。尽管如此，卖掉这处房产也不会让他伤心。"
"His heart was up in London.","他的心已经飞向伦敦了。"
"Sell?","卖了它？"
"That was to run before the hounds with a vengeance.","这未免太心急了。"
"No—no!—it wouldn’t come to THAT!","不——不！事情还没到那个地步！"
"He left the window and, turning up the lights, began the thousand and first tour of his pictures.","他离开窗户，打开电灯，第一千零一次巡视自己的藏画。"
"He had made some good purchases since Fleur’s marriage, and without wasting his money on fashionable favourites.","弗勒结婚以来，他买进好几件便宜货，而且没把钱浪费在追赶那些时髦的作品上。"
"He had made some good sales, too.","他也做过几笔好买卖。"
"The pictures in this gallery, if he didn’t mistake, were worth from seventy to a hundred thousand pounds; and, with the profits on his sales from time to time, they stood him in at no more than five-and-twenty thousand—not a bad result from a life’s hobby, to say nothing of the pleasure!","在他画廊里的那些画，要是没算错的话，值七万到十万镑。同时，若将时不时地卖出所获的利润算进去，这些画的成本还不到两万五千镑——一生的业余爱好有这样的成果总算不赖，更不用说其中的乐趣了！"
"Of course, he might have taken up something else—butterflies, photography, archaeology, or first editions; some other sport in which you backed your judgment against the field, and collected the results; but he had never regretted choosing pictures.","当然，他本来可能会对其他事物产生兴趣——如蝴蝶、摄影、考古，或者书籍首发本，或者在某项运动中下赌注而后收获结果。但他从未对自己选择收藏画而后悔。"
"Not he!","他才不后悔呢！"
"More to show for your money, more kudos, more profit, and more risk!","自己花的钱，可以给别人看更多东西，自己还能从中取得更大的名声、更多的利润，同时也会冒更大的风险！"
"The thought startled him a little; had he really taken to pictures because of the risk?","这种想法使他有点儿吃惊。他是因为要承担风险才喜欢画吗？"
"A risk had never appealed to him; at least, he hadn’t realised it, so far.","风险对他而言向来是没有吸引力的，至少到目前为止他还没认识到这一点。"
"Had his ‘subconscious’ some part in the matter?","是不是他的“潜意识”在这件事上起过一些作用呢？"
"He suddenly sat down and closed his eyes.","他突然坐下来，闭上眼睛。"
"Try the thing once more; very pleasant feeling, that morning, of not “giving a damn”; he never remembered having it before!","再来一遍那玩意试试看。那天早晨，有过一种“毫不在乎”的愉快感觉，他记得以前从来没有过这种感觉！"
"He had always felt it necessary to worry—kind of insurance against the worst; but worry was wearing, no doubt about it, wearing.","他一直觉得担心是必要的——像是一种对最恶劣情况的保险。但是担心令人疲惫，毫无疑问，令人疲惫。　"
"Turn out the light!","把灯关了！"
"They said in that book, you had to relax.","书里说，必须要放松。"
"In the now dim and shadowy room, with the starlight, through many windows, dusted over its reality, Soames, in his easy chair, sat very still.","此刻，这个房间朦胧而幽暗，星光透过窗口洒落在屋内，索姆斯静静地坐在安乐椅上，一动不动。"
"A faint drone rose on the words: “fatter and fatter” through his moving lips.","只有他嘴唇在颤抖，发出一种轻微深沉的嗡嗡声：“越来越胖。”"
"‘No, no,’ he thought: ‘that’s wrong!’","“不，不。”他想，“念错了！”"
"And he began the drone again.","于是他又发出嗡嗡声。"
"The tips of his fingers ticked it off; on and on—he would give it a good chance.","他的指尖在数着念句的次数；念了又念——他要给这种疗法一个好机会。"
"If only one needn’t worry!","但愿自己不必忧虑担心了！"
"On and on—“better and better!”","念了又念——“越来越好！”"
"If only—!","但愿——！"
"His lips stopped moving; his grey head fell forward into the subconscious.","他的嘴唇停止了颤动；他那灰白的脑袋垂在胸前，陷入了下意识。"
"And the stealing starlight dusted over him, too, a little unreality.","此时，悄然射入的星光洒在他身上，有点儿虚无缥缈。"

"Chapter X","第十章"
"But Takes No Chances","但是不冒险"
"Michael knew nothing of the City; and, in the spirit of the old cartographers: “Where you know nothing, place terrors,” made his way through the purlieus of the Poultry, towards that holy of holies, the offices of Cuthcott, Kingson and Forsyte.","迈克尔根本不了解伦敦城，于是他本着老制图员的精神：“警惕那些你不了解的地方”，穿过家禽街的边缘，走向那个最神圣的地方——卡斯考特、金森和福赛特事务所。"
"His mood was attuned to meditation, for he had been lunching with Sibley Swan at the Cafe C’rillon.","他此刻的状态适合思考问题，因为他刚刚在克里伦咖啡馆和西伯莱·斯旺用过午饭。"
"He had known all the guests—seven chaps even more modern than old Sib—save only a Russian so modern that he knew no French and nobody could talk to him.","他认识所有在那里用餐的客人——有七个人甚至比老西伯还要入时——只有一个俄国人除外，他太新潮了竟然不懂法语，以至于没有人能和他交谈。"
"Michael had watched them demolish everything, and the Russian closing his eyes, like a sick baby, at mention of any living name....","迈克尔看着他们吃光了所有的东西，看到只要有人提起任何一个尚在人世的人时，那个俄国人就会像一个病婴似的闭上眼睛……"
"‘Carry on!’ he thought, several of his favourites having gone down in the melee.","“继续吧！”他想道，有几个他最喜欢的人物已经在混乱的讨论中被否定了，"
"‘Stab and bludge!","“中伤吧！调侃吧！"
"Importance awaits you at the end of the alley.’","等着身后留名吧。”"
"But he had restrained his irreverence till the moment of departure.","但是他一直忍着，直到他要走的时候才把这些无礼的话说出来。"
"“Sib,” he said, rising, “all these chaps here are dead—ought they to be about in this hot weather?”","“西伯，”他站起来说，“这里的这些家伙都是死人——天气这么热他们怎么能出来活动呢？”"
"“What’s that?” ejaculated Sibley Swan, amidst the almost painful silence of the chaps.","“你说的是什么话？”在一帮人基本上都尴尬无语的时候，西伯莱·斯旺突然喊道。"
"“I mean—they’re alive—so they MUST be damned!”","“我是说——他们都还活着——所以他们都该见鬼去！”"
"And avoiding a thrown chocolate which hit the Russian, he sought the door.","他躲过一块扔过来的巧克力，夺门而出，结果那块巧克力打中了那个俄国人。"
"Outside, he mused: ‘Good chaps, really!","出门后，他若有所思地自语道：“这帮家伙，真是好样的！"
"Not half so darned superior as they think they are.","自以为才高八斗，其实连一半都没有。"
"Quite a human touch—getting that Russian on the boko.","扔那一下倒是有人情味——打中那个俄国佬的鼻子了。"
"Phew!","呼！"
"It’s hot!’","真热啊！”"
"On that first day of the Eton and Harrow match all the forfeited heat of a chilly summer had gathered and shimmered over Michael, on the top of his Bank ‘bus; shimmered over straw hats, and pale, perspiring faces, over endless other ‘buses, business men, policemen, shopmen at their doors, sellers of newspapers, laces, jumping toys, endless carts and cabs, letterings and wires, all the confusion of the greatest conglomeration in the world—adjusted almost to a hair’s-breadth, by an unseen instinct.","在伊顿和哈罗比赛的第一天，在堤岸公交车的顶层上，迈克尔觉得整个凉爽夏天消失了的暑热都集中到一起了，闪烁在自己身上、行人的草帽上、因流汗而苍白的脸上、川流不息的其他公交车上；闪烁在那些生意人、警察、店员、卖报纸的、卖花边的、卖跳动玩具的人的身上；闪烁在运货马车和出租车上以及文字和电报上、世界上最大的混合体的所有混乱上——世上种种万物在一种看不见的本能的作用下，都调整到只差分毫了。"
"Michael stared and doubted.","迈克尔瞪着眼看着，也疑惑着。"
"Was it possible that, with everyone pursuing his own business, absorbed in his own job, the thing could work out?","如果人人都忙于自己的事业，全神贯注于自己的工作，事情有可能发展成那样吗？"
"An ant-heap was not busier, or more seemingly confused.","成群的蚂蚁也不会比这里更热闹，或是看上去比这里更混乱。"
"Live wires crossed and crossed and crossed—inextricable entanglement, you’d say; and yet, life, the order needful to life, somehow surviving!","你会说，忙碌的人们有如有生命的电线一般穿来穿去，穿去穿来——难分难解地纠结在一起，然而，生活以及生活所需的秩序却以某种方式幸存了下来！"
"‘No slouch of a miracle!’ he thought, ‘modern town life!’","“忙碌的人们显奇迹！”他想道，“现代都市生活！”"
"And suddenly it seemed to cease, as if demolished by the ruthless dispensation of some super Sibley Swan; for he was staring down a cul-de-sac.","可是，生活貌似突然停止了，仿佛是被西伯莱·斯旺之类的超人以无情的天命为由毁灭了，因为出现在他眼前的是一条死胡同。"
"On both sides, flat houses, recently re-buffed, extraordinarily alike; at the end, a flat buff house, even more alike, and down to it, grey virgin pavement, unstained by horse or petrol; no cars, cats, carts, policemen, hawkers, flies, or bees.","胡同两边都是些单调的房子，新刷的浅黄色，极其相似。路的尽头还是一幢单调的浅黄色的房子，跟其他的没什么两样。通向它的这条灰色的路，没有行人走过的痕迹，也没有马车或是汽油的痕迹，没有汽车、马车、警察、小贩、猫咪、苍蝇或是蜜蜂。"
"No sign of human life, except the names of legal firms to right and left of each open doorway.","没有人类生活的迹象，只是每一扇敞开的门的左右两边都挂着法律事务所的招牌。"
"“‘Cuthcott, Kingson and Forsyte, Commissioners for Oaths: First Floor.’”","“‘卡思考特、金森和福赛特，宣誓公证人：请上二楼。’”"
"‘Rule Britannia!’ thought Michael, ascending wide stone steps.","“大英律例！”迈克尔一边想着，一边踏上了宽阔的石头台阶。"
"Entering the room to which he had been ushered, he saw an old and pug-faced fellow with a round grizzled beard, a black alpaca coat, and a roomy holland waistcoat round his roomy middle, who rose from a swivel chair.","按照引导，他走进了那房间，看到一个老人从转椅里站了起来。那个老人有一张狮子狗似的脸，花白胡须，穿着黑色羊驼毛外套，在宽大的腰身外面还罩着一件宽大的荷兰亚麻马甲。"
"“Aoh!” he said, “Mr. Michael Mont, I think.","“啊！”他说道，“我想您是迈克尔·蒙特先生吧。"
"I’ve been expecting you.","我一直在等您呢。"
"We shan’t be long about it, after Mr. Forsyte comes.","等会儿索姆斯来了以后，用不了太长时间就能办好。"
"He’s just stepped round the corner.","他刚到那边拐角处去了。"
"Mrs. Michael well, I hope?”","迈克尔太太身体还好吧？”"
"“Thanks; as well as—”","“谢谢，还好——”"
"“Ye-es: it makes you anxious.","“是啊，您在担心她。"
"Take a seat.","请坐吧。"
"Perhaps you’d like to read the draft?”","也许您想看看那份草稿吧？”"
"Thus prescribed for, Michael took some foolscap from a pudgy hand, and sat down opposite.","说完，他便用那肥大的手递给坐在他对面的迈克尔几张大页纸。"
"With one eye on the old fellow, and the other on the foolscap, he read steadily.","他一只眼看着老头，另一只眼看着草稿，从容地读着。"
"“It seems to mean something,” he said at last.","“这看起来有点儿意思。”他最后说。"
"He saw a gape, as of a frog at a fly, settle in the beard; and hastened to repair his error.","他看见那胡须下面老人的嘴张大了，就像青蛙看见苍蝇时咧着大嘴一样，于是他赶紧弥补自己的口误。"
"“Calculating what’s going to happen if something else doesn’t, must be rather like being a bookmaker.”","“在没有其他事发生的前提下计算将要发生的事，就像是在登记赛马赌注一样。”"
"He felt at once that he had not succeeded.","他立刻感觉到自己这句话并没有弥补之前的失言。"
"There was a grumpy mutter:","因为他听到对方生气地说："
"“We don’t waste our time, ‘ere.","“我们这儿可不浪费时间。"
"Excuse me, I’m busy.”","原谅我失陪了，我还有事要忙。”"
"Michael sat, compunctious, watching him tick down a long page of entries.","迈克尔懊悔地坐在那里，看着他在长长的一页条目上做标记。"
"He was like one of those old dogs which lie outside front doors, keeping people off the premises, and notifying their fleas.","他就像一只老狗一样，趴在大门外，不让人靠近屋子，警告人们别惹麻烦。"
"After less than five minutes of that perfect silence Soames came in.","就这样过了近五分钟的绝对寂静之后，索姆斯走了进来。"
"“You’re here, then?” he said.","“哦，你来了?”他说。"
"“Yes, sir; I thought it best to come at the time you mentioned.","“是的，先生。我觉得最好按照您说的那个时间来。"
"What a nice cool room!”","多么凉爽舒服的房间啊！”"
"“Have you read this?” asked Soames, pointing to the draft.","“你看过这个了吗？”索姆斯指着那份草稿问道。"
"Michael nodded.","迈克尔点了点头。"
"“Did you understand it?”","“看明白了吗？”"
"“Up to a point, I think.”","“看懂些要点吧，我是这么想的。”"
"“The interest on THIS fifty thousand,” said Soames, “is Fleur’s until her eldest child, if it’s a boy, attains the age of twenty-one, when the capital becomes his absolutely.","“这五万块钱的利息，”索姆斯说，“是给弗勒的，直到她的最大的孩子年满21岁。如果是儿子，那么此后的本金就全归他了。"
"If it’s a girl, Fleur retains half the income for life, the rest of the income becomes payable to the girl when she attains the age of twenty-one or marries, and the capital of that half goes to her child or children lawfully begotten, at majority or marriage, in equal shares.","如果是女儿，那么弗勒终身都享有这份收益的一半，其余的收益等这个孩子年满21岁或是出嫁时，再给她，这一半本金归这个孩子合法生育的孩子或孩子们所有，等他们成年或是成亲时，大家均分。"
"The other half of the capital falls into Fleur’s estate, and is disposable by her will, or follows the laws of intestacy.”","另一半本金则归入弗勒的财产，可以根据她的遗嘱或是根据无遗嘱的法律来处理。”"
"“You make it wonderfully clear,” said Michael","“您订立得很清楚。”迈克尔说。"
"“Wait!” said Soames.","“等一下！”索姆斯说，"
"“If Fleur has no children—”","“如果弗勒没有孩子——”"
"Michael started.","迈克尔吃了一惊。"
"“Anything is possible,” said Soames gravely, “and my experience is that the contingencies not provided for are those which happen.","“什么事都有可能，”索姆斯严肃地说，“而我的经验告诉我，没有防范到的事恰恰是会意外发生的事。"
"In such a case the income of the whole is hers for life, and the capital hers at death to do as she likes with.","在这种情况下，所有收益归她终身所有，本金也归她，等她死的时候按她的意愿处理。"
"Failing that, it goes to the next of kin.","如果未能处理，这笔财产就交给她关系最近的亲属。"
"There are provisions against anticipation and so forth.”","对于预先支取等情况，也有相应条款规定。”"
"“Ought she to make a fresh will?” asked Michael, conscious of sweat on his forehead.","“她是不是应该立一份新的遗嘱呢？”迈克尔问道，觉得自己额头上都出汗了。"
"“Not unless she likes.","“不必，除非她自愿。"
"Her present will covers it.”","她现在的遗嘱会把这个包括进去的。”"
"“Have I to do anything?”","“需要我做什么事情吗？”"
"“No. I wanted you to understand the purport before I sign; that’s all.","“不需要。我要你在我签字之前了解其中的要义，仅此而已。"
"Give me the deed, Gradman, and get Wickson in, will you?”","把那份契约给我，格雷德曼，再叫威克森进来，好吗？”"
"Michael saw the old chap produce from a drawer a fine piece of parchment covered with copper-plate writing and seals, look at it lovingly, and place it before Soames.","迈克尔看到那个老人从抽屉里拿出一张印有铜版雕刻的字迹和印章的羊皮纸，亲切地看了看，然后放在了索姆斯面前。"
"When he had left the room, Soames said in a low voice:","老人离开房间后，索姆斯低声说："
"“This meeting on Tuesday—I can’t tell!","“周二的会议——我自己也没把握！"
"But, whatever happens, so far as I can see, this ought to stand.”","但是，不管发生什么事情，依我所见，这份契约都应该订立。”"
"“It’s awfully good of you, sir.”","“您真是太好了，先生。”"
"Soames nodded, testing a pen.","索姆斯点了点头，拿出一支钢笔试了试能不能写出字来。"
"“I’m afraid I’ve got wrong with your old clerk,” said Michael; “I like the look of him frightfully, but I accidentally compared him to a bookmaker.”","“我担心我刚才得罪了您那位老办事员，”迈克尔说，“我非常喜欢他那副神情，但是我刚才不小心把他比作赛马赌注登记经纪人了。”"
"Soames smiled.","索姆斯笑了。"
"“Gradman,” he said, “is a ‘character.’","“格雷德曼，”他说，“是个‘有个性的人’。"
"There aren’t many, nowadays.”","现在，这种人不多了。”"
"Michael was wondering: Could one be a ‘character’ under the age of sixty?—when the ‘character’ returned, with a pale man in dark clothes.","迈克尔纳闷了：一个快60岁的人，能被称为“有个性的人”吗？这时，那个“有个性的人”回来了，还带来了一个穿深色衣服、面色苍白的人。"
"Lifting his nose sideways, Soames said at once:","索姆斯把鼻子朝旁边儿撇了一下，马上说道："
"“This is a post-nuptial settlement on my daughter.","“这是一份给我女儿的婚后财产赠与书。"
"I deliver this as my act and deed.”","我把它交出，作为我行动及契约凭证。”"
"He wrote his name, and got up.","他签下了自己的名字，然后站了起来。"
"The pale person and Gradman wrote theirs, and the former left the room.","那个面色苍白的人和格雷德曼也签了名，然后那个人就离开了。"
"There was a silence as of repletion.","这时大家都很满意，没有说话。"
"“Do you want me any more?” asked Michael.","“您还需要我做什么吗？”迈克尔问道。"
"“Yes.","“是的。"
"I want you to see me deposit it at the bank with the marriage settlement.","我想让你看着我把它存入银行，和结婚时的财产赠与书放在一起。"
"Shan’t come back, Gradman!”","我就不回来了，格雷德曼！”"
"“Good-bye, Mr. Gradman.”","“再见，格雷德曼先生。”"
"Michael heard the old fellow mutter through his beard half buried in a drawer to which he was returning the draft, and followed Soames out.","迈克尔听到那个老人的声音从胡子中间传出来。那胡子还有一半埋在抽屉里，因为老人正在把那份草稿放进抽屉里。然后，迈克尔就跟着索姆斯出来了。"
"“Here’s where I used to be,” said Soames as they went along the Poultry; “and my father before me.”","“这是我以前常呆的地方，”他们沿着家禽街走着的时候，索姆斯说，“在我之前是我父亲常呆的地方。”"
"“More genial, perhaps,” said Michael.","“也许更亲切些吧。”迈克尔说。"

"Here they are!”","他们已经来了！”"
"They had reached the bank, and in the entrance Michael saw two Forsytes between thirty and forty, whose chinny faces he dimly remembered.","他们到银行了。在入口处，迈克尔看到了那两个福赛特家的人，三四十岁年纪，他还模糊地记得他们那下巴突出的样子。"
"Escorted by a man with bright buttons down his front, they all went to a room, where a man without buttons produced a japanned box.","在一个胸前有闪亮纽扣的人的陪同下，他们进到一个房间里，那里一个胸前没有纽扣的人拿出一个漆盒子。"
"One of the Forsytes opened it with a key; Soames muttered an incantation, and deposited the deed.","一位福赛特家族的人拿钥匙把它打开了，索姆斯小声地念叨了点儿什么，然后把契约放了进去。"
"When he and the chinnier Forsyte had exchanged a few remarks with the manager on the question of the bank rate, they all went back to the lobby and parted with the words: “Well, good-bye.”","他和福赛特家那个下巴突出的人就银行利率问题跟经理聊了几句，然后大家一起回到了大厅，互相说了句“那么，再见了”，就分手了。"
"“Now,” said Soames, in the din and hustle of the street, “he’s provided for, so far as I can see.","“现在，”索姆斯在喧闹忙碌的街道上说，“据我所知，你们已经为他准备好了。"
"When exactly do you expect it?”","你们预计他到底什么时候出生呢？”"
"“It should be just a fortnight.”","“也就还有两周时间吧。”"

"“Fleur’s wonderfully calm; she does Coue night and morning.”","“弗勒很镇静。她每天早晚都在做库埃的心理暗示。”"
"“That!” said Soames.","“那种东西！”索姆斯说。"
"He did not mention that he himself was doing it, thus giving away the state of his nerves.","他并没有提及自己也在做心理疗法，以免暴露自己的精神状态，"
"“If you’re going home, I’ll come, too.”","“如果你准备回家的话，我也和你一起回去。”"
"“Good!”","“好的！”"
"He found Fleur lying down with Ting-a-ling on the foot of the sofa.","他发现弗勒躺在沙发上，小叮铃躺在沙发脚上。"
"“Your father’s here, darling.","“你父亲来了，亲爱的。"

"I expect he’d like to tell you all about it.”","我想他会很高兴地告诉你这件事的。”"
"Fleur moved restlessly.","弗勒不安地动了一下。"
"“Presently.","“马上就来。"
"If it’s going on as hot as this, it’ll be rather a bore, Michael.”","要是这么热下去的话，可就麻烦了，迈克尔。”"
"“Oh! but it won’t, ducky.","“哦！不会的，亲爱的。"
"Three days and a thunderstorm.”","热上三天就会有一场大雷雨的。”"
"Taking Ting-a-ling by the chin, he turned his face up.","他捏着小叮铃的下巴，抬起了它的头。"
"“And how on earth is your nose going to be put out of joint, old man?","“你怎么这么会争宠呀，老兄？"
"There’s no joint to put.”","根本没人和你争嘛。”"
"“He knows there’s something up.”","“它知道有事要发生了。”"
"“He’s a wise little brute, aren’t you, old son?”","“它是个聪明的小畜生，是不是啊，小子？”"
"Ting-a-ling sniffed.","小叮铃用鼻子嗤了一声。"
"“Michael!”","“迈克尔！”"
"“Yes, darling?”","“什么事，亲爱的？”"
"“I don’t seem to care about anything now—it’s a funny feeling.”","“我现在好像什么都不关心了——这种感觉很奇怪。”"
"“That’s the heat.”","“那是因为天气太热了。”"
"“No. I think it’s because the whole business is too long.","“不。我认为是因为这个事情拖得太久了。"
"Everything’s ready, and now it all seems rather stupid.","一切都准备好了，可是现在看来一切很傻。"
"One more person in the world or one more out of it—what does it matter?”","这世界上多一个人或是少一个人——有什么关系呢？”"
"“Don’t!","“别这么说！"
"It matters frightfully!”","关系可大了！”"
"“One more gnat to dance, one more ant to run about!”","“不过是多了一只跳舞的蚊子或是一只跑来跑去的蚂蚁罢了！”"
"Anguished, Michael said again:","迈克尔感到很痛苦，于是他又开口说："
"“Don’t, Fleur!","“别这么说，弗勒！"
"That’s just a mood.”","这只是一时的情绪罢了。”"
"“Is Wilfrid’s book out?”","“威尔弗里德的书出版了吗？”"
"“It comes out tomorrow.”","“明天出版。”"
"“I’m sorry I gave you such a bad time, there.","“很抱歉，你看，前一段时间让你很苦恼。"
"I only didn’t want to lose him.”","我只是不想失去他。”"
"Michael took her hand.","迈克尔拉着她的手。"
"“Nor did I—goodness knows!” he said.","“我也不想——苍天可鉴！”他说。"
"“He’s never written, I suppose?”","“我想他没来过信吧？”"
"“No.”","“没有。”"
"“Well, I expect he’s all right by now.","“不过，我想他现在应该挺好的。"
"Nothing lasts.”","没什么是持续不变的。”"
"Michael put her hand to his cheek.","迈克尔把她的手放在自己脸颊上。"
"“@I@ do, I’m afraid,” he said.","“恐怕，我是不会变的。”他说。"
"The hand slipped round over his lips.","那只手滑到了他的嘴唇上。"
"“Give Dad my love, and tell him I’ll be down to tea.","“替我向爸爸问好，告诉他我会下来喝茶的。"
"Oh!","哎呀！"
"I’m so hot!”","我太热了！”"
"Michael hovered a moment, and went out.","迈克尔犹豫了一下，然后出去了。"
"Damn the heat, upsetting her like this!","该死的热天，让她那么烦心！"
"He found Soames standing in front of the white monkey.","他看见索姆斯站在那幅白猿前面。"
"“I should take this down, if I were you,” he muttered, “until it’s over.”","“如果我是你的话，就把它摘下来，”他喃喃说道，“等孩子生了再挂出来。”"
"“Why, sir?” asked Michael, in surprise.","“为什么，先生？”迈克尔吃惊地问。"
"Soames frowned.","索姆斯皱了皱眉头。"
"“Those eyes!”","“那一双眼睛啊！”"
"Michael went up to the picture.","迈克尔走到那幅画前。"
"Yes!","是啊！"
"He was a haunting kind of brute!","这幅画是那种让人一见就难以忘怀的类型！"
"“But it’s such top-hole work, sir.”","“可是这是很棒的作品啊，先生。”"
"Soames nodded.","索姆斯点头认可了。"
"“Artistically, yes.","“从艺术上来说，是的。"
"But at such times you can’t be too careful what she sees.”","但是在这个关头，凡是她看到的东西你都得小心再小心。”"
"“I believe you’re right.","“我认为您是对的。"
"Let’s have him down.”","我们一起把它取下来吧。”"
"“I’ll hold him,” said Soames, taking hold of the bottom of the picture.","“我来托住它。”索姆斯一边说，一边托着画的底部。"
"“Got him tight?","“抓紧了吗？"
"Right-o.","好的——"
"Now!”","行了！”"
"“You can say I wanted an opinion on his period,” said Soames, when the picture had been lowered to the floor.","“就说我想鉴别一下它是什么年代的。”当把这幅画放到地板上的时候，索姆斯说。"
"“There can hardly be a doubt of that, sir—the present!”","“这有什么好怀疑的，先生——现代的！”"
"Soames stared.","索姆斯瞪着眼睛。"
"“What?","“什么？"
"Oh!","啊！"
"You mean—?","你是说——？"
"Ah!","啊！"
"H’m!","哎呀！"

"“That’ll look as if I’d taken him off.","“这样看起来就像我把画带走了。"
"You can hang him again, later.”","过些日子，你可以把画再挂起来。”"
"“Yes.","“好的。"
"Poor brute!” said Michael, bearing the monkey off to limbo.","可怜的家伙！”迈克尔说着，把那幅画带去关禁闭了。"

"Chapter XI","第十一章"
"With a Small ‘n’","大自然露出了本来面目"
"On the night of the Monday following, after Fleur had gone to bed, Michael and Soames sat listening to the mutter of London coming through the windows of the Chinese room opened to the brooding heat.","到了周一的晚上，等弗勒上床睡觉以后，迈克尔和索姆斯两人坐着倾听伦敦的喧嚣。因为天气闷热，那间中式的房间敞开了窗户，声音就是从那里传进来的。"
"“They say the war killed sentiment,” said Soames suddenly: “Is that true?”","“据说战争泯灭了人类的情感，”索姆斯突然说道，“这是真的吗？”"
"“In a way, yes, sir.","“在某种程度上说，是真的，先生。"
"We had so much reality that we don’t want any more.”","我们经历了那么多的现实，不想要更多的感情了。”"
"“I don’t follow you.”","“我不明白你的意思。”"
"“I meant that only reality really makes you feel.","“我是说人们只对现实才有感觉。"
"So if you pretend there IS no reality, you don’t have to feel.","因此，要是你假装世上没有现实，那么你也就不必对什么有感觉了。"
"It answers awfully well, up to a point.”","从某种程度上来讲，这是很好的解答。”"
"“Ah!” said Soames.","“啊！”索姆斯说，"
"“Her mother comes up tomorrow morning, to stay.","“她母亲明天早晨过来，住在这儿。"
"This P. P. R. S. meeting of mine is at half-past two.","下午两点半我去参加天佑再保险公司的股东大会。"
"Good-night!”","晚安！”"
"Michael, at the window, watched the heat gathered black over the Square.","迈克尔站在窗前，看着热气在广场上空凝聚成了乌云。"
"A few tepid drops fell on his outstretched hand.","他把手伸出窗外，接到了几滴温热的雨点。"
"A cat stole by under a lamp-post, and vanished into shadow so thick that it seemed uncivilised.","一只猫从街灯下面偷偷溜过去，消失在一片阴影中，那阴影如此厚重，以至于那里似乎像是蛮荒之地。"
"Queer question of ‘Old Forsyte’s’ about sentiment; odd that he should ask it!","“老福赛特”提出的那个关于伤感之情的问题很怪异，而且他居然会问起这样的问题来！"
"‘Up to a point!","“奇怪到了一定程度！"
"But don’t we all get past that point?’ he thought.","但是我们不都怪得超过这个程度了吗？”他想道。"
"Look at Wilfrid, and himself—after the war they had deemed it blasphemous to admit that anything mattered except eating and drinking, for tomorrow they died; even fellows like Nazing, and Master, who were never in the war, had felt like that ever since.","看看威尔弗里德，还有他自己——经历了战争之后，他们认为如果除了吃喝之外还有其他重要的事情，那就是在亵渎神明，因为明天可能就没命了。即便是内津、马斯特这样没上过战场的人，战后也有这样的感觉。"
"Well, Wilfrid had got it in the neck; and he himself had got it in the wind; and he would bet that—barring one here and there whose blood was made of ink—they would all get it in the neck or wind soon or late.","哎，威尔弗里德已经亲身体验到了痛苦，而他自己也虚惊一场，而且他愿意打赌——除了零零散散个别冷血的家伙之外——他们早晚也会和他俩一样体验痛苦或是虚惊。"
"Why, he would cheerfully bear Fleur’s pain and risk, instead of her!","哎呀，他倒是愿意由自己来替弗勒承受痛苦和风险，不要再让她承受了！"
"But if nothing mattered, why should he feel like that?","但是如果什么事情都不重要的话，他为何会有这样的感觉呢？"
"Turning from the window, he leaned against the lacquered back of the jade-green settee, and stared at the wall space between the Chinese tea-chests.","从窗边转过身来，他靠在翠绿色长椅那用油漆漆过的后背上，注视着两个中式茶柜之间的那块空白墙壁。"
"Jolly thoughtful of the ‘old man’ to have that white monkey down!","“老头子”把白猿取下来真是考虑得太周到了！"
"The brute was potent—symbolic of the world’s mood: beliefs cancelled, faiths withdrawn!","画中的畜生很有影响力——象征着这个世界的精神状态：没有信仰，没有信念！"
"And, dash it! not only the young—but the old—were in that temper!","该死！不仅年轻人——就连老人——都是这种心境！"
"‘Old Forsyte,’ or he would never have been scared by that monkey’s eyes; yes, and his own governor, and Elderson, and all the rest.","“老福赛特”就是这样，要不然他也不会害怕那只白猿的眼神，对了，还有自己的父亲，还有埃尔德森，还有其他的人都是这样。"
"Young and old—no real belief in anything!","不论老幼——对什么都没有真正的信仰！"
"And yet—revolt sprang up in Michael, with a whirr, like a covey of partridges.","然后——迈克尔的心里忽然涌起一股反感，像一群鹧鸪振翅飞过似的。"
"It DID matter that some person or some principle outside oneself should be more precious than oneself—it dashed well did!","除了自己之外，还有别的人或是某个原则比自己还要重要，这的确是件要紧的事——确确实实是的！"
"Sentiment, then, wasn’t dead—nor faith, nor belief, which were the same things.","那么，情感，并没有泯灭——信仰、信念也没有泯灭，这都是一回事。"
"They were only shedding shell, working through chrysalis, into—butterflies, perhaps.","它们也许只是在蜕壳，逐渐变成蛹，最后变成——蝴蝶。"
"Faith, sentiment, belief, had gone underground, possibly, but they were there, even in ‘Old Forsyte’ and himself.","信念、情感、信仰可能已经转入地下了，但是它们还在，甚至在“老福赛特”和自己身上。"
"He had a good mind to put the monkey up again.","他很想把那幅白猿再挂起来。"
"No use exaggerating his importance!...","无需夸大它的影响力……"
"By George!","糟糕！"
"Some flare!","闪电了！"
"A jagged streak of vivid light had stripped darkness off the night.","一道锯齿形的亮光划破了黑暗的夜空。"
"Michael crossed, to close the windows.","迈克尔走过去，把窗户关上。"
"A shattering peal of thunder blundered overhead; and down came the rain, slashing and sluicing.","头顶突然炸开了一阵响雷，接着就下雨了，倾盆大雨。"
"He saw a man running, black, like a shadow across a dark blue screen; saw him by the light of another flash, suddenly made lurid and full of small meaning, with face of cheerful anxiety, as if he were saying: “Hang it, I’m getting wet!”","他看到有人在跑，黑漆漆的，像一个影子从深蓝色的银幕前跑过。在另一道闪电的映照下，他看到那个人突然变得苍白而有内涵，脸上混杂着欢喜和焦急，仿佛在说：“该死的，把我淋湿了！”"
"Another frantic crash!","接着又是一阵狂乱的雷鸣！"
"‘Fleur!’ thought Michael; and clanging the last window down, he ran upstairs.","“弗勒！”迈克尔想着，他咣当一声关上了最后一扇窗户，然后跑上楼去。"
"She was sitting up in bed, with a face all round, and young, and startled.","她坐在床上，年轻的小脸圆圆的，受了惊吓。"
"‘Brutes!’ he thought—guns and the heavens confounded in his mind: ‘They’ve waked her up!’","“畜生！”他心里想——战场的枪炮声和天空的雷电在他脑子里混在一起，“它们把她吵醒了！”"
"“It’s all right, darling!","“别害怕，亲爱的！"
"Just another little summer kick-up!","只是打雷了！"
"Were you asleep?”","你刚才睡着了？”"
"“I was dreaming!”","“我正做梦呢！”"
"He felt her hand clutching within his own, saw a sudden pinched look on her face, with a sort of rage.","他感到她的手在他的手中攥得紧紧的，脸色因突然的紧张而变得苍白，好像还带着愤怒。"
"What infernal luck!","真背运！"
"“Where’s Ting?”","“小丁在哪儿呢？”"
"No dog was in the corner.","角落里没有狗。"
"“Under the bed—you bet!","“一定躲在床底下了！"
"Would you like him up?”","想让它到床上去吗？”"
"“No. Let him stay; he hates it.”","“不必了。让它呆在那儿吧，它怕打雷。”"
"She put her head against his arm, and Michael curled his hand round her other ear.","她把头靠在他胳膊上，迈克尔用手堵着她的另一只耳朵。"
"“I never liked thunder much!” said Fleur,” and now it—it hurts!”","“我从来都不怎么喜欢雷声！”弗勒说，“现在它——让我难过！”"
"High above her hair Michael’s face underwent the contortions of an overwhelming tenderness.","在弗勒的头发上方，迈克尔的脸温柔得都变形了。"
"One of those crashes which seem just overhead sent her face burrowing against his chest, and, sitting on the bed, he gathered her in, close.","雷声不断，有一个仿佛就在他们头顶炸响，吓得弗勒把脸埋进他的怀里去了。他乘势坐在床上，紧紧地搂住了她。"
"“I wish it were over,” came, smothered, from her lips.","“真希望快点儿结束。”她的声音闷闷地从双唇间传了出来。"
"“It will be directly, darling; it came on so suddenly!”","“马上就好了，亲爱的，它来得太突然了！”"
"But he knew she didn’t mean the storm.","但是他明白她说的并不是这场雷雨。"
"“If I come through, I’m going to be quite different to you, Michael.”","“要是我能熬过这一关，我会待你完全不同的，迈克尔。”"
"Anxiety was the natural accompaniment of such events, but the words, “If I come through” turned Michael’s heart right over.","遇上这种事，难免会焦虑，但是那句话，“要是我能熬过去”却将迈克尔的心揪了起来。"
"Incredible that one so young and pretty should be in even the remotest danger of extinction; incredibly painful that she should be in fear of it!","一个这么年轻、美丽的人哪怕是处于一丝濒临死亡的危险，这都让人难以置信，她为此而担心，这更是难以置信的痛苦了！"
"He hadn’t realised.","他以前从来没有意识到这一点。"
"She had been so calm, so matter-of-fact about it all.","在这件事情上，她一直是那么镇静，那么平淡。"
"“Don’t!” he mumbled; “of course you’ll come through.”","“别这么说！”他喃喃地说，“你当然可以熬过去。”"
"“I’m afraid.”","“我害怕。”"
"The sound was small and smothered, but the words hurt horribly.","她说话的声音小小的、闷闷的，但是这句话让人很难过。"
"Nature, with the small ‘n,’ forcing fear into this girl he loved so awfully!","大自然露出了本性，迫使她——这个他深爱的姑娘——害怕了！"
"Nature kicking up this godless din above her poor little head!","大自然在她的小脑瓜上面肆无忌惮地制造噪音。"
"“Ducky, you’ll have twilight sleep and know nothing about it; and be as right as rain in no time.”","“亲爱的，你会接受半麻醉分娩，不会有什么感觉的。然后就像下雨一样，一会儿就过去了。”"
"Fleur freed her hand.","弗勒把自己的手抽了出来。"
"“Not if it’s not good for him.","“要是对孩子不好的话，就别用了。"
"Is it?”","会对孩子有影响吗？”"
"“I expect so, sweetheart; I’ll find out.","“我想不会，亲爱的，我会弄清楚的。"
"What makes you think—?”","你怎么会想起——？”"
"“Only that it’s not natural.","“只是因为这不是自然生产。"
"I want to do it properly.","我想要个合适的做法。"
"Hold my hand hard, Michael.","抓紧我的手，迈克尔。"
"I—I’m not going to be a fool.","我——我不想当傻瓜。"
"Oh!","啊！"
"Some one’s knocking—go and see.”","有人敲门——去看看。”"
"Michael opened the door a crack.","迈克尔把门开了一条缝。"
"Soames was there—unnatural—in a blue dressing gown and scarlet slippers!","索姆斯站在那里——很奇怪——他穿着蓝色的睡衣和红色的拖鞋！"
"“Is she all right?” he whispered.","“她还好吗？”他小声问道。"
"“Yes, yes.”","“是的。还好。”"
"“In this bobbery she oughtn’t to be left.”","“这会儿这么闹，可不能让她自己呆着。”"
"“No, sir, of course not.","“不会的，先生。当然不会让她一个人呆着。"
"I shall sleep on the sofa.”","我会睡在沙发上的。”"
"“Call me, if anything’s wanted.”","“有需要的话，叫我一声。”"
"“I will.”","“我会的。”"
"Soames’ eyes slid past, peering into the room.","索姆斯的目光从他身上越过，向屋里张望了一下。"
"A string worked in his throat, as if he had things to say which did not emerge.","他喉头一紧，仿佛要说什么，却又没说出口。"
"He shook his head, and turned.","他只是摇了摇头，转身走了。"
"His slim figure, longer than usual, in its gown, receded down the corridor, past the Japanese prints which he had given them.","因为穿着睡衣，他那瘦削的身影显得比平时还要长，走过他送给他们的那几张日本版画，向走廊那边走去。"
"Closing the door again, Michael stood looking at the bed.","迈克尔再次把门关好，站在那里望着床。"
"Fleur had settled down; her eyes were closed, her lips moving.","弗勒已经躺下去了，眼睛闭着，嘴唇在动。"
"He stole back on tiptoe.","他踮着脚尖悄悄地走了回去。"
"The thunder, travelling away south, blundered and growled as if regretfully.","雷声渐渐向南去了，仿佛后悔似的断断续续地发出隆隆声。"
"Michael saw her eyelids quiver, her lips stop, then move again.","迈克尔看到她眼睑在颤动，嘴唇却停了下来，一会又动了起来。"
"‘Coue!’ he thought.","“库埃的心理暗示！”他心里想。"
"He lay down on the sofa at the foot of the bed, whence, without sound, he could raise himself and see her.","他躺在床角的沙发上，他可以从那里悄悄地抬起身子看着她。"
"Many times he raised himself.","他起身很多次。"
"She had dropped off, was breathing quietly.","她已经睡着了，安静地呼吸着。"
"The thunder was faint now, the flashes imperceptible.","雷声变弱了，闪电也感觉不到了。"
"Michael closed his eyes.","迈克尔闭上了眼睛。"
"A faint last mutter roused him to look at her once more, high on her pillows by the carefully shaded light.","最后一阵低语让他又看了她一眼。她枕着高高的枕头，灯光被细心地遮住了。"
"Young—young!","年轻——真年轻！"
"Colourless, like a flower in wax!","苍白无色，像是朵蜡制的花！"
"No scheme in her brain, no dread—peaceful!","脑子里没有什么计划，也没有畏惧——安安静静的！"
"If only she could stay like that and wake up with it all over!","要是她能保持这样，然后一觉醒来，事情都过去了，那就好了！"
"He looked away.","他看了看旁边。"
"And there she was at the far end, dim, reflected in a glass; and there to the right, again.","从镜子里看，她在远远的那一边，模模糊糊的；再看看右边，也是一样。"
"She lay, as it were, all round him in the pretty room, the inhabiting spirit—of his heart.","在这间漂亮的房间里，她仿佛躺在他的周围，守护着他的心灵。"
"It was quite still now.","这会儿安静极了。"
"Through a chink in those powder-blue curtains he could see some stars.","透过那些浅灰蓝色窗帘的缝隙，他可以看到几颗星星。"
"Big Ben chimed one.","大本钟敲1点钟了。"
"He had slept, perhaps, dozed at least, dreamed a little.","他大概睡着了，起码是打了个盹儿，还做了一会儿梦。"
"A small sound woke him.","一个微弱的声音吵醒了他。"
"A very little dog, tail down, yellow, low and unimportant, was passing down the room, trailing across it to the far corner.","一只很小的狗，黄色的，尾巴垂着，卑微而又不引人注意，正慢慢地横穿这个房间，朝远远的角落走去。"
"‘Ah!’ thought Michael, closing his eyes again: ‘You!’","“啊！”迈克尔想着，又闭上了眼睛，“是它啊！”"

"Chapter XII","第十二章"
"Ordeal by Shareholder","股东的严峻考验"
"Repairing, next day, to the Aeroplane Club, where, notably spruce, Sir Lawrence was waiting in the lounge, Michael thought: ‘Good old Bart! he’s got himself up for the guillotine all right!’","第二天，迈克尔到飞机俱乐部去。在那里，经过一番修饰显得格外潇洒的劳伦斯爵士正在休息室里等待，迈克尔想：“好一个老准爵爷！他已经打扮好准备上断头台了！”"
"“That white piping will show the blood!” he said.","“那条白色的拷边会把血显现出来的！”他说，"
"“Old Forsyte’s neat this morning, but not so gaudy.”","“老福赛特今天早上很整洁，但是不俗气。”"
"“Ah!","“啊！"
"How is ‘Old Forsyte’?","‘老福赛特’怎么样？"
"In good heart?”","情绪好吗？”"
"“One doesn’t ask him, sir.","“这可不方便问他，先生。"
"How do you feel yourself?”","您自己觉得怎么样？”"
"“Exactly as I used to before the Eton and Winchester match.","“和过去我在伊顿和温彻斯特比赛前的心情一模一样。"
"I think I shall have shandy-gaff at lunch.”","我想我要在吃午饭的时候喝点儿香迪啤酒。”"
"When they had taken their seats, Sir Lawrence went on:","他们坐下之后，劳伦斯爵士接着说："
"“I remember seeing a man tried for murder in Colombo; the poor fellow was positively blue.","“我记得在科伦坡看到一个人因为谋杀而受审，那个可怜的家伙可真够垂头丧气的。"
"I think my favourite moment in the past, Michael, is Walter Raleigh asking for a second shirt.","我认为过去我最得意的时候，迈克尔，是沃尔特·罗利再次向我索要衬衫的时候。"
"By the way, it’s never been properly settled yet whether the courtiers of that day were lousy.","顺便说一句，那时候的朝臣们身上是否长虱子，这个问题至今还没有定论。"
"What are you going to have, my dear fellow?”","你想吃点儿什么，亲爱的年轻人？”"
"“Cold beef, pickled walnuts, and gooseberry tart.”","“冷牛肉、盐渍核桃和醋栗馅饼。”"
"“Excellent for the character.","“这些东西非常适合你。"
"I shall have curry; they give you a very good Bombay duck here.","我要吃咖喱，这里的龙头鱼非常不错。"
"I rather fancy we shall be fired, Michael.","我很确信我们会被解雇的，迈克尔。"
"‘Nous sommes trahis!’ used to be the prerogative of the French, but I’m afraid we’re getting the attitude, too.","‘我们已经被人出卖了！’这向来是法国人特有的说法，但是恐怕我们也逐渐抱有这种态度了。"
"The Yellow Press has made a difference.”","黄色报刊是起了作用的。”"
"Michael shook his head.","迈克尔摇了摇头。"
"“We say it, but we don’t act on it; the climate’s too uncertain.”","“我们是这样说的，但是并没有这样做。风气太不稳定了。”"
"“That sounds deep.","“这话听起来很深刻。"
"This looks very good curry—will you change your mind?","这个咖喱看起来很不错——你要不要也换成咖喱？"
"Old Fontenoy sometimes comes in here; he has no inside.","老福坦诺有时候也到这儿来，他并不了解内情。"
"It’ll be serious for him if we’re shown the door.”","如果我们被赶了出去，事情对他来说就严重了。”"
"“Deuced rum,” said Michael suddenly, “how titles still go down.","“真奇怪，”迈克尔突然说，“贵族头衔怎么还很受欢迎。"
"There can’t be any belief in their business capacity.”","一点儿也不能相信他们做生意的能力。”"
"“Character, my dear fellow—the good old English gentleman.","“这是名誉地位，亲爱的年轻人——善良的英国老绅士。"
"After all, there’s something in it.”","毕竟，这是有点儿道理的。”"
"“I fancy, sir, it’s more a case of complex in the shareholders.","“我想，先生，在股东们中这更像是一种复杂情结。"
"Their parents show them a lord when they’re young.”","在他们小时候，父母就把有爵位的贵族指给他们看了。”"
"“Shareholders,” said Sir Lawrence; “the word is comprehensive.","“股东，”劳伦斯爵士说，“这个词涉及面很广泛。"
"Who are they, what are they, when are they?”","他们是谁，他们是干什么的，他们什么时候成为股东的？”"
"“This afternoon,” said Michael, “and I shall have a good look at them.”","“今天下午，”迈克尔说，“我可要好好看看他们。”"
"“They won’t let you in, my dear.”","“他们不会让你进去的，亲爱的。”"
"“No?”","“不让进？”"
"“Certainly not.”","“当然不让进了。”"
"Michael frowned.","迈克尔皱了皱眉头。"
"“What paper,” he said, “is sure not to be represented?”","“哪家报纸，”他说，“一定不会派代表来呢？”"
"Sir Lawrence gave his whinnying laugh.","劳伦斯爵士发出马嘶般的笑声。"
"“The Field,” he said; “The Horse and Hound; The Gardener’s Weekly.”","“《田野报》，”他说，“《马与猎犬报》、《园丁周报》。”"
"“I’ll slide in on them.”","“我就以他们的名义溜进去。”"
"“You’ll see us die game, I hope,” said Sir Lawrence, with sudden gravity.","“我希望你会看到我们宁死不屈。”劳伦斯爵士突然严肃地说。"
"They took a cab together to the meeting, but separated before reaching the door of the hotel.","他们一起乘出租车去开会，但是在到达宾馆门口之前就分开了。"
"Michael had thought better of the Press, and took up a position in the passage, whence he could watch for a chance.","迈克尔重新考虑之后，决定不以报社的名义混进去，他在走廊里找了个位置，在此等待机会。"
"Stout men, in dark suits, with a palpable look of having lunched off turbot, joints, and cheese, kept passing him.","穿着黑色西服的矮胖的人们不断从他身边经过，脸上明显带着一种午餐吃了大比目鱼、大块肉和奶酪的神情。"
"He noticed that each handed the janitor a paper.","他注意到每个人都递给看门人一张纸。"
"‘I’ll hand him a paper, too,’ he thought, ‘and scoot in.’","“我也递给他一张纸，”他想，“然后冲进去。”"
"Watching for some even stouter men, he took cover between two of them, and approached the door, with an announcement of ‘Counterfeits’ in his left hand.","他看到几个更加矮胖的人，便躲藏在其中两个人中间，走进门口，左手拿着一张“假冒的”通知。"
"Handing it across a neighbouring importance, he was quickly into a seat.","他越过身边的一个大人物把它递过去，就迅速坐在一个位子上。"
"He saw the janitor’s face poked round the door.","他看到看门人在门口探了一下头。"
"‘No, my friend,’ thought Michael, ‘if you could tell duds from shareholders, you wouldn’t be in that job!’","“不，我的朋友，”迈克尔想，“如果你能从股东中分辨出谁是冒牌货，你就不会做这份工作了！”"
"He found a report before him, and holding it up, looked at other things.","他发现面前有一份报告，就拿了起来，眼睛却看着别的东西。"
"The room seemed to him to have been got by a concert-hall out of a station waiting-room.","这个房间在他看来似乎是由一个车站候车室改建成的音乐厅。"
"It had a platform with a long table, behind which were seven empty chairs, and seven inkpots, with seven quill pens upright in them.","房间里面有一个平台，上面摆着一张长桌子，桌子后面有七把空椅子，桌子上面放着七只墨水瓶，里面插着七只鹅毛笔。"
"‘Quills!’ thought Michael; ‘symbolic, I suppose—they’ll all use fountain-pens!’","“鹅毛笔！”迈克尔想，“我想，这只是象征性的——他们都使用钢笔！”"
"Back-centre of the platform was a door, and in front, below it, a table, where four men were sitting, fiddling with notebooks.","平台后面的中央有一扇门，在门前的下方，有一张桌子，四个人坐在那里，拨弄着笔记本。"
"‘Orchestra,’ thought Michael.","“管弦乐队。”迈克尔想。"
"He turned his attention to the eight or ten rows of shareholders.","他把注意力转向八到十排的股东。"
"They looked what they were, but he could not tell why.","他们看上去还是老样子，他也说不上来为什么。"
"Their faces were cast in an infinity of moulds, but all had the air of waiting for something they knew they would not get.","他们的脸虽然长得各式各样，但是都带有一种神态，仿佛在等待他们明知自己不会得到的东西。"
"What sort of lives did they lead, or did their lives lead them?","他们过着什么样的生活，或者说他们的生活怎样造就了他们？"
"Nearly all wore moustaches.","几乎所有的人都留着小胡子。"
"His neighbours to right and left were the same stout shareholders between whom he had slipped in; they both had thick lobes to their ears, and necks even broader than the straight broad backs of their heads.","他左右两边的邻座就是他夹在他们中间溜进来的那两个矮胖的股东。他俩的耳朵都有大耳垂，脖子甚至比后脑勺还要粗。"
"He was a good deal impressed.","这给他留下了深刻的印象。"
"Dotted here and there he noticed a woman, or a parson.","他注意到在座之中还零星坐着一两位女士和牧师。"
"There was practically no conversation, from which he surmised that no one knew his neighbour.","几乎没有什么人在交谈，由此他推测出没有人认识自己的邻座。"
"He had a feeling that a dog somewhere would have humanised the occasion.","他觉得如果在某个地方有一条狗的话，会使这个场合显得人性化。"
"He was musing on the colour scheme of green picked out with chocolate and chased with gold, when the door behind the platform was thrown open, and seven men in black coats filed in, and with little bows took their seats behind the quills.","他正在沉思着室内那种在绿色的底色上点缀着巧克力色并镶嵌着金色的色彩搭配，这时平台后面的那扇门突然打开了，七个穿着黑色外套的人陆续走了进来，微微鞠躬之后，就坐在了鹅毛笔后面的位子上。"
"They reminded him of people getting up on horses, or about to play the piano—full of small adjustments.","他们使他想到了正在翻身上马的人，或者将要弹钢琴的人——都有许多小的调整动作。"
"That—on the Chairman’s right—would be old Fontenoy, with a face entirely composed of features.","那个——坐在董事长右边的——应该是老福坦诺，他的脸完全是由各种特征组成的。"
"Michael had an odd conceit: a little thing in a white top-hat sat inside the brain, driving the features eight-inhand.","迈克尔有一种奇怪的幻想：一个头戴白色大礼帽的小家伙坐在大脑里面，八马齐驱地驾驭着这些特征。"
"Then came a face straight from a picture of Her Majesty’s Government in 1850, round and pink, with a high nose, a small mouth, and little white whiskers; while at the end on the right was a countenance whose jaw and eyes seemed boring into a conundrum beyond the wall at Michael’s back.","之后的那张面孔好像直接是从1850年的女王陛下政府的一张画里出来的，粉红色的圆脸、高鼻梁、小嘴巴，还有一小撮白色的络腮胡子。而在右边的尽头有一张面孔，它的下巴和眼睛仿佛钻进了迈克尔背后那面墙之外的一个谜题里面去了。"
"‘Legal!’ he thought.","“法律！”他想。"
"His scrutiny passed back to the Chairman.","他的目光又绕了回来仔细观察董事长。"
"Chosen?","选举出来的？"
"Was he—or was he not?","他是——或者不是？"
"A bearded man, a little behind on the Chairman’s left, was already reading from a book, in a rapid monotonous voice.","一个留着胡子的人，在董事长的左边稍靠后一点儿的地方，已经在用一种又快又单调的嗓音照本宣科。"
"That must be the secretary letting off his minute guns.","那一定是秘书在放他的志哀礼炮。"
"And in front of him was clearly the new manager, on whose left Michael observed his own father.","在他前面的显然是新任的经理，在经理的左边，迈克尔看到了自己的父亲。"
"The dark pothooks over Sir Lawrence’s right eye were slightly raised, and his mouth was puckered under the cut line of his small moustache.","劳伦斯爵士右眼上的黑色单镜片框钩微微上扬，他的嘴巴缩拢在修剪整齐的小胡子下面。"
"He looked almost Oriental, quick but still.","他看上去简直就像个东方人，机敏而又沉稳。"
"His left hand held his tortoiseshell-rimmed monocle between thumb and finger.","他用左手的拇指和食指捏着他那玳瑁色边框的单片眼镜。"
"‘Not quite in the scene!’ thought Michael; ‘poor old Bart!’","“还不太适应这种场面呢！”迈克尔想，“可怜的老准爵爷！”"
"He had come now to the last of the row.","现在他的目光来到了这一排最后一个人的身上。"
"‘Old Forsyte’ was sitting precisely as if alone in the world; with one corner of his mouth just drawn down, and one nostril just drawn up, he seemed to Michael quite fascinatingly detached; and yet not out of the picture.","“老福赛特”坐在那里，完全就像全世界只有他孤身一人似的。他的一个嘴角垂下来，一个鼻孔拉上去，在迈克尔看来，他那副超然的样子十分迷人，然而他又不是置身事外的。"
"Within that still neat figure, whereof only one patent-leather boot seemed with a slight movement to be living, was intense concentration, entire respect for the proceedings, and yet, a queer contempt for them; he was like a statue of reality, by one who had seen that there was precious little reality in it.","在他那依然匀称的身材里，只有一只漆皮的靴子似乎轻微地动着，表明他是活的。他全神贯注，完全尊重会议程序，然而，对其又有一种奇怪的轻视。他就像是一座现实的雕塑，而塑造它的人发现其中几乎没有什么宝贵的现实。"
"‘He chills my soup,’ thought Michael, ‘but—dash it!—I can’t help half admiring him!’","“他让我倒胃口，”迈克尔想，“但是——该死——我忍不住有点儿佩服他！”"
"The Chairman had now risen.","现在董事长站了起来。"
"‘He IS’—thought Michael; ‘no, he isn’t—yes—no—I can’t tell!’","“他是”——迈克尔想，“不，他不是——是——不——我分辨不出来！”"
"He could hardly attend to what the Chairman said, for wondering whether he was chosen or not, though well aware that it did not matter at all.","他几乎无法专心听董事长说的话，因为他正在想他究竟是不是选举出来的，尽管他非常清楚这个问题无关紧要。"
"The Chairman kept steadily on.","董事长不慌不忙地继续说下去。"
"Distracted, Michael caught words and words: “European situation—misguided policy—French—totally unexpected—position disclosed—manager—unfortunate circumstances shortly to be explained to you—future of this great concern—no reason to doubt—”","由于思想不集中，迈克尔只听到了只言片语：“欧洲局势——被误导的方针政策——法国人——完全出乎意料——揭露出来的情况——经理——马上就会向你们解释这些不幸的情况——大家关注的公司未来——没有理由担心——”"
"‘Oil,’ thought Michael, ‘he is—and yet—!’","“废话，”迈克尔想，“他是——可是——！”"
"“I will now ask one of your directors, Mr. Forsyte, to give you at first hand an account of this painful matter.”","“现在我要请公司的董事之一，福赛特先生，向你们直接讲述这件令人痛心的事情。”"
"Michael saw Soames, pale and deliberate, take a piece of paper from his breast-pocket, and rise.","迈克尔看到索姆斯，脸色苍白而从容不迫，从胸前的口袋中掏出一张纸，然后站了起来。"
"Was it to the occasion?","他这是挺身而出吗？"
"“I will give you the facts shortly,” he said in a voice which reminded Michael of a dry, made-up wine.","“我把事实简单向大家汇报一下，”他说话的声音让迈克尔想起了一种调制的干葡萄酒，"
"“On the eleventh of January last I was visited by a clerk in the employ of the Society—”","“一月十一日那天，本公司雇佣的一名职员来见我——”"
"Familiar with these details, Michael paid them little attention, watching the shareholders for signs of reaction.","由于非常熟悉这些细节，迈克尔没有怎么仔细听，而是注视着股东们的反应。"
"He saw none, and it was suddenly borne in on him why they wore moustaches: They could not trust their mouths!","他看不出任何迹象，突然他想到他们为什么要留胡子：他们不能相信自己的嘴巴！"
"Character was in the mouth.","性格就在嘴巴里。"
"Moustaches had come in when people no longer went about, like the old Duke, saying: “Think what you damned well like of my character!”","胡子是在人们不再四处走动的时候流行起来的，就像那个老公爵，说：“这就是我的性格，你们爱怎么想就怎么想吧！”"
"Mouths had tried to come in again, of course, before the war; but what with majors, shareholders, and the working classes, they now had little or no chance!","当然，在战前，不留胡子的光嘴巴曾经试图再次流行起来，但是由于年长的人、股东以及工人阶级的原因，它们流行起来的机会很小或根本就没有机会！"
"He heard Soames say: “In these circumstances we came to the conclusion that there was nothing for it but to wait and see.”","他听到索姆斯说：“在这种情况下，我们得出的结论是，除了静待观望形势之外，，没有别的办法。”"
"Michael saw a sudden quiver pass over the moustaches, as might wind over grass.","迈克尔看到那些胡子突然颤动了一下，就像一阵风吹过草地。"
"‘Wrong phrase,’ he thought; ‘we all do it, but we can’t bear being reminded of it.’","“措辞不当，”他想，“我们都犯过这种错误，但是我们都不能容忍别人提起它。”"
"“Six weeks ago, however,” he heard Soames intone, “an accidental incident seems to have warned your late manager that Sir Lawrence and I still entertained suspicions, for I received a letter from him practically admitting that he had taken this secret commission on the German business, and asking me to inform the Board that he had gone abroad and left no property behind him.","“但是，六个星期之前，”他听到索姆斯拖长了声音，“一件意外的事情似乎警告了你们的前任经理，使他知道劳伦斯爵士和我对他仍然抱有怀疑，因为我收到了他的一封来信，信中实际上承认了他在德国业务中收受了秘密佣金，并要求我通知董事会，他已经出国了，并且没有留下任何财产。"
"This statement we have been at pains to verify.","我们已经尽力对这番陈述进行了核实。"
"In these circumstances we had no alternative but to call you together, and lay the facts before you.”","在这种情况下，我们别无选择，只能把大家召集起来，并把事实摆在你们面前。”"
"The voice, which had not varied an iota, ceased its recital; and Michael saw his father-inlaw return to his detachment—stork on one leg, about to apply beak to parasite, could have inspired no greater sense of loneliness.","一直没有丝毫变化的声音停止了陈述；迈克尔看到他的岳父又恢复了超然的状态——就像一只鹳鸟单腿站立着，正准备用嘴去啄食寄生虫，不会引起更加强烈的孤寂感了。"
"‘Too like the first account of the battle of Jutland!’ he thought: ‘He mentioned all the losses, and never once struck the human note.’","“太像日德兰海战的第一次战况报告了！”他想，“他提到了所有的损失，但是一次也没有打动人们的心。”"
"A pause ensued, such as occurs before an awkward fence, till somebody has found a gate.","接下来是一阵停顿，就像某人在还没有找到大门之前，面对着栅栏而感到的尴尬一样沉寂。"
"Michael rapidly reviewed the faces of the Board.","迈克尔迅速地观察了一下董事会成员们的脸。"
"Only one showed any animation.","只有一张脸表现出了一点儿生气。"
"It was concealed in a handkerchief.","这张脸掩盖在一张手帕后面。"
"The sound of the blown nose broke the spell.","一阵擤鼻子的声音打破了沉寂。"
"Two shareholders rose to their feet at once—one of them Michael’s neighbour on the right.","两个股东立刻站了起来——其中一个就是迈克尔右边的邻座。"
"“Mr. Sawdry,” said the Chairman, and the other shareholder sat down.","“索德利先生。”董事长说，于是另外那个股东坐了下来。"
"With a sonorous clearing of the throat, Michael’s neighbour turned his blunt red face towards Soames.","迈克尔的邻座响亮地清了清嗓子，把他那张生硬的红脸转向索姆斯。"
"“I wish to ask you, sir, why you didn’t inform the Board when you first ‘eard of this?”","“我想问您一下，先生，当您第一次听到这个消息的时候，为什么没有通知董事会？”"
"Soames rose slightly.","索姆斯微微起身。"
"“You are aware, I presume, that such an accusation, unless it can be fully substantiated, is a matter for criminal proceedings?”","“我相信您一定很清楚，如果没有充分的证据，这种告发行为是会引起刑事诉讼的吧？”"
"“No; it would ha’ been privileged.”","“不，这是可以获得豁免权的。”"
"“As between members of the Board, perhaps; but any leakage would have rendered us liable.","“在各位董事之间，也许是这样，但是任何消息的泄露都会使我们负有责任。"
"It was a mere case of word against word.”","这只不过是一件口说无凭的事情罢了。”"
"“Perhaps Sir Lawrence Mont will give us ‘is view of that?”","“也许劳伦斯·蒙特爵士会告诉我们他对这件事的看法吧？”"
"Michael’s heart began to beat.","迈克尔的心开始跳动起来。"
"There was an air of sprightliness about his father’s standing figure.","他父亲站在那里的姿态带有一种轻松愉快的样子。"
"“You must remember, sir,” he said, “that Mr. Elderson had enjoyed our complete confidence for many years; he was a gentleman, and, speaking for myself, an old schoolfellow of his, I preferred, in common loyalty, to give his word preference, while—er—keeping the matter in mind.”","“你一定记得，先生，”他说，“埃尔德森先生多年以来一直深受我们的信任，他是一个绅士，而且，就我个人而言，我是他的老同学，出于一般的忠诚，我更倾向于相信他的话，而——呃——把这件事记在心里。”"
"“Oh!” said Michael’s neighbour: “What’s the Chairman got to say about bein’ kept in the dark?”","“哦！”迈克尔的邻座说，“关于被蒙在鼓里，董事长有什么话要说吗？”"
"“We are all perfectly satisfied, sir, with the attitude of our co-directors, in a very delicate situation.","“在一种微妙的形势下，我们大家对于董事同僚们的态度，先生，是非常满意的。"
"You will kindly note that the mischief was already done over this unfortunate assurance, so that there was no need for undue haste.”","请您注意一下，在这笔不幸的保险业务上，损害已经造成了，所以没有必要过分性急。”"
"Michael saw his neighbour’s neck grow redder.","迈克尔看到他的邻座的脖子变得更红了。"
"“I don’t agree,” he said.","“我不同意这种说法，”他说，"
"“‘Wait and see’—We might have ‘ad that commission out of him, if he’d been tackled promptly.”","“‘静待观望形势’——如果能立刻把他抓住，我们可能已经把那笔佣金从他身上挖出来了。”"
"And he sat down.","说完他就坐了下来。"
"He had not reached mahogany before the thwarted shareholder had started up.","他还没来得及坐到红木椅子上，刚才那个被拦住的股东就突然跳了起来。"
"“Mr. Botterill,” said the Chairman.","“伯特利尔先生。”董事长说。"
"Michael saw a lean and narrow head, with two hollows in a hairy neck, above a back slightly bent forward, as of a doctor listening to a chest.","迈克尔看到一个又瘦又窄的脑袋，长毛的脖子上有两处凹陷，背部微微前倾，就像一个医生正在听诊胸部。"
"“I take it from you, then, sir,” he said, “that these two directors represent the general attitude of the Board, and that the Board were content to allow a suspected person to remain manager.","“那么，先生，听了您的话我的理解是，”他说，“这两位董事代表了董事会的总体态度，而董事会甘愿让一个可疑的人继续担任经理。"
"The gentleman on your extreme left—Mr. Forsyte, I think—spoke of an accidental incident.","在您最左边的那位先生——福赛特先生，我想是——说到过一件意外的事情。"
"But for that, apparently, we should still be in the hands of an unscrupulous individual.","如果没有那件事，很显然，我们仍然会处于一个无耻之徒的掌握之中。"
"The symptoms in this case are very disquieting.","这件事情的种种迹象非常令人不安。"
"There appears to have been gross over-confidence; a recent instance of the sort must be in all our minds.","这其中似乎存在严重的过度自信。最近出现的这个事例，我们必须谨记在心。"
"The policy of assuring foreign business was evidently initiated by the manager for his own ends.","承保国外业务的方针政策显然是那位经理出于自己的目的而发起的。"
"We have made a severe loss by it.","我们因此遭受了严重的损失。"
"And the question for us shareholders would seem to be whether a Board who placed confidence in such a person, and continued it after their suspicions were aroused, are the right people to direct this important concern.”","而我们这些股东们面临的问题似乎是，一个对这样一个人给予信任，并且在引起他们的怀疑之后还继续给予他信任的董事会，究竟是不是管理这个重要的公司的合适人选。”"
"Throughout this speech Michael had grown very hot.","在这段发言的整个过程中，迈克尔越听火气越大。"
"‘“Old Forsyte” was right,’ he thought; ‘they’re on their uppers after all.’","“‘老福赛特’说得对，”他想，“毕竟他们快要走投无路了。”"
"There was a sudden creak from his neighbour on the left.","他左边的邻座突然发出一阵嘎吱嘎吱的声音。"
"“Mr. Tolby,” said the Chairman.","“托尔比先生。”董事长说。"
"“It’s a seerious matter, this, gentlemen.","“这是一件严重的事情，这件事，先生们。"
"I propose that the Board withdraw, an’ leave us to discuss it.”","我提议董事会退席，我们留下来讨论这件事情。”"
"“I second that,” said Michael’s neighbour on the right.","“我赞成。”迈克尔右边的邻座说。"
"Searching the vista of the Board, Michael saw recognition gleam for a second in the lonely face at the end, and grinned a greeting.","迈克尔察看着董事会那一长排人，看到在排尾那张孤寂的脸上闪过一丝认出他的神情，于是他咧嘴笑着打招呼。"
"The Chairman was speaking.","董事长正在说话。"
"“If that is your wish, gentlemen, we shall be happy to comply with it.","“如果你们希望这样，先生们，我们乐于遵命。"
"Will those who favour the motion hold up their hands?”","请赞成这个提议的人举一下手好吗？”"
"All hands were held up, with the exception of Michael’s, of two women whose eager colloquy had not permitted them to hear the request, and of one shareholder, just in front of Michael, so motionless that he seemed to be dead.","所有的人都举起了手，除了迈克尔，还有因在专心谈话而没有听到这个请求的两位女士，以及坐在迈克尔正前方的一个股东，他一动也不动，好像死了一样。"
"“Carried,” said the Chairman, and rose from his seat.","“通过。”董事长说，然后就从座位上站了起来。"
"Michael saw his father smiling, and speaking to ‘Old Forsyte’ as they both stood up.","迈克尔看到他的父亲正在微笑，他在和“老福赛特”说着话，两个人都站了起来。"
"They all filed out, and the door was closed.","他们都陆续退了出去，然后那扇门就关上了。"
"‘Whatever happens,’ Michael thought, ‘I’ve got to keep my head shut, or I shall be dropping a brick.’","“无论发生什么事情，”迈克尔想，“我一定要保持镇定，否则我会闯祸的。”"
"“Perhaps the Press will kindly withdraw, too,” he heard some one say.","“新闻界也请退席吧。”他听到有人说。"
"With a general chinny movement, as if enquiring their rights of no one in particular, the four Pressmen could be seen to clasp their notebooks.","那四位记者都动了动下巴，仿佛是在询问他们是否没有特权似的，只见他们合上了笔记本。"
"When their pale reluctance had vanished, there was a stir among the shareholders, like that of ducks when a dog comes up behind.","当他们那几张苍白勉强的脸消失之后，股东们中间掀起了一阵骚乱，就像一群鸭子后面有一条狗追赶了上来似的。"
"Michael saw why, at once.","迈克尔立刻看出了原因。"
"They had their backs to each other.","他们彼此都背对着背。"
"A shareholder said:","一个股东说："
"“Perhaps Mr. Tolby, who proposed the withdrawal, will act as Chairman.”","“或许提议董事会退席的托尔比先生可以担当主席。”"
"Michael’s left-hand neighbour began breathing heavily.","迈克尔左边的邻座呼吸开始变得沉重起来。"
"“Right-o!” he said.","“好啊！”他说，"
"“Any one who wants to speak, kindly ketch my eye.”","“哪一位要发言，请示意我。”"
"Everyone now began talking to his neighbour, as though to get at once a quiet sense of proportion, before speaking.","这时每一个人都开始和邻座的人交谈起来，仿佛是要在发言之前立刻获得一种平静的分寸感。"
"Mr. Tolby was breathing so heavily that Michael felt a positive draught.","托尔比先生呼吸如此沉重，使得迈克尔都能感受到他呼出的一阵阵气浪。"
"“‘Ere, gentlemen,” he said suddenly, “this won’t do!","“呃，先生们，”他突然说，“这样不行啊！"
"We don’t want to be too formal, but we must preserve some order.","我们不需要太正式，但是我们必须保持点儿秩序。"
"I’ll open the discussion myself.","我自己来给讨论开个头吧。"
"Now, I didn’t want to ‘urt the feelin’s of the Board by plain speakin’ in their presence.","嗯，我不想当着董事会的面把话说得太直白，以免伤了他们的感情。"
"But, as Mr. What’s-’is-name there, said: The public ‘as got to protect itself against sharpers, and against slackness.","但是，正如刚才那里的某一位先生所说的：公众必须保护自己以防骗子欺诈，并且防止松懈懒散。"
"We all know what ‘appened the other day, and what’ll ‘appen again in other concerns, unless we shareholders look after ourselves.","我们大家都知道前些日子发生了什么事情，以及以后在其他公司还会发生什么事情，除非我们股东自己照顾自己。"
"In the first place, then, what I say is: They ought never to ‘ave touched anything to do with the ‘Uns.","那么，首先，我要说的是：凡是和德国佬有关的事情，他们根本就不应该碰。"
"In the second place, I say they showed bad judgment.","其次，我要说他们表现出拙劣的判断力。"
"And in the third place I say they were too thick together.","第三，我要说他们的关系太亲密了。"
"In my opinion, we should propose a vote of no confidence.”","在我看来，我们应该提议投不信任票。”"
"Cries of: “Hear, hear!” mixed with indeterminate sounds, were broken sharply by a loud: “No!” from the shareholder who had seemed dead.","与许多模糊不清的声音混杂着一起的“说得好，说得好！”的叫喊声，，突然被一声响亮的“反对”打破了，这是那个好像死了一样的股东喊出来的。"
"Michael’s heart went out to him, the more so as he still seemed dead.","迈克尔对他充满了好感，尤其是当他仍然好像死了一样一动不动时，这种好感便越发强烈了。"
"The negative was followed by the rising of a thin, polished-looking shareholder, with a small grey moustache.","随着这个否定的喊声，站起来一位瘦削文雅的、留着灰白色小胡子的股东。"
"“If you’ll forgive my saying so, sir,” he began, “your proposal seems to me very rough-and-ready justice.","“但愿您能原谅我这么说，先生，”他开始说道，“在我看来，您的建议似乎是一种甚为勉强的评判。"
"I should be interested to know how you would have handled such a situation if you had been on the Board.","我很想知道，如果您是董事会的成员，您将会如何处理这种局面。"
"It is extremely easy to condemn other people!”","谴责别人是非常容易的！”"
"“Hear, hear!” said Michael, astonished at his own voice.","“说得好，说得好！”迈克尔说，他对自己的声音感到惊讶。"
"“It is all very well,” the polished shareholder went on, “when any thing of this sort happens, to blame a directorate, but, speaking as a director myself, I should be glad to know whom one is to trust, if not one’s manager.","“发生了这种事情，”这位文雅的股东继续说，“去责备董事会是很容易的，但是，我自己作为一个董事而言，我很想知道，如果我不信任经理，又该信任谁。"
"As to the policy of foreign insurance, it has been before us at two general meetings; and we have pocketed the profit from it for nearly two years.","至于国外保险业务的方针政策，我们已经在两次股东大会上研究过了，而且我们由此获利已经差不多两年了。"
"Have we raised a voice against it?”","我们可曾对此提出过反对吗？”"
"The dead shareholder uttered a “No!” so loud that Michael almost patted his head.","那个死了一样的股东喊了一声“反对！”，那声音如此响亮，以至于迈克尔几乎要拍拍他的脑袋表示赞许。"
"The shareholder, whose neck and back were like a doctor’s, rose to answer.","那个颈部和背部像一个医生似的股东站起来回答了。"
"“I differ from the last speaker in his diagnosis of the case.","“我不同意刚才那位发言人对这个事件的判断。"
"Let us admit all he says, and look at the thing more widely.","我们姑且承认他所说的一切，同时从更加广泛的角度来看它。"
"The proof of pudding is in the eating.","布丁好不好吃，要吃了才知道。"
"When a Government makes a bad mistake of judgment, the electorate turns against it as soon as it feels the effects.","当一个政府在判断上出现了严重的错误，选民一旦感受到了它的后果，就会反对它。"
"This is a very sound check on administration; it may be rough and ready, but it is the less of two evils.","这是对于行政管理的一种非常合情合理的遏制。这种做法可能是差强人意的，但却是两害取其轻的做法。"
"A Board backs its judgment; when it loses, it should pay.","董事会支持自己的判断，当它失败了，它应该付出代价。"
"I think, perhaps, Mr. Tolby, being our informal Chairman, was out of order in proposing a vote of no confidence; if that be so, I should be happy to do so, myself.”","我认为，托尔比先生作为我们的非正式的董事长，提议投不信任票或许是有违议事规程的。如果一定要那样做的话，我自己很乐于对此投同样的不信任票。”"
"The dead shareholder’s “No!” was so resounding this time that there was a pause for him to speak; he remained, however, without motion.","那位死了一样的股东这次喊出的“反对！”如此响亮，以至于大家都停下来等他发言，然而，他还是一动不动。"
"Both of Michael’s neighbours were on their feet.","迈克尔两边的邻座都站了起来。"
"They bobbed at each other over Michael’s head, and Mr. Tolby sat down.","他们在迈克尔的头顶上互相谦让了一下，之后托尔比先生坐了下来。"
"“Mr. Sawdry,” he said.","“索德利先生。”他说。"
"“Look ‘ere, gentlemen,” said Mr. Sawdry, “and ladies, this seems to me a case for compromise.","“请注意，先生们，”索德利先生说，“女士们，在我看来，这件事得采取妥协的办法。"
"The Directors that knew about the manager ought to go; but we might stop at that.","那些了解经理的董事们应该离开，但是我们可以到此为止。"
"The gentleman in front of me keeps on saying ‘No.’","我前面的这位先生一直说‘反对’。"
"Let ‘im give us ‘is views.”","让他告诉我们他的意见。”"
"“No,” said the dead shareholder, but less loudly.","“反对。”那位死了一样的股东说，但是声音不那么响亮了。"
"“If a man can’t give ‘is views,” went on Mr. Sawdry, nearly sitting down on Michael, “‘c shouldn’t interrupt, in my opinion.”","“如果一个人不提出自己的意见，”索德利先生接着说，差一点儿坐到迈克尔的身上，“我认为，他就不应该打岔。”"
"A shareholder in the front row now turned completely round so that he faced the meeting.","前排的一个股东现在完全转过身来，面对着会场。"
"“I think,” he said, “that to prolong this discussion is to waste time; we are evidently in two, if not three, minds.","“我认为，”他说，“再讨论下去就是浪费时间。很显然，我们即使没有三种意见，也有两种。"
"The whole of the business of this country is now conducted on a system of delegated trust; it may be good, it may be bad—but there it is.","我们这个国家的一切事务目前都是按照委任信托制度进行的。这可能是好的，但也可能是不好的——但是情况就是这样。"
"You’ve got to trust somebody.","你不得不信任某个人。"
"Now, as to this particular case, we’ve had no reason to distrust the Board, so far; and, as I take it, the Board had no previous reason to distrust the late manager.","现在，关于这件特定的事情，到目前为止，我们没有理由不信任董事会。而且，在我看来，董事会之前也没有理由不信任前任经理。"
"I think it’s going too far, at present, to propose anything definite like a vote of no confidence; it seems to me that we should call the Board in and hear what assurances they have to give us against a repetition of anything of the sort in the future.”","目前提出诸如投不信任票之类的明确措施，我认为那样太过分了。我觉得我们应该把董事会成员叫进来，听一听他们必须给我们什么保证，以防将来再发生类似的事情。”"
"The sounds which greeted this moderate speech were so inextricable that Michael could not get the sense of them.","这番温和的发言所引起的反响是如此错综复杂，迈克尔无法听出他们的意思。"
"Not so with the speech which followed.","接下来的发言情况就不同了。"
"It came from a shareholder on the right, with reddish hair, light eyelashes, a clipped moustache, and a scraped colour.","那是右边的一个股东讲的，他长着浅红色的头发，淡淡的睫毛，胡子修剪得整整齐齐，脸刮得很干净。"
"“I have no objection whatever to having the Board in,” he said in a rather jeering voice, “and passing a vote of no confidence in their presence.","“我一点儿也不反对把董事会成员们叫进来，”他用一种十分嘲弄的声调说，“并且要当着他们的面投不信任票。"
"There is a question, which no one has touched on, of how far, if we turn them out, we could make them liable for this loss.","有一个问题还没有人提到，就是如果我们把他们赶出去，我们还能让他们对这笔损失承担多大的责任。"
"The matter is not clear, but there is a good sporting chance, if we like to take it.","这个问题现在还不清楚，但是如果我们愿意抓住这次机会的话，这会是一个很公平的机会。"
"Whereas, if we don’t turn them out, it’s obvious we can’t take it, even if we wish.”","反之，如果我们不把他们赶出去，即使我们想抓住机会，我们显然也抓不住了。”"
"The impression made by this speech was of quite a different order from any of the others.","此番发言给人们留下的印象和以前所有的发言完全不同。"
"It was followed by a hush, as though something important had been said at last.","这之后是一阵沉默，仿佛终于有人说出重要的话了。"
"Michael stared at Mr. Tolby.","迈克尔盯着托尔比先生。"
"The stout man’s round, light, rather prominent eye was extraordinarily reflective.","这个矮胖子那相当突出的浅色圆眼睛充满了深邃的思考。"
"‘Trout must look like that,’ thought Michael, ‘when they see a mayfly.’","“当鲑鱼看到蜉蝣的时候，”迈克尔想，“它们的眼睛一定是这个样子。”"
"Mr. Tolby suddenly stood up.","托尔比先生突然站了起来。"
"“All right,” he said, “‘ave ‘em in!”","“好吧，”他说，“叫他们进来！”"
"“Yes,” said the dead shareholder.","“好。”那个死了一样的股东说。"
"There was no dissent.","没有人表示反对。"
"Michael saw some one rise and ascend the platform.","迈克尔看到有人站了起来，登上平台。"
"“Let the Press know!” said Mr. Tolby.","“通知记者们！”托尔比先生说。"

"Chapter XIII","第十三章"
"Soames at Bay","索姆斯陷入绝境"
"When the door had closed behind the departing directors, Soames sought a window as far as possible from the lunch eaten before the meeting.","当董事们离开会场，关上门之后，索姆斯找了一个窗户，尽可能来消化在开会前吃的那顿午饭。"
"“Funeral baked meats, eh, Forsyte?” said a voice in his ear.","“葬礼中剩下的残羹冷炙，呃，福赛特？”他的耳边有一个声音说，"
"“Our number’s up, I think.","“我想我们的气数已尽了。"
"Poor old Mothergill’s looking very blue.","可怜的老马瑟吉尔看起来非常沮丧。"
"I think he ought to ask for a second shirt!”","我想他应该要求第二件衬衫了！”"
"Soames’ tenacity began wriggling within him.","索姆斯的执拗脾气开始发作了。"
"“The thing wants tackling,” he grumbled; “the Chairman’s not the man for the job!”","“这件事需要着手解决，”他喃喃地说，“董事长不是做这件事的合适人选！”"
"Shades of old Uncle Jolyon!","让人想起老乔里恩叔叔啊！"
"He would have made short work of this!","他一定能迅速解决这件事！"
"It wanted a masterful hand.","这需要强有力的手腕。"
"“Warning to us all, Forsyte, against loyalty!","“这是警告我们大家，福赛特，不要讲忠诚了。"
"It’s not in the period.","这不合时宜。"
"Ah!","啊！"
"Fontenoy!”","福坦诺！”"
"Soames became conscious of features rather above the level of his own.","索姆斯意识到有一个比他高的人在旁边。"
"“Well, Mr. Forsyte, hope you’re satisfied?","“哦，福赛特先生，你满意了吧？"
"A pretty damned mess!","这可真是该死的一团糟！"
"If I’d been the Chairman, I’d never have withdrawn.","如果我是董事长，我决不会退席。"
"Always keep hounds under your eye, Mont.","要时刻看住你的猎犬，蒙特。"
"Take it off, and they’ll go for you!","目光一离开，它们就会袭击你！"
"Wish I could get among ‘em with a whip; I’d give it those two heavy pug-faced chaps—they mean business!","真希望我能拿着鞭子跑到他们中间去，我要抽那两个哈巴狗脸似的胖家伙——他们是存心这样做的！"
"Unless you’ve got something up your sleeve, Mr. Forsyte, we’re dished.”","除非您有什么锦囊妙计，福赛特先生，否则我们就完蛋了。”"
"“What should I have up my sleeve?” said Soames coldly.","“我会有什么妙计？”索姆斯冷冷地说。"
"“Damn it, sir, you put the chestnuts in the fire; it’s up to you to pull ‘em out.","“真该死，先生，是你把栗子放进火里去的，应该由你把它们取出来。"
"I can’t afford to lose these fees!”","我可承受不起这笔酬劳费的损失！”"
"Soames heard Sir Lawrence murmur: “Crude, my dear Fontenoy!” and said with malice:","索姆斯听到劳伦斯爵士喃喃地说：“太粗鲁了，我亲爱的福坦诺！”于是他恶毒地说："
"“You may lose more than your fees!”","“也许你损失的不只是你的酬劳费！”"
"“Can’t!","“不可能！"
"They may have Eaglescourt tomorrow, and take a loss off my hands.”","也许明天他们就会成立鹰庭，承担我的损失。”"
"A gleam of feeling burned up suddenly in the old eyes: “The country drives you to the wall, skins you to the bone, and expects you to give ‘em public service gratis.","那双苍老的眼睛里突然燃起了同情的闪光：“国家把你逼得走投无路，把你剥得只剩骨头，还指望你无偿地为他们提供公共服务。"
"Can’t be done, Mont—can’t be done!”","办不到，蒙特——办不到！”"
"Soames turned away; he had an utter disinclination for talk, like one standing before an open grave, watching a coffin slowly lowered.","索姆斯转过身去，他完全不想说话，就像一个人站在敞开的墓穴前面，看着一口棺材慢慢地放下去。"
"Here was his infallibility going—going!","他那一贯正确的名声就这样完了——完了！"
"He had no illusions.","他不抱任何幻想。"
"It would all be in the papers, and his reputation for sound judgment gone for ever!","这件事会刊登在各家报纸上，他以出众的决断力而闻名的声誉一去不复返了！"
"Bitter!","真痛苦！"
"No more would the Forsytes say: “Soames says—” No more would old Gradman follow him with eyes like an old dog’s, grudging sometimes, but ever submitting to infallibility.","福赛特家的人再也不会说“索姆斯说——”了。老格雷德曼再也不会用那双像老狗一样忠诚的眼睛追随着他了，尽管有时候有些勉强，但是始终服从他那一贯正确的判断。"
"It would be a nasty jar for the old fellow.","这将使那个老家伙大为震惊。"
"His business acquaintances—after all, they were not many, now!—would no longer stare with envious respect.","他那些生意上的熟人——毕竟，现在不太多了！——再也不会用羡慕而尊敬的目光注视他了。"
"He wondered if the reverberations would reach Dumetrius, and the picture market!","他不知道这些反响会不会传到杜梅特里斯以及绘画市场上！"
"The sole comfort was: Fleur needn’t know.","唯一的安慰是：不必让弗勒知道。"
"Fleur!","弗勒！"
"Ah!","啊！"
"If only her business were safely over!","但愿她能平安顺利地生产！"
"For a moment his mind became empty of all else.","他的脑子里有一会儿只想着这件事，其他的什么都不想。"
"Then with a rush the present filled it up again.","接着，眼前的事情又突然一下子充满了他的脑子。"
"Why were they all talking as if there were a corpse in the room?","为什么他们讲话的时候都好像房间里有一具死尸似的呢？"
"Well!","哦！"
"There was—the corpse of his infallibility!","确实有——就是他那一贯正确的死尸！"
"As for monetary loss—that seemed secondary, remote, incredible—like a future life.","至于金钱上的损失——那似乎是次要的、遥远的、难以置信的——就像来世一样。"
"Mont had said something about loyalty.","蒙特说过一些关于忠诚的话。"
"He didn’t know what loyalty had to do with it!","他不知道这件事和忠诚有什么关系！"
"But if they thought he was going to show any white feather, they were extremely mistaken.","但是如果他们认为他会示弱的话，那他们就大错特错了。"
"Acid courage welled up into his brain.","他的心中涌起了犀利的勇气。"
"Shareholders, directors—they might howl and shake their fists; he was not going to be dictated to.","股东们，董事们——他们或许会咆哮怒吼并挥舞着拳头，但他不会任人摆布的。"
"He heard a voice say:","他听到一个声音说："
"“Will you come in, please, gentlemen?”","“请你们进来好吗，先生们？”"
"Taking his seat again before his unused quill, he noticed the silence—shareholders waiting for directors, directors for shareholders.","他又在那支他从未用过的鹅毛笔前坐了下来，他注意到全场一片沉寂——股东们在等着董事们发言，而董事们在等着股东们发言。"
"“Wish I could get among ‘em with a whip!”","“真希望我能拿着鞭子跑到他们中间去！”"
"Extravagant words of that ‘old guinea-pig’s,’ but expressive, somehow!","这是那个“老豚鼠”说的放肆话，但是不知怎么的，很有表现力！"
"At last the Chairman, whose voice always reminded Soames of a raw salad with oil poured over it, said ironically:","最后，董事长讽刺地说，他的声音总是让索姆斯想起一种上面浇过油的生沙拉："
"“Well, gentlemen, we await your pleasure.”","“哦，先生们，我们在等各位的指示呢。”"
"That stout, red-faced fellow, next to Michael, stood up, opening his pug’s mouth.","坐在迈克尔旁边的那个红脸矮胖子站了起来，张开了他那哈巴狗似的嘴。"
"“To put it shortly, Mr. Chairman, we’re not at all satisfied; but before we take any resolution, we want to ‘ear what you’ve got to say.”","“简单地说，董事长先生，我们一点儿也不满意。但是在我们做出任何决议之前，我们想要听一听你们有什么要说的。”"
"Just below Soames, some one jumped up and added: “We’d like to know, sir, what assurances you can offer us against anything of this sort in the future.”","就在索姆斯的下面，一个人跳了起来，补充道：“我们想要知道，先生，你们能向我们做出什么样的保证，以避免今后再发生这种事情。”"
"Soames saw the Chairman smile—no real backbone in that fellow!","索姆斯看到董事长在微笑——那个家伙没有真正的骨气！"
"“In the nature of things, sir,” he said, “none whatever!","“从道理上讲，先生，”他说，“什么保证也没有！"
"You can hardly suppose that if we had known our manager was not worthy of our confidence, we should have continued him in the post for a moment!”","你总不至于认为，如果我们已经知道了我们的经理不值得我们信任，我们还会继续让他担任这个职务吧！”"
"Soames thought: ‘That won’t do—he’s gone back on himself!’","索姆斯想：“这样说可不行——他的话自相矛盾了！”"
"Yes, and that other pug-faced chap had seen it!","果然，另外那一个哈巴狗脸似的家伙看出了这一点！"
"“That’s just the point, sir,” he was saying: “Two of you DID know, and yet, there the fellow was for months afterwards, playin’ ‘is own ‘and, cheatin’ the Society for all he was worth, I shouldn’t wonder.”","“关键就在这里，先生，”他说，“你们中间有两个人的确知道，然而，这个家伙之后又干了几个月，为他自己牟利，竭尽全力地欺骗公司，我觉得这不足为奇。”"
"One after another, they were yelping now:","此时他们一个接一个地都在叫嚷："
"“What about your own words?”","“你们自己说过的话算不算数？”"
