"“You admitted collective responsibility.”","“你们应承过会集体负责的。”"
"“You said you were perfectly satisfied with the attitude of your co-directors in the matter.”","“你们说过，你们对于董事同僚们在这件事情上的态度是非常满意的。”"
"Regular pack!","真是一群疯狗！"
"Soames saw the Chairman incline his head as if he wanted to shake it; old Fontenoy muttering, old Mothergill blowing his nose, Meyricke shrugging his sharp shoulders.","索姆斯看到董事长低下头，好像要摇头的样子，老福坦诺在喃喃自语，老马瑟吉尔在擤鼻子，梅里克在耸着他那瘦削的肩膀。"
"Suddenly he was cut off from view of them—Sir Lawrence was standing up between.","突然他观察他们的视线被挡住——劳伦斯爵士在中间站了起来。"
"“Allow me a word!","“请允许我说一句话！"
"Speaking for myself, I find it impossible to accept the generous attempt of the Chairman to shoulder a responsibility which clearly rests on me.","就我自己而言，董事长试图慷慨地承担明显应该由我负起的责任，对此我不能接受。"
"If I made a mistake of judgment in not disclosing our suspicions, I must pay the penalty; and I think it will clear the—er—situation if I tender my resignation to the meeting.”","如果我在没有公开我们的怀疑这一点上做出了错误的判断，那么我应该受到处罚，而且我认为如果我向大会提交辞呈，那将会使——呃——局势明朗一点儿。”"
"Soames saw him give a little bow, place his monocle in his eye, and sit down.","索姆斯看到他微微鞠了一躬，把他的单片眼镜架在眼睛前，然后坐了下来。"
"A murmur greeted the words—approval, surprise, deprecation, admiration?","这番话引起了阵阵私语——是赞成、惊讶、反对，还是佩服呢？"
"It had been gallantly done.","这件事做得很勇敢。"
"Soames distrusted gallantry—there was always a dash of the peacock about it.","索姆斯不相信勇敢的行为——总有一点儿炫耀的意思。"
"He felt curiously savage.","他感到莫名其妙的愤怒。"
"“I, apparently,” he said, rising, “am the other incriminated director.","“我，很显然，”他说着，站了起来，“是另一个被指控的董事。"
"Very good!","很好！"
"I am not conscious of having done anything but my duty from beginning to end of this affair.","这件事从头至尾，我觉得除了尽了我的职责之外，我没有做过任何事情。"
"I am confident that I made no mistake of judgment.","我确信我没有做出错误的判断。"
"And I consider it entirely unjust that I should be penalised.","而且我认为，如果我受到处罚，那是完全不公正的。"
"I have had worry and anxiety enough, without being made a scapegoat by shareholders who accepted this policy without a murmur, before ever I came on the Board, and are now angry because they have lost by it.","在我加入董事会之前，股东们已经毫无异议地接受了这项方针政策，现在他们因遭受了损失就发起脾气来，要拿我当替罪羊，即便他们不这样做，我也已经够担心和焦虑的了。"
"You owe it to me that the policy has been dropped: You owe it to me that you have no longer a fraudulent person for a manager.","多亏了我，这项方针政策才被放弃了：多亏了我，你们才不再让一个骗子当经理。"
"And you owe it to me that you were called together today to pass judgment on the matter.","还是多亏了我，你们今天才被召集到一起，对这件事作出判断。"
"I have no intention whatever of singing small.","我一点儿也不想变得沉默寡言。"
"But there is another aspect to this affair.","但是这件事还有另外一方面。"
"I am not prepared to go on giving my services to people who don’t value them.","对于那些不重视我的服务的人，我不准备继续为他们效劳了。"
"I have no patience with the attitude displayed this afternoon.","我无法容忍今天下午他们表现出来的这种态度。"
"If any one here thinks he has a grievance against me, let him bring an action.","如果这里有任何一个人对我不满的话，那就让他去起诉好了。"
"I shall be happy to carry it to the House of Lords, if necessary.","如果有必要的话，我很乐意把这场官司打到上议院去。"
"I have been familiar with the City all my life, and I have not been in the habit of meeting with suspicions and ingratitude.","我这一辈子非常熟悉这座城市，我可不习惯遭到怀疑，或者与背信弃义的人有来往。"
"If this is an instance of present manners, I have been familiar with the City long enough.","如果这就是当今的风俗的话，那我对这座城市熟悉得也够久了。"
"I do not tender my resignation to the meeting; I resign.”","我不向大会提交辞呈，我这就辞职。”"
"Bowing to the Chairman, and pushing back his chair, he walked doggedly to the door, opened it and passed through.","他向董事长鞠了个躬，把椅子往后一推，固执地走到门口，打开门就走了出去。"
"He sought his hat.","他寻找他的帽子。"
"He had not the slightest doubt but that he had astonished their weak nerves!","他毫不怀疑，他已经使他们那脆弱的神经大为震惊！"
"Those pug-faced fellows had their mouths open!","那些哈巴狗脸似的家伙们张着嘴！"
"He would have liked to see what he had left behind, but it was hardly consistent with dignity to open the door again.","他很想看一看他引起了什么反应，但是再把门打开是有失尊严的。"
"He took a sandwich instead, and began to eat it with his back to the door and his hat on.","他转而拿起一块三明治，背朝着房门，戴着帽子，开始吃了起来。"
"He felt better than he had for months.","他觉得几个月以来从没有这么轻松过。"
"A voice said:","一个声音说："
"“‘And the subsequent proceedings interested him no more!’","“‘接下来的议程不会使他感兴趣了！’"
"I’d no idea, Forsyte, you were such an orator!","我以前不知道，福赛特，你竟是这样一位演说家！"
"You gave it ‘em between the eyes!","你击中了他们的要害！"
"Never saw a meeting so knocked out!","从来没有见过一个会议如此令人震惊！"
"Well, you’ve saved the Board by focussing their resentment entirely on yourself.","哦，你把他们的怨恨全部集中在你自己身上，从而拯救了董事会。"
"It was very gallant, Forsyte!”","这样做非常英勇，福赛特！”"
"Soames growled through his sandwich:","索姆斯一边吃着三明治，一边愤愤地说："
"“Nothing of the sort!","“绝无此事！"
"Are you out, too?”","你也不干了吗？”"
"“Yes.","“是的。"
"I pressed my resignation.","我坚决要辞职。"
"That red-faced fellow was proposing a vote of confidence in the Board when I left—and they’ll pass it, Forsyte—they’ll pass it!","我离开的时候，那个红脸的家伙正在提议对董事会投信任票——他们会通过的，福赛特——他们会通过的！"
"Something was said about financial liability, by the way!”","顺便说一下，他们还说到了有关经济责任的问题！”"
"“Was there?” said Soames, with a grim smile: “That cock won’t fight.","“是吗？”索姆斯冷酷地微笑着说，“那一招不管用。"
"Their only chance was to claim against the Board for initiating foreign assurance ultra vires; if they’re re-affirming the Board, after the question’s been raised in open meeting, they’re dished.","他们唯一的机会就是提出董事会创办国外保险业务是越权行为。如果这个问题在公开大会上提出之后，他们重新确认了董事会，那他们就完蛋了。"
"Nothing’ll lie against you and me, for not disclosing our suspicions—that’s certain.”","没有任何理由可以起诉你和我，说我们没有公开我们的怀疑——那是肯定的。”"
"“A relief, I confess,” said Sir Lawrence, with a sigh.","“我承认，这的确让我如释重负，”劳伦斯爵士叹了一口气说道，"
"“It was the speech of your life, Forsyte!”","“这是你一生中最精彩的演讲，福赛特！”"
"Perfectly well aware of that, Soames shook his head.","索姆斯非常明白这一点，但他摇了摇头。"
"Apart from the horror of seeing himself in print, he was beginning to feel that he had been extravagant.","除了害怕在报纸上见到自己的名字以外，他开始觉得自己做得太过分了。"
"It was always a mistake to lose your temper!","发脾气总是不对的！"
"A bitter little smile came on his lips.","他的嘴角露出一丝苦笑。"
"Nobody, not even Mont, would see how unjustly he had been treated.","没有一个人，甚至蒙特，会明白他受到了多么不公平的待遇。"
"“Well,” he said, “I shall go.”","“哦，”他说，“我要走了。”"
"“I think I shall wait, Forsyte, and hear the upshot.”","“我想我要等一会儿，福赛特，听一听结果如何。”"
"“Upshot?","“结果？"
"They’ll appoint two other fools, and slaver over each other.","他们会任命另外两个傻瓜，然后互相奉承一番。"
"Shareholders!","股东们！"
"Good-bye!”","再见吧！”"
"He moved to the door.","他朝门口走去。"
"Passing the Bank of England, he had a feeling of walking away from his own life.","经过英格兰银行的时候，他有一种离开了自己的生活的感觉。"
"His acumen, his judgment, his manner of dealing with affairs—aspersed!","他的聪明、他的判断力、他处理问题的方式——都遭到了中伤！"
"They didn’t like it; well—he would leave it!","他们不喜欢，好吧——到此为止吧！"
"Catch him meddling, in future!","看他以后还多管闲事！"
"It was all of a piece with the modern state of things.","这和现代事物的状态是完全一致的。"
"Hand to mouth, and the steady men pushed to the wall!","过一天算一天，而稳健的人却被逼上绝路！"
"The men to whom a pound was a pound, and not a mess of chance and paper.","对这种人而言，一英镑就是一英镑，不是一堆乱七八糟的机会和纸张。"
"The men who knew that the good of the country was the strict, straight conduct of their own affairs.","这种人知道，对国家有利的事情就是严格、直接地管理好自己的事物。"
"They were not wanted.","现在不需要这种人了。"
"One by one, they would get the go-by—as he had got it—in favour of Jack-o’-lanterns, revolutionaries, restless chaps, or clever, unscrupulous fellows, like Elderson.","他们会一个接一个地被人冷落——正如他现在所遭受的那样——而得宠的却是那些捉摸不定的人、革命家、不安分守己的人，或者是那些聪明但不讲道德的人，就像埃尔德森那样。"
"It was in the air.","这已经成为一种风气了。"
"No amount of eating your cake and wanting to have it could take the place of common honesty.","贪得无厌取代了普通的诚实。"
"He turned into the Poultry before he knew why he had come there.","他不知不觉地转弯走进了家禽街。"
"Well, he might as well tell Gradman at once that he must exercise his own judgment in the future.","哦，他不妨立刻告诉格雷德曼，今后他必须运用自己的判断力了。"
"At the mouth of the backwater he paused for a second, as if to print its buffness on his brain.","在后街口处他停留了一会儿，仿佛要把那虚幻的景象印在脑子里。"
"He would resign his trusts, private and all!","他要辞去他所接受的委托，连同私人委托一起辞去！"
"He had no notion of being sneered at in the family.","他可不打算在家中被人耻笑。"
"But a sudden wave of remembrance almost washed his heart into his boots.","但是突然的一波回忆几乎使他惊慌失措。"
"What a tale of trust deeds executed, leases renewed, houses sold, investments decided on—in that back room up there; what a mint of quiet satisfaction in estates well managed!","在楼上后面的那个房间里——有过多少故事啊：执行信托书、续订租赁合同、出售房屋、决策投资，不知有多少次因为财产管理得当而暗自得意！"
"Ah! well!","啊！好吧！"
"He would continue to manage his own.","他还要继续管理他自己的财产。"
"As for the others, they must look out for themselves, now.","至于别人的，现在，他们必须自己去照顾了。"
"And a precious time they’d have of it, in face of the spirit there was about!","面对周围的这种风气，这样一来他们就会有好日子过了。"
"He mounted the stone steps slowly.","他慢慢地走上石阶。"
"In the repository of Forsyte affairs, he was faced by the unusual—not Gradman, but, on the large ripe table, a large ripe melon alongside a straw bag.","在福塞特事务所里，面对他的是不同寻常的东西——不是格雷德曼，而是，在那张又大又旧的桌子上，有一个熟透的大西瓜，旁边还有一个草袋。"
"Soames sniffed.","索姆斯闻了闻。"
"The thing smelled delicious.","这东西闻起来很香。"
"He held it to the light.","他拿着它对着光看。"
"Its greeny yellow tinge, its network of threads—quite Chinese!","它那黄中透绿的色彩，它那网状的线条——完全是中国式的！"
"Was old Gradman going to throw its rind about, like that white monkey?","难道老格雷德曼像那只白猿一样，要把瓜皮到处乱扔吗？"
"He was still holding it when a voice said:","他手里还拿着这个西瓜，这时一个声音说："
"“Aoh!","“噢！"
"I wasn’t expecting you today, Mr. Soames.","我没想到您今天会来，索姆斯先生。"
"I was going early; my wife’s got a little party.”","我正打算早点儿走呢，我的妻子搞了一个小聚会。”"
"“So I see!” said Soames, restoring the melon to the table.","“原来是这样！”索姆斯说着，把那个西瓜重新放回到桌子上，"
"“There’s nothing for you to do at the moment, but I came in to tell you to draw my resignations from the Forsyte trusts.”","“这会儿没有什么事情要你去做，我只是来告诉你，替我起草一份辞去福赛特信托的辞职信。”"
"The old chap’s face was such a study that he could not help a smile.","这个老家伙脸上的表情如此怪异，索姆斯忍不住笑了。"
"“You can keep me in Timothy’s; but the rest must go.","“你可以把在蒂莫西那里的职位给我保留着，但是其余的必须辞掉。"
"Young Roger can attend to them.","小罗杰能料理这些事。"
"He’s got nothing to do.”","反正他也无事可做。”"
"A gruff and deprecating: “Dear me!","一个粗鲁的、极力反对的声音说道：“哎呀！"
"They won’t like it!” irritated Soames.","他们会不乐意的！”这激怒了索姆斯。"
"“Then they must lump it!","“那他们必须得忍耐着点儿！"
"I want a rest.”","我要休息一下。”"
"He did not mean to enter into the reason—Gradman could read it for himself in the Financial News, or whatever he took in.","他不打算解释原因——格雷德曼自己可以在《金融时报》上，或者不管他订的什么报纸上看到。"
"“Then I shan’t be seeing you so often, Mr. Soames; there’s never anything in Mr. Timothy’s.","“那么我就不会经常见到您了，索姆斯先生。蒂莫西先生的信托向来就没有什么事情。"
"Dear me!","哎呀！"
"I’m quite upset.","我完全被搞糊涂了。"
"Won’t you keep your sister’s?”","难道您妹妹的也不保留了吗？”"
"Soames looked at the old fellow, and compunction stirred within him—as ever, at any sign that he was appreciated.","索姆斯看着这个老家伙，心中激起了内疚——如往常一样，只要有被人赏识的迹象，他就会这样。"
"“Well,” he said, “keep me in hers; I shall be in about my own affairs, of course.","“哦，”他说，“把她的也给我留下。当然，关于我自己的事务我还是要保留的。"
"Good afternoon, Gradman.","再见，格雷德曼。"
"That’s a fine melon.”","那个西瓜不错。”"
"He waited for no more words.","他没有再等他说话。"
"The old chap!","这个老家伙！"
"HE couldn’t last much longer, anyway, sturdy as he looked!","虽然他看起来很健壮，但不管怎样，他总有离开的那天！"
"Well, they would find it hard to match him!","哦，他们会发现很难与其相比！"
"On reaching the Poultry, he decided to go to Green Street and see Winifred—queerly and suddenly homesick for the proximity of Park Lane, for the old secure days, the efflorescent privacy of his youth under the wings of James and Emily.","走到家禽街的时候，他决定去格林街看一看威尼费雷德——非常奇怪，他竟突然怀念起公园巷附近一带，怀念起过去无忧无虑的日子，怀念起在詹姆斯和艾米丽的庇护下，他那风华正茂的青少年时代。"
"Winifred alone represented for him now, the past; her solid nature never varied, however much she kept up with the fashions.","现在对他来说，只有威尼弗里德一个人代表着过去，她那可靠的性格从来没有改变过。"
"He found her, a little youthful in costume, drinking China tea, which she did not like—but what could one do, other teas were ‘common!’","他看到了她，衣着显得有点儿年轻，喝着中国茶，虽然她并不喜欢——但是有什么办法呢，别的茶都“太普通”了！"
"She had taken to a parrot.","她养了一只鹦鹉。"
"Parrots were coming in again.","鹦鹉现在又流行起来了。"
"The bird made a dreadful noise.","这只鸟发出了一阵非常讨厌的吵闹声。"
"Whether under its influence or that of the China tea—which, made in the English way, of a brand the Chinese grew for foreign stomachs, always upset him—he was soon telling her the whole story.","不知是受了鹦鹉的影响还是中国茶的影响——这种茶，是按照英国的方式泡制的，是中国人为了迎合外国人的口味而种植的一种品牌，总是使他感到不舒服——他很快就把整件事都告诉了她。"
"When he had finished, Winifred said comfortably:","等他说完了，威尼弗雷德愉快地说："
"“Well, Soames, I think you did splendidly; it serves them right!”","“嗯，索姆斯，我认为你干得很漂亮，他们活该如此！”"
"Conscious that his narrative must have presented the truth as it would not appear to the public, Soames muttered:","索姆斯知道他的叙述一定已经呈现了公众所不了解的事实真相，他喃喃地说："
"“That’s all very well; you’ll find a very different version in the financial papers.”","“这一切都很对；但是你会在金融报纸上看到完全不同的说法。”"
"“Oh! but nobody reads them.","“哦！但是没有人会看那些报纸。"
"I shouldn’t worry.","我就不担心。"
"Do you do Coue?","你做库埃吗？"
"Such a comfortable little man, Soames; I went to hear him.","如此一个让人舒服的小人儿，索姆斯，我去听过他的讲座。"
"It’s rather a bore sometimes, but it’s quite the latest thing.”","这东西有时候相当沉闷，但是它确实是最时髦的东西。”"
"Soames became inaudible—he never confessed a weakness.","索姆斯不说话了——他从来不承认自己的弱点。"
"“And how,” asked Winifred, “is Fleur’s little affair?”","“还有，”威尼弗雷德问，“弗勒的那件小事怎么样了？”"
"“‘Little affair!’” echoed a voice above his head.","“‘小事！’”一个声音在他的头顶上附和着。"
"That bird!","那只鸟！"
"It was clinging to the brocade curtains, moving its neck up and down.","它正紧紧地抓着锦缎窗帘，脖子上下移动着。"
"“Polly!” said Winifred: “don’t be naughty!”","“波利！”威尼弗雷德说，“别淘气！”"
"“Soames!” said the bird.","“索姆斯！”那只鸟叫道。"
"“I’ve taught him that.","“那是我教它的。"
"Isn’t he rather sweet?”","它是不是很可爱？"
"“No,” said Soames.","“不可爱，”索姆斯说，"
"“I should shut him up; he’ll spoil your curtains.”","“要是我就把它关起来。它会弄坏你的窗帘的。”"
"The vexation of the afternoon had revived within him suddenly.","下午的烦心事突然又在他的心里翻腾起来了。"
"What was life, but parrotry?","生活是什么，不就是鹦鹉学舌吗？"
"What did people see of the real truth?","人们能看到什么真正的真理？"
"They just repeated each other, like a lot of shareholders, or got their precious sentiments out of The Daily Liar.","他们只是互相重复说过的话，就像许多股东一样，或者从《骗子日报》上找到他们宝贵的观点。"
"For one person who took a line, a hundred followed on, like sheep!","只要有一个人带头，就会有一百个人跟上去，就像羊群一样！"
"“You’ll stay and dine, dear boy!” said Winifred.","“你留下来吃饭吧，亲爱的！”威尼弗雷德说。"
"Yes! he would dine.","好的！他要吃饭。"
"Had she a melon, by any chance?","也许她有西瓜呢？"
"He’d no inclination to go and sit opposite his wife at South Square.","他不愿意回到南广场，和他的妻子面对面地坐着。"
"Ten to one Fleur would not be down.","十有八九弗勒不会下楼来的。"
"And as to young Michael—the fellow had been there that afternoon and witnessed the whole thing; he’d no wish to go over it again.","至于小迈克尔——这家伙一下午都在那里，目睹了事情的全部经过。他不想把这件事再经历一遍。"
"He was washing his hands for dinner, when a maid, outside, said:","他正在洗手准备吃饭，这时一个女仆在外面说："
"“You’re wanted on the ‘phone, sir.”","“有人打电话找您，先生。”"
"Michael’s voice came over the wire, strained and husky:","电话里传来了迈克尔的声音，又紧张又沙哑："
"“That you, sir?”","“是您吗，先生？”"
"“Yes.","“是我。"
"What is it?”","什么事？”"
"“Fleur.","“弗勒。"
"It began this afternoon at three.","今天下午3点就开始了。"
"I’ve been trying to reach you.”","我一直在找您。”"
"“What?” cried Soames.","“什么？”索姆斯喊道，"
"“How?","“情况怎么样？"
"Quick!”","快说啊！”"
"“They say it’s all normal.","“他们说一切正常。"
"But it’s so awful.","但是这真可怕。"
"They say quite soon, now.”","他们说很快就好了，唔。”"
"The voice broke off.","声音突然断了。"
"“My God!” said Soames.","“天啊！”索姆斯说，"
"“My hat!”","“我的帽子！”"
"By the front door the maid was asking: “Shall you be back to dinner, sir?”","到了前门口，那个女仆问：“您还回来吃饭吗，先生？”"
"“Dinner!” muttered Soames, and was gone.","“吃饭！”索姆斯咕哝着，走了出去。"
"He hurried along, almost running, his eyes searching for a cab.","他急急忙忙地向前走，几乎是在跑着，眼睛寻找着出租车。"
"None to be had, of course!","当然，一辆也没有！"
"None to be had!","一辆也没有！"
"Opposite the ‘Iseeum’ Club he got one, open in the fine weather after last night’s storm.","在伊昔姆俱乐部对面他找到了一辆，经过昨夜的暴风雨，今天天气晴朗，所以车篷敞开着。"
"That storm!","那场暴风雨啊！"
"He might have known.","他本来应该知道的。"
"Ten days before her time.","比她的预产期提前了十天。"
"Why on earth hadn’t he gone straight back, or at least telephoned where he would be?","他究竟为什么不直接回去，或者至少打个电话告诉他们他要去哪里？"
"All that he had been through that afternoon was gone like smoke.","那天下午他所经历的一切都烟消云散了。"
"Poor child!","可怜的孩子！"
"Poor little thing!","可怜的小东西！"
"And what about twilight sleep?","半麻醉分娩法怎么样？"
"Why hadn’t he been there?","为什么他没有早点儿到那里？"
"He might have—nature!","他本来可以的——大自然！"
"Damn it!","该死！"
"Nature—as if it couldn’t leave even her alone!","大自然——仿佛连她都不能放过似的！"
"“Get on!” he said, leaning out: “Double fare!”","“赶快！”他探出身子说，“车钱加倍！”"
"Past the Connoisseurs, and the Palace, and Whitehall; past all preserves whence nature was excluded, deep in the waters of primitive emotion Soames sat, grey, breathless.","车子经过鉴赏家俱乐部、白金汉宫和白厅，经过所有那些把大自然无法控制的禁区，头发灰白、气喘吁吁的索姆斯就坐在那里，深深地沉浸在原始的情感之中。"
"Past Big Ben—eight o’clock!","经过大本钟——8点整！"
"Five hours!","五个小时！"
"Five hours of it!","已经有五个小时了！"
"“Let it be over!” he muttered aloud: “Let it be over, God!”","“让它过去吧！”他大声咕哝道，“让它过去吧，上帝！”"

"Chapter XIV","第十四章"
"On the Rack","焦虑不安"
"When his father-inlaw bowed to the Chairman and withdrew, Michael had restrained a strong desire to shout: “Bravo!”","当他的岳父向董事长鞠躬退席的时候，迈克尔很想大喊一声“好！”但是他克制住了。"
"Who’d have thought the ‘old man’ could let fly like that?","谁会想到这个“老头”会如此大发雷霆呢？"
"He had ‘got their goats’ with a vengeance.","他已经彻底地“惹恼了他们”。"
"Quite an interval of fine mixed vociferation followed, before his neighbour, Mr. Sawdry, made himself heard at last.","经过很长一段时间混乱的叫喊声，他的邻座索德利先生终于能够发言了。"
"“Now that the director implicated has resigned, I shall ‘ave pleasure in proposing a vote of confidence in the rest of the Board.”","“既然与此事有牵连的董事已经辞职了，我愿意提议对董事会的其他董事投信任票。”"
"Michael saw his father rise, a little finicky and smiling, and bow to the Chairman.","迈克尔看到他的父亲站了起来，有点儿做作，面带微笑，向董事长鞠了一躬。"
"“I take my resignation as accepted also; if you permit me, I will join Mr. Forsyte in retirement.”","“我就当我的辞职也被接受了。如果您允许的话，我就和福赛特先生一起退席了。”"
"Some one was saying:","有人在说："
"“I shall be glad to second that vote of confidence.”","“我赞成投信任票。”"
"And brushing past the knees of Mr. Sawdry, Michael sought the door.","迈克尔擦过索德利先生的膝盖，向门口走去。"
"From there he could see that nearly every hand was raised in favour of the vote of confidence; and with the thought: ‘Thrown to the shareholders!’ he made his way out of the hotel.","他从那里看到几乎每一个人都举手赞成投信任票。他心里想：“扔给这些股东们吧！”他走出了这家旅馆。"
"Delicacy prevented him from seeking out those two.","出于体谅他们的心情，迈克尔没有去寻找那两位老人。"
"They had saved their dignity; but the dogs had had the rest.","他们保全了尊严，但是那些卑鄙小人得到了其余的一切。"
"Hurrying west, he reflected on the rough ways of justice.","他急急忙忙地向西走去，心里想着做到公正是多么艰难。"
"The shareholders had a grievance, of course; and some one had to get it in the neck to satisfy their sense of equity.","当然，股东们也有抱怨的理由，为了满足他们的公平感，就得有人受到惩罚。"
"They had pitched on Old Forsyte, who, of all, was least to blame; for if Bart had only held his tongue, they would certainly have lumped him into the vote of confidence.","他们选中了老福赛特，而他在所有人当中，是最不应该受到谴责的。至于准爵爷，如果他能保持缄默，他们一定会把他归入信任票之列的。"
"All very natural and illogical; and four o’clock already!","这一切都很自然，但很不合逻辑。现在已经4点了！"
"‘Counterfeits!’","《赝品》今天出版！"
"The old feeling for Wilfrid was strong in him this day of publication.","在这天，他对威尔弗里德以往的感情在心里又变得强烈起来。"
"One must do everything one could for his book—poor old son!","一个人必须为他自己的书尽一切力量——可怜的老朋友！"
"There simply must not be a frost.","绝不能失败。"
"After calling in at two big booksellers, he made for his club, and closeted himself in the telephone booth.","拜访了两位大书商之后，他就去了自己的俱乐部，并把自己关在电话间里。"
"In old days they ‘took cabs and went about.’","在过去人们“坐着出租车到处跑”。"
"Ringing-up was quicker—was it?","如今打电话要快一些——是吗？"
"With endless vexations, he tracked down Sibley, Nazing, Upshire, Master, and half-a-dozen others of the elect.","历经无穷的烦恼之后，他找到了西伯莱、内津、厄普夏、马斯特以及其他六个被选定的人。"
"He struck a considered note likely to move them.","他用了一种经过深思熟虑的、可能打动他们的声调。"
"The book—he said—was bound to ‘get the goat of the old guard and the duds generally’; it would want a bit of drum-beating from the cognoscenti.","这本书——他说——一定会“惹恼那些保守派和废物们”，不过它需要鉴赏家们稍微鼓吹一下。"
"To each of them he appealed as the only one whose praise really mattered.","他向每一个人发出请求，让对方觉得唯有对方的赞扬才是至关重要的。"
"“If you haven’t reviewed the book, old chap, will you?","“如果你还没有评论过这本书，老朋友，请您评论一下好吗？"
"It’s you who count, of course.”","当然，您是最重要的。”"
"And to each he added: “I don’t care two straws whether it sells, but I do want old Wilfrid to get his due.”","而且他会对每一个人补充说：“我一点儿也不在乎这本书能否卖出去，但是我的确希望老威尔弗里德能够得到他应有的赞誉。”"
"And he meant it.","而且他是认真的。"
"The publisher in Michael was dead during that hour in the telephone booth, the friend alive and kicking hard.","在电话间里的那一个小时里，作为出版商的迈克尔死去了，作为朋友的迈克尔生龙活虎。"
"He came out with sweat running down his forehead, quite exhausted; and it was half-past five.","他出来的时候满头大汗，筋疲力尽。这时已经是5点半了。"
"‘Cup of tea—and home!’ he thought.","“喝杯茶——然后回家！”他想。"
"He reached his door at six.","他6点钟到了家门口。"
"Ting-a-ling, absolutely unimportant, was cowering in the far corner of the hall.","小叮铃，一点儿也不显眼，畏缩在门厅远端的角落里。"
"“What’s the matter, old man?”","“怎么了，老朋友？”"
"A sound from above, which made his blood run cold, answered—a long, low moaning.","楼上传来的声音回答了他，这声音使他毛骨悚然——一阵又长又低沉的呻吟声。"
"“Oh, God!” he gasped, and ran upstairs.","“哦，上帝！”他喘息着，跑上楼去。"
"Annette met him at the door.","在房门口安妮特遇见了他。"
"He was conscious of her speaking in French, of being called “mon cher,” of the words “vers trois heures....","他意识到她在说法语，在喊他“亲爱的”，还有几句话是“3点钟的时候…"
"The doctor says one must not worry—all goes for the best.”","医生说不用担心——一切都很好。”"
"Again that moan, and the door shut in his face; she was gone.","那种呻吟声又来了，房门在他面前关上了，她走了。"
"Michael remained standing on the rug with perfectly cold sweat oozing from him, and his nails dug deep into his palms.","迈克尔仍然站在小地毯上，浑身直冒冷汗，指甲深深地掐进掌心里。"
"‘This is how one becomes a father!’ he thought: ‘This is how I became a son!’","“这就是一个人怎样成为父亲的！”他想，“这就是我怎样成为儿子的！”"
"That moaning!","那呻吟声啊！"
"He could not bear to stay there, and he could not bear to go away.","留在这里，他受不了，离开这里，他也受不了。"
"It might be hours, yet!","也许还得好几个钟头呢！"
"He kept repeating to himself: “One must not worry—must not worry!”","他不断重复地对自己说：“不必担心——不必担心！”"
"How easily said!","说得容易！"
"How meaningless!","毫无意义！"
"His brain, his heart, ranging for relief, lighted on the strangest relief which could possibly have come to him.","他的大脑、他的心，正在寻求安慰，他突然想到他可能会遇到最奇怪的安慰。"
"Suppose this child being born, had not been his—had been—been Wilfrid’s; how would he have been feeling, here, outside this door?","假如这个即将出生的孩子，不是他的——而是——而是威尔弗里德的，那么他在这里，在门外，会有什么感觉呢？"
"It might—it might so easily have been—since nothing was sacred, now!","这可能——这可能很容易就是这个样子——因为现在，没有什么东西是神圣的！"
"Nothing except—yes, just that which was dearer than oneself—just that which was in there, moaning.","除了——是的，就是那种比自己还要宝贵的东西——就是那正在里面的呻吟声。"
"He could not bear it on the rug, and went downstairs.","他站在小毯子上实在忍受不了，便走下楼去。"
"Across and across the copper floor, a cigar in his mouth, he strode in vague, rebellious agony.","他在红棕色地板上走来走去，嘴里叼着雪茄，心里怀着模糊而又难以控制的极度痛苦。"
"Why should birth be like this?","为什么生孩子会是这样？"
"And the answer was: It isn’t—not in China!","而答案是：它不是这样的——在中国就不是这样的！"
"To have the creed that nothing mattered—and then run into it like this!","他一直怀有一切都不重要的信条——然而却遇上了这样的事情！"
"Something born at such a cost, must matter, should matter.","以这样的代价产生的事物，一定是重要的，也应该是重要的。"
"One must see to that!","必须注意到这一点！"
"Speculation ceased in Michael’s brain; he stood, listening terribly.","迈克尔的大脑停止了思考，他站在那里，仔细地听着。"
"Nothing!","什么声音也没有！"
"He could not bear it down there, and went up again.","他在楼下也忍不住了，又跑上楼来。"
"No sound at first, and then another moan!","一开始没有声音，然后又是一阵呻吟声！"
"This time he fled into his study, and ranged round the room, looking at the cartoons of Aubrey Greene.","这一次他逃进自己的书房里，在房间里兜圈子，眼睛看着奥布里·格林的那几幅漫画。"
"He did not see a single one, and suddenly bethought him of ‘Old Forsyte.’","他一幅也看不进去，突然他想起了“老福赛特”。"
"He ought to be told!","应该告诉他！"
"He rang up the ‘Connoisseurs,’ the ‘Remove,’ and his own father’s clubs, in case they might have gone there together after the meeting.","他打电话到“鉴赏家俱乐部”、“利姆夫俱乐部”以及他父亲的几个俱乐部，说不定开完会后他们一起上那里去了。"
"He drew blank everywhere.","所有的地方他都扑空了。"
"It was half-past seven.","现在已经7点半了。"
"How much longer was this going on?","这件事还要持续多长时间呢？"
"He went back to the bedroom door; could hear nothing.","他回到卧室门口，什么也听不见。"
"Then down again to the hall.","然后他又下楼来到门厅。"
"Ting-a-ling was lying by the front door, now.","这时，小叮铃正卧在前门旁边。"
"‘Fed-up!’ thought Michael, stroking his back, and mechanically clearing the letter-box.","“烦死了！”迈克尔想，他一边捶着背，一边机械地清理着信箱。"
"Just one letter—Wilfrid’s writing!","只有一封信——威尔弗里德的笔迹！"
"He took it to the foot of the stairs and read it with half his brain, the other half wondering—wandering up there.","他把信拿到楼梯脚下，他用一半的心思读着信，另一半则在琢磨——于是这样徘徊到楼上去了。"
"“DEAR MONT,—I start tomorrow to try and cross Arabia.","“亲爱的蒙特，我明天就要动身，试着去穿越阿拉伯半岛了。"
"I thought you might like a line in case Arabia crosses me.","我想万一我过不去的话，你或许愿意收到我的一封信。"
"I have recovered my senses.","我已经恢复了理智。"
"The air here is too clear for sentiment of any kind; and passion in exile soon becomes sickly.","这里的空气对于任何一种情感而言都太清新了。放逐的激情很快就变得令人厌恶了。"
"I am sorry I made you so much disturbance.","很抱歉我以前给你带去了那么多的烦恼。"
"It was a mistake for me to go back to England after the war, and hang about writing drivel for smart young women and inky folk to read.","战后我回到英国，无所事事，写了些幼稚无聊的东西给那些聪明的年轻女性和肚子里有点儿墨水的人看，这是一个错误。"
"Poor old England—she’s in for a bad time.","可怜的老英格兰——她正处于一个困难时期。"
"Give her my love; the same to yourselves.","向她问好，也向你问好。"
"“Yours ever,","你永远的，"
"“WILFRID DESERT. ","威尔弗里德·德赛特。"
"“P. S.—If you’ve published the things I left behind, send any royalties to me care of my governor.—W. D.”","附言——如果你已经把我留下的东西出版了，请将版税转交于家父。——威·德。”"
"Half Michael’s brain thought: ‘Well, that’s that!","迈克尔的一半心思在想：“哦，那样就对了！"
"And the book coming out today!’","这本书今天出版！”"
"Queer!","奇怪！"
"Was Wilfrid right—was it all a blooming gaff—the inky stream?","威尔弗里德说得对不对呢——这一切是不是一个彻底的骗局呢——舞文弄墨的潮流？"
"Was one just helping on England’s sickness?","人们只是在加重英国的弊病吗？"
"Ought they all to get on camels and ride the sun down?","他们大家应不应该都骑上骆驼，一直骑到日落呢？"
"And yet, in books were comfort and diversion; and they were wanted!","然而，书里有安慰和消遣的东西，这正是人们所需要的！"
"England had to go on—go on!","英国必须继续前进——继续前进！"
"‘No retreat, no retreat, they must conquer or die who have no retreat!’...","“没有退路，没有退路，没有退路的人必须获胜，否则就是死路一条……”"
"God!","上帝啊！"
"There it was again!","那个声音又来了！"
"Back he flew upstairs, with his ears covered and his eyes wild.","他飞快地跑回楼上，双手捂着耳朵，眼睛像发疯一样。"
"The sounds ceased; Annette came out to him.","那个声音停止了，安妮特出来找他。"
"“Her father, mon cher; try to find her father!”","“她的父亲，亲爱的，想办法找到她的父亲！”"
"“I have—I can’t!” gasped Michael.","“我找过了——找不到！”迈克尔气喘吁吁地说。"
"“Try Green Street—Mrs. Dartie.","“试试格林街——达尔迪夫人那里。"
"Courage!","勇敢点儿！"
"All is normal—it will be quite sewn, now.”","一切正常——快好了，现在。”"
"When he had rung up Green Street and been answered at last, he sat with the door of his study open, waiting for ‘Old Forsyte’ to come.","当他打电话到格林街，终于得到回音之后，他打开书房的门，坐在那里等着“老福赛特”到来。"
"Half his sight remarked a round hole burnt in his trouser leg—he hadn’t even noticed the smell; hadn’t even realised that he had been smoking.","他的余光看到他的裤腿上烧了一个圆圆的洞——他甚至连烧焦的气味都没闻到，甚至没有意识到自己在抽烟。"
"He must pull himself together for the ‘old man.’","他必须振作起来，迎接这位“老头”。"
"He heard the bell ring, and ran down to open.","他听到门铃响了，便跑下楼去开门。"
"“Well?” said Soames.","“怎么样？”索姆斯说。"
"“Not yet, sir.","“还没生呢，先生。"
"Come up to my study.","上楼到我的书房去吧。"
"It’s nearer.”","那里比较近。”"
"They went up side by side.","他们肩并肩地走上楼去。"
"That trim grey head, with the deep furrow between the eyes, and those eyes staring as if at pain behind them, steadied Michael.","老人整齐而斑白的头发，两眼之间深深的皱纹，双眼仿佛凝视着隐藏在它们后面的痛苦，这一切使迈克尔镇定了下来。"
"Poor old chap!","可怜的老人家！"
"He was ‘for it,’ too!","他也在“为此担心”呢！"
"They were both on ‘their uppers!’","他们俩都“处于困境”了！"
"“Have a peg, sir?","“喝点儿饮料好吗，先生？"
"I’ve got brandy here.”","我这里有白兰地。”"
"“Yes,” said Soames.","“好的，”索姆斯说，"
"“Anything.”","“什么都行。”"
"With the brandies in their hands, half-raised, they listened—jerked their hands up, drank.","他们手里拿着白兰地，半举着杯子，耳朵倾听着——手猛地往上一抬，喝了下去。"
"They were automatic, like two doll figures worked by the same string.","他们都是无意识的，就像由一根绳子牵着的两个木偶似的。"
"“Cigarette, sir?” said Michael.","“抽烟吗，先生？”迈克尔说。"
"Soames nodded.","索姆斯点点头。"
"With the lighted cigarettes just not in their mouths, they listened, put them in, took them out, puffed smoke.","他点着香烟却并没有放进嘴里，他们倾听着，之后将香烟放进嘴里，拿出来，喷出烟雾。"
"Michael had his right arm tight across his chest.","迈克尔把右胳膊紧紧地放在自己的胸前。"
"Soames his left.","索姆斯的左胳膊也是如此。"
"They formed a pattern, thus, side by side.","就这样，他们肩并肩地坐着，构成了一幅图案。"
"“Bad to stick, sir.","“真难熬，先生。"
"Sorry!”","抱歉！”"
"Soames nodded.","索姆斯点点头。"
"His teeth were clenched.","他紧紧地咬着牙。"
"Suddenly his hand relaxed.","突然他的手放松了。"
"“Listen!” he said.","“听！”他说。"
"Sounds—different—confused!","许多声音——不同的声音——非常混乱！"
"Michael’s hand seized something, gripped it hard; it was cold, thin—the hand of Soames.","迈克尔的手抓住了什么东西，紧紧地握着。那东西冰冷枯瘦——那是索姆斯的手。"
"They sat thus, hand in hand, staring at the doorway, for how long neither knew.","他们就这样坐着，手握着手，眼睛盯着门口，谁也不知道过了多长时间。"
"Suddenly that doorway darkened; a figure in grey stood there—Annette!","突然门口的光线变暗了，一个穿着灰色衣服的人站在那里——安妮特！"
"“It is all r-right!","“一切顺——顺利！"
"A son!”","是个儿子！”"

"Chapter XV","第十五章"
"Calm","风平浪静"
"On waking from deep sleep next morning, Michael’s first thought was: ‘Fleur is back!’","第二天早上，迈克尔从酣睡中醒来，他的第一个念头就是：“弗勒回来了！”"
"He then remembered.","随后他记起来了。"
"To his: “O. K.?” whispered at her door, he received an emphatic nod from the nurse.","他在她的房门口低声问道：“都还好吗？”护士对他有力地点了点头。"
"In the midst of excited expectation he retained enough modernity to think: ‘No more blurb!","在兴奋的期待中，他保持着足够的现代观念在想：“别再废话了！"
"Go and eat your breakfast quietly!’","安安静静地去吃早饭吧！”"
"In the dining-room Soames was despising the broken egg before him.","在餐厅里，索姆斯正在用一种鄙视的神情看着他面前的那个磕开了的鸡蛋。"
"He looked up as Michael entered, and buried his face in his cup.","迈克尔进来的时候，他抬头看了一眼，然后就把脸埋在了杯子里。"
"Michael understood perfectly; they had sat hand in hand!","迈克尔完全明白，他们曾手握手地坐着！"
"He saw, too, that the journal opened by his plate was of a financial nature.","他还看到在他的盘子旁边打开的那份报纸是金融刊物。"
"“Anything about the meeting, sir?","“有关于股东大会的消息吗，先生？"
"Your speech must read like one o’clock!”","您的那篇演讲读起来一定津津有味！”"
"With a queer little sound Soames held out the paper.","索姆斯发出一小声奇怪的声音，把报纸递给了他。"
"The headlines ran: “Stormy meeting—resignation of two directors—a vote of confidence.”","标题写着：“激烈的会议——两名董事辞职——投信任票。”"
"Michael skimmed down till he came to:","迈克尔粗略地浏览下去，直到他看到："
"“Mr. Forsyte, the director involved, in a speech of some length, said he had no intention of singing small.","“与此事有关的一位董事，福赛特先生，在一篇相当长的讲话中，说他不打算变得沉默寡言。"
"He deprecated the behaviour of the shareholders; he had not been accustomed to meet with suspicions.","他反对股东们的行为，他不习惯受到怀疑。"
"He tendered his resignation.”","他提出了辞职。”"
"Michael dropped the sheet.","迈克尔放下了报纸。"
"“By Jove!” he said—”Involved—suspicions.’","“天啊！”他说——“‘有关的——怀疑。’"
"They’ve given it a turn, as though—!”","他们把事情弄颠倒了，好像——！”"
"“The papers!” said Soames, and resumed his egg.","“这些报纸！”索姆斯说着，又继续吃鸡蛋。"
"Michael sat down, and stripped the skin off a banana.","迈克尔坐了下来，剥掉香蕉皮。"
"‘“Nothing became him like his death,”’ he thought: ‘Poor old boy!’","“‘他真是视死如归啊，’”他想，“可怜的老头！”"
"“Well, sir,” he said, “I was there, and all I can say is: You and my father were the only two people who excited my respect.”","“哦，先生，”他说，“我当时在场，我所能说的是：只有您和我的父亲两个人让我尊敬。”"
"“That!” said Soames, putting down his spoon.","“是吗！”索姆斯说着，放下了他的勺子。"
"Michael perceived that he wished to be alone, and swallowing the banana, went to his study.","迈克尔感觉到他想一个人呆一会儿，于是他吞下那只香蕉，到书房去了。"
"Waiting for his summons, he rang up his father.","他在等着被召唤的同时，给他爸爸打了一个电话。"
"“None the worse for yesterday, sir?”","“昨天还好吧，先生？”"
"Sir Lawrence’s voice came clear and thin, rather high.","劳伦斯爵士的声音又清晰又尖细，声调相当高。"
"“Poorer and wiser.","“更穷了，但也更聪明了。"
"What’s the bulletin?”","情况怎么样？”"
"“Top-hole.”","“非常好。”"
"“Our love to both.","“替我们向母子俩问好。"
"Your mother wants to know if he has any hair?”","你母亲想知道他有没有头发？”"
"“Haven’t seen him yet.","“我还没有看到他呢。"
"I’m just going.”","我正要去呢。”"
"Annette, indeed, was beckoning him from the doorway.","的确，安妮特正在门口召唤他呢。"
"“She wants you to bring the little dog, mon cher.”","“她想让你把小狗带过来，亲爱的。”"
"With Ting-a-ling under his arm, and treading on tiptoe, Michael entered.","迈克尔抱着小叮铃，踮着脚尖，走了进去。"
"The eleventh baronet!","第十一代准男爵！"
"He did not seem to amount to much, beneath her head bent over him.","在她俯着的头下面，他看起来不太起眼。 "
"And surely her hair was darker!","她头发的颜色的确比较深！"
"He walked up to the bed, and touched it reverently.","他走到床边，恭敬地抚摸着。"
"Fleur raised her head, and revealed the baby sucking vigorously at her little finger.","弗勒抬起头，露出正在使劲吮吸她的小手指的婴儿。"
"“Isn’t he a monkey?” said her faint voice.","“他不就是一只猴子吗？”她那微弱的声音说道。"
"Michael nodded.","迈克尔点点头。"
"A monkey clearly—but whether white—that was the question!","明显是只猴子——但不是白色的——那是关键问题！"
"“And you, sweetheart?”","“你怎么样，亲爱的？”"
"“All right now, but it was—” She drew her breath in, and her eyes darkened: “Ting, look!”","“现在好了，但是那时——”她吸了一口气，她眼睛的颜色变深了，“丁，看啊！”"
"The Chinese dog, with nostrils delicately moving, drew backward under Michael’s arm.","这只中国狗，鼻孔微微地翕动着，在迈克尔的胳膊下往后缩。"
"His whole demeanour displayed a knowing criticism.","他的全部举动都表现出一种无所不知的评论。"
"“Puppies,” he seemed to say, “we do it in China.","“小狗嘛，”他仿佛在说，“我们在中国也是这样的。"
"Judgment reserved!”","我保留意见！”"
"“What eyes!” said Michael: “We needn’t tell HIM that this was brought from Chelsea by the doctor.”","“多么明亮的眼睛啊！”迈克尔说，“我们不必告诉它，这是医生从切尔西带来的。”"
"Fleur gave the tiniest laugh.","弗勒发出极为微弱的笑声。"
"“Put him down, Michael.”","“把它放下吧，迈克尔。”"
"Michael put him down, and he went to his corner.","迈克尔把它放下来，然后它就跑到自己的角落里去了。"
"“I mustn’t talk,” said Fleur, “but I want to, frightfully; as if I’d been dumb for months.”","“我不能说话，”弗勒说，“但是我非常想说话，好像我已经好几个月没有说话了。”"
"‘Just as I felt,’ thought Michael, ‘she’s been away, away somewhere, utterly away.’","“就像我的感觉一样，”迈克尔想，“她好像离开了，去了某个地方，彻底离开了。”"
"“It was like being held down, Michael.","“就像是被抑制住了，迈克尔。"
"Months of not being yourself.”","好几个月都身不由己。”"
"Michael said softly: “Yes! the process IS behind the times!","迈克尔温柔地说：“是啊！这一过程太漫长了！"
"Has he got any hair?","他有头发吗？"
"My mother wants to know.”","我母亲想知道。”"
"Fleur revealed the head of the eleventh baronet, covered with dark down.","弗勒露出了第十一代准男爵的头，上面覆盖着一层深色的绒毛。"
"“Like my grandmother’s; but it’ll get lighter.","“就像我祖母的头发，但是它会变浅的。"
"His eyes are going to be grey.","他的眼睛会变成灰色的。"
"Oh! and, Michael, about godparents?","哦！还有，迈克尔，关于教父教母怎么办？"
"Alison, of course—but men?”","艾莉森，当然啦——但是男的呢？”"
"Michael dwelled a little before answering:","迈克尔稍微思考了一下回答道："
"“I had a letter from Wilfrid yesterday.","“我昨天收到了威尔弗里德的来信。"
"Would you like him?","你想让他做吗？"
"He’s still out there, but I could hold the sponge for him in church.”","他还在国外，但是我可以在教堂里代表他拿海绵。”"
"“Is he all right again?”","“他恢复过来了吗？”"
"“He says so.”","“他是这么说的。”"
"He could not read the expression of her eyes, but her lips were pouted slightly.","他看不懂她眼中的表情，但是她的嘴唇微微撅了起来。"
"“Yes,” she said: “and I think one’s enough, don’t you?","“好的，”她说，“而且我认为一个就够了，你觉得呢？"
"Mine never gave me anything.”","我的教父从来没有给过我什么。”"
"“One of mine gave me a bible, and the other gave me a wigging.","“我的一个教父给了我一本圣经，另一个给了我一顿责骂。"
"Wilfrid, then.”","那么，就威尔弗里德吧。”"
"And he bent over her.","说着他朝她俯下身。"
"Her eyes seemed to make him a little ironic apology.","她的眼睛似乎向他表达了一丝略带讽刺的歉意。"
"He kissed her hair, and moved hurriedly away.","他吻了吻她的头发，就匆忙离开了。"
"By the door Soames was standing, awaiting his turn.","索姆斯站在门口，等着轮到他。"
"“Just a minute only, sir,” the nurse was saying.","“只能呆一分钟，先生。”护士说。"
"Soames walked up to the bedside, and stood looking at his daughter.","索姆斯走到床边，站在那里看着他的女儿。"
"“Dad, dear!”","“爸爸，亲爱的！”"
"Michael heard her say.","迈克尔听到她说。"
"Soames just touched her hand, nodded, as if implying approval of the baby, and came walking back, but, in a mirror, Michael saw his lips quivering.","索姆斯只是摸了摸她的手，点了点头，仿佛是在对这个婴儿表示赞许，然后就走了出来，但是，在镜子里，迈克尔看到他的嘴唇在颤抖。"
"On the ground floor once more, he had the most intense desire to sing.","再次回到一楼，他有一种强烈的想唱歌的渴望。"
"It would not do; and, entering the Chinese room, he stood staring out into the sunlit square.","这样不行，于是，他走进那个中式的房间，站在那里凝视着阳光普照的广场。"
"Gosh!","天啊！"
"It was good to be alive!","活着真好！"
"Say what you liked, you couldn’t beat it!","可以敞开心扉，但你无法逃避生活！"
"They might turn their noses up at life, and look down them at it; they might bolster up the future and the past, but—give him the present!","人们可能会对生活嗤之以鼻，看不起它；人们可以相信未来或者过去，但是——他只能拥有现在！"
"‘I’ll have that white monkey up again!’ he thought.","“我要把那幅白猿再挂起来！”他想，"
"‘I’ll see the brute further before he shall depress me!’","“我要趁它使我沮丧之前再好好看看这只畜生！”"
"He went out to a closet under the stairs, and, from beneath four pairs of curtains done up in moth-preserver and brown paper, took out the picture.","他走到楼梯下面的小房间里，然后，从用防蛀虫纸和牛皮纸包裹着的四对窗帘下面，拿出了那幅画。"
"He held it away from him in the dim light.","在微弱的灯光下，他把那幅画拿得远一点儿去看。"
"The creature’s eyes!","这只畜生的眼睛啊！"
"It was all in those eyes!","一切都在那双眼睛里！"
"“Never mind, old son!” he said: “Up you go!”","“没关系，老家伙！”他说，“你上去吧！”"
"And he carried it into the Chinese room.","于是他把它带到那个中国式的房间里去了。"
"Soames was there.","索姆斯在那里。"
"“I’m going to put him up again, sir.”","“我打算把它再挂起来，先生。”"
"Soames nodded.","索姆斯点点头。"
"“Would you hold him, while I hook the wire?”","“我把线挂上去，请您拿一下好吗？”"
"Soames held the picture.","索姆斯拿着这幅画。"
"Returning to the copper floor, Michael said:","迈克尔回到红棕色地板上，说："
"“All right, sir!” and stood back.","“好了，先生！”然后退后一步观画。"
"Soames joined him.","索姆斯和他站在一起。"
"Side by side they contemplated the white monkey.","他们肩并肩地一起注视着这只白猿。"
"“He won’t be happy till he gets it,” said Michael at last: “The only thing is, you see, he doesn’t know what IT is.”","“得不到他要的，它是不会高兴的，”最后迈克尔说，“唯一的问题是，你看，它不知道那东西究竟是什么。”"
